
-----title
开封 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fc753111158a4f2eb8f28365b5c30abb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc753111158a4f2eb8f28365b5c30abb");'><span id='fc753111158a4f2eb8f28365b5c30abb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=1000')">985-1000年</a>，1-16岁</div><div id='fc753111158a4f2eb8f28365b5c30abb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年9月</a>　九月，出生于开封。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=987')">986-987年</a>　本年，居开封？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，居开封？从师读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=990')">989-990年</a>　本年，居开封？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>　本年，居开封？学作诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年</a>　本年，居开封？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>　本年，居开封，学作赋，游太学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　本年，居开封？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=995&endYear=995')">995年</a>　本年，居开封？学作文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=996&endYear=996')">996年</a>　本年，在开封从学于姚铉，作《水赋》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=996&endYear=996')">996年</a>　本年，在开封作《放宫人赋》作品：放宫人赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《文庄集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1153382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>放宫人赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以宫阙幽闭，晓然情惬为韵。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（996年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153382")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153382'>隋失民望，唐开帝功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153382_comment'></div>降凤诏于丹陛，出娥眉于六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153382_comment'></div>夜雨未回，俨鬓云于帘户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153382_comment'></div>秋风渐老，失钗燕于房栊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153382_comment'></div>当其凤历频移，重门久闭，蚁聚螓首，帷连彩袂，步金莲而共叹无偶，对鸳瓦而徒伤失俪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153382_comment'></div>花冠不整，笼虿发以全疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153382_comment'></div>柳带低垂，映蜂腰而更细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153382_comment'></div>太宗于是矜绝态，轸深情，旧苑而何伤幽闭，新恩而尽放轻盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153382_comment'></div>莫不喜极如梦，心摇若惊，踟蹰而玉趾无力，盼眄而横波渐倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153382_comment'></div>鸾鉴重开，已有归鸿之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153382_comment'></div>凤笙将罢，皆为别鹤之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153382_comment'></div>于时银箭初残，琼宫乍晓，星眸争别于天仗，莲脸竞辞于庭沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153382_comment'></div>行分而掖路深沉，步缓而回廊缭绕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153382_comment'></div>嫦娥偷药，几年而不出蟾宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153382_comment'></div>辽鹤辞家，一旦而却归华表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153382_comment'></div>茍非帝德从俭，皇情烛幽，又焉得离永巷，别长秋，指燕赵之归路，望荆吴之故州？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153382_comment'></div>算回程而靥带新喜，思往事而眉含旧愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153382_comment'></div>罗衣而飐滟，轻云竞归巫峡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153382_comment'></div>宾髻而屈盘，娇凤争下秦楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153382_comment'></div>或绣辇香车，兰舟桂楫，指故里以思动，涉长途而意惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153382_comment'></div>飞腾自适，既疑齐女之蝉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153382_comment'></div>梦幻堪惊，且悟庄周之蝶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153382_comment'></div>已而别馆凄尔，离宫寂然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153382_comment'></div>动兰烛于残照，蔼薰笼于夕烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153382_comment'></div>萧条而竹换筠粉，</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1153382'>落而苔侵翠钿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153382_comment'></div>天上和风，送神仙之二八；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153382_comment'></div>人间丽日，迎桃李之三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153382_comment'></div>美夫入昏主之宫，出明君之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153382_comment'></div>千门而绮焕裳锦，九禁而云销鬓发，故宜其贝齿朱唇，歌太平之日月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1153382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=1000')">997-1000年</a>　本年，居开封？<br /></div><div class='label1' id='67d54f950d6b44e2933b4a14a5242d82_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("67d54f950d6b44e2933b4a14a5242d82");'><span id='67d54f950d6b44e2933b4a14a5242d82_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1005')">1002-1005年</a>，18-21岁</div><div id='67d54f950d6b44e2933b4a14a5242d82' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1003')">1002-1003年</a>　本年，居开封？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　本年，居开封，上书开封府长官，乞应举。作品：上开封府廉献书。<div id='poem_1153828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上开封府廉献书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153828")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153828'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153828'>伏以国家因袭唐制，小宗伯岁贡多士，率以至公之器，裁为慎选之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153828_comment'></div>而尚士流私议，泥而不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153828_comment'></div>身处孤寒，则望权门而怨豪族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153828_comment'></div>名籍礼部，则陵后生而幸青紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153828_comment'></div>故贤能之书未上，而毁訾之言已满，殊不问其艺如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153828_comment'></div>某以为银黄之族不无材智，金玉之室亦有忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153828_comment'></div>夫以乘黄越国，岂待十驾而迈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153828_comment'></div>逄蒙射鹄，何须再发而中？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153828_comment'></div>是以林居野处，不足以自贤，三应五上，不足以自贵，惟善之所在尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153828_comment'></div>但孤进有材，则居豪右之上，鼎族多艺，则冠士流之首，又何待略践场屋，多历年所，而后预等甲英杰者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153828_comment'></div>故某居寒贱未尝怨，肩隽造未尝忧，诚以公道有所属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153828_comment'></div>今伏遇执事斡张斯文，采撷英特，岂敢自昧默而不言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153828_comment'></div>伏念某四岁从师读书，七岁学诗，九岁学赋，十有一而学文，奈何天陋其辞，不能脱颖而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153828_comment'></div>今年甫冠带，方敢抱所有，冒乡举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153828_comment'></div>茍执事照之以龟鉴，量之以公器，哀其说，右其技，得致师文阵，贾其馀勇，辉焕士林，飞跃亨衢，则执事之惠非止谓生死而肉骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153828_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153828_comment'></div>以先王仁义之道取我者，我当以先王仁义之道报之，岂敢引蛇雀故事，饰为虚言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153828_comment'></div>惟执事者裁察之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1153828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　秋，在开封府举进士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年11月</a>　十一月，居开封，父夏承皓与契丹战，殁于大名府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年1月</a>　正月，居开封，以父战殁，被录为三班差使，因献诗宰相，改授润州丹阳县主簿。作品：野步。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三二。魏泰《东轩笔录》卷二谓夏竦以献诗李沆而改官，误。夏承皓殁于上年十一月，夏竦本年正月始得三班奉职，而李沆卒于上年七月（《续资治通鉴长编》卷五六）。）</span><div id='poem_193435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>野步</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193435")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193435'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193435'>顾步方塘上，西郊日渐曛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193435'>归心临远渡，晚色在闲云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193435'>垄势蜂腰接，溪流燕尾分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193435'>田歌知有意，丰美谢明君<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193435'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193435'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193435_0'>⑴ 原注：谨案《东轩笔录》云：夏竦以父殁王事，得三班差使。然自少好读书，工为诗。一日携所业，伺宰相李文靖沆退朝，拜于马首而献之。文靖读其诗，有山势蜂腰断，溪流燕尾分之句，深爱之，终卷皆佳句。翌日袖其诗呈真宗，及叙死事之后，乞与换文资，遂改润州金坛主簿。据此，则沆所见乃《野步》诗也。其改垄势为山势，改接为断，或《东轩笔录》得于传闻，故有不同耳。至厉鹗《宋诗纪事》但存山势二句，而不载全诗，则以未见竦集故也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193435_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='17e6603c9d024afe9d34daa22f299bf5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("17e6603c9d024afe9d34daa22f299bf5");'><span id='17e6603c9d024afe9d34daa22f299bf5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>，23岁</div><div id='17e6603c9d024afe9d34daa22f299bf5' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>闰五月七日，在京应贤良方正、能直言极谏制举，入第四次等，擢光禄寺丞，通判台州。作品：崇政殿御试贤良方正能直言极谏科制策。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一二。授官事参王德保、张丽《北宋前期四重臣与江西文化的兴盛》，中国社会科学出版社2012年版，第69页。）</span><div id='poem_1153697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>崇政殿御试贤良方正能直言极谏科制策</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年闰5月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153697")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153697'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153697'>皇帝若曰：朕克谨承先训，惟怀永图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153697_comment'></div>期化成于人文，实顺考于古道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153697_comment'></div>尚虑视听不广，心志未明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153697_comment'></div>寤寐增勤，忠规是伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153697_comment'></div>所以博延髦士，庶获嘉谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153697_comment'></div>昔姬德之隆，《周官》爰作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153697_comment'></div>建中立极，经世惠民，乃致颂声，以措刑辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153697_comment'></div>王风不竞，战国交兴，理贵从宜，俗多变古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153697_comment'></div>炎汉政令，十《志》粗存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153697_comment'></div>有唐宪章，《六典》备载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153697_comment'></div>既沿革而不一，亮损益之可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153697_comment'></div>曲礼三千，经礼三百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153697_comment'></div>虽难尽举，聊为敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153697_comment'></div>施之于今，往古之事何允；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153697_comment'></div>揆之于古，方今之法孰非？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153697_comment'></div>当商搉其大猷，无自执于小道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153697_comment'></div>仲尼之志，在乎《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153697_comment'></div>考旧史之文，明将来之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153697_comment'></div>授经左氏，发凡变例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153697_comment'></div>善恶必显，惩劝在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153697_comment'></div>由是后王，遵为彝训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153697_comment'></div>至若朝聘祭祀之礼，刑赏兵农之政，君臣励翼之迹，官司寅亮之辞，或可举而行，当直书其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153697_comment'></div>惟菁英而是取，顾糟粕而罔陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153697_comment'></div>六籍之存，日星是喻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153697_comment'></div>百氏之说，爝火攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153697_comment'></div>恶实尚华，寔繁厥类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153697_comment'></div>斲雕为朴，岂无其时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153697_comment'></div>欲使荐绅之民，并宗经术；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153697_comment'></div>青衿之士，专习圣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153697_comment'></div>能黜异端，渴闻谠论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153697_comment'></div>贡举之设，茂异斯求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153697_comment'></div>爰自唐朝，独考辞赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153697_comment'></div>虽云小辨破道，壮夫耻为，然而定妍否于有司，观工拙于作者，茍或舍兹衡石，诚虑失之毫釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153697_comment'></div>将俾俊乂用章，文风丕变，其用何术，以副虚怀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153697_comment'></div>《礼》有四民，农居其一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153697_comment'></div>《书》有八政，食在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153697_comment'></div>务劝力耕，亮由薄敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153697_comment'></div>或轻其赋调，即邦家之用不充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153697_comment'></div>或重彼科役，即编氓之力弥困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153697_comment'></div>至于榷酤之法，关市之征，将以惠人，亦思省去，复虑经费不给，游惰寖多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153697_comment'></div>盖欲蠲复民租，不禁山泽，而使野无旷土，府有羡财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153697_comment'></div>下靡趋于末利，上益丰于储蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153697_comment'></div>必有说也，宜无隐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153697_comment'></div>宰字之任，蒸黎所托，在乎铨择，尤所注怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153697_comment'></div>亦尝阅考绩于明廷，听保任于端士，暨于莅职，继以败官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153697_comment'></div>或边幅罔修，簠簋靡洁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153697_comment'></div>或佩韦罕诫，冠虎是侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153697_comment'></div>虽国有常刑，然民已受弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153697_comment'></div>今若峻其督责，必兴叹于凝脂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153697_comment'></div>缓彼简书，将漏罪于疏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153697_comment'></div>水火相济，琴瑟更张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153697_comment'></div>尔其谓何，子实翘想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153697_comment'></div>缅惟致治，诚在得贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153697_comment'></div>每恐下僚，寔沈英彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153697_comment'></div>或以类举，或自荐升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153697_comment'></div>负廉隅清白之名，常从加等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153697_comment'></div>驰干蛊端方之誉，亦示峻迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153697_comment'></div>然而鲜睹徇公，颇闻滥进，始由朋党，终陷刑章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153697_comment'></div>言念于兹，夙夜无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153697_comment'></div>欲使怀材者必达，荐士者绝私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153697_comment'></div>奏牍上陈，美恶可复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153697_comment'></div>爵赏下降，名实罔违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153697_comment'></div>极言澄汰之方，用资宵旰之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153697_comment'></div>矧子大夫蕴蓄器业，洞明政经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153697_comment'></div>副我详延，森然就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153697_comment'></div>靡悼后患，咸罄昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153697_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1153697'>对曰：臣闻百王公共不易之道者，惟谏而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153697_comment'></div>古者致治之君，莫不欲良臣在廷，忠言日至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153697_comment'></div>揭进善之旌，设敢谏之鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153697_comment'></div>太史陈诗以刺，百工执技以谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153697_comment'></div>暨汉孝文二年，始下贤良之诏，开纳言不讳之路，延直诚切谏之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153697_comment'></div>访天时之灾异，问朝政之阙失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153697_comment'></div>国家宅有神器，五十年间，上无逸德，下无遗政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153697_comment'></div>而陛下尚虑视听未广，心志未明，高张六科，躬访时事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153697_comment'></div>诚臣以济民利国之策，干陛下之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153697_comment'></div>臣生逢太平，幼读方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153697_comment'></div>睹盛衰治乱之际，未尝不愤悱而握卷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153697_comment'></div>闻忠蹇鲠直之风，未尝不激厉而抗节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153697_comment'></div>今幸以区区之学，应直言之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153697_comment'></div>有司不以臣之不材，升之于相府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153697_comment'></div>三公不以臣之不材，进之于外廷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153697_comment'></div>陛下不以臣之不材，问之于丹陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153697_comment'></div>敢不抉胸膈之所虑，尽耳目之所见，谨昧死上对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「昔姬德之隆，《周官》爰作，建中立极，经世惠民，乃致颂声，以措刑辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153697_comment'></div>王风不竞，战国交兴，理贵从宜，俗多变古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153697_comment'></div>炎汉政令，十《志》具存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153697_comment'></div>有唐宪章，《六典》备载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153697_comment'></div>既沿革而不一，亮损益而可知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻周监二代，文物周旋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153697_comment'></div>姬旦践阼，宪章昭备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153697_comment'></div>诏六官以政令，建五等以亲贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153697_comment'></div>礼行三雍，法垂象魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153697_comment'></div>故文武创业而臣工作颂，成康致治而刑措不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153697_comment'></div>洎平王东迁，皇纲解纽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153697_comment'></div>《黍离》之什，下列《国风》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153697_comment'></div>尔后九鼎渐轻，七雄分竞，强吞弱吐，干戈日寻，合从连衡，谈说锋起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153697_comment'></div>至有变衣裳以从俗，峻法令以任权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153697_comment'></div>轻忠信而重要约，坏井田而立阡陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153697_comment'></div>官不择行而择言，爵不尚贤而尚贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153697_comment'></div>事叛于古，败乱相乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153697_comment'></div>洎秦鹿野死，汉龙天飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153697_comment'></div>萧何约九章之法，叔孙制绵蕝之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153697_comment'></div>律历精密于盈虚，郊祀周旋于坛畤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153697_comment'></div>分郡国以王宗支，制歌舞以象功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153697_comment'></div>殊庸茂实，际天接地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153697_comment'></div>故朝廷之制，十《志》在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153697_comment'></div>洎三国分土，礼乐无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153697_comment'></div>垂数百载，而唐有天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153697_comment'></div>房杜议其律令，马周陈其法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153697_comment'></div>致太平于贞观，制礼乐于开元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153697_comment'></div>分爵九等，品有正从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153697_comment'></div>故职官之制，《六典》备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153697_comment'></div>今陛下问其沿革，询其损益，其将有所发于天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153697_comment'></div>臣愿朝廷鉴历代之所短，举唐汉之所长，文者损之，急者宽之，过者抑之，不至者进之，则古今之美，无不济于下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「曲礼三千，经礼三百，虽难备举，聊为敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153697_comment'></div>施之于今，往古之事何允；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153697_comment'></div>揆之于古，方今之法孰非？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153697_comment'></div>当商榷其大猷，无自执于小道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻先王本太一之道，观羔雁之象，制威仪三千，礼仪三百，所以教天下之恭让，闲万民之非辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153697_comment'></div>聊敷其要，盖有五焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153697_comment'></div>《记》曰：「礼，时为大，顺次之，体次之，宜次之，称次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153697_comment'></div>尧授舜，舜授禹，汤放桀，武王伐纣，时也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153697_comment'></div>天地之祭，宗庙之事，父子之道，君臣之义，伦也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153697_comment'></div>社稷山川之事，鬼神之祭，体也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153697_comment'></div>丧祭之用，宾客之交，义也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153697_comment'></div>羔豚而祭，百官皆足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153697_comment'></div>太牢而祭，不必有馀，称也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1153697_comment'></div>若穷礼乐之沿革，揆古今之得失，则上世帝王不相沿袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1153697_comment'></div>功成作乐，治定制礼，虽从宜而立法，必师古而可久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1153697_comment'></div>国家受天承命，造我区夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1153697_comment'></div>远观八世之典，近取开元之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1153697_comment'></div>文物之盛，流芬简策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1153697_comment'></div>但太常工师或怠其习，朝廷服章未明其列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1153697_comment'></div>珩璜之声不闻，豆笾之器罕用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1153697_comment'></div>鉴往观来，其仪可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1153697_comment'></div>今陛下富天启之资，有承平之业，固当制礼乐，易服色，定官名，发号令，建中于千古之上，立极于百代之下，则泥金勒玉，不足记其功德矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「仲尼之志在乎《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1153697_comment'></div>考旧史之文，明将来之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1153697_comment'></div>授经左氏，发凡变例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1153697_comment'></div>善恶必显，惩劝在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1153697_comment'></div>由是后王，遵为彝训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1153697_comment'></div>至若朝聘祭祀之礼，刑赏兵农之政，君臣励翼之迹，官师寅亮之辞，或可举而行，当直书其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1153697_comment'></div>惟菁英而是取，顾糟粕而罔陈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻周室将微，诸侯叛命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1153697_comment'></div>圣人有作，王文爰启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1153697_comment'></div>发周公之凡例，载鲁史之行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1153697_comment'></div>笔削既至，臣子皆惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1153697_comment'></div>故为列辟之彝章，王道之准的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1153697_comment'></div>汉氏有命，斯文盛行，朝廷诏诰，公卿章疏，必引经传，为事规矩，故历祚悠远，法度可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1153697_comment'></div>尔后中原多故，编简不完，有国之君，不遑逮此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1153697_comment'></div>国家兴起四方，穆清治本，建藏书之策，立雠校之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1153697_comment'></div>陛下旰食视事，乙夜观书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1153697_comment'></div>故下问小臣以大义，抉六经之奥秘，观百王之明睿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1153697_comment'></div>臣幼习史氏，颇详其学，以为丘明之传，繁富而诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1153697_comment'></div>臣请以经义条对如左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻朝以修制，聘以结好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1153697_comment'></div>时会以发四方之禁，间问以谕诸侯之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1153697_comment'></div>表著以昭序，玉帛以修贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1153697_comment'></div>考其道则在乎明班制而不僭，整威仪而可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1153697_comment'></div>动必以礼，不失其物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1153697_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》书「春，滕侯、薛侯来朝」者，天子无事，诸侯相朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1153697_comment'></div>书时者，美其正也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1153697_comment'></div>书「荆人来聘」者，荆，夷狄也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1153697_comment'></div>书人者，美其始能聘也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1153697_comment'></div>书「介葛卢来」，而不书朝者，以微国不能行其礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻祭以追养，祀以驭神，圣人为能飨帝，孝子为能飨亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1153697_comment'></div>外则尽物而献诚，内则尽诚而献礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1153697_comment'></div>备其馨香，奉以圭璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1153697_comment'></div>然则祭不欲黩，黩则不恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1153697_comment'></div>祀不欲烦，烦则不歆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1153697_comment'></div>谨按《春秋》书「春正月己卯烝」者，讥其数也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1153697_comment'></div>书「夏五月丁丑烝」，讥不时也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1153697_comment'></div>书「犹三望」者，犹者可止之辞也，讥其不知礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻刑赏者，国家之二柄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1153697_comment'></div>驭其有罪，则有刑赎废夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1153697_comment'></div>《语》曰「齐之以刑」，《书》曰「金作赎刑」，《周礼》曰「夺，以驭其贫」，「废，以驭其罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1153697_comment'></div>懋其有功，则有爵禄车服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1153697_comment'></div>《周礼》曰「爵以驭其贵」，「禄以驭其富」，《书》曰「车服以庸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1153697_comment'></div>盖刑者所罚寡而所戒众，赏者所费小而所劝大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1153697_comment'></div>故古者刑以秋冬，象天之瘁物也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1153697_comment'></div>赏以春夏，象天之惠物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1153697_comment'></div>然则刑之大要在乎去奸宄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1153697_comment'></div>奸宄不去，则罚失矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1153697_comment'></div>罚失则滥，滥则民不从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1153697_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》桓公之世，经不书「王」者，讥上之不能讨其罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1153697_comment'></div>赏之大要在正礼制，礼制不正，则劝失矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1153697_comment'></div>劝失则僭，僭则民不服矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1153697_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》云：「王使荣叔来锡桓公命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1153697_comment'></div>书「来锡」者，讥赏不正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻古之兵制，大夫有车百乘，诸侯有车千乘，天子有车万乘，所以威四夷，刑奸宄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1153697_comment'></div>必先教之以礼，而后讨之以罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1153697_comment'></div>故先王之制，甸服者祭，侯服者祀，宾服者享，要服者贡，荒服者王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1153697_comment'></div>有不祭则修意，有不祀则修言，有不享则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1153697", 1153697, "Clauses/509/Comments/0")'>修文</span>，有不贡则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1153697", 1153697, "Clauses/510/Comments/0")'>修名</span>，有不王则修德，序成而不至则修刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1153697_comment'></div>于是乎兵有常矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1153697_comment'></div>后之王者奉之，能行其礼，能守其正，则得其道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1153697_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》书「甲午治兵」者，美其得礼也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1153697_comment'></div>书「作丘甲」者，讥不正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻古之农政，夏后氏五十而贡，商人七十而助，周人百亩而彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1153697_comment'></div>所以供宗庙，备车服，必先限之以田，而后取之以赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1153697_comment'></div>先王之制，建步立亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1153697_comment'></div>六尺为步，步百为亩，亩百为夫，夫三为屋，屋三为井，井方一里，是为九夫，八家共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1153697_comment'></div>一夫一妇受私田百亩，公田十亩，输虞衡之税，供车马之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1153697_comment'></div>于是乎农有常矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1153697_comment'></div>后之王者奉之，不妨其时，不失其正，则得其道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1153697_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》书「新延厩」者，讥不时而悉农力也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1153697_comment'></div>书「初税亩」者，讥不正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1153697_comment'></div>至若君臣励翼之迹，官师寅亮之辞，考于左氏之传，寔繁大夫之对，然非圣人笔削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1153697_comment'></div>请以经义言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1153697_comment'></div>夫君臣励翼者，在乎尊卑不黩，上下不僭，罪不妄诛，刑不妄加，兴灭国，继绝世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1153697_comment'></div>《春秋》之义，尊不亲小事，卑不专大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1153697_comment'></div>谨按经有称「人」以杀大夫者，讨有罪也：称「国」以杀大夫者，罪累上也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1153697_comment'></div>经有书「夏灭项」而不言何国灭之者，为齐桓公讳也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1153697_comment'></div>《春秋》为贤者讳，桓公尝有继绝存亡之功，故君子为之讳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1153697_comment'></div>夫官师寅亮者，在乎夙夜儆戒，靖恭其位，贤愚有序，贵贱有列，安邦国，利万民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1153697_comment'></div>《春秋》之义，用贤治不肖，用贵治贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1153697_comment'></div>谨按经有书「秋，公子结媵陈人之妇于鄄，遂及齐侯、宋公盟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1153697_comment'></div>书「遂」者，美其有遂事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1153697_comment'></div>《春秋》之义，大夫受命不受辞，出境有可以安社稷、利国家者，专之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「六籍之存，日星是喻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1153697_comment'></div>百氏之说，爝火攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1153697_comment'></div>恶实尚华，寔繁厥类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1153697_comment'></div>斲雕为朴，岂无其时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1153697_comment'></div>欲使荐绅之民并宗经术，青衿之士专习圣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1153697_comment'></div>能黜异端，渴闻谠论」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻经纬天地，莫大乎六籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1153697_comment'></div>《诗》《书》标仁义之府，《礼》《乐》立教化之表，《春秋》五始以载褒贬，大《易》四象以观情伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1153697_comment'></div>从之则为正直，为圣贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1153697_comment'></div>叛之则为奸乱，为聋闇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1153697_comment'></div>万代而下，宗为格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1153697_comment'></div>然而去圣逾远，诸子锋起，各因文而述志，或希圣而扶经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1153697_comment'></div>至汉孝成帝时，已八十馀家矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1153697_comment'></div>尔后作者纷纭，竞为闳诞，违叛正道，棼泯斯文，致学者之多歧，遂务华而舍实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1153697_comment'></div>陛下注怀《坟》《索》，将抑百家，文明之朝，如转规耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1153697_comment'></div>然臣以为焚之则为非法，不若化之以道，教之以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1153697_comment'></div>自今而后，凡朝廷诏令之文，贡举诗赋之目，毋用诸家之语，必以六经之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1153697_comment'></div>上之所好，下必甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1153697_comment'></div>是以辐员之内，庠序之间，不禁而自绝，不令而自从，竞讽周孔之言，共排杨墨之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1153697_comment'></div>谅不数岁，尽变其风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1153697_comment'></div>洋洋乎《雅》《颂》之声，可以翘足而待矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「贡举之说，茂异斯求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1153697_comment'></div>爰自唐朝，独考辞赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1153697_comment'></div>虽云小辨破道，壮夫耻为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1153697_comment'></div>然而定妍否于有司，观工拙于作者，茍或舍兹衡石，诚虑失之毫釐，将俾俊乂用章，文风丕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1153697_comment'></div>其用何术，以副虚怀」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻王者不能独治天下，必择良能而共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1153697_comment'></div>故公卿大夫必选于俊乂，俊乂必取于多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1153697_comment'></div>四代荐贤，诸侯立三适之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1153697_comment'></div>两汉求士，公府有四科之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1153697_comment'></div>得贤之盛，无以踰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1153697_comment'></div>魏晋已降，南北离割，其间制度，无可纪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1153697_comment'></div>隋室立进士之科，李唐崇大其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1153697_comment'></div>国家龙兴，亦循其制，网罗贤俊，时号得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1153697_comment'></div>若辞赋之试，声律之限，盖非古也，而取一时之工焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1153697_comment'></div>陛下必欲革之而取茂异，又何患妍否之难定哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1153697_comment'></div>臣以为今之取士，其甚可疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1153697_comment'></div>乡举里选之制未尽明，察言观德之规未尽复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1153697_comment'></div>夫乡举里选，所以择其行也，而寄贯冒籍者有焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1153697_comment'></div>察言观德，所以择其材也，而矫厉虚誉者有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1153697_comment'></div>所以荐贡之始，不能皆知其行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1153697_comment'></div>明试之际，不能尽择其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1153697_comment'></div>以是爵命之间，不能无滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1153697_comment'></div>臣愿陛下先明乡里之制，次谨言德之规，然后试以策论，考其康济，非经意不得以对，非常道不得以言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1153697_comment'></div>则清浊自分，才德可辨，文风丕变，又何远乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「《礼》有四民，农居其一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1153697_comment'></div>《书》有八政，食在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1153697_comment'></div>务劝力耕，亮由薄敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1153697_comment'></div>或轻其赋调，即邦家之用不充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1153697_comment'></div>或重彼科役，即编氓之力弥困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1153697_comment'></div>至于榷酤之法，关市之征，将以惠人，亦思省去，复虑经费不给，游惰寖多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1153697_comment'></div>盖欲蠲复民租，不禁山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1153697_comment'></div>野无旷土，府有羡财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1153697_comment'></div>下靡趋于末利，上益丰于储蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1153697_comment'></div>必有说也，宜无隐焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻《语》曰：「百姓足，君孰与不足？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1153697_comment'></div>百姓不足，君孰与足」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1153697_comment'></div>故先王敷政设教，惟务富庶，藏财于民，取之以道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1153697_comment'></div>府藏益而国用充，元元安而百姓遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1153697_comment'></div>国家仁惠周普，刑政简清，但财赋未充，管榷未罢，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1153697_comment'></div>臣以为务农之制，足食之本，历观前世，盖有道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1153697_comment'></div>三代之际，其详阙矣，姬嬴而下，莫盛于汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1153697_comment'></div>臣请为陛下以西汉之事言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1153697_comment'></div>夫汉当文景之际，民田三十取一，而侯王分土，各食其租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1153697_comment'></div>关梁缓征算之制，民间有斗酒之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1153697_comment'></div>四方常贡，其入至寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1153697_comment'></div>而太仓之粟，流衍而露积；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1153697_comment'></div>京师之钱，贯朽而难校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1153697_comment'></div>守闾阎者食粱肉，阡陌之马成群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1153697_comment'></div>今国家地广前代，履亩而税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1153697_comment'></div>山泽舟车之赋，盐铁莞榷之利，一岁之入，十倍汉初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1153697_comment'></div>而用度丰盈未能相当，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1153697_comment'></div>岂非游手未去，重职未省，冗兵未减，仙释未戢，旷土未开，珠玉未弃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1153697_comment'></div>游手未去，则趋末牟利之弊未尽止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1153697_comment'></div>重职未省，则稍廪供亿之费未尽节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1153697_comment'></div>冗兵未减，则粮饷优给之用未尽一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1153697_comment'></div>仙释未戢，则邪伪蠹耗之源未尽闭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1153697_comment'></div>旷土未辟，则耒耜禾黍之利未尽获；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1153697_comment'></div>珠玉未弃，则梯航掊采之路未尽塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1153697_comment'></div>是以南亩之民，执耒而耕者无多人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1153697_comment'></div>故陛下虽躬行节俭，忧劳日昃，而制其岁用，则尚有未丰，议缓征算则将行复止者，良由是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1153697_comment'></div>愿陛下禁游惰以沮劝之典，并重职以简易之道，去冗兵以稽阅之法，抑仙释以正直之规，开旷土以优复之令，弃珠玉以俭素之教，则官府之用充仞而山积，亿兆之生敦厚而日富，丰食之道又何难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「宰字之任，蒸黎所托，在乎铨择，尤所注怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1153697_comment'></div>亦尝阅考绩于明廷，听保任于端士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1153697_comment'></div>暨于莅职，继以败官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1153697_comment'></div>或边幅罔修，簠簋靡洁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1153697_comment'></div>或佩韦罕诫，冠虎是侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1153697_comment'></div>虽国有常刑，而民已受弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1153697_comment'></div>今若峻其督责，必兴叹于凝脂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1153697_comment'></div>缓彼简书，将漏罪于疏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1153697_comment'></div>水火相济，琴瑟更张，尔其谓何，予实翘想」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻生民之命，系乎县邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1153697_comment'></div>故进任宰字，在乎择人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1153697_comment'></div>当进者进，则法令明，政教达，奸宄绝，私谒息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1153697_comment'></div>不当进者进，则王泽壅，刑辟滥，邪伪起，苞苴行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1153697_comment'></div>故古者仕不妄进，臣不虚受，盖恐下民之受弊于匪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1153697_comment'></div>国家之制，与古齐圣，而州县之吏，率多暴慢，不求洁白之名，罔垂缓急之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1153697_comment'></div>其故非他也，盖吏道颇杂，贡举未正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1153697_comment'></div>士则累场籍以求第，而不问其材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1153697_comment'></div>吏则叙久次以求迁，而不问其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1153697_comment'></div>未尝择行于三铨，但见分命于百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1153697_comment'></div>君子或淹久而后进，小人或夤缘而先达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1153697_comment'></div>复循唐氏流外之制，盛开百司恩泽之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1153697_comment'></div>选调既集，皆补令佐，蚕食元元，干冒宪网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1153697_comment'></div>详观其弊，良不远此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1153697_comment'></div>况复考课之法未尽行，论荐之科未尽至，按察之使未尽公，激劝之赏未尽重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1153697_comment'></div>臣愿陛下因革百王，详观两汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1153697_comment'></div>采诸家考课之法，而明其殿最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1153697_comment'></div>严百官论奏之典，而禁其趋附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1153697_comment'></div>选天下公正之士，出分八使之车；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1153697_comment'></div>擢州县循良之吏，入补金闺之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1153697_comment'></div>是则黄绶之间，竞为良善，又何有凝脂之叹，疏网之虞者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1153697_comment'></div>制策曰：「缅惟致治，诚在得贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1153697_comment'></div>每恐下僚，实沈英彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1153697_comment'></div>或以类举，或自荐升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1153697_comment'></div>负廉隅清白之名，常从加等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1153697_comment'></div>驰干蛊端方之誉，亦示峻迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1153697_comment'></div>然而鲜睹徇公，颇闻滥进，始由朋党，终陷刑章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1153697_comment'></div>言念于兹，夙夜无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1153697_comment'></div>欲使怀材者必达，荐士者绝私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1153697_comment'></div>奏牍上陈，美恶可复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1153697_comment'></div>爵赏下降，名实罔违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1153697_comment'></div>极言澄汰之方，用资宵旰之虑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1153697_comment'></div>臣闻王者前旒垂纩，无为而治，必举贤哲，用为股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1153697_comment'></div>故类举之典，君子所以达己知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1153697_comment'></div>自荐之制，英主所以拔寒畯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1153697_comment'></div>皆有国之规矩，求贤之轨辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1153697_comment'></div>然则类举不正则朋党者达，自荐不实则僭滥者进，必在乎以经义而制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1153697_comment'></div>谨按《春秋》书「吴子使季札来聘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1153697_comment'></div>吴，夷狄也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1153697_comment'></div>称子者，善使贤也，故进之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1153697_comment'></div>《春秋》之义，身贤贤也，使贤亦贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1153697_comment'></div>又按《书》云：「举能其官，惟尔之能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1153697_comment'></div>而今之论荐或非经意，保任之法颇重，得贤之赏未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1153697_comment'></div>夫经以使贤者为贤，举能者为能，若举状谬者既黜，举状实者未旌，则贤能之士何以劝励？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1153697_comment'></div>夫贤能不劝，则为善者怠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1153697_comment'></div>为善者怠，则欺妄者进矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1153697_comment'></div>于戏，自荐者权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1153697_comment'></div>古者帝王虑臣下妨塞贤路，乃为之制，在陛下裁之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1153697_comment'></div>若类举者道也，一日废之不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1153697_comment'></div>伏愿陛下所信任者各举所知，则楝梁柱石有馀材矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1153697_comment'></div>然则国家之大柄，王者之利器，赏罚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1153697_comment'></div>陛下明其科条，以驭荐举，不容应侯籍橐之请，而举胥臣先茅之赏，是则怀材必达，荐士绝私，可以复其美恶，而不违名实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1153697_comment'></div>臣诚不佞，罔知忌讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1153697_comment'></div>叨备清问，忧惶跼蹐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1153697_comment'></div>但幸遇陛下设直言之科，臣应极谏之召，圣策许臣「靡悼后患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1153697_comment'></div>夫贱士之虑，思补圣政万分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1153697_comment'></div>惟陛下少赐宸览，宽其鼎镬，则昧死幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1153697_comment'></div>臣谨对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_366_1153697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>闰五月七日，在京应贤良方正、能直言极谏制举，有诗赠人。作品：廷试。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三六。吴处厚《青箱杂记》卷五谓夏竦此诗赠杨徽之，误，杨徽之卒于咸平三年（1000）（苏颂《赠太子太师谥文庄杨公神道碑铭并序》））</span><div id='poem_193248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>廷试</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年闰5月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193248")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_193248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193248'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193248'>殿上衮衣明日月，砚中旗影动龙蛇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193248'>纵横礼乐三千字<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，独对丹墀日未斜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193248'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_193248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193248'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193248_0'>⑴ 《东轩笔录》卷二作帘内衮衣明黼黻，殿前旌旆杂龙蛇。纵横落笔三千字</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193248_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b62868ee25c446eea499a344cb1e365c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b62868ee25c446eea499a344cb1e365c");'><span id='b62868ee25c446eea499a344cb1e365c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1017')">1010-1017年</a>，26-33岁</div><div id='b62868ee25c446eea499a344cb1e365c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年5月28日</a>　五月二十八日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制迎圣像中路获金龙送还茅山。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制迎圣像中路获金龙送还茅山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1010年5月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193496")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193496'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193496'>巍巍真像范金成，瑞节棠舟远导迎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193496'>精衷励翼符神贶，藻卫葳蕤率礼经。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193496'>兰堤晓景涟漪静，神龙报降祥云映。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193496'>双上琼干采质明，旁临旌枻灵辉盛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193496'>台臣祗肃荐华芗，承贺凝贞拜露章。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193496'>羲氏官名高可拟，汉家年纪远难方。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193496'>凤盖分阴腾九色，蜿蜒共戏云裳侧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193496'>御天飞跃世空闻，瑞德萦盘今始识。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193496'>骙骙矫首仰中宸，丹扆深嘉美应臻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193496'>纾礼既能畴圣日，为霖当使福蒸人。<div id='poem_sentence_9_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_193496'>华阳翠壑贞灵地，星使送还彰睿志。<div id='poem_sentence_10_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_193496'>更播云章入管弦，昭昭亿载传金匮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_193496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_193496'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_193496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年9月</a>　九月，在京为秘书丞，进《瑞盐赋》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年12月</a>　十二月，在京为秘书丞，奉表上《河清赋》作品：进河清赋引表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1153643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进河清赋引表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1010年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153643")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153643'>臣某言：窃睹祀汾阴经度制置司陈尧叟奏黄河清于保平军者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153643_comment'></div>伏以惟德是辅，三世其昌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153643_comment'></div>俟河之清，一旦斯至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153643_comment'></div>光昭宗社之庆，焕发天人之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153643_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下茂大中之功，隆太上之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153643_comment'></div>本支百世，磐石非坚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153643_comment'></div>寿考万年，南山未永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153643_comment'></div>制礼作乐，类帝禋宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153643_comment'></div>六龙将幸于汾祠，九曲载清于陕服，儒宫献颂，学馆陈诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153643_comment'></div>臣虽典豆区，叨亲简谍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153643_comment'></div>极言中选，曾叨多士之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153643_comment'></div>奏赋歌诗，敢继大夫之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153643_comment'></div>仰干震耀，惧切冰渊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1153643_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年12月</a>　十二月，在京为秘书丞，上《河清赋》作品：河清赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《文庄集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1153371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河清赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1010年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153371")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153371'>有客谓臣曰：「朝廷将祀汾南，为民祈谷，大河载清，于陕之服，子尝闻其说而颂其异乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153371_comment'></div>臣曰：「传遽之吏，罕聆朝议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153371_comment'></div>愿客摅抱剧谈，开我以嘉瑞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153371_comment'></div>客曰：「唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153371_comment'></div>盖闻滔滔灵源，发自昆崙，导于积石，出于龙门，怀砥柱而势迥，播钜鹿而派分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153371_comment'></div>三王先之于祭，四渎宗以为尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153371_comment'></div>千里兮一曲，浊流兮浑浑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153371_comment'></div>乘春则桃花竞涌，赴下则竹箭争奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153371_comment'></div>若澄清而变色，实千祀而畴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153371_comment'></div>为中夏之经渎，故其应有常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153371_comment'></div>通上天之绛河，故其灵不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153371_comment'></div>洎我国家秉皇图，宣帝力，尊百神，朝万国，光明乎遐绝，馨香乎霄极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153371_comment'></div>禅云亭而广厚，玉简既封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153371_comment'></div>祀汾脽而颂祗，鸾旂未饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153371_comment'></div>西人清候而望幸，六官戒期而励翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153371_comment'></div>爰荐祉而炳灵，滟澄波之湜湜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153371_comment'></div>徒观其祥风荡漾，非烟蒙幂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153371_comment'></div>浮休气于川上，汎荣光于岸侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153371_comment'></div>失汹涌之黄流，湛清泠之素液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153371_comment'></div>银潢之影横秋，帝台之浆映日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153371_comment'></div>江练初静，壶冰乍释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153371_comment'></div>鉴秋毫及纤尘，露金沙与银砾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153371_comment'></div>神鱼龙马，泳深渊而不隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153371_comment'></div>紫阙珠宫，扩洪流而可觌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153371_comment'></div>合济渎兮安辨，委沧溟兮竞碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153371_comment'></div>吉蠲自等于明水，嘉号宜尊于清涤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153371_comment'></div>可以颂于庙，式告元符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153371_comment'></div>赞于史，以永大谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153371_comment'></div>岂比夫兰叶朱文，涌黄灵之箓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153371_comment'></div>芝泥玉柙，汎帝妫之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153371_comment'></div>登夏子之巍巍，掩汉唐之区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153371_comment'></div>子盍献议外廷，上封公车，请以水而纪官，以瑞而建元？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153371_comment'></div>然后登歌而率舞，岂非士大夫之职乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153371_comment'></div>臣曰：「客知其一，未知其二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153371_comment'></div>上之功不可以方策载，上之道不可以金石纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153371_comment'></div>感通靡间于洪纤，周流罔滞于形器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153371_comment'></div>六合而万区，肃穆而昌炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153371_comment'></div>元符而景命，纷纶而沸渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153371_comment'></div>天地清而阴阳既序，边鄙清而干戈不试，政教清而无远弗怀，刑罚清而有生咸遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153371_comment'></div>道德为休而神灵幽赞，仁义为祥而富寿攸暨，礼乐为符而上下昭假，贤材为瑞而中外允治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153371_comment'></div>乔岳未分则三篇降，汾祀将祷则真文至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153371_comment'></div>旁无垠而高无际，充乎天而溢乎地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153371_comment'></div>盖盛德与大业也，夫岂河清而已矣」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153371_comment'></div>客于是色沮魂悸，逡巡而退。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1153371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年1月24日</a>　正月二十四日，在京为秘书丞，有上表。作品：圣驾离京次日上第一表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年1月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153553")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153553'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153553'>臣某等言：伏以奉祠方泽，将奠于黄琮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153553_comment'></div>案御清畿，初张于翠盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153553_comment'></div>望徐銮之效驾，历吉日以布和<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153553_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下膺千载之期，御元气之辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153553_comment'></div>总集瑞命，已仪炳于灵篇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153553_comment'></div>咸秩无文，遂躬修于毖祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153553_comment'></div>矧省方之伊始，谅储祉以无疆<span class='inlineComment2'>（《文庄集》卷四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153553_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1153553'>原题作「圣驾离京次日上第一表」，下仅题「第二表」，至「第十七表」止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153553_comment'></div>按各表内容，实为大中祥符四年真宗祀汾阴期间，自正月离京至四月返京先后所上，并非均作于「离京次日」，故改作今题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1153553_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年1月</a>　正月，在京为秘书丞，有上表。作品：第二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第四表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153555")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153555'>臣某等言：今月二十六日，入内内侍省内侍高品谭元吉至，伏蒙圣慈特传宣抚问者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153555_comment'></div>翠盖时迈，将毖祀于汾阴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153555_comment'></div>使者星驰，遽侧聆于天语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153555_comment'></div>俯炳丹青之旨，如亲咫尺之颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153555_comment'></div>伏念臣某等幸遇会昌，久尘禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153555_comment'></div>属省方于脽壤，俾留镇于都畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153555_comment'></div>虽比屋之民，富庶而既教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153555_comment'></div>揭法之地，桴鼓而不鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153555_comment'></div>岂兹梼昧之能，治此浩穰之俗！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153555_comment'></div>纵虔遵于训典，庸莫副于倚毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153555_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下文致时雍，德膺天庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153555_comment'></div>静则合宫衢室，垂衣裳而向明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153555_comment'></div>动则温洛荣河，授龟龙之荐瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153555_comment'></div>已垂鸿于阳祉，遂昭事于柔祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153555_comment'></div>盖致孝于两仪，亦祈民之百谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153555_comment'></div>垂圣心于覆露，轸臣下之勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153555_comment'></div>臣等未效涓尘，特邀眷待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153555_comment'></div>王言所被，与华衮而同褒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153555_comment'></div>睿旨初闻，共阳春而交感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153555_comment'></div>誓罄匪躬之节，上酬不报之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1153555_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第四表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153556")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153556'>臣某等言：伏以肃若旧典，肇禋明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153556_comment'></div>祀方泽之皇祇，望属车于驰道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153556_comment'></div>臣某等恭惟尊位皇帝陛下重光御极，上圣膺图，方展仪于河汾，盖推功于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153556_comment'></div>风后陪乘，羽卫由是纂严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153556_comment'></div>苍灵奉涂，福禄以之攸降。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1153556_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年2月</a>　二月，在京为秘书丞，有上表。作品：第五表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第六表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第七表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第八表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第九表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第五表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153557")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153557'>臣某等言：伏以毖祀高脽，星言法驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153557_comment'></div>将展省方之盛礼，式符徯后之群心<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153557_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下广覆尧仁，升闻舜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153557_comment'></div>答三灵之蕃祉，宣二圣之重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153557_comment'></div>伸孝享于鄈丘，奠皇祇于冀壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153557_comment'></div>既集礼神之馆，伫闻宝鼎之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153557_comment'></div>王度之贞，式如金而如玉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153557_comment'></div>天道下济，固为龙以为光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153557_comment'></div>臣等迹远陪銮，心驰就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153557_comment'></div>帝车爰止，莫参禹会之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153557_comment'></div>日驭将施，但效封人之祝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1153557_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第六表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153558")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153558'>臣某等言：伏以五坛巡祭，昭事于汾脽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153558_comment'></div>万国骏奔，同趋于禹会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153558_comment'></div>方恪居于官次，莫亲奉于天颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153558_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下诞受丕图，钦承宝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153558_comment'></div>致美黻冕而九庙储休，洁粢牲牷而百神荐祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153558_comment'></div>帝德广运，咸苏徯后之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153558_comment'></div>皇泽如春，载洽怀生之类。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1153558_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第七表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153559")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153559'>臣某等言：伏以国家振举阙文，讲求缛礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153559_comment'></div>顺蒲人之望幸，严汾水之亲祠<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153559_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下建极临民，握图听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153559_comment'></div>方鸣鸾于军道，将奠玉于嘉坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153559_comment'></div>谅洋溢于讴歌，允飞腾于英茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153559_comment'></div>惟天为大，如日之升。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1153559_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第八表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153560")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153560'>臣某等言：恭以国家顺河汾之徯后，奠牲帛于柔祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153560_comment'></div>诸侯陈执玉之仪，多士结望云之恳<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153560_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下明德恤祀，展仪省方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153560_comment'></div>历览于图书之渊，斋绂于静冥之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153560_comment'></div>大车弭节，方严穆穆之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153560_comment'></div>祥风绕坛，将降穰穰之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153560_comment'></div>臣某等恪居官次，驰恋皇轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153560_comment'></div>除地给薪，莫诣侍祠之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153560_comment'></div>拖绅鸣佩，深怀拱极之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1153560_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第九表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153561")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153561'>臣某等言：得行在进奏官状报，伏承今月某日皇帝躬祀汾阴礼毕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153561_comment'></div>无文咸秩，表上圣之寅恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153561_comment'></div>明德惟馨，见至诚之昭荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153561_comment'></div>崇庞鸿之大业，举旷绝之盛仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153561_comment'></div>降及飞沈，率同欢抃<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153561_comment'></div>臣某等闻，乾知太始而坤作成物，混元之大化也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153561_comment'></div>父事于天而母事于地，圣王之至孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153561_comment'></div>洪惟厚载，职彼资生，配刚健于运行，兆阴灵之正位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153561_comment'></div>成周之奠大泽，由八变而出地祇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153561_comment'></div>炎汉之祠素汾，升五坛而集神贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153561_comment'></div>若时能事，属在昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153561_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下睿览穆清，至仁渊静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153561_comment'></div>挺克明之睿德，绍累洽之鸿基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153561_comment'></div>帝顼依仁，奉若于天道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153561_comment'></div>唐尧稽古，于变其时雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153561_comment'></div>声明文物之相宣，雍容揄扬而咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153561_comment'></div>六府既正，九叙惟歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153561_comment'></div>向以昊穹储休，图书锡瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153561_comment'></div>奉符展寀，既增乔岳之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153561_comment'></div>勒崇垂鸿，聿大丕天之律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153561_comment'></div>已推功于上帝，肃昭事于柔祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153561_comment'></div>兰台时英，稽四巡而献颂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153561_comment'></div>蒲津黎老，愿万乘而启行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153561_comment'></div>丹诏往俞，近臣先置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153561_comment'></div>圣心虔巩而戒事，灵物纷纶而降祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153561_comment'></div>若影响之相随，明天人之交际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153561_comment'></div>及清畿时迈，法驾星陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153561_comment'></div>华盖承辰，见惠风之和畅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153561_comment'></div>黼帷藻野，属春日之载阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153561_comment'></div>洎升坛荐鬯之辰，受嘉气矞云之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153561_comment'></div>百灵效祉，岂惟三烛之神光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153561_comment'></div>万祥毕臻，不独登歌于宝鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153561_comment'></div>懿铄度越于千古，休烈烜赫于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153561_comment'></div>岂凿井耕田而不知，固跂行喙息而遂性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153561_comment'></div>巍巍荡荡，谅无得而名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153561_comment'></div>穆穆皇皇，知大事在祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153561_comment'></div>臣等亲逢旦暮，仰颂形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153561_comment'></div>酆宫会朝，莫陪于法从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153561_comment'></div>明堂上寿，即奉于宸严。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1153561_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153562")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153562'>臣某等言：伏以汾曲禋严，已毕奠琮之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153562_comment'></div>方明朝会，式陈班瑞之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153562_comment'></div>就尧日以驰诚，祈舜聪而逖听<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153562_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下体乾立极，抱一居尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153562_comment'></div>齐律度于万殊，宝慈俭于六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153562_comment'></div>声教所暨，盈溢于天区；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153562_comment'></div>德泽滂流，汪洋于海外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153562_comment'></div>故得荐膺景贶，纷委嘉符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153562_comment'></div>岱岳增封，答三灵之蕃祉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153562_comment'></div>汉脽亲祀，收百代之阙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153562_comment'></div>拥社稷之神休，显帝王之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153562_comment'></div>今者嘉坛袭吉，槱燎升烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153562_comment'></div>九壤蒸黎，仰太阳之委照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153562_comment'></div>上都耆艾，俟鸣跸以倾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153562_comment'></div>皇猷已冠于古今，令誉更孚于夷夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153562_comment'></div>伏冀皇帝陛下早回仙仗，归格神京，治庶汇之由庚，俾普天之同庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153562_comment'></div>臣等保釐京邑，夙夜公家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153562_comment'></div>尽瘁之心，敢忘于丹臆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153562_comment'></div>拱辰之列，伫望于清光。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1153562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年3月</a>　三月，在京为秘书丞，有上表。作品：第十一表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十四表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十五表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十六表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>第十七表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153563")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153563'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153563'>臣某等言：伏以礼崇盥鬯，既颁赐于汾祠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153563_comment'></div>孝享园陵，适亲临于洛邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153563_comment'></div>矧王畿之接畛，迎制跸以倾心<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153563_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下怀柔百神，同风三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153563_comment'></div>圣德加乎海内，文教溢于天区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153563_comment'></div>遒人采诗，已供于夜诵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153563_comment'></div>诸侯执玉，率庆于会朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153563_comment'></div>惟象魏之在瞻，谅中外之禔福。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1153563_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153564")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153564'>臣某等言：伏以斋礼神之馆，已升燎于高脽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153564_comment'></div>登颂祇之堂，方回舆于近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153564_comment'></div>望轩游而俯迩，瞻尧日以欢心<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153564_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下清洁明禋，讲求逸礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153564_comment'></div>素汾奠玉，已昭鱼舞之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153564_comment'></div>温洛受图，更显凤衔之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153564_comment'></div>矧休应之纷委，属诏跸以言旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153564_comment'></div>式宴清宫，洽皇恩于恺乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153564_comment'></div>受釐宣室，凝帝道于穆清。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1153564_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153565")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153565'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153565'>臣某等言：伏以鸣玉銮于汾水，已殚报本之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153565_comment'></div>荫华盖于洛都，载展奉先之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153565_comment'></div>仰鸿仪之备举，肃禁卫以言旋<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153565_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下敷祐四方，交修百祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153565_comment'></div>为人祈谷，验膏泽于丰年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153565_comment'></div>采诗观风，知民耕于帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153565_comment'></div>日驭方回于黄道，涂歌先洽于清畿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1153565_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十四表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153566")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153566'>臣某等言：伏以礼盛亲祠，膺三灵之眷命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153566_comment'></div>庆成归格，顺万国之欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153566_comment'></div>仰日驭以非遥，望翠华而窃忭<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153566_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下恢崇鸿业，宣畅皇猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153566_comment'></div>尚质贵诚，已肇禋于泰折；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153566_comment'></div>布德行惠，复统政于明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153566_comment'></div>授时之令惟新，及物之恩弥广。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1153566_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十五表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153567")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153567'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153567'>臣某等言：伏以方鼎升庖，神既歆于嘉享；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153567_comment'></div>徐銮弭驭，诏以示于先期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153567_comment'></div>瞻有穆之睟容，祝无疆之景福<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153567_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下丕承圣绪，光阐帝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153567_comment'></div>唐尧稽古而聪明，高阳洁诚而祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153567_comment'></div>察事地之礼，嘉生由是均和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153567_comment'></div>修颂祇之书，丰泽以之大赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153567_comment'></div>式臻神贶，允集天休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153567_comment'></div>臣等目注回舆，心驰迎跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153567_comment'></div>望六龙之御，莫及于前驱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153567_comment'></div>率百辟之班，伫朝于近甸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1153567_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十六表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153568")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153568'>臣某等言：今月二十五日，龙图阁待制查道至，伏蒙圣慈以车驾还都，特赐诏书抚问者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153568_comment'></div>伏以方泽奠琮，礼成于严祀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153568_comment'></div>皇舆复路，诏示于先期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153568_comment'></div>辱圣眷之便蕃，走欢声于遐迩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153568_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下重光御极，执象临民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153568_comment'></div>怀生被广育之仁，制礼尽大中之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153568_comment'></div>济河之日，尧承刻玉之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153568_comment'></div>祀汾之初，汉膺宝鼎之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153568_comment'></div>既协坤灵之荐祉，俄瞻日驭以言旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153568_comment'></div>臣叨荷宸衷，俾司留务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153568_comment'></div>无涓尘之微效，有葵藿之至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153568_comment'></div>荐沐鸿慈，俯颁芝检，捧妫泉之绿字，贲大帝之宝文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153568_comment'></div>闻效驾于和鸾，固踊跃之无极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153568_comment'></div>藏赐书于巾箧，实荣耀以难偕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1153568_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝祀汾阴第十七表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153569")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153569'>臣某等言：伏以瑞气宵凝，既显坤灵之荐祉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153569_comment'></div>欢声雷动，式当诏跸之言旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153569_comment'></div>凡属照临，悉同欢忭<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153569_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下帝德广运，人文化成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153569_comment'></div>顺万物由庚之宜，考太一省方之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153569_comment'></div>抚空桑之瑟，已降于地祇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153569_comment'></div>清甸师之畿，即回于云䍐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153569_comment'></div>俯兹青陆，更拥鸿休。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1153569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年6月25日</a>　六月二十五日，在京应学士院试，赋优，诗稍优，诏直集贤院，有谢表。作品：谢直集贤院表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢直集贤院表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年6月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153580")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153580'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153580'>臣某言：蒙恩以本官直集贤院者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153580_comment'></div>北开禁省，给青简以试言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153580_comment'></div>东观直庐，降紫泥而命职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153580_comment'></div>莫逭假人之器，式彰遇主之荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153580_comment'></div>窃以承明设待诏之官，实汉朝之芳润；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153580_comment'></div>丽正启修书之院，乃唐氏之英华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153580_comment'></div>浚图书之渊，敞龙凤之署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153580_comment'></div>自非弓裘继世，章句名家，通授羲畀姒之灵篇，闲书笏珥彤之故事，则何以继成康之嘉颂，考宣武之懿文，陪法从于甘泉，奉宸游于属玉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153580_comment'></div>况当圣日，允属简求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153580_comment'></div>如臣者学不传经，文非近史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153580_comment'></div>「青青子佩」，虽见刺于劳心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153580_comment'></div>「翘翘错薪」，亦滥期于刈楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153580_comment'></div>筮仕胜衣之岁，荐名象日之畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153580_comment'></div>方博带以观光，遽墨衰而沿牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153580_comment'></div>寻遇国家诞敷尺诏，增广六科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153580_comment'></div>方栖枳以徒劳，遂上封而自荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153580_comment'></div>始交文于鳌苑，旋试可于鼎司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153580_comment'></div>亟趋文石之墀，遂忝延英之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153580_comment'></div>击辕度曲，敢望于九成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153580_comment'></div>萦带分墉，俄登于百雉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153580_comment'></div>升象河之属吏，佐分虎之方州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153580_comment'></div>爰受代于瓜时，遂归朝于幄坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153580_comment'></div>典陈陈之粟，阅山委之丘区；<div class='inline'
