id='poem_sentence_22_1153580_comment'></div>从九九之车，总丝棼之案牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153580_comment'></div>暨还衡脽壤，舍爵太宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153580_comment'></div>既谐引籍于金闺，将佐于蕃于熊轼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153580_comment'></div>又虑沉迷簿领，废坠简编，负公朝振举之科，辜圣主详延之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153580_comment'></div>遂杀青而奏技，果出綍以推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153580_comment'></div>禁林俾试于雕虫，书殿遽令其抱椠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153580_comment'></div>阅上帝之册府，目眩星辰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153580_comment'></div>登道家之蓬山，足践云气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153580_comment'></div>奉长者之馀论，与先生而并行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153580_comment'></div>分直石渠，地接严更之宇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153580_comment'></div>纵观金匮，门连著作之廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153580_comment'></div>载惟蝼蚁之躯，莫报乾坤之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153580_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下事寝庙以至孝，奉灵祇而克诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153580_comment'></div>流鸿藻于绝垠，铄景炎于往号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153580_comment'></div>以文明而行健，体柔克以居高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153580_comment'></div>纵观唐汉之大猷，备举黄虞之故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153580_comment'></div>睿藻和而六同韵，天章丽而五佐飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153580_comment'></div>恢崇务广于斯文，奖擢不遗于小道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153580_comment'></div>遂使至孤之士，获尘非次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153580_comment'></div>东陵遽拟于西山，羔裘遂登于狐腋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153580_comment'></div>歌《卫风》而合雅，鬻齐紫而杂良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153580_comment'></div>诚当洁节于素丝，敢不盟心于白水，益三思而出话，弥九复以穷经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153580_comment'></div>永冰渊惕励之心，奉日月照临之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153580_comment'></div>庶逭素餐之谤，仰酬明主之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153580_comment'></div>愧惧所深，兢惶不已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1153580_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年11月8日</a>　十一月八日，在京为秘书丞，有进和御制诗表。作品：进和御制占城国贡师子诗表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1153642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进和御制占城国贡师子诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年11月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153642")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153642'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153642'>臣某言：瑞兽来庭，薰弦发唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153642_comment'></div>获继帝庸之作，实非臣和之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153642_comment'></div>载省疏芜，但增惭恧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153642_comment'></div>窃念臣叨尘官序，际会文明，莫勤日益之功，徒奉化成之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153642_comment'></div>此者伏遇尊位皇帝陛下言惟妙物，道实通微，懿文德以经天，靡圣风而柔远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153642_comment'></div>夐兹荒服，承献灵猊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153642_comment'></div>用昭式于休光，遂敷施于睿藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153642_comment'></div>协筦弦而振律，润竹素以垂鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153642_comment'></div>造物之功，寻楷模之可究；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153642_comment'></div>秉阳之象，仰躔次而可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153642_comment'></div>臣叨奉恩私，俾令赓载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153642_comment'></div>但覃研之精爽，唯罄竭于顽驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153642_comment'></div>用缀芜音，少酬天奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153642_comment'></div>上尘旒纩，唯积忧兢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1153642_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　本年，在京为秘书丞，被增补为《太祖太宗两朝国史》编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　本年，在京为秘书丞，被增补为《历代君臣事迹》编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年10月17日</a>　十月十七日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制为政歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制为政歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1012年10月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193492")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193492'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193492'>黼帐夜分常监寐，凤轩端委敷文治。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193492'>肇建元封陟介丘，寝寻毖祀临汾水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193492'>茂烈馨香久际天，精心励翼弥恭已。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193492'>体道推仁洽惠和，斲凋归厚蠲华侈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193492'>怀柔四貊尽来庭，边圉无尘似平砥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193492'>尧德钦明惇茂族，汉条宽大措祥刑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193492'>永观禹画同文轸，更伫虞巡审量衡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193492'>睿政无为犹日慎，布昭谟训掩汤铭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193492'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_193492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年闰10月7日</a>　闰十月七日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制奉先歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制奉先歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1012年闰10月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193497")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193497'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193497'>皇家兮仙祖，上世兮圣神。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193497'>承云兮分治，驾羽兮临民。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193497'>诞昭兮馨烈，高陟兮元真。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193497'>载乘土运临三古，属象羲农振遐武。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193497'>爰炳明灵陟上苍，绵绵圣绪庆悠长。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193497'>既积仁兮累德，爰振耀兮流芳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193497'>罄二仪兮垂祐，弥万祀兮开祥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193497'>巍巍烈祖兮膺宸历，御瑶图兮建鳌极。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193497'>东征西怨兮振群黎，下舞上歌兮康庶国。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193497'>优游亮直显敦仁，锡羡休嘉符拓迹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_193497'>四貊名王尺组羁，九涯远道安车适。<div id='poem_sentence_10_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_193497'>圣功耆定实登三，方赆骏奔惟旅百。<div id='poem_sentence_11_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_193497'>赫赫神宗廓帝纮，昭广运兮洽和平。<div id='poem_sentence_12_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_193497'>礼适素青兮沿夏子，化归醲粹兮复胥庭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_193497'>宪六学兮昭地纬，事七庙兮奉天经。<div id='poem_sentence_14_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_193497'>震叠威霆兮踰朔幕，汪洋惠露兮浃编氓。<div id='poem_sentence_15_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_193497'>偃节灵台兮黜武，漏鱼宽网兮蠲刑。<div id='poem_sentence_16_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_193497'>三叶缉熙兮隆绍继，皇穹右序兮隤繁祉。<div id='poem_sentence_17_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_193497'>徘徊飙歘兮授元符，焜耀樵蒸兮修茂礼。<div id='poem_sentence_18_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_193497'>思文成颂兮迪先谋，多黍申歌兮昭乐岁。<div id='poem_sentence_19_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_193497'>参侔开阖已无为，虔巩盈成弥若厉。<div id='poem_sentence_20_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_193497'>惟寤寐兮符通，实天人兮合契。<div id='poem_sentence_21_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_193497'>降仙驭兮自三清，谕灵源兮踰百世。<div id='poem_sentence_22_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_193497'>遐锡鸿休茂本枝，永符盛德昭明类。<div id='poem_sentence_23_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_193497'>荐徽册，致清衷，斋明兮显至。<div id='poem_sentence_24_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_193497'>款太空，告繁禧，监观兮斯暨。<div id='poem_sentence_25_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_193497'>对越兮储精，聿怀兮忘寐。<div id='poem_sentence_26_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_193497'>舄奕千龄播德芬，钦崇茂典协经纶。<div id='poem_sentence_27_193497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_193497'>神化有开彰密命，庆基无际等高旻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_193497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年11月3日</a>　十一月三日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制朝元殿朝谢玉皇大帝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三五。）</span>奉和御制朝谢玉皇大帝致斋夜天书道场观鹤下临。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_193474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制朝元殿朝谢玉皇大帝</a><span class='authorDate'>（1012年11月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193474'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193474'>三清右序储繁祉，万乘钦明答上穹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193474'>圣化诞敷书轨混，仙游昭假地天通。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193474'>灵辉熠煜充丹禁，瑞雾霏微翳碧空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193474'>积累有开鸿绪远，顾怀无际庆基隆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193474'>精心展彩威颜肃，法曲迎真睿藻融。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193474'>象舞在庭功夐异，宝符先道古难同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193474'>奉朝嘉服祇群后，赞帝鸿仪俨上公。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年1月13日</a>　正月十三日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制笔歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span>奉和御制砚歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193505?labeling=true' "poem_title_193505")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193505'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193505'>古今罔不达，淑慝将何逃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制砚歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1013年1月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193503")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193503'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193503'>南方潜璞出寒溪，沉沉紫蔚凝坚姿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193503'>两仪肖象磨砻异，三趾承隅琢饰奇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193503'>银带参华贡双阙，玉蟾分滴润圆池。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193503'>微波澄淡当晴景，旌旗半浸龙蛇影。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193503'>轻浮春絮拂犀干，微动日华明绮井。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193503'>蕊简交辉九禁深，玉枝斜照中宵永。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193503'>列璇台兮今得地，迩清光兮叶灵契。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193503'>宣丝旨兮扬圣谟，赞云章兮熙睿志。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193503'>弥彰盛德冠生民，务以文明化兆人。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193503'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_193503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年2月5日</a>　二月五日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制清心殿水清木再连理。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_193398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193398?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193398'>禁中迟日照南荣，瑞木联祥耀国经。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193398'>合干旧临宫槛密，交柯重接帝梧青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193398'>华平对植行侵陛，若木相辉影满亭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193398'>况是斋心延贶地，愈昭天意答惟馨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193398'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年2月11日</a>　二月十一日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制墨歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193511?labeling=true' "poem_title_193511")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193511'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193511'>昔造图书兮纪方志，铅黄丹漆兮初为贵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193511'>后世增华兮迈昔贤，松烟布色兮明且妍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193511'>一枝均赐官仪备，九子分形吉礼全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193511'>写功咏德盈缃帙，体物缘情遍绮笺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193511'>阴山潜璞兮琢金池，相须艺圃兮事攸宜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193511'>湘川青管兮束圆锋，并列璇台兮用本同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193511'>垂大训，述微言，孔墨之教兮长存。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193511'>腾藻翰，赞仪形，渊云之妙兮惟精。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193511'>上圣敦仁崇俭约，厥篚珍奇诏皆却。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193511'>唯许隃糜岁贡臻，式彰文德化生民。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_193511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年3月6日</a>　三月六日，在京为秘书丞，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制太清楼屏风柏连理。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_193494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制太清楼屏风柏连理</a><span class='authorDate'>（1013年3月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193494")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193494'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193494'>禁园绮合群芳茂，瑞柏屏开秀色呈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193494'>托植久依仙杏密，附枝俄接帝梧荣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193494'>非烟结翠和风细，滴露凝华晓日明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193494'>况是岁寒坚节异，亭亭千载表殊祯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193494'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年8月</a>　八月，在京为秘书丞，因参修之《册府元龟》书成，迁判三司都磨勘司，复迁右正言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年8月</a>　八月，在京为右正言，受命为宰相、兖州景灵宫朝修使王旦掌奏笺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年10月</a>　十月，在京为右正言，代丁谓作贺表。作品：代丁相公贺元德皇后祔庙礼毕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_1153670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代丁相公贺元德皇后祔庙礼毕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1013年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153670")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153670'>臣某言：鸿仪茂举，至孝允孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153670_comment'></div>凡在照临，咸同庆忭<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153670_comment'></div>臣闻鲁尊先妣，姜嫄始立于閟宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153670_comment'></div>唐重母仪，昭后终迁于太室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153670_comment'></div>徽音匪远，彝制具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153670_comment'></div>恭以元德皇后作合先朝，诞生上圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153670_comment'></div>自别崇于庙享，庸未极于礼章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153670_comment'></div>伏惟尊位皇帝陛下锡类推仁，追恩著德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153670_comment'></div>体周文之翼翼，极虞舜之烝烝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153670_comment'></div>仰惟帝母之尊，虔纳辅臣之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153670_comment'></div>用钦崇于尊谥，恭升配于神宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153670_comment'></div>涓选灵辰，宣臻熙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153670_comment'></div>百官承式，奉徽册以惟寅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153670_comment'></div>万世不祧，致明禋而永穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153670_comment'></div>丕显奉先之礼，茂昭维则之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153670_comment'></div>先置真祠，仰闻大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153670_comment'></div>趋阙庭而靡及，增蹈颂以攸深。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1153670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年12月</a>　十二月，在京为右正言，为王益文集作序。作品：桂籍追荣序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1153834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桂籍追荣序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1013年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153834")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153834'>枢密相国太原公次子、故卫尉寺丞某字庆之，幼而辩悟，不乐戏玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153834_comment'></div>始就外傅，卓如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153834_comment'></div>属咏景物，动会辞律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153834_comment'></div>洎胜衣趋拜，风度弥远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153834_comment'></div>客卿沉敏，若怀将相之器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153834_comment'></div>褚陶清谈，自得坟典之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153834_comment'></div>志慕老、庄，誉等终、贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153834_comment'></div>尝耻由官荫，刻志缃素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153834_comment'></div>曾未丱岁，文藻粲然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153834_comment'></div>金籯之言，发于邹鲁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153834_comment'></div>玉树之秀，茂于庭阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153834_comment'></div>咸以为天资美才，性识早立，沐浴圣化，被服诗礼，固将腾天路，摩绛霄，超野绝群，一日千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153834_comment'></div>御屏隔坐，绍亮骘之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153834_comment'></div>缁衣改为，宣桓武之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153834_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153834_comment'></div>天道云远，大化难谌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153834_comment'></div>育而不苗，闻者增欷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153834_comment'></div>上闵其幼慧，赠襚有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153834_comment'></div>追赐进士及第，以成其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153834_comment'></div>有诗赋杂文二十卷，题曰《桂籍追荣集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153834_comment'></div>所以纪漏泉之泽，昭夙成之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153834_comment'></div>死而不朽，其在兹乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153834_comment'></div>时大中祥符六年十二月日具衔某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1153834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年1月</a>　正月，在京为右正言，真宗幸亳州，为东京留守推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年1月</a>　正月，在京为右正言，有贺表。作品：贺五色云见表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span>贺奉祀太清宫礼毕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺五色云见表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153570")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153570'>臣言：伏审今月二十日圣驾至真源县，有五色云见者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153570_comment'></div>徐銮夙驾，总驷于名区；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153570_comment'></div>卿霭晨敷，流晖于紫宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153570_comment'></div>繁禧允集，率舞咸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153570_comment'></div>窃以云物凝祥，简编攸载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153570_comment'></div>帝鸿纪事，肇采于官名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153570_comment'></div>虞舜协华，赓歌于瑞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153570_comment'></div>盖太和之积粹，畴至德以呈符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153570_comment'></div>仰属昌期，愈彰丕应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153570_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下参侔邃古，率育黎蒸，绍隆累洽之基，懋建太宁之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153570_comment'></div>宝图候日，丕显于灵猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153570_comment'></div>真祖在天，茂昭于道荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153570_comment'></div>式举朝修之礼，弥臻顾諟之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153570_comment'></div>当恭馆之斋心，有非烟之效祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153570_comment'></div>纷纶绚采，散赤水之馀霞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153570_comment'></div>焕衍腾文，凝吉云之晓露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153570_comment'></div>耸群瞻而庆异，垂信史以弥芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153570_comment'></div>昭万寿之遐龄，迪三清之景祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153570_comment'></div>某限居□□，宜从鸾旗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153570_comment'></div>仰听殊尤，唯增抃蹈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1153570_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1153571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺奉祀太清宫礼毕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153571")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153571'>臣某言：伏睹诏书，今月某日奉祀太清宫礼毕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153571_comment'></div>茂典庆成，繁禧允集，照临所暨，抃蹈咸同<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153571_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下寅畏时中，惠和逮下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153571_comment'></div>丕承帝箓，绍举于皇仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153571_comment'></div>钦奉真游，躬闻于道诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153571_comment'></div>爰徇黎元之请，虔趋仁圣之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153571_comment'></div>达精意于萧芗，荐鸿名于宝册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153571_comment'></div>诞受聿怀之福，允济雍熙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153571_comment'></div>茂昭善贷之仁，永宣至治。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1153571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年7月</a>　七月，在京为右正言，有诗。作品：大中祥符七年七月锦州奏天庆观修圣祖殿毕五色云三朵各方丈余见于殿上。<div id='poem_193332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大中祥符七年七月锦州奏天庆观修圣祖殿毕五色云三朵各方丈馀见于殿上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193332")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193332'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193332'>仙祠成秘殿，远郡在卢阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193332'>旭日初流景，卿云忽降祥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年11月</a>　十一月，在京为右正言，玉清昭应宫修成，有贺表。作品：贺昭应宫成表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺昭应宫成表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153552")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153552'>臣某言：良辰协吉，恭馆告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153552_comment'></div>凡在照临，率同庆抃<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153552_comment'></div>伏惟尊位皇帝陛下寅威体道，慈俭时中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153552_comment'></div>顺乾则以推仁，奉先猷而追孝，至诚以临亿兆，洁志以奉灵祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153552_comment'></div>由是景命昭通，真图申锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153552_comment'></div>授太元之神策，式集于皇仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153552_comment'></div>侔曲密之仙都，肇营于秘宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153552_comment'></div>度鸿庞之久制，鸠瑰异之伟材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153552_comment'></div>揆日出以辨方，候定中而经始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153552_comment'></div>尊三清之正位，载严真祖之庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153552_comment'></div>范二后之睟仪，爰设百灵之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153552_comment'></div>罄钦崇之精意，极神丽之宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153552_comment'></div>工有技而咸程，物有珍而必效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153552_comment'></div>式属仲冬之序，聿成大壮之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153552_comment'></div>洒宸翰于银题，繁禧沓至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153552_comment'></div>列荣班于金戺，鸿庆方隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153552_comment'></div>臣限守官曹，恭刊帝箓，顾莫陪于著位，但俯积于欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153552_comment'></div>抃蹈之诚，夐异伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1153552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年11月</a>　十一月，在京为右正言，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制玉清昭应宫成。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_193462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193462?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_10_193462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年11月27日</a>　十一月二十七日，在京为右正言，充玉清昭应宫判官，赐金紫，有谢表。作品：谢赐昭应宫判官兼赐章服表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐昭应宫判官兼赐章服表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年11月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153581")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153581'>臣某言：伏蒙圣慈赐臣敕牒一道，官告一通，授臣本官充玉清昭应宫判官，兼面赐章服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153581_comment'></div>钦承恩渥，俯积兢荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153581_comment'></div>伏念臣幸会亨期，最为孤进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153581_comment'></div>自先臣之尽节，始沿牒以效官，折腰初佐于县庭，承乏遽参于州幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153581_comment'></div>偶六科之选士，趋三府以试言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153581_comment'></div>擿埴索涂，误攀于俊轨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153581_comment'></div>以蠡测海，谬对于圣题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153581_comment'></div>才叨上第之荣，遂忝属丞之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153581_comment'></div>佐凭熊于丹峤，属抚玉于云封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153581_comment'></div>亟迁秩于芸扃，旋侍祠于汾壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153581_comment'></div>由是升华仙室，引籍于朝闺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153581_comment'></div>较艺禁林，振缨于学馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153581_comment'></div>践宣猷之近省，备太史之后陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153581_comment'></div>䌷百氏之格言，缉两朝之大典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153581_comment'></div>兼总金刀之务，俄尘谏诤之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153581_comment'></div>顾蹇蹇以无闻，但容容而自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153581_comment'></div>矧属旧臣居守，特预于宾从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153581_comment'></div>元辅朝脩，爰司于奏记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153581_comment'></div>念践扬而无取，荷柬擢以尤深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153581_comment'></div>书言动于宸墀，总勾稽于会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153581_comment'></div>夙宵一志，虽坚金石之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153581_comment'></div>尸素十年，莫著涓尘之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153581_comment'></div>此者伏遇尊位皇帝陛下虔尊道奥，祗若灵心，奉三境之真文，绍九重之圣绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153581_comment'></div>体密都之神丽，扩恭馆之穆清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153581_comment'></div>地有宝以皆呈，山有材而必效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153581_comment'></div>聿举庆成之典，载严置使之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153581_comment'></div>皆眷命于公台，式尊崇于宪度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153581_comment'></div>仍分众职，肃奉攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153581_comment'></div>载惟倅事之臣，允极当朝之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153581_comment'></div>尤谓博求鸿硕，登用俊良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153581_comment'></div>岂意颛蒙，误膺推择，授之纶綍，宠以金章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153581_comment'></div>锵瑶佩于绛台，夐希于仙品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153581_comment'></div>奉蕊书于紫馆，绝异于慈荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153581_comment'></div>重念臣本以孤平，素无伎蓺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153581_comment'></div>微近亲可以仰给，乏先畴可以取资，唯赖鸿私，妄阶荣路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153581_comment'></div>爰从乐育，以跂甄升，未有秋毫，不由帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153581_comment'></div>天高地厚，固报德以无阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153581_comment'></div>恩重命轻，誓竭心而有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153581_comment'></div>敢不服勤官次，祗事真庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153581_comment'></div>永坚寅畏之心，上副钦崇之旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1153581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年12月</a>　十二月，在京为玉清昭应宫判官月余，奏宝符阁奉神果实。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　本年，在京为右正言，因王旦荐，教庆国公赵祯法书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　本年，在京为右正言，抗疏排丁谓等言符瑞之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年1月3日</a>　正月三日，在京为右正言，有诗。作品：八年正月天庆节上清宫行香锡庆院御筵日扬辉有非烟非雾之云。<div id='poem_193330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八年正月天庆节上清宫行香锡庆院御筵日扬辉有非烟非雾之云</a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年1月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193330")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193330'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193330'>宝箓标嘉节，需云锡惠筵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193330'>烈晖腾爱景，瑞彩拟非烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193330'>焜耀璿霄外，轮囷绛阙前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193330'>居歆方屡告，伟兆溢祥编。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193330'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193330_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年1月</a>　正月，在京为右正言，请赐玉清昭应宫国子监印本书各一部。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年2月</a>　二月，在京为右正言，奉敕为赵元佐作谢恩表。作品：楚王谢恩表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1153660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楚王谢恩表<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153660")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153660'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153660'>臣某言：伏奉制恩特受臣天策上将军、行兴元牧，赐剑履上殿、书诏不名，依前守太师、尚书令，依旧在宅养疾，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153660_comment'></div>恩制诞宣，徽章载峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153660_comment'></div>仰戴加崇之典，俯怀非据之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153660_comment'></div>臣闻隆器大名，必先于有德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153660_comment'></div>殊荣异数，岂及于无功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153660_comment'></div>如臣者托体宗枝，承晖宝萼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153660_comment'></div>乏间平之令誉，异周召之元勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153660_comment'></div>位冠中台，任隆西省，总钩陈之近卫，分列轸之奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153660_comment'></div>礼徒厚于脤膰，效罔阶于尘雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153660_comment'></div>唯赖宠私大庇，友爱曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153660_comment'></div>宴处安安，俾阶于养素；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153660_comment'></div>夙兴翼翼，莫展于在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153660_comment'></div>常自省循，尤为冒昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153660_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇尊号皇帝陛下德绥九族，惠育群黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153660_comment'></div>谊常切于展亲，化方深于教睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153660_comment'></div>继先猷之久大，丕显于孝思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153660_comment'></div>绍真绪之延鸿，务均于道荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153660_comment'></div>式稽良日，爰赐命书，备褒宠之殊猷，极优隆之贵范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153660_comment'></div>葭孚至薄，荷敦叙以何胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153660_comment'></div>麟趾实繁，顾徽荣而特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153660_comment'></div>未遂内朝之礼，但衔右戚之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153660_comment'></div>感抃兢荣，倍万伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1153660_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年3月3日</a>　三月三日，在京为右正言，作楚昭辅赠中书令制。作品：故赠侍中楚昭辅赠中书令制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1153501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故赠侍中楚昭辅赠中书令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（大中祥符八年三月三日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153501")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153501'>敕：朕昨者荐玉真区，观风近甸，眷兴王之旧壤，怀佐命之勋臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153501_comment'></div>存则懋延赏之恩，没则峻追荣之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153501_comment'></div>具官某端介自守，沉鸷有谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153501_comment'></div>早事先朝，罄输亮节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153501_comment'></div>尝总司夫枢务，实备竭于忠规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153501_comment'></div>属兹均庆之辰，宜霈漏泉之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153501_comment'></div>西台重地，右相崇资，允极哀荣，永昭幽穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153501_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1153501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1153501'><span class='label'>按：</span>年月据《宋会要辑稿》仪制一二之一五补。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1153501_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年4月</a>　四月，在京为右正言，有诗。作品：明州进芝草图。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明州进芝草并图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193513")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193513'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193513'>四明开奥壤，三秀发灵芝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193513'>如盖殊形耸，无根瑞气滋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193513'>晨敷台岭异，日茂下房奇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193513'>善气方回复，充图献玉墀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193513'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193513_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年7月24日</a>　七月二十四日，在京为右正言，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读史记诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>御制读史记诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年7月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193373")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193373_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_193373_0'>① 原缺，据孔跋本、院抄本补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193373'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193373'>陶唐明历象<span class='inlineComment2'>（尧钦若昊天、历象日月星辰。）</span>，茂气与天通<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193373'>举正分星度<span class='inlineComment2'>（以四方中星定分至。）</span>，归馀定岁功<span class='inlineComment2'>（以闰月正四时。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193373'>孟陬名不殄，南正道弥隆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193373'>自此垂三代，循环协大中<span class='inlineComment2'>（三王之正如循环，穷则反本。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193373'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193373'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193373_0'>⑴ 尧明时正度，茂气所生，民无大疫。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193373_0'>⑵ 颛顼命南正重司天，三苗乱德，孟陬殄灭。尧复重黎之后，使典之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193373_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193374?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年7月24日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193374'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193374'>昭昭齐鲁事，千载著良箴<span class='inlineComment2'>（齐鲁报政，可为箴规。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193374'>欲辨为邦体，先观布政心<span class='inlineComment2'>（为邦之否臧，系政之繁简。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193374'>变民非远略<span class='inlineComment2'>（伯禽曰：变其俗，革其礼。）</span>，从简是徽音<span class='inlineComment2'>（太公曰：简其君臣礼，从其俗。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193374'>北面无馀意，诚因惠物深<span class='inlineComment2'>（周公曰：鲁后世，其北面事齐矣。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193374'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193374_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_193375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193375?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年7月24日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193375'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193375'>汉武将从禅，须如亟释兵<span class='inlineComment2'>（武帝将封禅，先北巡释兵于须如。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193375'>甘泉诚毖祀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，乔岳纪尊名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193375'>加礼崇休祉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，修封盖号荣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193375'>岂同承帝箓，肆觐正权衡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193375'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193375'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193375_0'>⑴ 武帝至甘泉，为且用事太山，先类祠太一。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193375_0'>⑵ 司马相如封禅文云：建显号，施尊名。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193375_0'>⑶ 武帝上封毕，纵诸奇物，颇以加礼。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193375_0'>⑷ 汉武帝凡五修封。封禅文曰：盖号以况荣。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193375_0'>⑸ 国家奉元符，封云岱，肆朝觐。考律度，非汉所及也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193375_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年8月7日</a>　八月七日，在京为右正言，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读前汉书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读前汉书<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193390")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193390'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193390'>酂侯依日月<span class='inlineComment2'>（赞曰：萧何汉兴，依日月之末光。）</span>，天汉叙隆昌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193390'>迈德居三杰<span class='inlineComment2'>（何与张良、韩信为三杰。）</span>，观时定九章<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193390'>过因王尉辩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，功赖鄂君扬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193390'>终以同心美<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>，清宁赞后王<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193390'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193390'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193390_0'>⑴ 沛公初不欲王汉中。何曰：语云天汉，其称甚美。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193390_0'>⑵ 何捃摭秦法，取合于时者，作律九章。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193390_0'>⑶ 何为民请上林空地，下廷尉。王卫尉谏出之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193390_0'>⑷ 诸将争功，鄂千秋进曰：何功当第一。高祖曰：何虽有功，待鄂君乃得明。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193390_0'>⑸ 赞曰：何与曹参，二人同心，遂安海内。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193390_0'>⑹ 曹参相惠帝，民歌曰：萧何为法，讲若画一。曹参代之，守而勿失。载其清靖，民以宁壹。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193390_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193388?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月7日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193388'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193388'>子房天授汉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，不战道尤尊<span class='inlineComment2'>（良未尝有战斗功，而为王者师。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193388'>秘法盈编受<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，危机借箸论<span class='inlineComment2'>（郦生谋挠楚权，良借前箸筹之。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193388'>避封昭止足<span class='inlineComment2'>（良避齐三万户）</span>，辟谷厌尘喧<span class='inlineComment2'>（辟谷，不食谷。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193388'>莫讶萧规茂，从容有绪言<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193388'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193388'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193388_0'>⑴ 沛公常用张良策，良曰：沛公殆天授。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193388_0'>⑵ 父老授良书一编，乃《太公兵法》。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193388_0'>⑶ 良劝高祖立萧何为相，从容言天下事甚众。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193388_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193389?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月7日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193389'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193389'>高祖宽仁主<span class='inlineComment2'>（汉高宽仁大度。）</span>，淮阴变诈才<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193389'>设坛诚有礼<span class='inlineComment2'>（高祖设坛场，拜信为大将。）</span>，推食本无猜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193389'>怀惠初颙若<span class='inlineComment2'>（武涉、蒯通说信，信终不忍背汉）</span>，夸功抑殆哉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193389'>何如中正者，千载仰高裁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193389'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193389'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193389_0'>⑴ 赞曰：韩信等皆徼一时之权变，以诈力成功。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193389_0'>⑵ 信曰：汉王授我上将军，帅数万之众。解衣衣我，推食食我，言听计用。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193389_0'>⑶ 信对高祖曰：陛下不过能将十万，臣多多益善。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193389_0'>⑷ 赞曰：异姓而王者八国，终于灭亡。惟吴芮之起，不失正道。庆流支庶，著于甲今而称忠也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193389_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年8月18日</a>　八月十八日，在京为右正言，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读后汉书诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读后汉书诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193378")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193378'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193378'>明帝章朝物<span class='inlineComment2'>（赞曰：备章朝物。）</span>，三雍复旧常<span class='inlineComment2'>（光武建三朝之礼，帝始行之。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193378'>籯金赏西域<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，雅乐奏南阳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193378'>拜老鸿徽茂<span class='inlineComment2'>（赞曰：临雍拜老。）</span>，祈农盛典彰<span class='inlineComment2'>（帝耕籍田，以祈农事。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193378'>珍符昭美应，献寿表隆昌<span class='inlineComment2'>（百官以帝祥物显应，奉觞上寿。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193378'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193378'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193378_0'>⑴ 永平中复通西域，诸国皆遣子入侍。《西域传序》曰：先驯则赏籯金。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193378_0'>⑵ 十年，帝幸南阳。祠旧宅，作雅乐。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193378_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193377?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月18日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193377'>独行惩浇俗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，嘉名动远荒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193377'>至诚祈夏雨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，严意励冬霜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193377'>果行推陵险<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>，丰规叹履方<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193377'>孤高惟大逊，寿考茂祺祥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193377'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193377_0'>⑴ 历代惟《后汉书》有《独行传》，序云：以事非圆通而风轨有足怀者为传云。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193377_0'>⑵ 王烈，以德感（原作威，据《后汉书》改）人。居辽东，夷人奉之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193377_0'>⑶ 谅辅为广汉五官掾，积薪祈请，未日中而雨，世称至诚。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193377_0'>⑷ 序云：意严于冬霜。戴就、陆续也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193377_0'>⑸ 序云：蹈义（原作于，据《后汉书》改）陵险。缪彤、李善也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193377_0'>⑹ 赞曰：乘方不忒（原作成，据《后汉书》改）。注云：独行之人，乘履方正。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193377_0'>⑺ 李充字大逊，有高节，年八十，为国三老。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193377_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193376?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月18日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193376'>昭公详汉律，求比礼三千<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193376'>刻敝深文息<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，宽平治德全<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193376'>芳猷宣辅弼<span class='inlineComment2'>（宠为司空，奏议温粹，为相称职。）</span>，馀庆茂忠贤<span class='inlineComment2'>（宠子忠，为尚书令，忠正敢言。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193376'>方验来嘉瑞，仁矜理最先<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193376'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193376'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193376_0'>⑴ 陈宠字昭公，为廷尉，钩校律令，求删除为三千条，以应礼威仪三千。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193376_0'>⑵ 宠为奏，每附经典，从宽恕。深文刻敝于此少衰。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193376_0'>⑶ 宠上言：愿荡涤烦苛，以全至德。章帝纳之，务于宽厚。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193376_0'>⑷ 章帝纳宠言，除惨酷科禁五十馀事，是后人俗和平，屡有嘉瑞。又云，宠性仁矜。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193376_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年8月24日</a>　八月二十四日，在京为右正言，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读三国志诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读三国志诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193358")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193358'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193358'>白马当涂兆，黄家得岁兴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193358'>金符威既重，玉版事堪凭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193358'>汉火承前运，谯龙合旧徵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193358'>青云开后叶，下武倍兢兢<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193358'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193358'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193358_0'>⑴ 白马令李云曰：许昌气见于当涂高者，魏也。或遗太祖书曰：黄家当立。芝曰：得岁星者道始兴，今岁在大梁，魏之分也。太祖初封魏王，受虎符。《春秋玉版》曰：代赤者魏公子。苏林曰：魏以土德，承汉之火。汉熹平中，黄龙见谯。单飏曰：其国当有王者，不五十年亦当再见。中平四年，文帝生于谯。延康元年，嗣魏王位，黄龙复见。文帝之生，有青云如车盖。尝著《汉太宗论》曰：尉佗称帝，抚以恩德。吴王不朝，赐之几杖。时孙权不服，班其论于天下，亦不愿征伐也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193358_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193359?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月24日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193359'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193359'>许昌功未逞，江表地初平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193359'>汉帝居非远，吴侯志欲迎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193359'>壮图虽未遂，嘉虑实惟精。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193359'>终阙尊崇礼，何关慎器名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193359'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193359'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193359_0'>⑴ 曹公都许昌，孙策平江南。曹公力未能逞，以弟女配策小弟匡。后曹公与袁绍相拒于官渡，策时为吴侯，阴欲袭许迎汉帝，遭刺客不遂。评曰：割据江东，策之基兆也。而权尊崇未至。孙盛曰：权岂吝名器者乎？</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193359_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193360?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年8月24日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193360'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193360'>家乘桑盖瑞，国富卧龙才。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193360'>汉水神晖彻，灵图密命开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193360'>横天嘉气应，继日景云来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193360'>傥乏英雄器，三分亦殆哉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193360'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193360'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193360_0'>⑴ 先主舍东南，有桑如车盖，或谓当出贵人。徐庶谓先主曰：诸葛孔明，卧龙也。刘豹等上言曰：《河图》、《洛书》皆有备称皇之文。又时有景云祥风，从璿玑下来，数有气如旗，从西至东，中天而行，必有天子出其方。评曰：先主有高祖（原作谊，据《三国志》改）之风，英雄之器，时与吴魏三分天下。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193360_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年9月13日</a>　九月十三日，在京为右正言，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读晋书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读晋书<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年9月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193395")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193395'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193395'>安石陵霞致<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，清言振玉音<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193395'>鸿勋济世久<span class='inlineComment2'>（刘裕以安勋德济世。）</span>，厚德感人深<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193395'>朱组虽然袭<span class='inlineComment2'>（史臣曰：安禠薜萝而袭朱组。）</span>，虚舟岂易沉<span class='inlineComment2'>（赞曰：太保浮沉，旷若虚舟。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193395'>东山高志在，潇洒谢尘襟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193395'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193395'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193395_0'>⑴ 谢安，字安石，史臣曰：萧然有凌霞之致。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193395_0'>⑵ 安少诣王濛清言，濛曰：此客亹亹，为来逼人。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193395_0'>⑶ 安新城筑埭，后人追思之，名为召伯埭。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193395_0'>⑷ 安虽受朝寄，然东山之志，始末不渝，形于言色。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193395_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193396?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年9月13日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193396'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193396'>李重推清雅，初传友爱名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193396'>嘉言为时发，大谊傅经明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193396'>崇德诚堪慕，修身岂易倾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193396'>留心众才举，千载仰铨衡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193396'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193396'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193396_0'>⑴ 李重清雅，以友爱著称。赞曰：嘉言在兹。重迁中书郎，每疑议，参以经典。为平阳太守，崇德化，正身率下。为吏部郎，群才毕举。史臣曰：重锐志铨衡，留心隐逸。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193396_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193394?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年9月13日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193394'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193394'>士行勤武力，机鉴信良哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193394_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193394'>国赖桓文业，人推葛陆才。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193394_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193394'>殊祥双鹤至，吉梦八门开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193394_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193394'>终始全高节，诚因左翼推<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193394_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193394'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193394_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193394'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193394_0'>⑴ 陶侃字士行，累立武功。尝运甓斋外，曰：吾方致力中原，恐不堪事。其励志勤力，皆此类也。侃机神明鉴似魏武，忠顺勤劳似孔明、陆抗。成帝诏曰：乃者桓、文之勋，伯舅是凭。初侃丁母忧，有二客来吊，化为双鹤，冲天而去。又梦飞上天，见天门九重，已登其八，坠地伤左翼。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193394_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年9月</a>　九月，在京为右正言，受命同管勾景灵宫、会灵观公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年10月</a>　十月，在京为右正言，迁尚书礼部员外郎、知制诰，有谢表。作品：谢知制诰表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。任知制诰月份据夏竦此年仕历推定。）</span><div id='poem_1153582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知制诰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153582")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153582'>臣某言：伏奉制命，特授臣尚书礼部员外郎、知制诰，依旧玉清昭应宫判官、同修起居注、同管勾景灵宫公事，散官勋赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153582_comment'></div>紫微秘掖，获书命之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153582_comment'></div>丹屏仪曹，叨奏疏之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153582_comment'></div>仍兼载笔，尚赞殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153582_comment'></div>恩奖特隆，心颜无措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153582_comment'></div>窃惟二帝常典，以雅奥成章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153582_comment'></div>两汉训辞，以深厚为体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153582_comment'></div>上则记言于国史，次则视草于台郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153582_comment'></div>洎当涂应期，建通事之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153582_comment'></div>至天监在御，有知诰之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153582_comment'></div>命令攸资，选授殊重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153582_comment'></div>李唐之盛，良士继登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153582_comment'></div>奉四禁于锁闱，总六曹于画省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153582_comment'></div>在夫掌画，尤耸殊荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153582_comment'></div>况属昌辰，弥彰异举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153582_comment'></div>自非丰规茂识，环质明姿，则何以藻润帝谟，晖华时望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153582_comment'></div>如臣者文非近雅，材不逮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153582_comment'></div>幸对昌期，最为单绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153582_comment'></div>而自谏科赐问，学馆升华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153582_comment'></div>抱椠宣猷，类芳尘于往躅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153582_comment'></div>汗青史阁，颂鸿烈于先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153582_comment'></div>由是分校钱刀，佐司筦籥，遂叨书于言动，仍迁掌于勾稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153582_comment'></div>日就月将，仅成于注记；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153582_comment'></div>朱出墨入，才辨于纲条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153582_comment'></div>伏遇国家观象密都，奉符恭馆，适庆成而置使，俄倅事以叨荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153582_comment'></div>矧属寿域欢康，飙舆降格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153582_comment'></div>广太微之宪度，昭事于九皇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153582_comment'></div>集灞会之威神，钦崇于五镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153582_comment'></div>遽膺明命，并预攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153582_comment'></div>夫何琐微，有此荣庆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153582_comment'></div>敢不斋心紫府，竭虑清场，仰体精衷，肃祈灵鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153582_comment'></div>然而颛愚难变，震慄倍增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153582_comment'></div>未尝茍悦于人，亦无微忤于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153582_comment'></div>重念臣艺文至陋，资地素寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153582_comment'></div>衡门本乏于官荣，先父止供于传遽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153582_comment'></div>在臣所得，揣分已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153582_comment'></div>虽白首以不迁，亦甘心而知幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153582_comment'></div>岂谓尊位皇帝陛下仁深昭远，道极包荒，浚发鸿慈，主张孤进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153582_comment'></div>特预传于密旨，俾先示于试期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153582_comment'></div>仍亲择于近题，用曲全于懵学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153582_comment'></div>拔之群萃，置在清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153582_comment'></div>玷郎选而甚优，仗王言而斯重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153582_comment'></div>暨兼修于众职，实茂耸于荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153582_comment'></div>特达之恩，固无阶而可报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153582_comment'></div>恳激之意，惟刻骨以自铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153582_comment'></div>誓当更效涓埃，倍怀霜雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153582_comment'></div>秦官汉表，博考于旧仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153582_comment'></div>周诰汤盘，铺观于大要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153582_comment'></div>或奉真之暂暇，即温故以求新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153582_comment'></div>庶逃彼己之讥，上答非常之遇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1153582_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年10月</a>　十月，在京为右正言，迁尚书礼部员外郎、知制诰，有启谢某官。作品：谢授知制诰启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授知制诰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153797")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153797'>蒙恩特授前件官充职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153797_comment'></div>紫微秘掖，尘书命之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153797_comment'></div>丹屏仪曹，叨奏疏之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153797_comment'></div>尚兼载笔，仍赞殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153797_comment'></div>恩奖有加，心颜无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153797_comment'></div>此盖某官蚤垂颜采，曲借光仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153797_comment'></div>是致鸿钧，误甄微物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153797_comment'></div>矧蓍龟先见，尝昭示于前期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153797_comment'></div>松柏后彫，忽远流于荣问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153797_comment'></div>夫何后进，辱此重知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153797_comment'></div>顾报遇而末由，但衔恩而有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153797_comment'></div>区区之恳，莫喻万分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1153797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年10月4日</a>　十月四日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读宋书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读宋书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年10月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193385")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193385'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193385'>汉宗开圣绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋武帝，汉楚元王交之后也。）</span>，得岁与周同<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193385'>金石终移律<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，山河始誓功<span class='inlineComment2'>（《封宋公策》曰：永祚山河。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193385'>飞名传秘记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，嘉谶起游童<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193385'>能使奸豪詟，诚为一世雄<span class='inlineComment2'>（桓灵宝曰：帝足为一世之雄）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193385'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193385'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193385_0'>⑴ 帝初封宋公，岁在大火，与武王克商同。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193385_0'>⑵ 史臣曰：至于金石变声，柴火改物。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193385_0'>⑶ 《河洛谶》曰：二口建戈不能方，刘字也。空穴无主奇入中，寄字也。女子独立又为双，奴字也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193385_0'>⑷ 童谣曰：木亘当北度，走入浩浩乡。金刀既以克，亹亹金城中。木亘，言桓灵宝也。金刀，刘也。亹亹，盛也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193385_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193384?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年10月4日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193384'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193384'>镇恶才明举，英雄想冠时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193384'>推锋平内侮，直指定西陲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193384'>向使鸿勋就，宁忧霸业衰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193384'>如何丧方召，遗烈漫伤咨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193384'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193384'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193384_0'>⑴ 王镇恶平刘毅于江陵，灭姚泓于长安，馀寇未殄，为沈田子所害。宋高祖表之曰：镇恶机略明举。又曰：荆南搆衅，忧兼内侮。镇恶轻舟先迈，一朝雾散。王师西伐，有中原入渭之捷。指麾无前，实国之方、召也。殊绩未酬，宜蒙追宠。赠左将军。史臣曰：镇恶推锋直指，前无彊阵。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193384_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年12月23日</a>　十二月二十三日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读陈书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读陈书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年12月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193386")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193386'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193386'>猛奴多勇槩，大槊事戎征<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193386'>新蔡凶围陷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，鱼梁寇垒倾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193386'>溯风轻古法<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>，间道贵奇兵<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193386'>懋赏宜开府，番禺已尽平<span class='inlineComment2'>（文育平广州，以功授开府。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193386'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193386'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193386_0'>⑴ 周文育，小字猛奴。父荟，令兄子辞教书计，文育曰：谁能学此取富贵但有大槊耳。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193386_0'>⑵ 文育往新蔡慰劳，白水蛮谋执之。文育前锋陷阵，勇冠军中。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193386_0'>⑶ 初，武帝表文育为府司马，李仙仕将杜平虏于鱼梁作城，文育击之，平虏弃城而走。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193386_0'>⑷ 武帝拒徐嗣徽，将战，风急。帝曰：矢不溯风。文育曰：何用古法。抽槊上马，众军随之，风亦寻转。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193386_0'>⑸ 余孝顷举兵应萧勃，文育烧栅伪退，间道信宿达芊韶，据其中间，筑城飨士。贼徒大骇。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193386_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193387?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年12月23日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193387'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193387'>灵洗虽骁勇<span class='inlineComment2'>（程灵洗，少以勇力闻。）</span>，忠规讵可轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193387'>石城尝力战<sup class='reference
