inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，黟歙本连盟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193387'>京口殊勋茂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，临川叛寇惊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193387'>既能明号令，何惜务宽平<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193387'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193387'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193387_0'>⑴ 灵洗事王僧辨。武帝诛僧辨，灵洗力战于石头西门，招谕久之乃降，帝深义之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193387_0'>⑵ 初，侯景之乱，灵洗据黟歙聚徒拒景，奉新安太守萧隐主盟。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193387_0'>⑶ 武帝授灵洗兰陵太守，助防京口。平徐嗣徽有功，封侯。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_193387_0'>⑷ 周迪重寇临川，灵洗为都督，击之，迪走山谷间。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193387_0'>⑸ 灵冼性严急，御下苛刻，而号令分明。与士卒同甘苦，众亦以此德之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193387_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，有诗讽丁谓。作品：观藏珠。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三六。）</span><div id='poem_193251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观藏珠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193251")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_193251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193251'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193251'>敏手机心颇自安，遮藏有路巧千般。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193251'>主公当面无因见，只怕旁人冷眼看<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193251'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_193251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193251'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_193251_0'>⑴ 此诗出《宋文鉴》。原本缺，今补入。按：《墨客挥犀》卷八云：丁晋公与夏英公会宴斋宫，伶人有杂手技号藏擪者在焉。丁顾夏曰：古无咏藏擪诗，内翰可作一首。即席献诗云：舞拂跳珠复吐丸，遮藏巧技百千般。主公端坐无由见，却被傍人冷眼看。《东轩笔录》载此事，又易藏擪为弄碗，注皆与《文鉴》小异，故附录焉。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193251_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年1月26日</a>　正月二十六日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读后魏书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读后魏书<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年1月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193382")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193382'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193382'>伟哉登国世，灵武定戎兵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193382'>拓土能图大，求才实励精。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193382'>公侯新爵重，台省旧风清。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193382'>自匪谟长世，鸿图岂易成<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193382'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193382'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193382_0'>⑴ 道武奋其灵武，遂启中原。拔擢才识，宪章故实，制爵四等，追录旧臣，启建台省，悉用文士，制作经谟，咸在长世。登国，道武之纪号也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193382_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193506?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年1月26日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193506'>高祖宽仁主，哀矜信有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193506'>严刑几尽措，黎庶获安居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193506'>旧法躬刊定，繁文再刬除。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193506'>既平财谒路，清白励簪裾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193506'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193506'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193506_0'>⑴ 高祖驭宇，留心刑法，诏曰：参详旧典，务从宽仁。帝哀矜庶狱，卒从降恕，京师决死狱，岁不过五、六。置谨法者数百人，防喧斗于街衢，使民安其职业。命中秘官修改律令旧文，经御刊定。诏曰：门房之诛，犹在律策。可更议之，删除繁酷。又遣使循行天下，纠守宰之不法，食禄者跼蹐，财谒之路殆绝。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193506_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193383?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年1月26日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193383'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193383'>真君昭密命，纪号表兴隆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193383'>瑞著洪河外，文成翠石中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193383'>帝名传祖祢，历数感王公。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193383'>三五方兴运，明符事亦同<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193383'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193383'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193383_0'>⑴ 世祖奉《天文图录》，纪太平真君之号。五年，乐安王范等奏曰：臣闻帝王之兴，必有受命之符，三五之盛，莫不同之。今张掖郡列言大柳谷石，青质白章成文，记国家祖宗讳，著受命历数之符。王公已下，莫不感动。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193383_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年1月27日</a>　正月二十七日，在京为知制诰，作张士逊、崔遵度充寿春郡王友制。作品：工部郎中张士逊可户部郎中直昭文馆充寿春郡王府官制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1153405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>工部郎中张士逊可户部郎中直昭文馆充寿春郡王府官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年1月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153405")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153405'>敕：朕以爱子膺封建之礼，慎选端士以辅导之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153405_comment'></div>俾其居处出入之际，闻忠孝方正之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153405_comment'></div>故朕久思其人，未易轻授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153405_comment'></div>自非耆重，孰副柬求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153405_comment'></div>以尔具官张某资惟淑均，理尚清简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153405_comment'></div>纠弹宪府，漕挽外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153405_comment'></div>端懿之风，硕茂斯允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153405_comment'></div>以尔具官崔某业文甚雅，守道不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153405_comment'></div>引籍谏垣，励精史局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153405_comment'></div>老成之德，慰荐良多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153405_comment'></div>是用简自朕心，命之王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153405_comment'></div>第进左民之秩，或兼上馆之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153405_comment'></div>尔其祗荷宠章，协宣懿效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153405_comment'></div>规讽礼谊，以臻于道，予有望于汝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153405_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1153405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年2月13日</a>　二月十三日，在京为知制诰，因参修之《太祖太宗两朝国史》书成，迁户部员外郎，有谢表。作品：谢授户部员外郎表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。迁官事参王珪《夏文庄公竦神道碑铭》（《华阳集》卷四七））</span><div id='poem_1153583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授户部员外郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153583")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153583'>臣某言：伏蒙圣恩，特授臣尚书户部员外郎，依前玉清昭应宫判官、知制诰、同修起居注、同管勾景灵宫会灵观公事，散官勋赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153583_comment'></div>兰台约史，本无尘雾之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153583_comment'></div>画省分曹，遽进版图之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153583_comment'></div>顾增华于清禁，实交悸于营魂<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153583_comment'></div>伏念臣胄绪单平，艺文浅陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153583_comment'></div>而自父兄早世，族属无依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153583_comment'></div>弱冠自公，但冀寒宗之有后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153583_comment'></div>遗孤聚首，止期寸禄以代耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153583_comment'></div>岂意逢辰，夐踰始望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153583_comment'></div>翠绣华组，早齿于贵游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153583_comment'></div>秘掖殊庭，继尘于清选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153583_comment'></div>既容容而昧进，故碌碌以无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153583_comment'></div>乃者伏遇国家颂次先猷，总裁大法，获编联于注记，或是正于疑讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153583_comment'></div>最处后陈，莫效覃研之力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153583_comment'></div>尤为未至，曾微岁月之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153583_comment'></div>讵期金匮之成书，将预龙纶之第赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153583_comment'></div>况臣近叨殊渥，盖未踰时，犹夕惕之不遑，何宠灵之敢觊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153583_comment'></div>岂谓云雷播泽，靡间于寒荄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153583_comment'></div>日月分晖，遂通于幽隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153583_comment'></div>载循非次，实愧徼荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153583_comment'></div>此盖尊位皇帝陛下昭式孝思，俯矜微物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153583_comment'></div>察其遇主，本不因人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153583_comment'></div>申九重特达之知，开四海孤寒之望，靡拘常牒，务表鸿慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153583_comment'></div>敢不更励疲顽，仰承丹采？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153583_comment'></div>心非木石，固举族以衔恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153583_comment'></div>命等蜂蛾，奈无阶而报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153583_comment'></div>唯誓夙宵之志，仰酬焘育之仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1153583_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年2月21日</a>　二月二十一日，在京为知制诰，作《李氏可才人制》作品：李氏可才人制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1153504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李氏可才人制</a><span class='authorDate'>（大中祥符九年二月丙申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153504")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153504'>敕：某谦祗率礼，端懿传芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153504_comment'></div>自恪奉于宸闱，实荐更于岁籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153504_comment'></div>久播柔嘉之誉，宜推甄奖之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153504_comment'></div>俾升嫔侍之荣，用劝肃恭之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153504_comment'></div>钦兹宠渥，更励夙宵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153504_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1153504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年3月9日</a>　三月九日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读北齐书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读北齐书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年3月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193372")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193372'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193372'>段氏推忠武，论兵特造微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193372'>历朝功并建，诸将令咸依。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193372'>重位无矜色，高门有德辉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193372'>当时勋贵族，孰不仰家肥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193372'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193372'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193372_0'>⑴ 段韶，谥忠武，善于御众，得将士心，临敌之日，人人争奋。教训子弟，闺门雍肃。当世勋贵之家罕有及者。高祖曰：吾与韶论兵，殊有英概。史臣曰：韶辅相七君，志谢矜功，名不逾实。又赞云：韶大其门，望以德尊。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193372_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193371?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年3月9日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193371'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193371'>咸阳诚赳赳，倚任极维师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193371'>贵势隆门绪，忠诚翼帝基。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193371'>享年常戒满，避宠或兴咨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193371'>不学良无愧，嘉名已自垂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193371'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193371'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193371_0'>⑴ 斛律金为太师，封咸阳郡王。一门一皇后、二太子妃、三公主。尊宠之盛，当时莫比。尝谓子曰：我虽不读书，古来外戚无不倾灭。我家直以立勋抱忠致富贵，岂藉女也，尝以为忧。史臣曰：金以高祖拨乱之始，翼成王业，忠款之至，成此大功，故能终享遐年，位高百辟。观其盈满之戒，见动之几微者也。又赞云：赳赳咸阳，邦家之晖。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193371_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年3月19日</a>　三月十九日，在京为知制诰，因赵安仁之请，与刘筠并为宗正寺修玉牒官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　春，在京为知制诰，奉诏为顺容邵昭明作墓志铭。作品：故顺容邵氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1153898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故顺容邵氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153898")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153898'>大中祥符九年春二月甲午，顺容邵氏薨于京师太和宫本院之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153898_comment'></div>越三月壬子，葬于开封县清远乡繁台村奉先资福禅院之东北原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153898_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153898_comment'></div>顺容讳昭明，广陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153898_comment'></div>生禀嘉庆，赋质柔和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153898_comment'></div>泳汉方江，动谣于南国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153898_comment'></div>规图照史，秘景于华宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153898_comment'></div>先圣在潜，懿藩初建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153898_comment'></div>金房入侍，实首于庶姬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153898_comment'></div>璿室沉英，尝悲于外馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153898_comment'></div>洎攀鳞上汉，列职司衣，奉禓袭之宜，辨采章之品，肇封近郡，寔启博陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153898_comment'></div>爰以燕寝献功，女侍更直，佩环异等，礼序多仪，乃进号于小君，实并长于九御，被之紫服，昭以宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153898_comment'></div>矧属革辂吊民，躬平大卤，宸旒耀武，出抚魏都，束带从行，羽书狎至，罄宣懿立，以及凯旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153898_comment'></div>繇是赐涂金之裳，升荣于太监；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153898_comment'></div>辟冀国之壤，列位于尚宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153898_comment'></div>肃奉曾闱，总司众职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153898_comment'></div>严筦籥于扃禁，谨琮玺于缄縢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153898_comment'></div>法式并修，出纳惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153898_comment'></div>暨夫白云厌代，苍震承祧，改荥波之邑封，奉寿宫之象设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153898_comment'></div>西陵极望，莫从于神游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153898_comment'></div>中禁言旋，复司于旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153898_comment'></div>逮珍符锡瑞之纪号，乔岳上封之明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153898_comment'></div>超践宫正之资，载疏安陆之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153898_comment'></div>翼宣忠训，纠肃群居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153898_comment'></div>闲练典章，详明启奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153898_comment'></div>下推耆重之德，上嘉该总之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153898_comment'></div>遂开张楚之封，特拜司宫之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153898_comment'></div>寔创斯号，以旄厥劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153898_comment'></div>然而进退有常，终始一志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153898_comment'></div>含华凝曜，久冠于小星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153898_comment'></div>积德累勤，继充于彤史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153898_comment'></div>上肇崇位置，尊奖老成，宠以绛袍，列于嫔职，翟钧九等，班亚三妃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153898_comment'></div>感泣帝宸，赐予加数，承颜姒幄，进见异仪，宫掖之荣，近代无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153898_comment'></div>旋以忧劳成疹，年德寝高，深恻上仁，迁居别馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153898_comment'></div>勉膳之使，承诏之医，自冬涉春，相望于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153898_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153898_comment'></div>收华丽日，丧淑泉扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153898_comment'></div>常珍之期不及者二岁，向用之福咸备于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153898_comment'></div>黼帐悼怀，椒涂颁赗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153898_comment'></div>佳城既卜，幽隧将封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153898_comment'></div>爰诏左言，图徽沉碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153898_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1153898'>瑶台降芬，甘棠遗庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153898_comment'></div>德茂材淑，性资渊令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153898_comment'></div>参华六列，尽瘁两朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153898_comment'></div>闲练仪范，勤劳夙宵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153898_comment'></div>徽序方隆，馀年奄谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153898_comment'></div>结恋昌期，衔哀长夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153898_comment'></div>图形蕊馆，卜宅金园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153898_comment'></div>饰终之典，永贲重原。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1153898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年4月11日</a>　四月十一日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读后周书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读后周书<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年4月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193380")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193380'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193380'>思道怀廉慎，童年类老成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193380'>郡豪尝詟服，边寇亦清平。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193380'>临难输忠节，辞荣保令名。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193380'>贤哉蹈仁义，举世可为程<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193380'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193380'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193380_0'>⑴ 泉企字思道，九岁类成人。授讨寇将军，屡破边敌。为雍州刺史，豪右屏迹。忠尚廉慎，每除一官，忧见颜色，至于频辞。史臣曰：企临难慷慨，有人臣之节。岂非蹈仁义欤。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193380_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193379?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年4月11日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193379'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193379'>南荆推德厚，千里远从师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193379'>奥识通三教，清声冠一时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193379'>就招虽暂至，恋本固难移。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193379'>故老称前事，儒宗道益滋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193379'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193379'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193379_0'>⑴ 沈重字德厚，专心儒学，从师不远千里。仕梁为都官尚书，周太祖致书招之，令于紫极殿讲三教，朝士、儒生、桑门、道士至者二千馀人，凡所解释，咸为所推。后表请还梁，高祖诏答不忘恋本，深是嘉之。传序云：高祖命輶轩而致玉帛，招沈重于南荆。史臣曰：每闻故老称，重所学非止六经，故能驰声海内，为一代儒宗。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193379_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193381?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年4月11日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193381'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193381'>迁哲承华绪，深谋事战征。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193381'>艰危思大节，慷慨得群情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193381'>惠爱均戎旅，威名震敌城。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193381'>江陵摧寇势，宵遁赖奇兵<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193381'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193381'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193381_0'>⑴ 李迁哲少仕梁，袭沌阳侯，慷慨善谋画，群下甚得其情。后降周，太祖问之，对曰：世荷梁恩，不能死节。太祖嘉之，拜车骑将军，往略巴蜀，皆望风送款。与士卒均食，亲加医药，故军感之，人思效命。后陈寇江陵，迁哲往救，乘闇出兵击之，陈人乃遁</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193381_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年5月14日</a>　五月十四日，在京为知制诰，以景灵宫成，受赐袭衣、金带、器币。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年5月17日</a>　五月十七日，在京为知制诰，以景灵宫成，迁礼部郎中，有谢表。作品：谢授礼部郎中诸宫观充职表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。系年月日据《续资治通鉴长编》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1153584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授礼部郎中诸宫观充职表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年5月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153584")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153584'>臣某言：伏蒙圣恩，特授臣尚书礼部郎中，依前知制诰、同修起居注、充玉清昭应宫判官、同管勾景灵宫会灵观公事，散官勋赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153584_comment'></div>恭馆庆成，方均于大赉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153584_comment'></div>严宸第赏，猥及于无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153584_comment'></div>闻命已还，揣躬增惕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153584_comment'></div>伏念臣材质驽下，门绪寒微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153584_comment'></div>金马之中，乏葭莩之薄援；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153584_comment'></div>赤墀之右，无蟠木之先容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153584_comment'></div>不谓逢辰，误尘清选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153584_comment'></div>殊庭倅事，已耸于荣观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153584_comment'></div>禁掖代言，更踰于始望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153584_comment'></div>每励省循之志，深怀止足之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153584_comment'></div>此者伏遇国家挺尊祖之鸿徽，载崇于秘宇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153584_comment'></div>奉奠方之明德，并进于严祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153584_comment'></div>既成大壮之规，载洽《斯干》之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153584_comment'></div>爰曲覃于茂典，特进秩于中仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153584_comment'></div>揆景僝工，既非于己力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153584_comment'></div>偷荣昧宠，实愧于朝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153584_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下乐育群材，主张公道，怜其遇主，本不由人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153584_comment'></div>曲持特达之恩，用慰单平之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153584_comment'></div>天高地厚，欲报德以何阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153584_comment'></div>檗苦冰寒，但誓心而有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153584_comment'></div>周章感惧，倍百常钧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1153584_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年5月22日</a>　五月二十二日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读隋书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读隋书<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年5月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193397")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193397'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193397'>里仁怀远度，大雅擅嘉名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193397'>制礼通时变，求书赞治平。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193397'>推心清选举，从俭化黎氓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193397'>终始承恩遇，芳猷冠老成<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193397'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193397'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193397_0'>⑴ 牛里仁为秘书监，请开献书之路。为太常卿，定雅乐，议新礼。为吏部尚书，务在审慎，推心任委，隋之选举，于斯为盛。里仁荣宠当世，车服卑俭。隋室旧臣，终始信任，一人而已。史臣曰：里仁怀旷远之度，可谓大雅君子矣。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193397_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193508?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年5月22日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193508'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193508'>荣定诚嘉器，攀鳞属盛时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193508'>赏劳恩特异，知足志惟熙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193508'>壮节承昭感，崇基保燕诒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193508'>但能思卫霍，自可比蓍龟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193508'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193508'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193508_0'>⑴ 窦荣定沉深有器局，娶安成长公主。少小与高祖相厚，后以佐命功拜上柱国。迁秦州总管，逐虏于高越原，无水，荣定仰天太息，俄而澍雨。帝欲以为公，荣定上书云：西朝卫、霍，东都梁、邓，宠积骄盈，必致倾覆。上乃止。史臣曰：荣定运属时来，以功懋赏，保其禄位，贻厥子孙，崇基弗坠，盛矣。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193508_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193507?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年5月22日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193507'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193507'>子盖怀英断，南荒久驻留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193507'>清通承眷奖，恭顺望巡游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193507'>异宠荣乡党，丹诚破寇仇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193507'>边民思旧爱，刻石在西州<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193507'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193507'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193507_0'>⑴ 樊子盖为循州总管。十年，授武威太守。炀帝下诏曰：子盖干局通敏，履操清洁。又曰：宜加褒显，以昭奖励。后帝幸陇川宫，子盖倾望銮舆，帝下诏曰：卿夙怀恭顺，闻朕西巡，欣然望幸。是岁，朝于江都，帝曰：富贵不还故乡，衣绣夜行耳。敕庐江郡设三千人会，使谒坟墓。当时荣之。及留守东都，破杨玄感。帝谓曰：杨玄感之反，神明故以彰公赤心耳。后武威吏民刻石颂德。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193507_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年8月4日</a>　八月四日，在京为知制诰，作王随加工部郎中制。作品：刑部员外郎知制诰新知扬州王随可工部郎中余依旧制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1153414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刑部员外郎知制诰新知扬州王随可工部郎中馀依旧制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年8月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153414")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153414'>敕某：朕魏脽覃庆，多历岁年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153414_comment'></div>中外庶官，已从考陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153414_comment'></div>左右近职，宜有褒优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153414_comment'></div>以尔早列纶闱，出司留籥，能以宽政，惠兹蒸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153414_comment'></div>方别寄于藩条，宜特隆于郎选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153414_comment'></div>伫闻治迹，以称朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153414_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1153414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年8月</a>　八月，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制甘雨应祈。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_193355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制甘雨应祈</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193355")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193355'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193355'>少皞九秋当季月，成汤六祷动灵心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193355'>中宵甘澍均丰浸，尽日层云结远阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193355'>销去骄阳为瑞重，招来嘉应感人深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193355'>侧身修道殊千古，仍叔焉能播德音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193355'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193355_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年10月7日</a>　十月七日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读唐书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读唐书<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年10月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193391")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193391'>天祚文皇德，元成雅道施。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193391'>纳忠裨阙政，偃革致昌期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193391'>宴喜刀方解，人亡鉴遽隳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193391'>数行遗奏在，犹可动神祗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193391'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193391_0'>⑴ 魏徵字元成。太宗尝曰：徵劝朕偃革兴文，天下大宁。又宴日谓侍臣曰：徵献纳忠谠，古之名臣，何以加也。解佩刀赐之。徵亡，太宗曰：朕以三鉴防己，今亡一鉴矣。遣人就宅，得遗表一纸，数行可辨，云：任善人则国安，任恶人则国危。公卿之间，时有爱憎，所宜详慎。太宗曰：侍臣可书之于笏。史臣曰：徐邈、山涛、谢朏，比文贞雅道，不有遗行乎？</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193391_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193392?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年10月7日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193392'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193392'>哲辅延清问，元和致治平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193392_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193392'>从人成庶务，求瘼济群氓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193392_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193392'>务远能无怠，求材可倚成。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193392_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193392'>乃知虞舜德，恭已固难名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193392_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193392'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193392_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193392'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193392_0'>⑴ 元和初，杜黄裳为相。宪宗问以前代帝王之事，对曰：帝王之务，宵旰以求民瘼，舍己从人，不宜怠肆安逸。事有纲领小大，当务知其远者大者。固不可代下司职，但择人委任，责其成效，《传》称帝舜之德曰：夫何为哉，恭己南面而已。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193392_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193393?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年10月7日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193393'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193393'>贤哉段忠烈，振迹自邠宁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193393'>动必怀刚毅，何尝废典刑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193393'>英规方贯古，乐石谅难铭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193393'>密议初如用，艰危岂易形<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193393'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193393'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193393_0'>⑴ 段秀实初为安西别将，节度梁宰怀异图，秀实直言折之。寻为邠宁都虞候，号令严一，军府安泰，代宗闻而嗟赏之。后笏击朱泚遇害，德宗褒赠甚厚，官为立碑。初，秀实谏以禁兵少，不足以备非常，德宗不能用。后文宗时，宰臣李石曰：自古没身以卫社稷者，无如秀实之贤。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193393_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年11月2日</a>　十一月二日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制玉清昭应宫甘露歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制玉清昭应宫甘露歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年11月2日）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193495'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193495'>祝圣清场初展礼，鸿都向晓彰繁祉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193495'>郁郁纤枝正后凋，瀼瀼瑞采俄雰委。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193495'>吉云五色比还疏，况是严冬岁律馀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193495'>承以玉杯甘若蜜，凝于翠幄皎如珠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193495'>荐宸居，称寿酒，宣大庆兮仰归元首。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193495'>香馥馥，旆央央，建灵坛兮茂对多祥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193495'>天心信与人心会，诞节将临遽沾霈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193495'>式昭真荫祚君王，永锡遐龄齐覆载。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_193495_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年11月4日</a>　十一月四日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制会灵观甘露。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_193464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制会灵观甘露</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年11月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193464")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_193464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193464'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193464'>岳灵飞观耸神州，上圣钦崇德日休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193464'>嘉露霄零甘特异，贞条膏被势何稠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193464'>昆山宝器今初贮，汉苑仙盘昔未浮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193464'>自可纪年昭瑞应，更殊添海助洪流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193464'>堇荼变味承馀润，图牒腾芳焕大猷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193464'>愿采朝华和美玉，仰资宸算倍千秋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193464'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_193464_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年12月13日</a>　十二月十三日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读五代梁史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读五代梁史<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年12月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193369")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193369'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193369'>李唐危汉祚，巢寇盛黄巾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193369'>嘉士逢多难，忠言变逆伦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193369'>决疑归大顺，定策戮奸臣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193369'>宜享崇高赠，千年道更新<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193369'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193369'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193369_0'>⑴ 唐季之乱，危于汉末，巢寇之党，盛于黄巾。进士谢曈，投迹梁祖，说以归顺唐室。梁祖曰：我意素决，又复何疑？即日定策，戮伪监军使，悉众归顺。僖宗授曈太子率更令。开平初，追赠司徒</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193369_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193370?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年12月13日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193370'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193370'>赞贞怀武鸷，转斗历炎凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193370'>诚感泉源异，兵严士庶康。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193370'>临危见忠愤，对敌擅威强。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193370'>终始心无改，遗言更可伤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193370'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193370'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193370_0'>⑴ 牛存节字赞贞，武鸷有大节，威名闻于敌境，战斗累载有功。初，授潞州步军都指挥使，法令严整，士庶安之。为同州节度使，岐人迫城，城中井水咸苦，人不可饮，存节乃肃拜虔祝，择地凿八十馀井，味皆甘淡，以为至诚之感，病渴且消。河北用兵，存节忠愤弥笃，未尝言病。将终，戒其子以忠孝，不言及他</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193370_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　冬，在京为知制诰，奉诏为王中正撰写墓志铭。作品：故金紫光禄大夫检校礼部尚书右神武卫大将军致仕使持节康州诸军事康州刺史充本州团练使上柱国开国伯食邑七百户赠镇南军节度使太原王公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1153895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故金紫光禄大夫检校礼部尚书右神武卫大将军致仕使持节康州诸军事康州刺史充本州团练使上柱国开国伯食邑七百户赠镇南军节度使太原王公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1016年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153895")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153895'>夫天人之际，畴德以交；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153895_comment'></div>神明之后，因圣斯启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153895_comment'></div>故在汉则太一下降，著画法于寿宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153895_comment'></div>在唐则气祖有言，告鸿绪于仙李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153895_comment'></div>帝祚炎宋，真荫在天，挺生异人，潜达灵命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153895_comment'></div>清徽既往，故可得而纪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153895_comment'></div>公讳中正，字平叔，本名捷，汀州长汀县人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153895_comment'></div>其先缑岭疏源，将兵者三代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153895_comment'></div>太原辨族，世禄者四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153895_comment'></div>累紫重金，实繁于京洛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153895_comment'></div>分枝辨叶，或播于瓯闽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153895_comment'></div>礼让传家，乡闾观法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153895_comment'></div>至公曾祖安，卷道怀宝，洒落尘迹，与物无累，越世自高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153895_comment'></div>乃后李氏据有江表，急于聚兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153895_comment'></div>王父靖以州里之豪，屈致戎校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153895_comment'></div>伪置百里指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153895_comment'></div>烈考成，以事继烈，军始终于伪置宣猛指挥使，累赠左屯卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153895_comment'></div>然皆命不逢辰，职非所好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153895_comment'></div>绰有繁祉，茂启后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153895_comment'></div>公资气淑均，秉性淳质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153895_comment'></div>幼失怙恃，旁无周亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153895_comment'></div>逮于成人，勉率贾用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153895_comment'></div>杂良以苦，既不忍为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153895_comment'></div>欲赢恶嚣，终非其乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153895_comment'></div>以咸平初祀，憩星子故墟，偶会羽人，实姓赵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153895_comment'></div>一见如旧，叵测于灵契；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153895_comment'></div>信宿后别，徵有于绪言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153895_comment'></div>迨及其冬，再遇茅岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153895_comment'></div>长房奉酒，虽未入于壸中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153895_comment'></div>君贤负笈，遂同游于江介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153895_comment'></div>继市铅汞，对成白金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153895_comment'></div>乃访奇草于沥阳，辨灵液于庐岫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153895_comment'></div>五图金纪，授以采掇之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153895_comment'></div>九井玉横，传以合和之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153895_comment'></div>仍别付《灵方》、《环剑》、《缄縢》之书，戒曰：「非遇人君，慎勿轻述」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153895_comment'></div>宝诲方毕，烟驾俄隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153895_comment'></div>公乃累诣京室，求见无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153895_comment'></div>还过上饶，佯狂自异，坐抵常禁，谪戍岭南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153895_comment'></div>艰危之中，颠沛之际，保护所授，不敢少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153895_comment'></div>未几，灵游荐至，慰其忧虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153895_comment'></div>复取神剑、缄书，且云当候异日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153895_comment'></div>时供奉官、閤门祗候谢德权适总巡兵，颇闻异述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153895_comment'></div>及公私还毂下，置对有司，德权时方在朝，奏请免释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153895_comment'></div>乃礼之私第，鍊成药银，上献帝宸，遂解军籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153895_comment'></div>德权乐公之道，欸待累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153895_comment'></div>制伏之珍，尽畀而无吝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153895_comment'></div>秘授之事，万计而不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153895_comment'></div>一夕潜归，追及于路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153895_comment'></div>灵贶幽启，睿听有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153895_comment'></div>始命景福使、新州观察、勾当皇城司刘承圭案问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153895_comment'></div>缺甚隐，惟坚请于面陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153895_comment'></div>物色可知，固潜与于心会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153895_comment'></div>承圭因为改名中正，俾诣登闻，始得召见于龙图阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153895_comment'></div>云井之瑞，备对于绮窗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153895_comment'></div>柏寝之言，悉验于金刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153895_comment'></div>乃授许州散掾，留止京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153895_comment'></div>多与道人偶语于市，承圭诘之，乃曰：「即授法圣师也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153895_comment'></div>王君既来，遂容于请见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153895_comment'></div>金母将至，亦有于传言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153895_comment'></div>遂以景德四年降皇城司廨舍纱厨中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153895_comment'></div>戴冠佩剑，服皆青色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153895_comment'></div>玉文云襡，虽亚虚皇之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153895_comment'></div>紫羽华衣，迥异上卿之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153895_comment'></div>时承圭新堂方构，灵御频格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153895_comment'></div>金童列侍，咸佩于印章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153895_comment'></div>天官时来，若校于名籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153895_comment'></div>承圭窃聆旅语，始知乃司命真君焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153895_comment'></div>国家每欲究皇仪，展帝容，受乾文，袭黄瑞，公皆密致真诲，有开必先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153895_comment'></div>所以荐玉钦柴，祥兆咸报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153895_comment'></div>超图溢牒，见象日昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153895_comment'></div>洎夫登岱勒封，昭姓纪氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153895_comment'></div>刻日千里之外，时无纤尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153895_comment'></div>陟降万仞之上，安若平地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153895_comment'></div>非元真幽赞，百神奉涂，则孰预于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153895_comment'></div>粤以大中祥符三年，加上圣号曰九天司命天尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153895_comment'></div>擢授公银青光禄大夫、神武军将军致仕，乃给全奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153895_comment'></div>环列为重，方比于钩陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153895_comment'></div>奉身甚高，弥富于天爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153895_comment'></div>四年春，薶牲脽上，荐礼后皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153895_comment'></div>金辉发于大河，伟兆腾于冀壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153895_comment'></div>舄奕嘉应，觉悟蒸黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153895_comment'></div>乃授公本卫大将军，领高州刺史，赐勋上柱国，加金紫光禄大夫阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153895_comment'></div>五年冬，宫籥既严，夜漏将半，彤霞采雾，上属庆霄，芝盖云装，下临秘殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153895_comment'></div>绵绵圣胄，长发其祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153895_comment'></div>翼翼帝心，聿怀多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153895_comment'></div>乃奉上号圣祖上灵高道九天司命保生天尊大帝，赐公爵平晋县开国男，食邑四百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153895_comment'></div>七年春，仁里肇禋，嘉坛大报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153895_comment'></div>徽册登陛而密雪罢零，法驾在郊而烈风遽息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153895_comment'></div>肸蚃之际，昭报甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153895_comment'></div>乃进公爵开国伯，增邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153895_comment'></div>俄以本官检校礼部尚书，领本州刺史，兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153895_comment'></div>会稽未还，尝承衣绣之问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153895_comment'></div>辽东远别，甚慰华表之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153895_comment'></div>八年，以分刺之权，兼荣有日，诸武之卫，久次当迁，遂改左武卫大将军、康州团练使，皆使任如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153895_comment'></div>若乃国家举增高之典，以扬鸿徽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153895_comment'></div>展颂祇之仪，以答贶施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153895_comment'></div>荐混元之号，以尊妙本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153895_comment'></div>侔曲密之规，以事上帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153895_comment'></div>法太微之制，以昭祖德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153895_comment'></div>肇五门之宇，以崇岳镇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153895_comment'></div>新六寝之位，以壮宸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153895_comment'></div>在展寀之初，庆成之始，咸有灵命，以药金银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153895_comment'></div>为公贡献者，累巨万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153895_comment'></div>辉彩绝异，不类世宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153895_comment'></div>灵喻于方丈，价倍于朱提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153895_comment'></div>岂止丹砂可成，方为食器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153895_comment'></div>太山所出，遂铸袅蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153895_comment'></div>然自高真之降格也，崇奉之际，唯承圭预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153895_comment'></div>卒后玉清昭应宫资善堂都监、崇仪使、入内内侍省押班周怀政以慎重齐明，嗣掌其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153895_comment'></div>皇城司新堂遂改为元符观，及承圭私第曰东宅，公之通济坊私第曰南宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153895_comment'></div>皆碧辇停飙之地，太霞顿辔之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153895_comment'></div>琼干素羽，藻卫常严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153895_comment'></div>玉籁云钧，遗响相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153895_comment'></div>唯公得奉见给使，恭侍左右焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153895_comment'></div>九年秋，霜露缠忧，龙蛇起叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153895_comment'></div>王人临视，太医承诏，使者半道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153895_comment'></div>帝梦于来言，玉馆在庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153895_comment'></div>公知其独召，有加之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153895_comment'></div>真诲复宣曰：「慎密类汝者少，塑形于景灵宫，为吾辅，勿忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153895_comment'></div>初，公居甘泉坊第，徙居南宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153895_comment'></div>疾亟，遂还甘泉坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153895_comment'></div>以十月乙亥启手足，享年五十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153895_comment'></div>上嗟悼久之，命怀政监护葬事，赠镇南军节度使，仍塑像于景灵宫天兴殿之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153895_comment'></div>达巷之香，显十旬之异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153895_comment'></div>特吊之客，有双鹤之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153895_comment'></div>以十二月甲申窆于开封县之汴阳乡槲罔村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153895_comment'></div>娶渤海施氏，累封吴兴郡君，以公昭赠加等，特进封本郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1153895_comment'></div>夫人生于景胄，夙茂于闺风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1153895_comment'></div>同穴之言，尝盟于皦日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1153895_comment'></div>偕老之痛，盖极于帷堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1153895_comment'></div>子四人，曰世宁、世长、世昌、世融，并任右班殿直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1153895_comment'></div>学礼而立，象贤以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1153895_comment'></div>既冠胜衣，已闻于警悟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1153895_comment'></div>作室肯构，伫见于蕃昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1153895_comment'></div>女四人，姆训甚严，淑德皆备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1153895_comment'></div>奉嫔庆旅，未闻鸣凤之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1153895_comment'></div>率礼公宫，将奉采蘩之祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1153895_comment'></div>而皆靡瞻颒泣，何怙衔哀，孺慕无时，柴毁过礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1153895_comment'></div>有后之美，岂曰诬哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1153895_comment'></div>公通简有常，慎默无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1153895_comment'></div>自肃祗真眷，传致灵心，非觌至尊，未尝轻泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1153895_comment'></div>至于黄冶所就，靡敢忘施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1153895_comment'></div>贡献之馀，则周济贫乏，崇奉仙释，时论善之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1153895_comment'></div>哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1153895_comment'></div>隙驷难留，藏舟易失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1153895_comment'></div>青乌卜宅，虽示于归全；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1153895_comment'></div>太阴练形，未知其化去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1153895_comment'></div>佳城既启，远日有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1153895_comment'></div>虑宰木之将折，惧芳猷之或坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1153895_comment'></div>仰承中诏，俾勒坚珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1153895_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_150_1153895'>灵王之穆，世烈滋芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1153895_comment'></div>誓淮献吉，解佩归祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1153895_comment'></div>奕叶弥繁，异人挺出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1153895_comment'></div>性易言简，体放心逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1153895_comment'></div>仰缘灵契，夙契元真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1153895_comment'></div>潜通密命，昭启昌辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1153895_comment'></div>庆发祥流，礼交乐举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1153895_comment'></div>三境开光，百神合序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1153895_comment'></div>朱房七映，密侍睟容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1153895_comment'></div>丹经九籥，潜侔化工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1153895_comment'></div>官重训齐，任隆环卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1153895_comment'></div>忽痛兰摧，尽疑蝉蜕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1153895_comment'></div>将坛追宠，仙馆留形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1153895_comment'></div>重原既卜，幽隧爰扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1153895_comment'></div>草茫茫兮风烈烈，素骖断兮哀笳绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1153895_comment'></div>岸之曲兮水之阳，露寒泣兮秋云苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1153895_comment'></div>繄夜台兮叵测，唯令誉兮弥彰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_166_1153895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，受诏与赵安仁等重修《太祖实录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年1月12日</a>　正月十二日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制恭谢南郊。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_193504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制恭谢南郊</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年1月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193504")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_193504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193504'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193504'>高真降佑开鸿业，哲后祈禠福下民。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193504'>靖馆斋心成钜典，嘉坛报贶奉严禋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193504'>时遵夏历春当孟，礼宪周郊日在辛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193504'>图箓先登符命显，祖宗昭配孝思伸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193504'>侍祠卿士衣缨列，随兆星辰俎豆陈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193504'>穆穆苍灵潜扈跸，寥寥风伯豫清尘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193504'>再登午陛虔诚达，三烛奔精美应臻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193504'>万寿无疆增介祉，永蠲牲玉事神明。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193504'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_193504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年1月22日</a>　正月二十二日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读五代史后唐史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读五代史后唐史<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年1月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193362")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193362'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193362'>燕赵生奇士，仇方决志平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193362'>十年常竭节，一剑早知名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193362'>自取河南镇，终辞霸府兵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193362'>飞鹰昭庆路，穷达有高情<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193362'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193362'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193362_0'>⑴ 符习少事王镕，镕为张文礼所害，诉于庄宗。曰：臣本赵人，事王氏。故使常授臣一剑，俾臣平荡凶寇，愿悉本军诛其逆党。庄宗令阎宝等助讨之，诛文礼。庄宗割相卫二郡置义宁军，以习为节度。习对曰：魏博六州，见系霸府，不宜遽有割隶。但授臣河南一镇，臣自攻取。乃授天平军节度。庄宗十年，沿河战守，常以本军从，心无顾望。后安重诲不说，授太子太师致仕，归故里赵州昭庆县。飞鹰痛饮，周游田里。史臣曰：符习乃赵之奇士也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193362_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193361?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年1月22日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193361'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193361'>长兴秉钧者，子晦道攸隆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193361'>刚介昌言远，忠清茂泽丰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193361'>懿文常体道，妙略早从戎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193361'>可惜亏同德，当年阻建功<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193361'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193361'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193361_0'>⑴ 李愚字子晦，长兴初入相。后秦王恣横，权臣避祸不暇，无敢言者。愚性刚介，往往形言，人无唱和者。不治第宅，官借延宾馆居之。常有疾，近臣宣谕，延之中堂，设席惟莞秸，明宗特赐帷帐茵褥。尝为文曰《仲尼遇》、《颜子寿》等篇，人皆称之。初，以翰林学士从魏王征蜀，郭崇韬（原作安重诲，据《旧五代史》改）问计，皆中。后冯道出镇，与刘煦同在中书。煦与道婚家，或旧事不便要釐革者，对论不定，由是罢相。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193361_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制读五代晋史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span>奉和御制读五代汉史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span>奉和御制读五代周史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_193367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193367?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读五代晋史<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193367")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193367'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193367'>子文怀妙识，奥学洞天常。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193367'>恬淡游莲幕，谦虚践玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193367'>至仁周仆御，大雅变词章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193367'>慎默诚无怠，危机可尽防<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193367'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193367_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193367'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193367_0'>⑴ 崔棁字子文，好学，博涉经史，闲居二十年，专以著述为事。王瓒表为从事，性恬淡，不汲汲于荣利。为翰林，撰乐章新词，教舞童歌之，高帝嘉之。有人借文本写者，则曰：有前贤，有来者，安用此。端坐寡言，尝云：非止致人爱憎，或干人之忌讳。指命仆役，亦用礼节。盛暑祁寒，不使冒犯。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193367_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193368?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193368'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193368'>大雅怀忠孝，当年效战征。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193368'>询谋无败事，临敌有奇兵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193368'>安陆祅狂殄，宗城寇难平。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193368'>察廉能恻下，何患政难成<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193368'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193368'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193368_0'>⑴ 马全节字大雅，历博、单、郢、沂四州刺史，在郡有政声。迁金川防御使，会蜀兵攻城，出奇拒战，贼乃退。后为义武军节度，国家有所调发，朝受命而夕行，治生馀财必充贡奉。事母王氏至孝，温凊面告，毕尽其礼。动与幕客谋议，故鲜有败事。镇中山日，杜威奏括民粟。全节曰：边民遇蝗旱，家食方困，官司复扰之，则民不堪命矣，我为廉察。安忍效尤。百姓称其德。史臣曰：全节平安陆之祅，预宗城之战，功既茂矣，贵亦宜然。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193368_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读五代汉史<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193364")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193364'>危邦有贤哲，力战镇州平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193364'>革弊还疲庶，从宽悦众情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193364'>爱人惟责已，徇节几忘生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193364'>青史惟馨在，千年仰令名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193364'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193364'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193364_0'>⑴ 王周累历郡守，安重荣以镇州叛，从杜重威讨平之，授贝州节度使。移镇泾州，前帅张彦泽苛虐，部民逃者五千户，周下车革前弊，逃民复归。迁镇州节度，禀性宽惠，人庶便之。杜重威引契丹，临城谕之。周曰：受国重恩，不能死战，而以兵降，何面目南行见人主与士大夫乎？乃痛饮欲引决，家人止之。初，守信都，桥败覆民租车，周曰：刺史之过也。乃还所沈粟，出私财以修之，民庶悦焉。史臣曰：晋汉之际，取符竹者多矣，其间有及民之惠，如王周之阃政，盖其优者也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193364_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193363?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193363'>求益诚贤牧，廉平致乐康。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193363'>欢谣腾近辅，盛典茂徽章。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193363'>旧相亲褒记，黎民竞感伤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193363'>丰碑应不朽，千载咏惟良<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193363'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193363'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193363_0'>⑴ 刘审交字求益，累任州郡，绥抚有术，凋弊复苏。为汝州防御使，汝为近辅，号称难治，审交尽去烦弊，百姓歌之。卒，郡人聚哭，乞留葬，立碑起祠。诏曰：褒贤奖善，岂限彝章，可特赠太尉。吏民所请宜依。故相冯道曰：知其为人廉平慈善，无害之良吏也，吏民怀感如此。著《痛哭词》六章，镌于碑阴。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193363_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制读五代周史<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首并注）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193366")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193366'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193366'>文懿艰危际，虚心自晏宁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193366'>依违惭问战，闲淡贵无刑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193366'>镇俗惩浮躁，尊儒镂典经。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193366'>忠诚亏美谥，良足愧幽灵<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193366'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193366'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193366_0'>⑴ 冯道历相四朝，虽逢艰危，不易其度。怀才抱业者皆引用，履行浮躁者必抑而镇之。节制同州日，闲淡，狱市无扰。晋祖尝以兵事问道，对曰：神武睿略，须从独断，臣本自书生，为陛下在中书，不敢有一毫之失也。命学官刊板流布。谥曰文懿。史臣曰：事四朝，相六帝，可得谓之忠乎？不得谥为文忠、文正者，盖谓此矣。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193366_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193365?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193365'>文伯怀明识，英规世所推。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193365'>济时陈策画，急用备论思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193365'>隘郭爰增广，烦音亦改为。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193365'>温恭非不济，感遇志如兹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_193365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193365'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《文庄集》卷三一<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_193365_0'>⑴ 王朴字文伯，世宗时言平边策，世宗重其器识。世宗以英武自任，有包举天下之志。计事者不喻其志，惟朴神气劲峻，性刚决有断，凡所谋画，动惬世宗之意，故急于登庸。为端明殿学士，命广京城，靡不由其心匠，未几迁枢密使。星纬声律，毕殚其妙，所撰《律准》，并行于世。史臣以为太刚，不能济之以温恭。臣以为朴感世宗之遇，急于行事，无所顾望，故如斯也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193365_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年2月5日</a>　二月五日，在京为知制诰，有诗和宋真宗。作品：奉和御制宣读天书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_193499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制宣读天书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年2月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193499")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193499'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193499'>赫赫穹符迪庆基，巍巍真绪拥繁禧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193499'>控飙灵御传天意，候日珍文告帝期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193499'>奉诣乔丘彰锡祉，胙壤濑乡修茂礼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193499'>宸闱薰祓款云舆，戎候耕耘櫜象弭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193499'>纪号惟新岁历呈，三元初吉协休辰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193499'>徽册奉天熙事蒇，丕名尊祖皇仪展。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193499'>太宫荐鬯孝思伸，阳位升烟鸿庆远。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193499'>瑞应纷纶百福同，寅威宝命务尊崇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193499'>布宣精意诚明显，申饬攸司宪度隆。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193499'>将披秘蕴昭灵契，欲使万方知帝意。<div id='poem_sentence_9_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_193499'>肆眚端门诏毕旋，灵场预启百枝燃。<div id='poem_sentence_10_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_193499'>夙陈路寝敷瑶席，躬荐真香奏瑞烟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_193499'>三辰淳耀居斋室，阶满祥蓂当望日。<div id='poem_sentence_12_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_193499'>大裘陟降既登歌，群后延登皆上笏。<div id='poem_sentence_13_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_193499'>元辅披縢圣训扬，枢臣援翰宝文彰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_193499'>有虞出洛龟休跃，唐氏衔图凤罢翔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_193499'>辞若洞章皆擿句，字如龙篆宛分行。<div id='poem_sentence_16_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_193499'>森沉虎旆严真卫，肃穆珠旒增洁志。<div id='poem_sentence_17_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_193499'>敬受丹书岂易侔，式旌玉刻诚难继。<div id='poem_sentence_18_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_193499'>修修羽帐降星辰，杳杳飙斿驻圣真。<div id='poem_sentence_19_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_193499'>庭际烟霞辉晔晔，天中鸾鹤羽兟兟。<div id='poem_sentence_20_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_193499'>微密妙言爰备举，庞鸿盛则已宣臻。<div id='poem_sentence_21_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_193499'>一一嘉猷保元后，谆谆深旨为含生。<div id='poem_sentence_22_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_193499'>写成别笈缄藏密，荐献礼周弥袭吉。<div id='poem_sentence_23_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_193499'>恍恍真心显道枢，穰穰景佑归宸历。<div id='poem_sentence_24_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_193499'>升闻璿宙洽神欢，昭纪琅函为睿式。<div id='poem_sentence_25_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_193499'>万灵潜卫极寅威，九序相趋皆励翼。<div id='poem_sentence_26_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_193499'>绵宇弥隆清净风，虚晨益鉴馨香德。<div id='poem_sentence_27_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_193499'>岂独飞英冠百王，祗延道荫永欢康。<div id='poem_sentence_28_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_193499'>薰弦浚发南风咏，丕显清衷报彼苍。<div id='poem_sentence_29_193499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_193499'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_193499_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年3月16日</a>　三月十六日，在京为知制诰，作夜落隔归化为怀宁顺化可汗制。作品：甘州外甥回纥王伊噜格勒可特进怀宁顺化汗王制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1153502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甘州外甥回纥汗王伊噜格勒可特进怀宁顺化汗王制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年3月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153502")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153502'>敕：王者孝治万方，盖重展亲之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153502_comment'></div>恩加群后，务昭崇德之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153502_comment'></div>矧在吾甥，久绥远略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153502_comment'></div>特举褒优之命，用伸眷倚之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153502_comment'></div>具官某茂烈传家，英威服众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153502_comment'></div>智虑深邃，详练于武经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153502_comment'></div>志行直方，克敦于臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153502_comment'></div>而自抚临西夏，屏翰中原，允彰保塞之勋，特茂勤王之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153502_comment'></div>仍远修于职贡，是愈见于忠诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153502_comment'></div>实简朕心，特隆朝奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153502_comment'></div>进褒功之懿号，兼驭贵之殊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153502_comment'></div>夐越等威，用旌忠毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153502_comment'></div>噫，山河誓宠，朕务在于推恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153502_comment'></div>金石盟心，尔无忘于报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153502_comment'></div>终始一志，以保令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153502_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1153502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年7月</a>　七月，在京为知制诰，作魏咸信赠中书令制。作品：故保平军节度使同中书门下平章事驸马都尉魏咸信可赠中书令制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1153499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故保平军节度使同中书门下平章事驸马都尉魏咸信可赠中书令制</a><span
