class='authorDate'>（1017年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153499")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153499'>敕：国家褒崇密戚，伤悼茂功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153499_comment'></div>中铉联荣，久参于眷倚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153499_comment'></div>西台正位，早极于追旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153499_comment'></div>具官某文武兼资，箕裘济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153499_comment'></div>受勋荫于怀衽，禀命略于庭闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153499_comment'></div>博通礼乐之原，周知教化之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153499_comment'></div>而自降嫔鲁馆，推毂汉坛，出总藩条，入陪鼎席，勤王之业，纪在太常，体国之忠，书于甲令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153499_comment'></div>方全飨用之福，遽兴慭遗之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153499_comment'></div>特加右相之崇，用极惟亲之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153499_comment'></div>英魂不昧，尚服宠灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153499_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1153499_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年9月</a>　九月，在京为知制诰，作祭王旦文。作品：中书祭故太尉尚书令王文贞公文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1153900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书祭故太尉尚书令王文贞公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153900")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153900'>炎正宣精，昴灵储粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153900_comment'></div>载降英贤，允怀明懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153900_comment'></div>心有常照，材无定器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153900_comment'></div>沉寂内融，于严外贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153900_comment'></div>润色谟训，藻丽词丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153900_comment'></div>周旋枢近，识箴言忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153900_comment'></div>爰裨衮职，克亮天功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153900_comment'></div>畴咨熙载，若时登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153900_comment'></div>虑善兴谋，协中布画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153900_comment'></div>非恤人言，务均王泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153900_comment'></div>内靖九流，外清四貉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153900_comment'></div>画像云台，镂勋丹册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153900_comment'></div>萝图锡祉，飙御延禧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153900_comment'></div>梁阴让德，脽壤奉祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153900_comment'></div>朝元景亳，荐号真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153900_comment'></div>交窥秘藏，首赞鸿仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153900_comment'></div>懿彼嘉猷，遘兹亨会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153900_comment'></div>旷古难偕，前良罕对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153900_comment'></div>异宠云游，隆恩泽霈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153900_comment'></div>礼绝地尊，功高贵倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153900_comment'></div>封踰万室，位冠三阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153900_comment'></div>忧民瘁志，体国劳怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153900_comment'></div>辞荣中铉，进秩东台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153900_comment'></div>叩阍斯切，出綍终回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153900_comment'></div>荐陟上公，靖颛司馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153900_comment'></div>霜露增忧，龙蛇起叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153900_comment'></div>玉麈停挥，瑶琴罢玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153900_comment'></div>疹积膏肓，身悲梦幻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153900_comment'></div>青霞难挹，琼蕊无徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153900_comment'></div>太医连袂，中使盈庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153900_comment'></div>载纡诏跸，深恻皇情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153900_comment'></div>拖绅犹对，逝水俄倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153900_comment'></div>痛极歼良，哀深抚几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153900_comment'></div>制服推恩，易名进美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153900_comment'></div>宅兆将安，涂刍既备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153900_comment'></div>衢巷辍舂，都城罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153900_comment'></div>某等早陪伊鼎，获奉萧规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153900_comment'></div>情条共惨，嵩恒方隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153900_comment'></div>徘徊素馆，顾慕容衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153900_comment'></div>恭陈宿奠，永隔清徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153900_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1153900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　秋，在京为知制诰，奉诏为赵允诚继室吕氏作墓志铭。作品：皇侄康州团练使夫人吕氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1153899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇侄康州团练使夫人吕氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153899")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153899'>夫人吕氏，故丞相赠司徒正惠公之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153899_comment'></div>正惠公之贵也，鲁祖衮赠中书令，祖琦赠太师、尚书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153899_comment'></div>其先太岳述职，仰悟灵心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153899_comment'></div>尚父表海，下因旧俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153899_comment'></div>景祐垂世，积德在人，门生忠贤，亦启明淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153899_comment'></div>夫人夙禀家训，幼勤女职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153899_comment'></div>动则申礼，保阿是咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153899_comment'></div>烝而献功，纮綖悉备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153899_comment'></div>言念诗史之意，步中珩璜之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153899_comment'></div>加以文绣设色，必穷其丽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153899_comment'></div>哀筝度次，尤尽其音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153899_comment'></div>国家璿源炽昌，仙绪蕃衍，选建明德，广封连城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153899_comment'></div>棣萼相依，犬牙错峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153899_comment'></div>上隆惇叙之化，下嘉信厚之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153899_comment'></div>扶植基干，毕侯支庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153899_comment'></div>崇右戚之惠，尽家人之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153899_comment'></div>至若宗子授室，王姬下嫁，必选令族，以纳多祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153899_comment'></div>楚王亲则帝兄，位极人爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153899_comment'></div>宝玉分器，芝兰在庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153899_comment'></div>其第四子天水郡公允诚生禀粹和，早闻诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153899_comment'></div>怀金上序，结绶内朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153899_comment'></div>号为宗英，特茂宸宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153899_comment'></div>始娶赠邠州观察使潘惟正女，不幸早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153899_comment'></div>宗臣上言，礼当继室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153899_comment'></div>上乃念正惠之昔佐先帝，厥有大劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153899_comment'></div>当缀衣之辰，受傅圣之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153899_comment'></div>寝丘之封虽远，高门之庆未移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153899_comment'></div>乃诏申以婚姻，宠其阀阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153899_comment'></div>枚卜献吉，踰八世之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153899_comment'></div>大璋纳礼，丰六版之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153899_comment'></div>夫人遂以大中祥符五年夏六月乙丑，召见汉幄，进对尧门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153899_comment'></div>象服晖华，拜赐于中禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153899_comment'></div>油軿拥从，言旋于旧居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153899_comment'></div>观者荣之，忠臣知劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153899_comment'></div>越明年秋七月辛亥，归于郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153899_comment'></div>六珈盛饰，百两亲迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153899_comment'></div>仆御授绥，傅姆加景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153899_comment'></div>华烛光炤，煌煌如昼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153899_comment'></div>从者毕袗，祁祁若云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153899_comment'></div>有司相仪，太官供具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153899_comment'></div>婚姻之礼，特盛于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153899_comment'></div>洎五月中参，三月庙见，象揥居手，宝翟在衣，动止肃雍，词气舒婉，式瞻贵里，为宪宗家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153899_comment'></div>若乃荐豆公侯之宫，胖载旧姑之室，匪鸡之勤儆戒，惟丝之求善匹，蘋藻之意柔洁，山河之体容润，固已极图传之言，岂止率鞶缡之训者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153899_comment'></div>方将下司封之诏，举从夫之典，启汤沭之邑，增车服之数，而蕣华易落，隙驹难驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153899_comment'></div>德宫永逝，虽大化之攸同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153899_comment'></div>硕人无子，痛芳音之莫继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153899_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153899_comment'></div>以七年秋九月壬寅终于内寝，享年十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153899_comment'></div>尚宫赐襚，辍朝二日，权厝于奉先资福禅院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153899_comment'></div>以天僖元年八月己酉，葬于河南府永安县南訾乡漫流村潘夫人墓之西北原，从吉卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153899_comment'></div>诏左骐骥使、澄州刺史、入内内侍省都知张景宗营葬事，以著作郎、直集贤院徐奭摄大鸿胪监护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153899_comment'></div>歛封有日，执綍将行，乃命史臣，图芳幽础。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153899_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1153899'>降神灵绪，赐履遥源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153899_comment'></div>间生邦媛，选俪宗贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153899_comment'></div>顾史永箴，披图问礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153899_comment'></div>德盛年阙，华繁实委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153899_comment'></div>梁台遣奠兮组帐烟空，文园安宅兮松路尘封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153899_comment'></div>哀兰仪之永閟，唯玉誉之无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1153899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年11月</a>　十一月，在京为知制诰，为魏咸信作墓志铭。作品：故保平军节度使同中书门下平章事驸马都尉赠中书令魏公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1153896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故保平军节度使同中书门下平章事驸马都尉赠中书令魏公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153896")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153896'>方国家东禅之七祀，上朝景亳，驻跸睢阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153896_comment'></div>肇为京都，纪兴王之壤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153896_comment'></div>永怀祖德，思逮事之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153896_comment'></div>以忠武军节度使、驸马都尉钜鹿公亲旧兼崇，勋贤莫贰，内出明制，进位中台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153896_comment'></div>赴上于鼎司，接武于诸相，进退体貌，无与比焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153896_comment'></div>越明年冬十月，上斋居宣室，勤恤万区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153896_comment'></div>以全魏近藩，朔垂右地，边圉之势胜，京师之屏翰，士马雄壮，非元功不足以镇重，遂以公判天雄军府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153896_comment'></div>政治宽简，狱讼衰止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153896_comment'></div>吏民守阙，请立石而纪颂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153896_comment'></div>嘉谷生境，方优诏而旌美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153896_comment'></div>不幸起龙蛇之叹，罹霜露之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153896_comment'></div>天禧元年正月，国家奉有帝之册，荐尊祖之名，祼鬯庙祧，升烟郊兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153896_comment'></div>天子均聿怀之庆，举先亲之典，制授公保平军节度使，相国如故，且诏赴阙，肩舆就第，中使相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153896_comment'></div>虚中日望其有瘳，搢绅方咏其多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153896_comment'></div>无何秋气始至，疢疹增剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153896_comment'></div>载纡诏跸，慰以圣言，俾加勉膳之勤，尚期勿药之喜，仍赐白金三百斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153896_comment'></div>天不憖遗，福善则虚，七月甲子以不起闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153896_comment'></div>上抚几震悼，临哭出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153896_comment'></div>书忠甲令，弥念于良臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153896_comment'></div>画像云台，方追于英烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153896_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，真命世之贤佐，生人之间杰也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153896_comment'></div>公讳咸信，字国宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153896_comment'></div>其先大名献兆，屯固流祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153896_comment'></div>西汉肇高平之封，东晋启剧阳之土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153896_comment'></div>冠冕奕世，谱牒联华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153896_comment'></div>公之远祖，始家汲郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153896_comment'></div>唐失天命，禄去王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153896_comment'></div>鲁王父楚，卷怀琛宝，遁世而长往，累赠太师兼侍中、魏国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153896_comment'></div>鲁祖妣郭氏，追封燕国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153896_comment'></div>王父韬，袭善以处躬，含和而味道，累赠中书令、越国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153896_comment'></div>祖妣李氏，追封晋国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153896_comment'></div>烈考仁溥，仰承积德，生蕴明略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153896_comment'></div>往佐周命，厥有大勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153896_comment'></div>爰立鼎司，兼崇枢府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153896_comment'></div>金印双导，盖极宠露之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153896_comment'></div>火德应天，首宣欣戴之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153896_comment'></div>嘉谋懿范，国史详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153896_comment'></div>公之受脉于藩，登庸继业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153896_comment'></div>屡奉明祀，载洽鸿禧，有司累赠烈考尚书令，追封秦王，谥曰宣懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153896_comment'></div>母李氏，封秦国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153896_comment'></div>继母李氏，追封韩国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153896_comment'></div>公韵宇沉邃，资质丰硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153896_comment'></div>积怀衽之善教，耸公侯之奇表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153896_comment'></div>话言详雅，动止有度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153896_comment'></div>初补宣懿随使都校，建隆初起家授朝散大夫、右春坊、太子通事舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153896_comment'></div>先是太祖启运立极英武睿文神德圣功至明大孝皇帝龙德在潜，人望攸属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153896_comment'></div>秦国太夫人获奉昭宪太后，太后亦降秦国之第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153896_comment'></div>公在幼稚，不乐戏弄，瞻视审谛，有如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153896_comment'></div>太后奇之，始议姻戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153896_comment'></div>洎乾德五年五月，太宗至仁应道神功圣德文武睿烈大明广孝皇帝方尹京邑，遣判官刘鳌至第，语宣懿以昭宪雅意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153896_comment'></div>翌日召公于南宫延见，诲谕久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153896_comment'></div>八月，复召公亲引对于讲武殿，太祖谓曰：「知善弓马」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153896_comment'></div>命射四十馀发，太祖嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153896_comment'></div>命太宗赐酒食，太宗且谕之云：「既精射御，当留意文学」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153896_comment'></div>公由是刻志坟索，耽味图传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153896_comment'></div>五经、十七代史，尤其该总，复得三式风角之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153896_comment'></div>后太祖频召对命射，常称其善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153896_comment'></div>五年三月，复召赴讲武殿，令带御器械党进钦等四人同射，以较其能，薄暮方罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153896_comment'></div>未几，太宗再遣左右陈信召公，谕以选尚之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153896_comment'></div>四月，复召公于内中就食厅，引对于万岁殿，赐袭衣玉带闹装鞍勒马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153896_comment'></div>七月，永庆公主出降，特授检校尚书、右卫将军、兼御史大夫、驸马都尉，赐安定里大第一区，夏屋千馀间，园馆台榭备焉，仍分御沟水以灌池沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153896_comment'></div>六年，加检校尚书左仆射、吉州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153896_comment'></div>太宗即位，加检校司空，超授本州防御使，仍备环列之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153896_comment'></div>太平兴国元年，并寇未宾，寅库再驾，赐公白金三百觔以治装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153896_comment'></div>公擐五属之甲，从六尺之舆，左右不违，晨夕匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153896_comment'></div>太宗既平大卤，直趋卢龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153896_comment'></div>乘百胜之气，遂乘亡之敌，将幸山北，尽埽区落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153896_comment'></div>公与驸马都尉王承衎从容献谏，太宗纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153896_comment'></div>三年郊祀，加检校司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153896_comment'></div>四年加检校太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153896_comment'></div>六年特诏常奉外月加给钱十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153896_comment'></div>七年授镇州观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153896_comment'></div>雍熙三年以獯鬻犯边，王师薄伐，朝廷旰食，冀方绎骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153896_comment'></div>太宗分命懿亲，藩屏近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153896_comment'></div>乃以王承衎镇大名，驸马都尉石守信守河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153896_comment'></div>而澶渊要区，喉咽之地，慎择能臣，无易公者，遂命公往抚之，赐白金五千两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153896_comment'></div>是年冬，公以河水湍悍，旧堤回曲，备御告劳，科率为患，乃径凿新渠二十里，以直水势，繇是十馀年间无衍溢之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153896_comment'></div>端拱元年，朝廷扢青坛，修黛耜，将籍千亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153896_comment'></div>而郡界河水清彻见底，味如甘醴，乃盛以银缶，因公主上之，中外称贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153896_comment'></div>礼毕，超授彰德军节度使，寻诏兼本州马步军都总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153896_comment'></div>淳化元年正月，驿召归阙，公主改封齐国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153896_comment'></div>九月，澶州河大决，坏城壁，断浮梁，垫居民，阻边奏，物价踊贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153896_comment'></div>太宗召公于崇政殿，谕以方略，令驰传而往，面赐白金万两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153896_comment'></div>今上时为寿王，赐宴于含芳园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153896_comment'></div>公下车之日，抚疲瘵，赈乏绝，境内以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153896_comment'></div>先是朝廷命内殿崇班阎承翰修复河桥，比公视事久之，功犹未集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153896_comment'></div>太宗令健行亲事官日赍诏书催督，公与谋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153896_comment'></div>而承翰执谊，以为方冬聚凌如山，水势涌急，难为施力，遽入奏，乞俟来春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153896_comment'></div>公既饯承翰回，鸠集诸工，自乘小舸，截巨浪，排层冰，绋纚造舟，是日亟就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153896_comment'></div>乃遣健步上状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153896_comment'></div>承翰方入对陈难成之势，而公奏继至，太祖大悦，顾谓入内内侍省都知李神福曰：「朕选魏某，果能集事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153896_comment'></div>翌日公主入贺，太宗复嘉叹，有晋武孟津之赏，密赐珠玉金宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153896_comment'></div>时都大提点河堤崇仪使刘永恭大庀役徒，修筑堤塞，盛寒皲瘃，人皆苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153896_comment'></div>公列上其事，乞至春初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153896_comment'></div>太宗遣健步赍诏，自京一日而至，亟命罢役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153896_comment'></div>五年春将修长堤，当役夫二万，公自保程其工，省去大半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153896_comment'></div>太宗令高班内品李信宣旨，命公图上减工在所，寻降诏依之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153896_comment'></div>时境内田隰，水退皆填淤加肥，而民漂陷之馀，耕无首种，相聚愁叹，坐待流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153896_comment'></div>公奏贷麦数万斛，是夏大稔，民乐输还官，襁属不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153896_comment'></div>由是人皆处业，贫者更富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153896_comment'></div>又以州狱久系，逋欠官物，又保任之民资产已竭，追偿无出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153896_comment'></div>公将上言，并诏蠲免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153896_comment'></div>今上即位，加定国军节度使，公主封许国长公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153896_comment'></div>咸平二年八月讲武于东郊，诏充在京新旧城内都巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153896_comment'></div>十月郊禋，充旧城内巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153896_comment'></div>十一月，以控弦入寇，边城晏开，革辂将行，羽书狎至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153896_comment'></div>命公充贝冀路行营都总管，初无辨严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153896_comment'></div>时方镇各控重兵以自卫，公至天雄军，始得步骑二千以随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153896_comment'></div>劲敌之垒，烟火相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153896_comment'></div>公左实右伪，虚振军声，倍道兼行，直抵边郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153896_comment'></div>敌亦惮公威名，辟易而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153896_comment'></div>寻命公男昭亮传诏，召赴行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153896_comment'></div>景德元年，上亲握武节，北守澶渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153896_comment'></div>公扈从星陈，以及凯入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153896_comment'></div>二年郊祀，加武成军节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153896_comment'></div>复以西衮奥区，旧俗豪悍，乃命公知曹州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153896_comment'></div>先是广济渠两岸积水，居田千顷，民用匮乏，莫输其租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153896_comment'></div>公乃度其地宜，置水门导之入河，人获其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153896_comment'></div>州下先多为盗，逆旅之舍，皆日暮扃户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153896_comment'></div>赁宿者巾屦难保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153896_comment'></div>至公之治也，民不敢欺，无夜吠之警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153896_comment'></div>上朝陵巩洛，诏从车舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153896_comment'></div>四年，曹南耆寿，列奏借留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153896_comment'></div>朝议方以三城右地，股肱剧郡，经渎所控，屯兵甚多，遂辍公镇河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153896_comment'></div>民吏望风畏惮，刑罚罕用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153896_comment'></div>大中祥符元年，密命开先，珍图荐降，上让德云岱，归功祖祢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153896_comment'></div>公屡陪近辅，夙侍严祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1153896_comment'></div>礼毕，加检校太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1153896_comment'></div>二年，敌使至阙，宴豆屡颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1153896_comment'></div>上知公善弧矢，命公伴射，赐予加等，所以旌绝艺而威远人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1153896_comment'></div>三年，禋祭脽壤，合答后祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1153896_comment'></div>西巡之路颇遥，北门之寄尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1153896_comment'></div>乃命公知澶州，兼驻泊马步军都总管，提举澶、濮、齐、郓等州、德清军寇盗公事，赐银挝、大剑各十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1153896_comment'></div>上幸瑞圣园射弓，命内侍宣旨：「卿每苦臂痛，今日之宴不可辞也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1153896_comment'></div>公奔驰赴召，射中银缶，上亲解之，赐闹装鞍勒马，非常典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1153896_comment'></div>四年礼毕，就加忠武军节度，复召归阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1153896_comment'></div>尔后真舆昭格，钜典交修，宠命便蕃，礼数尊异，以至开公府，正台极，岁给公用缗钱加至七百万，任兼文武，宠冠勋戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1153896_comment'></div>窦固之久居大位，每被访于边事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1153896_comment'></div>杜预之既立战功，唯耽思于文籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1153896_comment'></div>洎出临魏郡也，豪右屏迹，囹圄屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1153896_comment'></div>雅歌投壸，有儒者之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1153896_comment'></div>轻裘缓带，得名将之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1153896_comment'></div>洎染疾归第，恩礼勤渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1153896_comment'></div>殚太医之妙伎，极内府之良药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1153896_comment'></div>命也不淑，奄归窀穸，享年六十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1153896_comment'></div>诏废朝三日，赠中书令，命内侍省部知蛮州刺史窦神宝营葬事，太常博士、秘阁校理李垂摄大鸿胪监护，太常考行定谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1153896_comment'></div>发引之日，有司具一品卤簿鼓吹，太常博士、秘阁校理慎镛遣奠于顺天门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1153896_comment'></div>以十一月丁酉，葬于河南府洛阳县贤相乡勋德里，从先茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1153896_comment'></div>公一历东朝，一践环卫，八临藩服，五换旌旄，累阶至开府仪同三司，策勋上柱国，进爵为公，食邑至一万三千九百户，真食四千七百户，加凌烟之号，为推忠保节同德守正翊戴功臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1153896_comment'></div>禄位宠荣，并极人爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1153896_comment'></div>若乃自刺史陟防秋，由廉车正节钺，皆靡限官序，度越等夷，斯又国家急贤之恩于是乎在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1153896_comment'></div>恭惟许国长公主，太祖皇帝之第三女也，淑质纯茂，柔仪肃祗，处约惟勤，在贵能降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1153896_comment'></div>唐襄城之礼度，为诸亲之楷则；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1153896_comment'></div>汉平阳之慈爱，享累世之崇重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1153896_comment'></div>先公十九年而薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1153896_comment'></div>尝献瑞牡丹一丛，花皆千叶，色润殊绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1153896_comment'></div>太祖命以一枝著金壸中，盛以玉盘，令待诏黄居寀图之，以赐公主，至今存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1153896_comment'></div>男三人：长昭易，任内园使，顷持使节，远聘穹庐，中涂感疾，先公而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1153896_comment'></div>次昭亮，今任东上閤门使、恩州团练使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1153896_comment'></div>器宇不群，识度殊远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1153896_comment'></div>太宗以其与王承衍男世隆皆嫡外孙，特爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1153896_comment'></div>幼岁召入，并赐坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1153896_comment'></div>以昭亮好学，命吟《赏花诗》，立成，特赐缗钱御酒，命共游于后苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1153896_comment'></div>初未名，太宗一日御笔书二名赐之，曰从训、昭亮，令择名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1153896_comment'></div>起家授如京使，自是每令昭亮押赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1153896_comment'></div>公加恩纶告，两聚贵族，继赐白金万两以充六礼之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1153896_comment'></div>洎公正位国相，出临魏郡，昭亮往赐生辰礼物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1153896_comment'></div>贺席方半，而驿置俄至，特降纶綍，授昭亮恩州团练使，仍兼上閤之职，闻者荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1153896_comment'></div>然而昭亮生于贵戚，雅好儒术，妙达时务，详练旧章，受诏同定阖门仪制，广溢甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1153896_comment'></div>箕裘之业，蕃昌庆大，人皆望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1153896_comment'></div>次昭侃，今任内殿承制，风度清粹，操履温重，夙禀谊方，蔚为德器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1153896_comment'></div>女二人：长寿县主，率礼公宫，式瞻贵里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1153896_comment'></div>副笄之日，太宗赐白金饰肩舆，重七百两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1153896_comment'></div>亦以嫡孙特恩，非常例也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1153896_comment'></div>适内殿崇班、閤门祗候张士宗，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1153896_comment'></div>次女蕙问夙闻，蕣华易落，适右班殿直、閤门祗侯王从益而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1153896_comment'></div>孙一人，东头供奉官馀庆，学禀诗书，德茂兰玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1153896_comment'></div>孙女二人：长适故左领军、卫将军致仕赵保勋男宗奭，次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1153896_comment'></div>皆从训保阿，照言图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1153896_comment'></div>盖宣懿之积德累仁，公之常善齐物，厥后繁衍，奕叶隆昌者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1153896_comment'></div>及公之薨也，朝廷追录大勋，诞推延赏，授昭亮四方馆使，团练如故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1153896_comment'></div>昭侃迁礼宾副使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1153896_comment'></div>侄殿中丞昭庆迁国子博士、左侍禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1153896_comment'></div>昭用迁西头供奉官、赞善大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1153896_comment'></div>昭文迁殿中丞、左侍禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1153896_comment'></div>昭素及孙馀庆，并授閤门祗候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1153896_comment'></div>初，遗奏之上也，昭亮以事非礼制，独不列名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1153896_comment'></div>又虑国恩均被，遂上封预辞，乞居丧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1153896_comment'></div>恩旨允之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1153896_comment'></div>斯又忠孝之训，有后之美也如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1153896_comment'></div>公资性方严，秉心纯一，至诚待物，正色在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1153896_comment'></div>其出奉民政也，决事明敏，嫉恶如雠，彊暴詟服，冤滞毕达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1153896_comment'></div>所至之地，人皆爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1153896_comment'></div>是以历事三朝，宠眷日隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1153896_comment'></div>太祖日于巩洛道中，命御龙官，以金盘盛含桃赐于马上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1153896_comment'></div>太宗尝因寒食日遣内侍岑保正赐御笔，令召王承衍等习射于家园，并赐银缶腥饩等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1153896_comment'></div>后公镇澶渊，太宗射于后苑，翌日以御射中银缶，命公主赐公，令书于家信曰：「朕昨日赏花射弓，甚思卿，故有是赐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1153896_comment'></div>其恩宠尤异也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1153896_comment'></div>然公虽幼享崇贵，深承顾待，而每鉴前代之戒，小心兢慎，过自修抑，故出入五十馀载，终始无玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1153896_comment'></div>加以忠厚之节，发于天性，一物之异，不敢家藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1153896_comment'></div>太祖幸洛，公以园第宏敞，奉表献之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1153896_comment'></div>又世有芙蓉丹砂一枚，重将一镒，以承隙日，则室中皆明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1153896_comment'></div>后令寿光县主以服饵法献于太宗，旋降御笔褒之，赐黄金器五百两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1153896_comment'></div>近岁国家新宫阙之制令，昭亮恳奏，愿纳奉入以助经费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1153896_comment'></div>上优诏不允，论者美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1153896_comment'></div>又仲兄太仆少卿某之疾也，自澶渊乞赴阙侍疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1153896_comment'></div>及其有加也，上章乞授少卿长子昭度一官，寻授太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1153896_comment'></div>其弟悌皆此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1153896_comment'></div>每好夜坐，召儿侄辈谕以君子立身之道，雅合经典之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1153896_comment'></div>自感疾至薨，气貌不衰，精识自若，人皆以为修德之报焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1153896_comment'></div>佳城既卜，远日有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1153896_comment'></div>诸子以某备列西台，久尘吏职，稔闻世德，尝奉绪言，见索斐辞，以识徽烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1153896_comment'></div>让不获已，谨为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1153896_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_213_1153896'>炎正启运，帝赉忠贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1153896_comment'></div>九功并建，百度勤宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1153896_comment'></div>下宁海域，仰清垂象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1153896_comment'></div>教化之重，倚之国相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1153896_comment'></div>内抚方岳，外清边尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1153896_comment'></div>军旅之要，付之将臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1153896_comment'></div>允显魏公，位兼文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1153896_comment'></div>槐鼎登庸，节旄分土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1153896_comment'></div>左右王室，事上以忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1153896_comment'></div>股肱右地，待下以公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1153896_comment'></div>睿圣之心，念功惟旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1153896_comment'></div>白水攀龙，湛恩克懋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1153896_comment'></div>惇叙之典，立爱惟亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1153896_comment'></div>秦台降凤，宠眷斯勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1153896_comment'></div>佐国承家，谓之世德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1153896_comment'></div>阀阅之勋，载于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1153896_comment'></div>安人去患，谓之民政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1153896_comment'></div>藩屏之治，播于谣咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1153896_comment'></div>密谋潜虑，莫际其涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1153896_comment'></div>献赞帷幄，惟圣用嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1153896_comment'></div>高风远度，莫窥其奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1153896_comment'></div>仪表绅冕，惟贤是效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1153896_comment'></div>哀哉良相，百福宜全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1153896_comment'></div>呜呼彼苍，何夺之年！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1153896_comment'></div>桃茢临丧，密章加秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1153896_comment'></div>帝极哀悼，礼赠优恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1153896_comment'></div>寒风剽兮愁云暮，卤簿陈兮班剑布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1153896_comment'></div>卷组帐兮空烟，俨灵輀兮戒路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1153896_comment'></div>哀笳咽兮楚挽悲，邙之麓兮洛之湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1153896_comment'></div>从先王兮魂不昧，掩幽穸兮夜何其。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1153896_comment'></div>有旂常兮令名不朽，有琬琰兮英威可久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1153896_comment'></div>繄似续之良贤兮，永蕃昌于厥后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_244_1153896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年11月</a>　十一月，在京为知制诰，有谢魏昭亮启。作品：谢魏阁使启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢魏閤使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153808")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153808'>伏以太尉先令公维嵩宅粹，间气凝祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153808_comment'></div>妫汭降嫔，极三朝之眷待；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153808_comment'></div>台槐袭庆，陟四近之尊崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153808_comment'></div>功在旂常，政传谣颂，仰图英烈，允属鸿儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153808_comment'></div>岂谓某官特示哀诚，见求鄙制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153808_comment'></div>虽早承知奖，备熟于音徽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153808_comment'></div>而载罄庸虚，莫周于事实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153808_comment'></div>缉粹音而仅就，镂翠琬以为惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153808_comment'></div>敢冀仁明，过垂恕察？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153808_comment'></div>兢灼之至，不任下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153808_comment'></div>谨斋沐撰成先令公墓志铭一首，随状呈纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1153808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年12月26日</a>　十二月二十六日，在京为知制诰，乞代母赴台证事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年12月26日</a>　十二月二十六日，在京为知制诰，与妻杨氏不睦，责授职方员外郎、知黄州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，与修之《太祖实录》书成。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='67e12655dc6a4c8c8131fddbe2fe296e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("67e12655dc6a4c8c8131fddbe2fe296e");'><span id='67e12655dc6a4c8c8131fddbe2fe296e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1033')">1025-1033年</a>，41-49岁</div><div id='67e12655dc6a4c8c8131fddbe2fe296e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年1月</a>　正月，丁母忧，回籍守制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年7月23日</a>　七月二十三日，在京得张怀德、王钦若相助，起复为户部郎中、知制诰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年7月</a>　七月，在京，有表辞起复知制诰。作品：辞起复知制诰表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞起复知制诰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153586")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153586'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153586'>臣某言：伏奉制命授臣起复知制诰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153586_comment'></div>私门凶咎，馀喘仅存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153586_comment'></div>上圣矜嗟，隆恩猥及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153586_comment'></div>闻命交悸，悼心靡图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153586_comment'></div>臣某诚哀诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153586_comment'></div>伏念臣门地素寒，父兄早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153586_comment'></div>而自操觚学舍，结绶仕途，唯母与臣，更相为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153586_comment'></div>遽遘靡依之痛，何胜罔极之哀，而况宅兆未安，杯圈如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153586_comment'></div>蒙慈幼之育，凡四十一年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153586_comment'></div>报免怀之恩，止二十七月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153586_comment'></div>岂可遽亡□□，亟袭衣缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153586_comment'></div>自顾馀生，弥增钜痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153586_comment'></div>伏望圣慈念臣执丧日短，报国日长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153586_comment'></div>许事几筵，俾终祥禫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153586_comment'></div>永将躯命，仰答恩私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1153586_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年7月</a>　七月，在京，有表谢起复知制诰。作品：谢起复知制诰表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢起复知制诰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153587")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153587'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153587'>臣某言：伏奉制命，特授臣起复尚书户部郎中、知制诰，散官勋封赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153587_comment'></div>哀纪称情，未报劬劳之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153587_comment'></div>宸慈念旧，忽膺图任之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153587_comment'></div>祗□靡从，拜受增惕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153587_comment'></div>伏念臣如弦谬直，伺兔本愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153587_comment'></div>不知巧宦之方，但罄朴忠之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153587_comment'></div>先皇帝怜其若是，悯以至孤，俾入事于龙潜，实久趋于鹤禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153587_comment'></div>单平寡援，间隙易乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153587_comment'></div>由是出守一麾，连更六郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153587_comment'></div>九年电击，万里火驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153587_comment'></div>层阙连云，止期于梦到；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153587_comment'></div>残骸吊影，敢冀于生还？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153587_comment'></div>适属咎积私门，悲缠陟屺，爰扶旅榇，远泛重江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153587_comment'></div>四海无家，指都畿而归葬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153587_comment'></div>六亲聚首，顾生计之屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153587_comment'></div>毁灭未能，饥寒是迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153587_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇尊位皇帝陛下体天育物，爱下延慈，记藩邸之旧臣，轸穆清之圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153587_comment'></div>特颁赙赗，俯恤哀茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153587_comment'></div>方祗奉于几筵，且渐营于宅兆，冀终丧制，式罄孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153587_comment'></div>岂谓皇帝陛下再轸宸衷，俯矜微物，特降夺情之命，曲乖牵复之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153587_comment'></div>戴重施以何胜，还故栖而增感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153587_comment'></div>谨当书心誓节，刻骨铭肌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1153587_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年7月</a>　七月，在京为知制诰，有表谢皇太后。作品：谢皇太后表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年7月</a>　七月，在京为知制诰，有启谢某官。作品：谢起复授知制诰启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153798' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153798' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153798?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢起复授知制诰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153798")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153798_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153798'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153798'>伏奉制命，前件官陈避不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153798_comment'></div>靡依茹痛，瞻风木以陨心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153798_comment'></div>图旧延慈，俾墨衰而从政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153798_comment'></div>未能毁灭，惟窃震惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153798_comment'></div>窃念某本以诸生，尝阶近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153798_comment'></div>如弦谬直，伺兔甚愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153798_comment'></div>爰六剖于铜符，遽九迁于圭籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153798_comment'></div>采兰就养，解绶而靡遑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153798_comment'></div>陟屺衔哀，号天而罔续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153798_comment'></div>式遵治命，归葬近畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153798_comment'></div>宅兆未安，柸圈如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153798_comment'></div>岂谓误传诏版，许复故栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153798_comment'></div>三岁免怀，乞终于丧纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153798_comment'></div>两宫爱下，莫寝于徽章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153798_comment'></div>强整残躯，再司旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153798_comment'></div>此盖某官荐延有素，保宥特深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153798_comment'></div>致兹放浪之踪，荐游清切之禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153798_comment'></div>怀铅久废，但重学于画脂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153798_comment'></div>弄杼非工，敢更言于织素？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153798_comment'></div>唯期尽瘁，少谢生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153798_comment'></div>卑情不任感愧哀咽之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1153798_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年7月</a>　七月，在京为知制诰，为景灵宫判官，判集贤院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年8月22日</a>　八月二十二日，在京为知制诰，受命与孙奭等详定茶法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年9月1日</a>　九月一日，在京为知制诰，受命为契丹生辰使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年9月6日</a>　九月六日，在京为知制诰，表辞契丹生辰使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年9月</a>　九月，在京为知制诰，上某官启，请辞契丹生辰使。作品：免奉使启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1153796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免奉使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153796")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153796'>比膺使指，往奉欢盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153796_comment'></div>选授至艰，道涂差近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153796_comment'></div>况多侑币，实济空拳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153796_comment'></div>然念顷岁先人没于行阵，春初母氏始弃孤遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153796_comment'></div>义不戴天，难下单于之拜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153796_comment'></div>哀深陟屺，忍闻禁佅之音？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153796_comment'></div>车府露章，槐庭泣血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153796_comment'></div>王姬筑馆，接仇人之礼既嫌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153796_comment'></div>鲁子回车，胜母之游遂辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153796_comment'></div>荷两宫之大庇，载三事之昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153796_comment'></div>退安四壁之贫，如获万金之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153796_comment'></div>某官力持名教，数奖孤寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153796_comment'></div>属商利于摘山，阙言心于奏记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153796_comment'></div>何图驿置，先坠书筠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153796_comment'></div>俯哀蹈义之心，不辱资忠之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153796_comment'></div>永唯佩服，何但铭藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153796_comment'></div>卑情不任感咽依归之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1153796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年9月</a>　九月，在京为知制诰，上疏乞许民请佃荒田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年12月6日</a>　十二月六日，在京为知制诰，作鲁宗道加给事中制。作品：右谏议大夫参知政事鲁宗道可给事中余如故制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1153387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右谏议大夫参知政事鲁宗道可给事中馀如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年12月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153387")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153387'>敕：朕绍隆景业，大庇中区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153387_comment'></div>实赖股肱之臣，燮和天地之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153387_comment'></div>务在尊宠，式表眷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153387_comment'></div>具官某神禀岳灵，气载弦直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153387_comment'></div>文章雅正，道艺深明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153387_comment'></div>方重敢言，忠厚无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153387_comment'></div>简自先圣，辅予冲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153387_comment'></div>不吐刚而茹柔，常疾非而甄善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153387_comment'></div>倡率群后，翊赞正司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153387_comment'></div>洽兹重熙，莫匪嘉绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153387_comment'></div>宜升劳于琐闼，示嘉宠于黄扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153387_comment'></div>更赖尽规，奉若时命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153387_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1153387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年12月6日</a>　十二月六日，在京为知制诰，作晏殊加刑部侍郎制。作品：枢密副使礼部侍郎晏殊可刑部侍郎余如故制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1153412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密副使礼部侍郎晏殊可刑部侍郎馀如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年12月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153412")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153412'>敕：内枢之重，密命是资，允赖忠贤，参综兵要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153412_comment'></div>眷惟勋旧，宜峻等威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153412_comment'></div>具官某道艺该明，资性方格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153412_comment'></div>自怀名教之乐，淡于荣进之涂，简自先朝，列于储寀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153412_comment'></div>辅朕初载，克畅于大猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153412_comment'></div>登汝近司，愈昭于懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153412_comment'></div>宜进天台之秩，用增机轴之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153412_comment'></div>更伫吁谟，启迪予志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153412_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1153412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年11月30日</a>　十一月三十日，在京为知制诰，作王钦若赠太师中书令制。作品：故守司空兼门下侍郎平章事王钦若可赠太师中书令制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1153500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故守司空兼门下侍郎平章事王钦若可赠太师中书令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年11月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153500")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153500'>敕：国有元老，遂阶成勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153500_comment'></div>天乎难谌，曾不慭遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153500_comment'></div>特稽殊等之礼，用章亏体之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153500_comment'></div>故具官某峻极降神，生民总秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153500_comment'></div>逮事先帝，久服大僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153500_comment'></div>勒封岱宗，偃仆师节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153500_comment'></div>辅致鸿业，格于皇穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153500_comment'></div>肆予冲人，灵承景命，实赖尽规之力，绍隆累盛之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153500_comment'></div>及兹云亡，深用哀悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153500_comment'></div>尚父维师之重，周官内史之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153500_comment'></div>并刻密章，以付幽穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153500_comment'></div>死且不朽，永贲忠魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153500_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1153500_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　本年，以左司郎中为翰林学士，同勾当三班院，寻兼侍读学士、知审官院，又兼龙图阁学士，又兼译经润文官，有《谢宣召入院状》作品：谢宣召入院状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1153732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153732?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢宣召入院状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153732")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153732'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153732'>右，臣今月某日，翰林待诏某至臣所居，奉宣圣旨，召臣入院充学士者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153732_comment'></div>使轩倏降，恭被于褒言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153732_comment'></div>宸泽旁流，擢升于内禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153732_comment'></div>循涯失措，荷宠若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153732_comment'></div>伏念臣本乏异能，仰逢昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153732_comment'></div>先皇帝初临轩陛，首赐科名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153732_comment'></div>遂结绶于仕途，俄滥巾于显次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153732_comment'></div>本西垣更直，叨预于司言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153732_comment'></div>内阁参荣，弥惭于备问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153732_comment'></div>自尔践更中外，迁贸星霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153732_comment'></div>出则分铜竹之符，乏龚黄优异之绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153732_comment'></div>入则游龙凤之馆，非严乐侍从之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153732_comment'></div>去岁以式罢藩条，归朝法坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153732_comment'></div>改画省贰卿之列，附神皋内史之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153732_comment'></div>辇毂密清，盖仰遵于圣训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153732_comment'></div>条纲明具，实动禀于朝经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153732_comment'></div>仅免旷官，敢期进秩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153732_comment'></div>遽推恩于中旨，俾厕职于内庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153732_comment'></div>矧玉府之近扃，拟金鳌之真境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153732_comment'></div>论思为重，或接于睿谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153732_comment'></div>演润攸施，式严于密命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153732_comment'></div>岂期孱昧，可称甄升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153732_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下上智烛幽，纯仁求旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153732_comment'></div>以臣一门遭遇，荷异宠于累朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153732_comment'></div>念臣孤迹践扬，历清涂于二纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153732_comment'></div>特垂纶渥，擢寘禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153732_comment'></div>谨当仰副文明，虔脩职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153732_comment'></div>虽已临于暮齿，亦勉励于琐才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153732_comment'></div>奉四境之文，谨裁于书诏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153732_comment'></div>循三辅之政，用肃于都畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153732_comment'></div>报国是图，捐躯斯在。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1153732_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　春，在京为翰林学士，为王钦若撰行状。作品：赠太师中书令冀国王公行状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1153894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠太师中书令冀国王公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153894")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153894'>公之先，周王子晋之后，世家太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153894_comment'></div>唐末，高祖讳遐，随曾祖冀公倅江西廉幕，始占籍新喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153894_comment'></div>祖郑公，生而警悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153894_comment'></div>三岁，冀公教诵书，日数百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153894_comment'></div>七岁，遂熟五经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153894_comment'></div>伪吴顺义初，赐童子及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153894_comment'></div>弱冠，伪唐调伪授本县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153894_comment'></div>屡宰剧邑，阴布德惠，专以宽刑利物为意，诸郡累表为戎佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153894_comment'></div>仕至常州都团练判官、检校水部郎中、通判军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153894_comment'></div>归朝，终于濠州团练判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153894_comment'></div>父晋公，幼有志节，刻诵坟典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153894_comment'></div>江南明经登科选限，未选，复举五经，与故龙图阁学士、刑部侍郎杜公镐同榜擢第，特授本县尉，治有风迹，秩满而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153894_comment'></div>初，晋公侍郑公任鄂州通判日，秦国夫人有娠，就蓐之旦，江水暴溢，将坏廨舍，亟迁于黄鹤楼，既夕生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153894_comment'></div>或言汉阳居人遥望楼际，若有气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153894_comment'></div>公幼而秀异，资性机敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153894_comment'></div>六岁丁秦国夫人之丧，十二钟晋公之戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153894_comment'></div>哀瘠以礼，有如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153894_comment'></div>初，秦国夫人疾，启郑公曰：「此儿生时颇有异，将大王氏门户，愿爱之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153894_comment'></div>郑公视如子，保育于鲁国夫人，教于家庭，不就外傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153894_comment'></div>涉猎书传，词笔早成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153894_comment'></div>郑公之在冀幕也，公甫十八，太宗皇帝吊伐大卤，撰《平晋赋论》献于行在而还，郑公益奇之，待以宾礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153894_comment'></div>郑公移濠梁，公应进士举，将拔覃怀解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153894_comment'></div>郑公三止之曰：「吾年七十有三，恐不逮汝之返也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153894_comment'></div>公既行踰时，郑公忽一夕沐浴易衣，会家人置酒，夜分，疏记后事，且曰：「吾历官五十馀载，慎刑罚，活人多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153894_comment'></div>后有兴者，其在吾孙乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153894_comment'></div>遽舍笔就枕而薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153894_comment'></div>府中闻乐声泠然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153894_comment'></div>公淳化三年第十一人擢第，释褐试秘书省校书郎、亳州防御推官，励精吏职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153894_comment'></div>属朝廷遣著作佐郎、直史馆曾会、中使李知信察近郡风俗，吏民状公政迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153894_comment'></div>会等上之，有诏褒谕，就迁防御判官，加文散十阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153894_comment'></div>尚书屯田员外郎舒公荐公艺文可称，温裕有素，特改秘书郎，司市征于淝上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153894_comment'></div>真宗即位，就迁太常丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153894_comment'></div>时大统初集，急于用人，诏近臣举转运使副、三司判官，给事中乔公维岳首以公应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153894_comment'></div>召赴阙，主判三司凭由、理欠司，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153894_comment'></div>公抗疏请尽蠲宿逋，用广宽惠，辞甚详切，上嘉纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153894_comment'></div>未几，命宰府召试《孝为德本颂》，授右正言、知制诰，历判大理寺、审刑院，赐服金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153894_comment'></div>三年，权知贡举，召入翰林为学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153894_comment'></div>时蜀寇始剪，反仄未安，朝廷切于绥集，以公充西川安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153894_comment'></div>宽宥枝党，蠲去逋租，驿奏便宜，大惬上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153894_comment'></div>趣遣使召还，授左谏议大夫、参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153894_comment'></div>明年郊祀，加给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153894_comment'></div>景德中，契丹寇北鄙，驾将幸澶渊，特加工部侍郎、判天雄军，兼兵马都总管，并参豫如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153894_comment'></div>敌骑引退，王师凯旋，公以台席不协，恳退时柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153894_comment'></div>迁刑部侍郎，上特置资政殿学士员以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153894_comment'></div>有司定议，班在翰林学士之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153894_comment'></div>寻充南郊卤簿使，礼讫，撰《卤簿记》上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153894_comment'></div>改兵部侍郎，充资政殿大学士，位在翰林承旨之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153894_comment'></div>寻知承进银台司兼门下封駮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153894_comment'></div>三年，迁尚书左丞，知枢密院事，修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153894_comment'></div>明年，瑞命集于东阙，改元大中祥符，泰山父老请纪云岱，公首建大议，将明上志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153894_comment'></div>遂以公充封禅制置礼仪使，兼判兖州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153894_comment'></div>礼毕，加礼部尚书，受诏撰《社首坛颂》，加户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153894_comment'></div>从祀脽丘，加吏部尚书，并掌机密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153894_comment'></div>明年，加检校太傅，充枢密使、同中书门下平章事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153894_comment'></div>有诏，仍带天官之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153894_comment'></div>九皇降格，加检校太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153894_comment'></div>七年，罢枢要，以吏部尚书奉朝请，再典银台之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153894_comment'></div>未几，复拜枢密使如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153894_comment'></div>九年，典校道书毕，加检校太师，寻兼群牧制置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153894_comment'></div>明年改元天禧，上《玉皇宝册》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153894_comment'></div>礼毕，加右仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153894_comment'></div>寻兼判礼仪院，充会灵观使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153894_comment'></div>亟迁左仆射，兼中书侍郎、平章事，监修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153894_comment'></div>明年，充景灵宫使，都总管、判祥源观事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153894_comment'></div>三年，授太子太保、判杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153894_comment'></div>岁馀召还，复为资政殿大学士，加司空，寻制授山南道节度使，检校太师、中书门下平章事、判河南府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153894_comment'></div>舆疾还第，除司农卿，分司南都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153894_comment'></div>今上即位，改秘书监，分司如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153894_comment'></div>旋起授太常卿、知濠州，迁刑部尚书、知江宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153894_comment'></div>天圣元年九月诏还，制授司空，门下侍郎、平章事，充玉清昭应宫使、昭文馆大学士，监修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153894_comment'></div>《真宗实录》毕，加司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153894_comment'></div>二年郊祀，封冀国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153894_comment'></div>三年，冬十月，兼译经使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153894_comment'></div>赴上于传法院，归第感疾，请告踰月，诏使国医相望于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153894_comment'></div>十一月丙午，圣驾临问，赐白金五千两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153894_comment'></div>戊申，薨于东京永定坊第之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153894_comment'></div>遗命归葬濠梁，从祖茔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153894_comment'></div>翌日，皇太后车驾临哭出涕，制赠太师、中书令，辍朝三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153894_comment'></div>遣起居郎、直史馆、修起居注李仲容摄鸿胪卿护丧，内侍省都知、雅州防御使韩守英副之，官给经费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153894_comment'></div>十二月乙卯，上内殿成服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153894_comment'></div>哀荣之礼，近世无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153894_comment'></div>公五子，并先公而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153894_comment'></div>次子从益，仕至赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153894_comment'></div>第三子庆之，终于卫尉寺丞，追赐进士及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153894_comment'></div>女二人：长早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153894_comment'></div>次适大理评事张瑰，故参知政事洎之嫡孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153894_comment'></div>孙女一人，适太子中舍陈执礼，故尚书左丞恕之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153894_comment'></div>外孙女一人，男一人，并幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153894_comment'></div>遗奏之上，嗣男将作监丞寅亮，诏授大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153894_comment'></div>诸父，比部员外郎、判尚书刑部司农寺仲微，素负吏干，累更事任，特授司勋员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153894_comment'></div>馀戚属授官者九，亲信录用者十五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153894_comment'></div>夫人李氏，世本名宗，允怀淑德，累封崇国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153894_comment'></div>公尝言：往岁曾行圃田，宿村舍，夜起视天中，有赤文成紫微二大字，光耀夺目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153894_comment'></div>使蜀还褒城，路中遇异人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153894_comment'></div>视刺字，乃唐相裴度晋公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153894_comment'></div>告公以默定之语，而隐公之贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153894_comment'></div>遂留心羽化之事，凝神云汉之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153894_comment'></div>多用道家科仪，建坛场以礼神，朱篆「紫微」二字陈于醮所，以馀俸脩晋公祠于圃田，自撰文书石以纪其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153894_comment'></div>永定在御，真荫方隆，谒欸神灵，对越天地，尊尚道德，布宣符瑞，创图访对，多自于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153894_comment'></div>注意沃心，无与为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153894_comment'></div>若乃颂祗脽壤，奠璧濑乡，扢恭谢之坛，增耀魄之号，公皆为礼仪使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153894_comment'></div>法驾之展盛容也，奉宝文以先道，公继为天书礼仪副使，同天书仪卫使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153894_comment'></div>路寝之尊景命也，披帝箓以肇宣，公为读天书礼仪使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153894_comment'></div>良金之范真仪也，公为迎奉圣像礼仪使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153894_comment'></div>温玉之勒乾文也，公为天书同刻玉使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153894_comment'></div>前后所赐手诏玺书无虑二百函，奉和御制及御和赐所进歌诗仅三百馀首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153894_comment'></div>初罢参庶务，备问内殿，特赐宸章，辞极褒贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153894_comment'></div>西镇洛师，南抚浙水，皆有睿作宠行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153894_comment'></div>荣冠一时，事超千古，逢辰之盛，理绝名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153894_comment'></div>尤善笔劄，势甚峭劲，自成一家，老而益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153894_comment'></div>好奕棋以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153894_comment'></div>尝奉诏撰集《翊圣保德真君传》三卷，《先天纪》三十卷，《五岳广闻》一百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153894_comment'></div>与诸贤同撰集《册府元龟》一千卷，《彤管懿范》二百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153894_comment'></div>又奉诏撰僖祖、太祖、太宗谧册，今上徽号册文，汾阴朝觐坛颂，西京应天禅院、太原资圣禅院碑铭，《天书祥符赞》，《彤管仪范序》，《广孝泉崇真桥记》，《冉耕封东平公赞》，皆为大笔，或藏秘馆，或行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153894_comment'></div>公出入两府，时将二纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153894_comment'></div>敏于见事，详于敷奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153894_comment'></div>智术过人，慎勤无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153894_comment'></div>朝廷大议，帷幄潜虑，或造膝以言，或密封先达，诡词焚藁，世莫得闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153894_comment'></div>其茂功懿绩，藏在盟府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153894_comment'></div>景行嘉猷，播诸物听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153894_comment'></div>谨次官阀，敢告良史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153894_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_121_1153894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　春，在京为翰林学士，奉诏为王钦若撰墓志铭。作品：故守司徒兼门下侍郎同中书门下平章事充玉清昭应宫使昭文馆大学士监修国史冀国公赠太师中书令谥文穆王公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1153897' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153897' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153897?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故守司徒兼门下侍郎同中书门下平章事充玉清昭应宫使昭文馆大学士监修国史冀国公赠太师中书令谥文穆王公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153897")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153897'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153897'>天圣三祀，岁次星纪，黄钟布序，丙午建辰，皇帝御雕舆，诏金跸，出景龙门，幸永定坊北第，视大丞相冀公之疾，赐白金五千两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153897_comment'></div>戊申，丞相薨于位，享年六十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153897_comment'></div>两宫震悼，皇太后车驾临哭尽哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153897_comment'></div>天子素服，三日不视朝，以太子中书令告第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153897_comment'></div>大小歛遣尚宫吊祠，法赙加等，有司谥曰文穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153897_comment'></div>命左史摄鸿胪卿副内侍太监送丧，官给经费，具本品卤簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153897_comment'></div>以明年仲春之壬申，归全于濠州钟离县广德乡西原之祖茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153897_comment'></div>有诏侍臣书其徽烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153897_comment'></div>公讳钦若，字定国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153897_comment'></div>其先缑山远系，颍阳茂绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153897_comment'></div>武冈雎陵之材，启国于晋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153897_comment'></div>永宁清源之德，胙土于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153897_comment'></div>本居太原，世为鼎族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153897_comment'></div>高祖讳遂，以巢寇之乱，避地江楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153897_comment'></div>喜玉笥之岑寂，惟厥田之沃衍，始家宜春之新喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153897_comment'></div>遂生遐，仕至江南西道盐铁巡官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153897_comment'></div>遐生郁，幼而警悟，不乐嬉戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153897_comment'></div>遍诵五经，伪吴童子擢第，释褐本县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153897_comment'></div>诸郡累表为戎佐，视秩台郎，关决郡务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153897_comment'></div>归朝，为怀、冀、濠三州判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153897_comment'></div>郁生仲华，夙有志尚，刻诵坟索，为唐明经中选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153897_comment'></div>又以五经登科，复尉本县，时议荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153897_comment'></div>公即濠州府君之孙，新喻府君之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153897_comment'></div>及公之贵，三代皆赠太师、尚书令兼中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153897_comment'></div>曾门封冀，祖庙封郑，祢室封晋，皆为国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153897_comment'></div>恭惟郑公当五代纷竞，仕伪唐之僭据，转侧江介，间关世路，而能治尚清约，志在平反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153897_comment'></div>爱哲孙以字升卿，高门闾以容驷马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153897_comment'></div>克祚厥后，何其盛欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153897_comment'></div>公聪识早成，性资强敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153897_comment'></div>六岁丧母，十二而孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153897_comment'></div>郑公爱之，保育于祖妣鲁国太夫人，教于家庭，不就外傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153897_comment'></div>道艺兼该，辞笔赡逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153897_comment'></div>弱冠初拔进士解，淳化中策高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153897_comment'></div>试吏芸局，从事谯幕，加倅职，再毗戎务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153897_comment'></div>被举，迁秘书郎，典关市于淝上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153897_comment'></div>升朝为太常丞，理通欠于计司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153897_comment'></div>以右正言历掌内外书命，授左谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153897_comment'></div>再迁工部侍郎，并参大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153897_comment'></div>以刑部侍郎充资政殿学士，改兵部，充大学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153897_comment'></div>繇尚书左丞三转至吏部尚书，皆知枢密院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153897_comment'></div>自检校太傅再加至检校太师、行尚书右仆射，并使东枢，实兼宰职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153897_comment'></div>俄以左揆兼中书侍郎，监修国史，对掌魁柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153897_comment'></div>以太子太保判馀杭，归朝，再为资政大学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153897_comment'></div>寻拜司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153897_comment'></div>未几，视秩维师，兼荣铉府，节制襄岘，居守伊洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153897_comment'></div>舆疾还第，左迁司农卿，改秘书监，并分务南都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153897_comment'></div>起授太常卿，典濠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153897_comment'></div>转刑部尚书、知江宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153897_comment'></div>召还，复序正司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153897_comment'></div>再升中书兼门下侍郎，充昭文馆大学士，实首台席，遂作司徒，乃封冀壤，勋阶爵邑名数咸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153897_comment'></div>初，永定在御，宪章大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153897_comment'></div>以駉牧之重，领于枢臣，公尝为群牧制置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153897_comment'></div>肇玉清昭应宫以事有帝，崇景灵宫以奉真祖，营会灵观以礼岳镇，并建职局，综于两府，公继为三宫观使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153897_comment'></div>惟公事三朝，相二帝，嘉猷亮节，深图远算，秘诸信使，此不获书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153897_comment'></div>若夫建隆以还，万国上计，辟名既辨，断盗未偿，领于司存，列之辞案，人生有讫，吏责无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153897_comment'></div>公抗疏切陈，援赦蠲弛，深达国体，克称上仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153897_comment'></div>注意之求，实自于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153897_comment'></div>咸平初，寇剧缘间，摇乱益部，偏师致讨，刬削厉阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153897_comment'></div>武臣尚威，伤斩过当，馀孽亡命，反仄靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153897_comment'></div>公往宣使指，悉贳枝党，处置机事，彼方遂宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153897_comment'></div>召参台衡，刻印以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153897_comment'></div>景德始，边城晏开，羽檄四驰，烽火相照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153897_comment'></div>公感愤激节，慷慨请行，并护将臣，克全魏壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153897_comment'></div>洎乎元符候日，奉高望幸，三事优游而未决，礼官希阔而难讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153897_comment'></div>公首抗大义，先置乔岳，芝英醴泉之品，矞云叶气之祥，图素写形，使驿言状，旁午亭传，觉悟黔黎，此其昭昭者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153897_comment'></div>若乃尊事神祇，专精斋祭，寅威妙本，校正真科，交集上仪，莫匪嘉虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153897_comment'></div>是以再长枢轴，三陟正司，中外迭居，左右更践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153897_comment'></div>体貌无比，论议必从，宠冠一时，年踰二纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153897_comment'></div>至若薶牲脽壤，徐銮曲里，登魄宝之号，熙报况之坛，奉贞像于琳宫，宣宝文于路寝宫，断掌礼仪，并持使印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153897_comment'></div>又若明禋蒇事，珍符先道，聿严容典，奉以金舆，公三职仪卫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153897_comment'></div>殊庭考阁，常箓是藏，内出丹书，勒于瑶简，公同司刻玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153897_comment'></div>并兼置使之重，益为希代之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153897_comment'></div>祥符之间，天下大治，制有破觚之易，法有漏鱼之宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153897_comment'></div>太和陶蒸，善气回袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153897_comment'></div>云物绚色，羽毛綷质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153897_comment'></div>百嘉茂育，万瑞毕臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153897_comment'></div>天子好文，挺睿辞以昭绍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153897_comment'></div>惟公顺美，著嘉颂以游扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153897_comment'></div>前后赐御制属和并御和赐歌诗仅三百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153897_comment'></div>若夫入干庶绩，出抚近封，铺陈密议，条对急政，所受诏答，将二百函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153897_comment'></div>又奉命纂集《翊圣保德真君传》三卷，撰进《先天纪》三十卷，《五岳广闻》一百卷，《卤簿记》三卷，与诸儒同集《册府元龟》一千卷，《彤管懿范》二百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153897_comment'></div>又封祀既毕，归尊宗庙，承诏撰僖祖、太祖、太宗谥册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153897_comment'></div>神圣纂服，初受鸿名，奉制撰今上徽号册文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153897_comment'></div>及前后被旨撰社首坛、汾阴朝觐坛颂，西京应天禅院、太原资圣院碑铭，天书祥瑞、西祀瑞赞，《彤管懿范序》、《广孝泉崇真桥记》、《冉耕封东平公赞》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153897_comment'></div>博雅多文，尽在兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153897_comment'></div>公尝言：初晋公侍郑公之任武昌也，公母秦国夫人有娠，江水坏廨舍，徙居黄鹤楼，既夕而生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153897_comment'></div>或言汉口居人遥望楼际，若有气象然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153897_comment'></div>公居景亳，行视圃田，暮宿村庐，夜分偶起，见天中有赤文成「紫微」字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153897_comment'></div>使蜀言旋，次褒成驿，有客为谒，具唐相晋国裴公之名，告公以默定之期而隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153897_comment'></div>公尝朱篆所见文字，及因鄂守增饰黄鹤楼，又以俸钱修圃田晋公祠，为文书石以纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153897_comment'></div>常练气于朝霞，期脱屣于尘世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153897_comment'></div>姚顗承白衣之报，子房慕赤松之游，参实于斯，谅不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153897_comment'></div>雅好奕棋，善于笔劄，乐醇旨之饮，喜清商之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153897_comment'></div>第有北园，叠石为陂，甘果美木，荫庇其下，退食休浣，于焉游息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153897_comment'></div>晚年亲历艰难，颇厌富贵，延问高释，留心真际，遂兼译经使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153897_comment'></div>二府柄臣送上于传法院，梵卿荐香，大官具食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153897_comment'></div>归第感疾，请告累旬，侍医盈门，诏使系道，锡万金之良药，殚九折之妙伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153897_comment'></div>天乎不吊，命将柰何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153897_comment'></div>辍相兴谣，见于斯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153897_comment'></div>夫人李氏，山河象德，图史时宪，哀深惟殡，痛极终天，送往尽哀，庇亲惟睦，累封崇、许二国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153897_comment'></div>有子五人，皆先公而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153897_comment'></div>内次子从益，仕至赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153897_comment'></div>第三子庆之，终于卫尉寺丞，追赐进士及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153897_comment'></div>女二人，长早亡，次适故参知政事张公洎之嫡孙、秘书省校书郎环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153897_comment'></div>孙女一人，适故尚书左丞陈公恕之子、大礼寺丞执礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153897_comment'></div>并懿行美材，大宗良配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153897_comment'></div>外孙男元寿、女寿姐，并幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153897_comment'></div>遗奏之上也，二宫哀轸，录旧念勋，并加常制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153897_comment'></div>嗣男将作监丞寅亮，授大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153897_comment'></div>环迁大理评事、充秘阁校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153897_comment'></div>执礼改太子中舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153897_comment'></div>又以公叔父仲微剖竹列城，累书吏课，握兰建礼，实综虞衡，兼秋曹之覆刑，主大农之平籴，特除司勋员外郎、充淮南提点刑狱、劝农使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153897_comment'></div>自馀戚属授官，亲信叙用者二十有四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153897_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153897_comment'></div>高朗令终，宠灵显赫，会元公之殡，送文恭之丧，极人臣之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153897_comment'></div>公以臣尝豫寮旧，屡刊史谍，爰有治命，请志幽础。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153897_comment'></div>仰奉宸旨，不获固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153897_comment'></div>谨作铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_117_1153897'>兵政宥密，机轴穹崇，惟公再践，昭事功兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153897_comment'></div>将钺在庭，相印垂组，惟公保釐，兼文武兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153897_comment'></div>洪垆造物，威柄御人，惟公三人，秉国均兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153897_comment'></div>龙章在躬，庭槐表位，惟公经邦，极名器兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153897_comment'></div>帝师尊异，内枢隆显，襚以印章，丰赠典兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153897_comment'></div>乘舆缟素，笳吹悲鸣，送以纁玉，尽哀荣兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_122_1153897_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年3月29日</a>　三月二十九日，在京为翰林学士，景灵宫牡丹双跗共干，受诏作赋。作品：景灵宫双头牡丹赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《文庄集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1153372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>景灵宫双头牡丹赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（应制并序）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年3月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153372")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153372'>国家升禅之五祀，圣祖上灵高道九天司命保生天尊大帝降禁中之延恩殿，真宗文明武定章圣元孝皇帝躬欸飙斿，祗若灵训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153372_comment'></div>璿源长发，真荫克开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153372_comment'></div>建景灵之宫以置祠宫，构天兴之殿以尊肖像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153372_comment'></div>献而不祼，唐太微之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153372_comment'></div>水以节观，周辟雍之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153372_comment'></div>回廊四注，双渠交属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153372_comment'></div>植之美木，间以幽石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153372_comment'></div>丛薄互映，萝蔓相萦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153372_comment'></div>固列仙之幽馆，实有帝之下都也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153372_comment'></div>先皇厌代，飙驾上宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153372_comment'></div>圣文睿武仁明孝德皇帝、应元崇德仁寿慈圣皇太后哀极孝思，礼尊昭事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153372_comment'></div>乃建奉真之殿于天兴之左，备严像设，对越威神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153372_comment'></div>宪曲察之规模，兼顾成之法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153372_comment'></div>其右则皇帝肃明福之馆，其后则太后启鸿祐之廷，并为斋居，恪奉时享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153372_comment'></div>普观六艺，眇觌百王，尊祖奉先，莫大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153372_comment'></div>是宜灵鉴博临，嘉生诞降，丕显盛德，觉悟蒸黎者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153372_comment'></div>天圣四年，岁次析木，甘澍充浃，太和丰融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153372_comment'></div>惟时季春，吉日丙午，羽人动色，宫吏告祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153372_comment'></div>有牡丹之芳丛，拆双跗而共干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153372_comment'></div>枢臣谨职以承献，两闱传视而嗟异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153372_comment'></div>爰命国素，临写英蕤，仍诏词臣，昭纪嘉贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153372_comment'></div>上意以为先圣奉真祖之礼至虔，真祖眷先帝之意尤显，是彰美应，发为奇芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153372_comment'></div>臣窃考旧闻，仰迪阴骘，天意若曰：太后以至慈保右嗣圣，皇帝以至孝恭顺母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153372_comment'></div>总决万几，大康兆庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153372_comment'></div>真祖降鉴，先圣在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153372_comment'></div>乐兹重熙，锡以嘉瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153372_comment'></div>二花并发者，两宫修德，同膺福祉之象也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153372_comment'></div>双枝合干者，两宫共治，永安宗社之符也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153372_comment'></div>昔棣萼承华，召公流咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153372_comment'></div>芝茎连叶，汉帝登歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153372_comment'></div>窃比兹芳，岂容并日！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153372_comment'></div>仰应宸旨，谨为赋曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1153372'>维五行之嘉秀，钟百卉以流形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153372_comment'></div>伊牡丹之淑艳，实造化之鸿英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153372_comment'></div>杂五色以交丽，间千叶以敷荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153372_comment'></div>结紫心而函实，散黄蕊以传馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153372_comment'></div>干扶疏而四擢，枝绰约以相承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153372_comment'></div>久潜芳于药录，肆阙载于幽经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153372_comment'></div>首春华而擅美，冠花品以腾名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153372_comment'></div>何分丛于帝圃，遂得地于殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153372_comment'></div>荫琪珠之璀璨，藉瑶草之葱青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153372_comment'></div>润五云之滋液，对六羽之威灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153372_comment'></div>吐双葩而并发，效神贶以潜呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153372_comment'></div>红纷敷而接萼，翠杳袅以联茎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153372_comment'></div>较襛纤而不异，等高下以无倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153372_comment'></div>若霞裳之对举，类凤羽之偕升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153372_comment'></div>表两宫之睿圣，共一德以隆兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153372_comment'></div>实诒谋之燕翼，固道荫之章明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153372_comment'></div>愿书芳于信史，永传美于千龄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1153372_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年4月18日</a>　四月十八日，在京为翰林学士，上言请禁江西、闽越之民采大龟，又请于金山等地募水工拯救危溺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年5月2日</a>　五月二日，在京为翰林学士，以舍人院无知制诰，受诏草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年5月15日</a>　五月十五日，在京为翰林学士，受诏撰《赐杭州灵隐山景德灵隐寺常住田记》<div id='poem_1153864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153864' class='poemTitle
