showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐杭州灵隐山景德灵隐寺常住田记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年5月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153864")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153864'>会稽之西部，吴郡之东境，山之美者，武林在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153864_comment'></div>晋咸和初，常有梵僧叹其峻极，以为鹫峰别岭飞至兹地，由是依山起刹，名曰灵隐，盖言灵山之隐于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153864_comment'></div>奇迹既彰，历世增葺，缭垣危磴，丛楹钩槛，楼观之华，势胜之美，首于馀杭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153864_comment'></div>善巧启导之师，若灯炬以相续；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153864_comment'></div>精勤愤悱之士，譬云雾而毕臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153864_comment'></div>世有人焉，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153864_comment'></div>国家同文区夏，洎声葱雪，五天飞锡，四海浮杯，访道而来，解装相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153864_comment'></div>天圣之间，有众七百，每结趺聚饭，应器如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153864_comment'></div>俱罗之施难充，维摩之化靡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153864_comment'></div>爰有上首，始议垦田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153864_comment'></div>乃献像于东阙，请播种于南亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153864_comment'></div>我尊号皇太后恩深外护，心等大慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153864_comment'></div>授诸佛之记言，布群生之胜利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153864_comment'></div>威光所照，物成金色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153864_comment'></div>慧力之感，地见宝严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153864_comment'></div>若夫平决万几，将明百志，动遵法度，慎守典彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153864_comment'></div>以为道释名田，禁于创置；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153864_comment'></div>国之旧制，岂敢废焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153864_comment'></div>然吾保育嗣皇，绍隆景业，素依佛宝，孚祐帝躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153864_comment'></div>冀其万寿无疆，百祥申锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153864_comment'></div>在诸服玩，予何爱焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153864_comment'></div>乃赐直百万，市田二十五亩以施之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153864_comment'></div>岁输旧赋，天下之为公也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153864_comment'></div>永充净供，福田之无极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153864_comment'></div>彼给孤施园，非续命之要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153864_comment'></div>妙意设食，无宿饱之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153864_comment'></div>若此因缘，则为殊胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153864_comment'></div>乘天时以稼穫，绝水火之虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153864_comment'></div>治防庸以蓄泄，靡旱潦之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153864_comment'></div>地种尽墨而可穷，此功德无穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153864_comment'></div>恒沙皆宝而可尽，此布施无尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153864_comment'></div>诸菩萨僧观是田者，应合释迦如来以信心为种，以精进耘锄，因田以悟法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153864_comment'></div>诸大比丘受是食者，应念香积如来以甘露为味，以大悲普熏，因食而證道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153864_comment'></div>然而悟无所悟者正悟也，證无所證者真證也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153864_comment'></div>无离尘垢以染于净，无求寂默以住于空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153864_comment'></div>三界不见于身心，万法本忘于封境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153864_comment'></div>举足所之，皆是道场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153864_comment'></div>适意而居，莫非宴坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153864_comment'></div>夫如是者，始可以享斯田施，消此饭香，报两宫之慈恩，续诸佛之慧命也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153864_comment'></div>臣幸预译场，叨观秘藏，遐推往记，切考兹山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153864_comment'></div>能仁出世千载而神僧建寺，七百载而圣人施田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153864_comment'></div>由是知山川龙象抑有冥数，以待圣神乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153864_comment'></div>奉命昭纪，刻彼灵区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153864_comment'></div>皇太后右序嗣君，崇修妙果，施夫疆畎，教天下之至慈也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153864_comment'></div>皇帝尊事母仪，布宣圣爱，勒于金石，教天下之至孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153864_comment'></div>率土之滨，含生之品，一切见闻，得不踊跃于兹辰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153864_comment'></div>时天圣四年岁次析木仲夏望日谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1153864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年8月23日</a>　八月二十三日，在京为翰林学士，为《铜人针灸经》作序。作品：铜人腧穴针灸图经序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（孙谱系此事于天圣五年（1027）十月二十六日，此据夏竦《铜人腧穴针灸图经序》（《铜人针灸经》卷首）改。）</span><div id='poem_1153848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>铜人腧穴针灸图经序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年8月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153848")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153848'>臣闻圣人之有天下也，论病以及国，原诊以知政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153848_comment'></div>王泽不流，则奸生于下，故辨淑慝以制治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153848_comment'></div>真气不荣，则疢动于体，故谨医砭以救民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153848_comment'></div>昔我圣祖之问岐伯也，以为善言天者，必有验于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153848_comment'></div>天之数十有二，人经络以应之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153848_comment'></div>周天之度三百六十有五，人气血以应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153848_comment'></div>上下有纪，左右有象，督任有会，腧穴有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153848_comment'></div>穷妙于血脉，参变乎阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153848_comment'></div>始命尽书其言，藏于金兰之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153848_comment'></div>洎雷公请问其道，乃坐明堂以授之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153848_comment'></div>后世之言明堂者以此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153848_comment'></div>由是关灸针刺之术备矣，神圣工巧之艺生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153848_comment'></div>若越人起死，华佗愈躄，王纂驱邪，秋夫疗鬼，非有神哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153848_comment'></div>皆此法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153848_comment'></div>去圣寖远，其学难精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153848_comment'></div>虽列在经诀，绘之图素，而粉墨易糅，豕亥多讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153848_comment'></div>丸艾而坏肝，投针而失胃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153848_comment'></div>平民受弊而莫赎，庸医承误而不思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153848_comment'></div>非夫圣人，孰救兹患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153848_comment'></div>洪惟我后，勤哀兆庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153848_comment'></div>迪帝轩之遗烈，祗文母之慈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153848_comment'></div>命百工以脩政令，敕太医以谨方技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153848_comment'></div>深惟针艾之法，旧列王官之守，人命所系，日用尤急，思革其谬，求济于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153848_comment'></div>殿中省尚药奉御王惟一素授禁方，尤工厉石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153848_comment'></div>竭心奉诏，精意参神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153848_comment'></div>定偃侧于人形，正分寸于腧募。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153848_comment'></div>增古今之救验，刊日相之破漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153848_comment'></div>总会诸说，勒成三篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153848_comment'></div>上又以古经训诂至精，学者封执多失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153848_comment'></div>传心岂如会目，著辞不若案形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153848_comment'></div>复令创铸铜人为式，内分腑脏，旁注溪谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153848_comment'></div>井荥所会，孔穴所安，窍而达中，刻题于侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153848_comment'></div>使观者烂然而有第，疑者涣然而冰释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153848_comment'></div>在昔未臻，惟帝时宪，乃命侍臣，为之序引，名曰《亲铸铜人腧穴针灸图经》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153848_comment'></div>肇颁四方，景式万代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153848_comment'></div>将使多瘠咸诏，巨刺靡差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153848_comment'></div>案说蠲痾，若对谈于涪水；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153848_comment'></div>披图洞视，如旧饮于上池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153848_comment'></div>保我黎蒸，介乎寿考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153848_comment'></div>昔夏后叙六极以辨疾，帝炎问百药以惠人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153848_comment'></div>固当让德今辰，归功圣域者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153848_comment'></div>时天圣四年，岁次析木，秋八月丙申谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1153848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1153848'><span class='label'>按：</span>《铜人针灸经》卷首，当归草堂医学丛书初编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1153848_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年9月30日</a>　九月三十日，在京为翰林学士，受命与蔡齐、程琳等重删定编敕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年12月4日</a>　十二月四日，在京为翰林学士，上《国朝译经音义》七十卷，获赐器币。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　本年，在京兼侍读学士，与宋绶始请日读《唐书》一传，仍参释义理。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年1月27日</a>　正月二十七日，在京为翰林学士，迁右谏议大夫、枢密副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在京为枢密副使，受命与吕夷简等人修《真宗国史》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年5月</a>　五月，在京为枢密副使，受命与吕夷简提举管勾删定大中祥符七年至天圣五年编敕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年11月2日</a>　十一月二日，在京为枢密副使，奉诏撰《慈孝寺铭》<div id='poem_1153891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慈孝寺铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153891")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153891'>维天圣四载冬十二月，洛苑副使、入内内侍省押班江德明被旨，治故燕国英惠长公主第为佛寺，资福于真宗文明武定章圣元孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153891_comment'></div>始圣上以皇太后浚发鸿誓，祗迪净因，图创美名，永昭慈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153891_comment'></div>三事之臣相与进曰：「陛下以聪哲广运承燕翼之谋，太后以宽仁勤俭膺顾托之重，垂帘访对，斋居听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153891_comment'></div>雨露均泽，荣悴毕沾，日月并明，忠邪洞判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153891_comment'></div>阳郊再卜，岁历五颁，六幕晏清，百嘉楙育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153891_comment'></div>此太后至慈以佑嗣圣，景贶博临；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153891_comment'></div>陛下至孝以事母仪，黎苗欢服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153891_comment'></div>在昔名寺，方册具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153891_comment'></div>或以纪年，或以盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153891_comment'></div>今愿以慈孝为名，庶称道于无穷，晖映于前代」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153891_comment'></div>有制可之，仍命近臣铭于乐石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153891_comment'></div>臣闻东汉已还，有天下者继体承基，尊祖亲祢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153891_comment'></div>黄流玉瓒，观盥之享严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153891_comment'></div>高燎清坛，外宥之容备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153891_comment'></div>属象馀烈，顾慕遗恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153891_comment'></div>奉先之典有终，欲报之哀无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153891_comment'></div>或以佛国追福，或以释像荐灵，旁行不流，厥惟旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153891_comment'></div>唐氏中微，五代短祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153891_comment'></div>寇剧摇乱，群雄纷扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153891_comment'></div>载祀踰于二百，历世几乎三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153891_comment'></div>文辉昏祲，山川圮裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153891_comment'></div>空庐生荆棘，郛郭成煨尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153891_comment'></div>大块之载欲空，下民之命垂尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153891_comment'></div>我国家天人合应，祖宗重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153891_comment'></div>并剪鲸鲵，再造畿夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153891_comment'></div>胜残去杀，解百王之弊纽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153891_comment'></div>题期立象，拥五精之王气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153891_comment'></div>宪洪范，顺乾则，置国以建永图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153891_comment'></div>刬霸轨，拓皇衢，纳民以遵大道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153891_comment'></div>功有震叠燀耀，格天光表，而太山之高未增；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153891_comment'></div>德有旁魄曼羡，蒸云润海，而梁父之基未附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153891_comment'></div>上帝储蕃祉而有待，先圣膺宝命而惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153891_comment'></div>其宅藩房，践储邸，则三鸡问寝，四时省膳，周文之孝德也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153891_comment'></div>尹正京毂，宠绥都畿，有虞之历试也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153891_comment'></div>其步天阶，御神器，则攸纵多能，宣精道艺，陶唐之文思也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153891_comment'></div>躬案六师，外攘夷狄，成汤之圣武也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153891_comment'></div>大哉，以日跻之美，承天赞之业，仁经之，义纬之，根本于道德，粉饰乎礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153891_comment'></div>信以来远，忿鸷之兵寝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153891_comment'></div>虚以受人，鲠亮之臣进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153891_comment'></div>万景以之昭晰，元化以之絪缊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153891_comment'></div>包举大宁，参侔遂始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153891_comment'></div>故能延飙驾，席萝图，萃坤珍，辑天瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153891_comment'></div>纪官立制，克称乎神物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153891_comment'></div>升中降禅，不显于上仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153891_comment'></div>鄈丘颂祗，曲里尊道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153891_comment'></div>秩无文以拜贶，篆名山而纪迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153891_comment'></div>均大赉，赐明宥，复太素，宣至和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153891_comment'></div>子黎庶之恩丰，宾万灵之礼洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153891_comment'></div>方将祓靖馆，斋大庭，而思帝所以甚欢，厌天下之为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153891_comment'></div>彻琴瑟而弗怿，倦舆马而罢游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153891_comment'></div>圣人入侍兴居，冠带不褫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153891_comment'></div>太后亲尝药石，夙夜必躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153891_comment'></div>靡爱牲牷，遍走群望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153891_comment'></div>载罄圭璧，并植三坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153891_comment'></div>屑琼蕊而无功，谇玉灵而罔效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153891_comment'></div>于是祈竺乾之秘教，舍沁水之名园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153891_comment'></div>行冀有瘳，即程庶役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153891_comment'></div>靡获梦龄之感，终稽肜日之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153891_comment'></div>弓遗髯断，荆山之鼎空成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153891_comment'></div>钟䀟酒清，钧天之游不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153891_comment'></div>宇宙惨怛，人神震动，六宫攀号，万国缟素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153891_comment'></div>皇帝起初载，临宸极，章明百度，履德包元，以仪形乎风烈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153891_comment'></div>皇太后恭遗制，保重熙，平决万枢，博照兼览，以对越乎威神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153891_comment'></div>以为能类帝者圣人，善飨亲者孝子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153891_comment'></div>乃缘先朝之意，寖讲昭事之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153891_comment'></div>以真皇之受元符，膺秘记，层宙之顾怀也，始严安圣之殿于玉清之廷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153891_comment'></div>奉谆诲，迪璿源，六羽之监观也，继作奉真之殿于灵景之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153891_comment'></div>又以洛师吉壤，艺祖降灵，有应天之院；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153891_comment'></div>雎阳奥区，王业资始，有鸿庆之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153891_comment'></div>四范睟容，并安宝宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153891_comment'></div>尽汉祖龙颜之妙，增开元玉石之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153891_comment'></div>皆衣冠是游，旒扆如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153891_comment'></div>荐樱献鲔，驰传相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153891_comment'></div>濡露履霜，因时增怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153891_comment'></div>又以为礿祀极乎礼，异幽赞之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153891_comment'></div>哀戚竭乎情，无名助之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153891_comment'></div>乃复畴近职，命有司申述绪言，继成曩志，即凤台之馀阯，建鹿苑之精庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153891_comment'></div>因旧垣而不广，虑民居也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153891_comment'></div>鸠庶工而惟简，形人力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153891_comment'></div>□□□祗植之园，设像兼顾成之庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153891_comment'></div>岩洞隐饰，疑堂邑之山林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153891_comment'></div>赞呗传闻，变平阳之歌舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153891_comment'></div>回廊四注，飞观相临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153891_comment'></div>落《斯干》之雅章，成《春秋》之遂事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153891_comment'></div>以五年冬十月诏择练僧三十以奉重修，置净人二十有五以给洒扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153891_comment'></div>设官守之局，俾德明以董之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153891_comment'></div>议尊奉之制，命太常以参之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153891_comment'></div>先置禁中，肖像文考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153891_comment'></div>是月壬申乃率迩臣，戒宗室，导自天章之阁，至于会庆之殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153891_comment'></div>紫幄奏香，空歌达旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153891_comment'></div>翌日群后晨谒，百灵备从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153891_comment'></div>申命上公，奉安于寺之崇真殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153891_comment'></div>缁黄先道，仪卫清路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153891_comment'></div>幡华旗旆，左右相见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153891_comment'></div>钟磬笙簧，前后间作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153891_comment'></div>帷帟设次，簪绂在廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153891_comment'></div>太史候辰，攸司错事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153891_comment'></div>言瞻殿榜，出于宸翰，飞毫举凤，拂素腾龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153891_comment'></div>孝德圣能，并焕兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153891_comment'></div>甲戌，上运法驾，率公卿，以奉馨荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153891_comment'></div>越翌日，太后御雕舆，总嫔侍，以献令芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153891_comment'></div>都人隘涂，轩车击毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153891_comment'></div>或鼓舞蹈德，或感泣怀恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153891_comment'></div>望帝卿之云，惨凄共色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153891_comment'></div>听鱼山之梵，赞叹相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153891_comment'></div>先帝付受之道光矣，后圣恭事之礼至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153891_comment'></div>《书》所云「克笃前烈」，《诗》所云「聿追来孝」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153891_comment'></div>史官奉诏，谨为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_107_1153891'>有宋赫赫，两宫明明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153891_comment'></div>慈昭神育，孝总天经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153891_comment'></div>思文真皇，悲哀罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153891_comment'></div>鲁馆方虚，给园斯辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153891_comment'></div>斗城北望，广路东披。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153891_comment'></div>采楹丛倚，绀瓦翚飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153891_comment'></div>宝网罗空，金绳表道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153891_comment'></div>满月光明，青莲相好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153891_comment'></div>有殿中峙，实奉先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153891_comment'></div>彫云丽幄，绮栋陵歊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153891_comment'></div>隆准如生，清辉若在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153891_comment'></div>祗荐馨香，疑闻謦欬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153891_comment'></div>供帐咸具，服御毕陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153891_comment'></div>履綦虽远，手泽犹新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153891_comment'></div>閒馆旁连，藻扃相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153891_comment'></div>庭有寓龙，山多垒玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153891_comment'></div>严卫岑寂，灵游往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153891_comment'></div>雨华纷馥，飙驭徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153891_comment'></div>日监孝思，永锡纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153891_comment'></div>时万斯年，在宥天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_126_1153891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年3月17日</a>　三月十七日，在京为枢密副使，加给事中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年8月1日</a>　八月一日，在京为枢密副使，奉诏撰《御书慈孝寺碑额记》<div id='poem_1153865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御书慈孝寺碑额记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153865")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153865'>慈孝寺成，朝廷命史官颂故实，将昭铭于金石，永垂耀于文象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153865_comment'></div>圣上穆清之暇，熏韨以观，且曰：「先帝大猷，太后圣德，备在兹矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153865_comment'></div>非天下之妙翰，孰为奇丽之观？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153865_comment'></div>非朕躬之亲笔，罔罄寅威之礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153865_comment'></div>由是上自题额，命翰林学士绶书文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153865_comment'></div>百工相趋，万区载跃，以为极帝王之能事，敦恭爱之大本，英华圣域，焜耀国经，巍巍乎亘千古而不朽者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153865_comment'></div>皇太后叹嘉睿志，浚发慈旨，申命史氏，识诸碑阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153865_comment'></div>臣闻圣人因亲严以教民，故能感天地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153865_comment'></div>本文治以化下，故能纬风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153865_comment'></div>然则召至和之应，成惟几之务，垂世烈而润皇业者，必繇斯道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153865_comment'></div>洪惟上圣，天纵多能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153865_comment'></div>厥初启朱藩，践震邸，典学时敏，博志大成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153865_comment'></div>及乎集丕统，迪诒谋，益复研精书林，垂思艺圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153865_comment'></div>探七经之奥赜，鉴百王之治乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153865_comment'></div>非仁义不图于政，非礼乐不访于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153865_comment'></div>而又师臣劝讲之馀，硕儒进读之暇，宝跗在御，昼漏移刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153865_comment'></div>秦峰之篆，颉篇之楷，倒薤之妙，拂素之工，出自生知，动超神品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153865_comment'></div>尝以为开元以降，御题碑榜，标桐柏以尊道，揭丽正以崇儒，未足以移雅俗之风，恢至要之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153865_comment'></div>故是寺之建也，飞白崇真之额，所以奉先猷，摅永慕，昭定陵之遗烈，以继文而教天下也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153865_comment'></div>玉篆慈铭之首，所以宣懿铄，阐慈训，尊长乐之美业，以爱亲而训四海也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153865_comment'></div>昔羲画八卦，以启人文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153865_comment'></div>禹锡九畴，以赞皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153865_comment'></div>参之圣功，偕为盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153865_comment'></div>若乃翔翚结宇，液金填画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153865_comment'></div>腾虬龙于螭首，润云露于翠珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153865_comment'></div>映调御之相光，阴词臣之妙墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153865_comment'></div>奎躔婉其钩曲，珠斗焕乎阑干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153865_comment'></div>固将太一下观，百灵潜卫，为亿祀君臣之法，昭两宫孝爱之德也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153865_comment'></div>臣忝贰近枢，荐拜嘉诏，仰钦累盛之懿，弥负重陈之怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153865_comment'></div>唯颂次典则，勒诸左右云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153865_comment'></div>天圣六年八月朔日谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1153865_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年2月8日</a>　二月八日，在京为枢密副使，拜参知政事，领祥源观使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年闰2月</a>　闰二月，在京为参知政事，请复制举，广置科目，以收遗才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年闰2月</a>　闰二月，在京为参知政事，请复百官转对，置理检使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年7月</a>　七月，在京为参知政事，与吕夷简、张旻请罢辅臣所领宫观使名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年8月5日</a>　八月五日，在京为参知政事，因与吕夷简不相能，加刑部侍郎，复为枢密副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年3月19日</a>　三月十九日，在京为枢密副使，有应制诗。作品：观唐明皇山水字流杯石应制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_193450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观唐明皇山水字流杯石应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年3月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193450")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_193450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193450'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193450'>开元留翠刻，昭代奉宸游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193450'>绿酒联杯汎，红泉满字流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193450'>澄清涵玉宇，潋滟转银钩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193450'>霄堮奎躔布，龟图洛画浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193450'>偃波分密坐，垂露直前旒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193450'>若许铭天德，圜青岂易俦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193450'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_193450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年6月12日</a>　六月十二日，在京为枢密副使，因《真宗国史》修成，进兵部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年8月6日</a>　八月六日，在京为枢密副使，有应制诗。作品：元真殿烧香观太宗真宗御书仁宗飞白书并瑞谷应制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_193448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元真殿烧香观太宗真宗御书仁宗飞白书并瑞谷应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年8月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193448")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_193448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193448'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193448'>兰炷薰琳殿，霓旄映绿莎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193448'>九青真荫远，三母睿慈多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193448'>阁道陪銮往，唐中奉诏过。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193448'>熙陵遗札启，祢庙宝文罗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193448'>继志颁宸翰，飞毫动偃波。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193448'>史臣书绝瑞，钩盾对嘉禾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193448'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_193448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　本年，在京为枢密副使，与王曙上大藏经《名礼忏经》十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年3月17日</a>　三月十七日，在京为枢密副使，有应制诗。作品：赏花钓鱼应制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_193485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赏花钓鱼应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年3月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193485")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_193485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193485'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193485'>上苑乘春启，奇花效祉新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193485'>连房红萼并，合干绿枝匀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193485'>剪献尊长乐，分颁宠辅臣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193485'>从游过水殿，凝跸近龙津。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193485'>黼座临雕槛，文竿引翠纶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193485'>波香投桂饵，萍暖漾金鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193485'>湛露芳尊酒，钧天广乐陈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193485'>多欢千载遇，何以报严宸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193485'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_193485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在京为枢密副使，以与修之《三朝宝训》书成，受赐器币。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年5月</a>　五月，在京为枢密副使，请注释御制《三宝赞》及皇太后发愿文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年11月15日</a>　十一月十五日，在京为枢密副使，进尚书左丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年12月7日</a>　十二月七日，在京为枢密副使，受命为太庙藉田桥道顿递使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年1月22日</a>　正月二十二日，在京为枢密副使，与吕夷简上所注御制《三宝赞》及皇太后发愿文，得与一子改官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年4月24日</a>　四月二十四日，在京为枢密副使，罢为礼部尚书、知襄州，未行，改颍州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='61de9c7b8ac24c9a937b4fdf4e4490a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("61de9c7b8ac24c9a937b4fdf4e4490a9");'><span id='61de9c7b8ac24c9a937b4fdf4e4490a9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1039')">1038-1039年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='61de9c7b8ac24c9a937b4fdf4e4490a9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年6月26日</a>　六月二十六日，在京为三司使，受诏看详司马池等所上茶法利害。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月11日</a>　十二月十一日，在京为三司使，拜奉宁军节度使、知永兴军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月17日</a>　十二月十七日，在京，受诏兼永兴军路都部署，提举乾、耀等州军马，泾原秦凤路安抚使，听便宜行事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月22日</a>　十二月二十二日，在京，乞预借月俸，以办行李，诏特借一季。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　本年，在京为三司使，奉诏撰《大安塔碑铭》<div id='poem_1153892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大安塔碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153892")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153892'>有宋封禅后十祀，建大安塔于左街护国禅院，从尼广慧大师妙善之请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153892_comment'></div>今上宝元体天法道钦明聪武圣神孝德皇帝在宥之十有七载，诏史臣书其事，从尼慈懿福慧大师道坚之请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153892_comment'></div>妙善，长沙人，姓胡，字希圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153892_comment'></div>母既孕，不茹荤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153892_comment'></div>妙善胜衣，志求事佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153892_comment'></div>马氏之乱，略为姬侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153892_comment'></div>尝被毁逢怒，忧在叵测，默诵普门名称，舍利见于额中，马氏异而礼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153892_comment'></div>国初，宣徽使兼枢密副使李处耘南定湘川，得之郡邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153892_comment'></div>尝以素誓未伸，断谷谢病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153892_comment'></div>梦异人曰：「我文殊也，汝第食，胜缘近矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153892_comment'></div>明年处耘捐馆，遂依洛阳天女寺，剃发受具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153892_comment'></div>往来两京，高行著闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153892_comment'></div>太宗皇帝以椒涂之旧，锡以懿名，被之华服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153892_comment'></div>大姓袁溥舍第起刹，赐额妙觉禅院，令妙善主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153892_comment'></div>自是肃禅仪，练律学，给瑜珈之会，演《华严》之说，五陟岱山，一汎泗水，皆中贵护送，傅舍供拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153892_comment'></div>皇帝巡狩河朔，刺血上疏，玺书褒叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153892_comment'></div>是时万年中参，恩爱异众，宸闱进见，礼数踰等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153892_comment'></div>赠中书令忠武公李继隆每以保阿，尊事尤谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153892_comment'></div>洎元符降格，法御上封，妙善即朝日之郊，卜布金之地，讽甘露法品，祈东禅灵祐，帝意嘉之，赐名护国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153892_comment'></div>天禧元年，湘东邃谷有钜石，重累数十百丈，屹若浮图，昔隐今见，诏遣使案视，建寺度僧以旌其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153892_comment'></div>妙善志往瞻礼，有大弟子道坚以师腊既高，衡阳云远，恳留不已，先事以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153892_comment'></div>翌日，妙善请告南游，真宗曰：「汝老矣，何遽远适？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153892_comment'></div>如来性海，随处现前，傥有至诚，皆可供养」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153892_comment'></div>妙善遂求建今塔，特诏许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153892_comment'></div>会江宁府长千塔成，绘图来上，促召妙善于护国，将赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153892_comment'></div>道坚在妙觉，地近先至，访对称旨，受图以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153892_comment'></div>首事创规，实始于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153892_comment'></div>由是涓日置臬，肇基宝甃，冶金砻石，作于地宫，将秘庄献明肃太后所赐驮都，逮妙善曩得佛骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153892_comment'></div>会妙善示灭，尽以塔事嘱累道坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153892_comment'></div>妙善享年七十有六，尼夏五十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153892_comment'></div>宫闱震嗟，赙赠加品，建坊立刹，赐额宝胜，以道坚兼主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153892_comment'></div>道坚尽礼苍皴，入谢扃禁，且陈妙善遗誓云：「此塔今世不成，来生愿就」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153892_comment'></div>先帝恻然，赐以潜邸珍玩三千万直，仍命内侍分董其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153892_comment'></div>明年春，法坚制金衬宝函，纳前舍利等入奉于内道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153892_comment'></div>赞呗三夕，两街威仪导自滋福殿，帝荐香以送之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153892_comment'></div>季商协吉，藏于石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153892_comment'></div>五年，继赐乘舆副物货镪万缗，以供馀费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153892_comment'></div>乾兴初，又以塔心殿栋须合抱修干，既选未获，贳于皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153892_comment'></div>上方以天下为公，且重违其请，庄太后时为皇太妃，乃以奁金五百万输于内府，市材以施之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153892_comment'></div>天圣改元，内出明德太后宝器价二百六十万，洎庄献服用千馀万付之公帑，易金铜，铸轮盖以施之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153892_comment'></div>美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153892_comment'></div>四门九级，岌嶪天中，十盘八绳，晃曜云际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153892_comment'></div>道坚又以圬墁虽毕丹采，剖劂未完，遍募檀信，获缗一万八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153892_comment'></div>洎法坚禀给馀赀三百二十万以偿其工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153892_comment'></div>上继志有严，奉先惟孝，宅心凝觉，追福太官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153892_comment'></div>由二级而上，命奉安祢庙至宣祖皇帝四室神御，并列环卫，拱侍左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153892_comment'></div>自馀缘塔功德未具者，皆省服御成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153892_comment'></div>由是贤劫之象，萨埵之容，五佐星纬，八部人天，分次峻层，罔不咸备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153892_comment'></div>七年功毕，诏赐兹额金榜，始严罽軿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153892_comment'></div>临视谈赞五尼，赉紫方袍，并赐近院官舍九十区，僦直充供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153892_comment'></div>明道二载，上给白金五十镒，俾营献殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153892_comment'></div>先有陈元虔舍僧伽像，张延泽施罗汉像，颇极精巧，精坚复建二殿夹峙于塔以奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153892_comment'></div>又营讽《法华》、《孔雀经》二殿以次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153892_comment'></div>景祐中，上赐钱千万，创二楼于塔前，右安特旨所赐龙藏作香轮以转千函，左挂庄惠所舍钟树彫格以维九乳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153892_comment'></div>其斜廊壁绘罗汉迦文像，亦庄惠之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153892_comment'></div>粤自营创，逮夫圆成，则有宗藩施三门洎无量寿像，邓国贵主施报身像，尚宫武氏施法身像，朱氏施药师像，何氏施下生像，晋国夫人张氏施工绘献殿壁，颍川郡君韩氏舍圃于西，戈水杜航舍地于东，及其季尚继献金录，寿春王文献缗钱，义学比丘端琛指教相文字，比丘惟俨著塔录，吴门应德兴为匠石，皆道坚愿力所召，共周能事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153892_comment'></div>厥初妙善尝梦塔相止于双足，谈者以为上足善继之祥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153892_comment'></div>塔成，忽一日远望如失，灵祇环绕之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153892_comment'></div>道坚，故通事舍人杜志儒之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153892_comment'></div>母，明德从父姨，再适故殿前指挥使、武成军节度杨信，封陇西郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153892_comment'></div>道坚生九岁即斋素，十有一求舍家，兴国八年剃度得戒，明年赐紫伽梨，十有六授慈懿师名，嗣掌妙觉，月给俸料，三时赐衣，岁度僧荐紫各二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153892_comment'></div>陇西夫人随子剃染，期月归寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153892_comment'></div>道坚天机警悟，资性严整，有大丈夫风槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153892_comment'></div>尝诵《法华》千卷，《华严》、《首楞》、《净名》、《圆觉》皆数百过，记忆教藏，该通大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153892_comment'></div>塔之规模，尽出智匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153892_comment'></div>总三院之务，安数百之众，以慈悲摄嗔恚，以精通摄懈怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153892_comment'></div>故能念举而物应，身动而众随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153892_comment'></div>群蜂表异，纤鳞示应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153892_comment'></div>作大因缘，终始圆就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153892_comment'></div>明道中，诏加福慧之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153892_comment'></div>尝谈经于观文殿，有旨赐尼众食料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153892_comment'></div>道坚以为出家分行，折伏骄慢，赴请之饭，犹起诸漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153892_comment'></div>彷徨移晷，切辞仰给，每院但受月廪作糜米十斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153892_comment'></div>闻者与之，谓其知分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153892_comment'></div>夫以柔弱之赋，婉劄之姿，其间具明淑之德，习师傅之训，不过佩服诗礼，蹈履谦祗，体蘋蘩之柔洁，法山河之容润而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153892_comment'></div>其能断弃爱染，脱离尘垢，以坚固为佛事，以勇猛趋实际，浚发心华，坐空蕴树者，何其伟欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153892_comment'></div>古之后族出入宫掖，凭藉声势，狃忕恩泽，外交王侯，旁出姻援，不期骄而自速，靡羡侈而极怀，载之前闻，为鉴来辙者有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153892_comment'></div>其能委远光宠，杜绝徼望，辞荣于宗属，等志于贫贱，以喜舍化俗，以高洁自持者，抑为难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153892_comment'></div>宜乎万乘待遇，六宫景慕，成支提之上缘，到无生之彼岸者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153892_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153892_comment'></div>是塔庀功二十年，规平三百尺，高二引有六丈，经用一亿，旁庑佗舍，无虑五百楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153892_comment'></div>自非景祚和平，累朝信奉，设有大愿，乌可成邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153892_comment'></div>是知诸佛慧命，其待时而兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153892_comment'></div>夫议者皆以为圣上于是塔大美者四：中出宝币，形民力也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153892_comment'></div>日就胜因，畅先谟也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153892_comment'></div>敦劝于下，使趋善也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153892_comment'></div>命书厥劳，庸展亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153892_comment'></div>所宜鬼神潜卫，海域延仰，永集纯嘏，施及怀生者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153892_comment'></div>臣早预翻经，尝更约史，仰被台札，靡敢固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153892_comment'></div>谨按塔者，梵云窣堵坡，此云灵庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153892_comment'></div>在乎诸天，则藏佛爪发衣钵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153892_comment'></div>在于西度，则记佛降生经行演说圆寂之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153892_comment'></div>一以表人胜，次以生地信，三以报重恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153892_comment'></div>四果之位，能超三界，故有初级至四级者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153892_comment'></div>如来出十二因缘，故极于十有二级焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153892_comment'></div>迦叶灭后，婆罗奈王起七宝塔为作铭记，岂非刻石之识抑有初邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153892_comment'></div>或问古今哲王之导黎庶，不专讲六艺，而参用三乘，岂其大抵同归于善乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153892_comment'></div>臣尝试论之：夫有生之源本始清净，寂则绝待于一物，感则资始于万缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153892_comment'></div>至灵无方，至虚善应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153892_comment'></div>觉者则圆通罔碍，湛寂自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153892_comment'></div>内不立于寸心，外无累于群境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153892_comment'></div>不为世界之所流转，不为幻妄之所变移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153892_comment'></div>迷者则奔驰万有，昏翳五欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153892_comment'></div>习动而不能静，入业而不能舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153892_comment'></div>失本明而不知，沉诸趣而不恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153892_comment'></div>所以能仁悯之，出现于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153892_comment'></div>法不广大，不能包种性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153892_comment'></div>喻不善巧，不能破根蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153892_comment'></div>穷理而至命，《象》、《系》之旨也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153892_comment'></div>率性而达道，《中庸》之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153892_comment'></div>好生恶杀，仁义之均也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153892_comment'></div>防非致和，礼乐之则也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153892_comment'></div>圣人以为外可以扶世训，佑生民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153892_comment'></div>内可以澡心源，还妙本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153892_comment'></div>所以崇其塔庙，尊其教戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153892_comment'></div>自东汉以来，历世多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153892_comment'></div>其间执分别之论，起归向之疑，废之而逾盛，毁之而逾信，岂非言厎乎不诬，理冥乎至当者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153892_comment'></div>昔有人云：百家之乡，一人持戒，则十人淳谨，百人和睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153892_comment'></div>夫能行一善，则去一恶而息一刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153892_comment'></div>一刑息于家，则百刑措于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153892_comment'></div>以此观之，则斯法之来，裨我之治，盖亦多矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153892_comment'></div>上具大智慧，有大威德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153892_comment'></div>神道以设教，文明以化人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153892_comment'></div>晏坐黼帷，铺观贝牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153892_comment'></div>信解出于天纵，悟入自于生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153892_comment'></div>指曹溪顿门，则言高达摩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153892_comment'></div>览竺乾半字，则义中悉昙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1153892_comment'></div>实玉毫之化身，托金轮而救物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1153892_comment'></div>未阶铺砌，孰望清光？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1153892_comment'></div>而况投笔端闱，属鞬远戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1153892_comment'></div>据案受简，摩盾操觚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1153892_comment'></div>但缘外护之仁，少叙重熙之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1153892_comment'></div>谨裁二十有四颂，以勒铭云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_132_1153892'>于铄帝宋氏，睿明继临照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1153892_comment'></div>百度恢大功，三归崇正法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1153892_comment'></div>辰居宪紫微，东郊配苍震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1153892_comment'></div>有大除馑女，肇营晏坐场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1153892_comment'></div>九级缔层楹，两朝施宝玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1153892_comment'></div>八觚回日月，百寻切云霓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1153892_comment'></div>七佛俨金容，四圣崇睟表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1153892_comment'></div>瑑刻具千觉，图绘周万灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1153892_comment'></div>钩槛荫璇题，高檐幕珠网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1153892_comment'></div>龙天乍来去，烟霞时蔽亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1153892_comment'></div>我闻上帝宫，昔在庄严殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1153892_comment'></div>八万窗牖柱，众宝极彫饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1153892_comment'></div>曷若佛灭后，随缘崇庙貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1153892_comment'></div>设利罗如芥，苏偷婆如果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1153892_comment'></div>有盘若枣叶，有像若䵃麦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1153892_comment'></div>其福已胜彼，无量千百亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1153892_comment'></div>况惟此聚相，密迩于国城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1153892_comment'></div>楼观相飞注，康庄四通达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1153892_comment'></div>宰官引铙吹，公侯联旆旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1153892_comment'></div>都人集袂帷，王姬传车水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1153892_comment'></div>流景启清旦，行月丽中宵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1153892_comment'></div>幡影铺九衢，铃风闻百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1153892_comment'></div>我愿瞻仰者，应起大乘解，悟此见闻性，充满于十方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1153892_comment'></div>我愿供养者，应发菩提心，觉此烦恼燄，本是清凉源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1153892_comment'></div>我愿扫除者，应生精进力，反此尘劳身，径度禅定业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1153892_comment'></div>我愿旋绕者，应作三昧观，转此颠倒想，顿入清凉慧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1153892_comment'></div>寂念以为地，般若以为基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1153892_comment'></div>正受为花鬘，解脱为宝箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1153892_comment'></div>藏此无价珍，非空亦非色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1153892_comment'></div>远谢修證垢，并祛照觉荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1153892_comment'></div>水澄滓乃去，火尽灰亦飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1153892_comment'></div>法缚既解除，神通自游戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1153892_comment'></div>若于权实际，犹有一微尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1153892_comment'></div>欲求见如来，尚隔须弥聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1153892_comment'></div>佛祖秘密印，华梵微妙言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1153892_comment'></div>语默及思维，不越于此义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1153892_comment'></div>后之登塔者，应知建塔因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1153892_comment'></div>盖表调御德，起发净信心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1153892_comment'></div>掩日不为多，聚沙不为少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1153892_comment'></div>但能复本觉，即成无上道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1153892_comment'></div>朝家光四叶，尊重于宝乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1153892_comment'></div>真祖创妙缘，鸿禧昌厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1153892_comment'></div>吾皇授曩记，成此殊胜果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1153892_comment'></div>寿考亿万年，永庇大千界。</div><div id='poem_sentence_175_1153892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年1月</a>　正月，在京，荐举张昪。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1ee1f60693354039a09ca1a04af0ecc0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1ee1f60693354039a09ca1a04af0ecc0");'><span id='1ee1f60693354039a09ca1a04af0ecc0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>，59岁</div><div id='1ee1f60693354039a09ca1a04af0ecc0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月8日</a>　四月八日，因台谏交章论其怯于用兵，罢枢密使，受诏赴本镇。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e6109fd29c7e430e84f38a0d1630718b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6109fd29c7e430e84f38a0d1630718b");'><span id='e6109fd29c7e430e84f38a0d1630718b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1048')">1047-1048年</a>，63-64岁</div><div id='e6109fd29c7e430e84f38a0d1630718b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年4月8日</a>　四月八日，在京为枢密使，上言察敌之策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年6月</a>　六月，在京为枢密使，上言石介说敌弗从，更为富弼往登、莱结金坑凶恶数万人欲作乱，请发棺验视，朝廷因而复诏监司体量。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年8月11日</a>　八月十一日，在京为枢密使，受诏书写宋真宗加谥册文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年9月</a>　九月，在京为枢密使，挟故怨黜张亢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年12月8日</a>　十二月八日，在京为枢密使，郊祀加恩，进爵英国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　本年，在京为枢密使，建议河北忠顺乡兵与正兵参戍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年1月</a>　正月，在京为枢密使，沮明镐攻贝州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月2日</a>　闰正月二日，在京为枢密使，请解送贝州反者王则来京覆视。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月22日</a>　闰正月二十二日，在京为枢密使，与丁度争，上言请御史同宦官即禁中勘问崇政殿亲从官颜秀等谋变事，以庇护杨怀敏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月25日</a>　闰正月二十五日，在京为枢密使，以美人张氏有扈跸功，倡言宜讲求所以尊异之礼，因张方平、陈执中反对作罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年3月16日</a>　三月十六日，在京为枢密使，为宋仁宗谋以策访大臣，面使条对，欲以困陈执中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年5月24日</a>　五月二十四日，在京，罢枢密使，出判河南府，兼西京留守，乞一殿学士职名留京师，以何郯之议，不许。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='46c70532bf764e5383bc6df2be68959a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("46c70532bf764e5383bc6df2be68959a");'><span id='46c70532bf764e5383bc6df2be68959a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，67岁</div><div id='46c70532bf764e5383bc6df2be68959a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年9月7日</a>　九月七日，卒于京师，赠太师、中书令，谥文庄。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南通
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ebd7add149ec496790daabdefb217330_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ebd7add149ec496790daabdefb217330");'><span id='ebd7add149ec496790daabdefb217330_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>，17岁</div><div id='ebd7add149ec496790daabdefb217330' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　本年，初侍其父夏承皓监通州狼山盐场，有诗。作品：狼山渡口有作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_193429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狼山渡口有作<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193429")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_193429_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_193429_0'>① 按：《渑水燕谈录》卷七：夏文庄公竦初侍其父监通州，狼山盐场渡口诗云云。时年十七。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193429'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193429'>渡口人疏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>黯翠烟，登临犹喜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>夕阳天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193429'>残云右倚江都<sup inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>古寺，电驱甘雨过闲田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193429'>季鹰死后无归客，江上鲈鱼不直钱。<div
