-----title
丹阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cd42af745b2c43389016d9cc6a6e3329_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd42af745b2c43389016d9cc6a6e3329");'><span id='cd42af745b2c43389016d9cc6a6e3329_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1007')">1005-1007年</a>，21-23岁</div><div id='cd42af745b2c43389016d9cc6a6e3329' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年11月</a>　十一月，在丹阳主簿任，上疏乞应制举。作品：上章圣皇帝乞应制举书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一六。夏谱系于景德三年（1006），此据文中所记时间改。）</span><div id='poem_1153728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上章圣皇帝乞应制举书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153728")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153728'>景德二年十一月，将仕郎、守润州丹阳县主簿臣夏竦谨斋戒昧死再拜，上书崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下：伏以国家采汉唐故事，恢复制科，网罗贤俊，镕范太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153728_comment'></div>陛下圣政日跻，广分条品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153728_comment'></div>崇二圣之丕绪，冠百王之盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153728_comment'></div>万方文明，多士勇进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153728_comment'></div>《嘉鱼》有得贤之咏，《白驹》无空谷之恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153728_comment'></div>臣生逢圣明，幼肄简谍，久困寒贱，不能自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153728_comment'></div>去年秋荐名天府，属边障多故，羽书蜂午，陛下临遣宰臣，折冲河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153728_comment'></div>先臣供传遽之职，立矢石之地，忘家殉国，失身行阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153728_comment'></div>陛下哀臣孤幼，任之州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153728_comment'></div>鞅掌之暇，服膺稽古，欣睹明诏，遽释忧虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153728_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153728_comment'></div>陛下广文武之科，而兴文武之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153728_comment'></div>夫铅椠方策，文之器也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153728_comment'></div>辞藻辩博，文之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153728_comment'></div>御器以道，则仁义忠信无所不至矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153728_comment'></div>御用以变，则刑政教化无所不达矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153728_comment'></div>步骑金革，武之器也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153728_comment'></div>敢毅勇捷，武之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153728_comment'></div>御器以道，则奇正威惠无所不逮矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153728_comment'></div>御用以变，则盈虚纡直无所不计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153728_comment'></div>盖古者爱其道，而今也爱其器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153728_comment'></div>古者观其变，而今也观其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153728_comment'></div>故文武之材比及于古者可多得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153728_comment'></div>若能临器而知道，临用而知变，精儒墨者兼之以韬略，善攻取者赞之以学术，则将相之材，去此焉往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153728_comment'></div>愿陛下详而察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153728_comment'></div>若陛下必择狂夫之言，思纳愚者之虑，垂旒下拱，渴待忠谠，则臣愿以贤良方正能直言极谏科召赴明试，则贤良之科斯为具体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153728_comment'></div>夫贤者智之苑囿，良者德之蹊径，方者慎履名教，正者斥远邪佞，直言足以陈时弊，极谏足以敷谠议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153728_comment'></div>时弊既陈，则明于体用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153728_comment'></div>谠议既敷，则造于教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153728_comment'></div>明体用者，岂昧于六建？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153728_comment'></div>达教化者，岂微于七德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153728_comment'></div>故臣之区区，尽在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153728_comment'></div>惟陛下□□所志，辨而明之，裁而择之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153728_comment'></div>若陛下以枕石漱流为达，则臣世居市井；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153728_comment'></div>若陛下以金榜丹桂为材，则臣未忝科第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153728_comment'></div>若陛下以鸠杖骀背为德，则臣始踰弱冠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153728_comment'></div>若陛下以荷戈控弦为勇，则臣生本绵弱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153728_comment'></div>若陛下令臣待诏公车，条问急政，对扬紫宸，指陈时事，犹可与汉唐诸儒方辔并驱而校其先后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153728_comment'></div>伏愿陛下念忠臣之后，宽万死之责，召诣阙下，令毕其辞，退就鼎镬，死且无恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153728_comment'></div>干忤圣德，臣无任待罪战汗惶惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153728_comment'></div>臣某稽颡顿首，死罪死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1153728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，重修丹阳县门楼，并为之作记。作品：重修润州丹阳县门楼记。<div id='poem_1153863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修润州丹阳县门楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153863")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153863'>县门楼，建鼓之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153863_comment'></div>号令之发，始乎钟鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153863_comment'></div>兴居之期，启闭之节，由是乎达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153863_comment'></div>故其墉岿如，其楼轩如，冠厅事旁屋，状人之有冠冕，若之何毁之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153863_comment'></div>今年夏初，予视厥职，悯夫斯楼积有年所，墙败于左，木隳其右，风雨所陵，埃壒所侵，官而弗省，其谁治之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153863_comment'></div>乃役工百馀指，伐木十馀本，易其数梁，替其数楹，涂其墉，赭其栏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153863_comment'></div>取其壮而不取其宏，务其完而不务其华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153863_comment'></div>后负练塘，前压驿道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153863_comment'></div>山阜表其东，津梁续其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153863_comment'></div>望之敞然，有宫府之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153863_comment'></div>登之廓然，有小天下之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153863_comment'></div>使吾民如楼之完善，政如楼之新，则百里之间可以无疮痏矣，后之为政者可不勉之哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1153863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，上书润州知州陈天丽，乞荐己应制科。作品：上知润州陈天丽书。<div id='poem_1153827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上知润州陈天丽书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153827")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153827'>伏以外诸侯之重，二千石之贵，唱首太平，必举贤隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153827_comment'></div>夫良药之厩，乘黄伏皂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153827_comment'></div>工倕之室，楩楠在御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153827_comment'></div>岂有贤太守之庭而无良士，盖知与不知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153827_comment'></div>伏念某四岁结发从师，执铅椠者十五馀载矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153827_comment'></div>去年再践场屋，荐名天府，方将交辟春闱，鼓行文阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153827_comment'></div>属边阵多事，简书蜂午，遣宰辅折冲河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153827_comment'></div>先人奉辟请之命，供传遽之职，发兵间道，陷于戎事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153827_comment'></div>帝用追念，行加等之赠，举嗣袭之典，命于柴毁之际，固让不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153827_comment'></div>外廷有补以县吏，夙心素业，堙郁无诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153827_comment'></div>今者岂谓遭遇执事总秉部政，威望隆峻，铨度人物，哀恤孤幼，故敢以片言薄技深自媒荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153827_comment'></div>所望执事近观厥言，远察其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153827_comment'></div>萧艾之畹，可择兰菊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153827_comment'></div>凫鹥之渚，亦有鸿鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153827_comment'></div>勿谓冗官，而非秀孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153827_comment'></div>《诗》云：「惟其有之，是以似之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153827_comment'></div>《书》云：「知人则哲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153827_comment'></div>《传》曰：「举尔所知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153827_comment'></div>《礼》称：「推贤而进达之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153827_comment'></div>《易》谓：「拔茅连茹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153827_comment'></div>故文子之举管库，赵孟之出淹滞，善有所在，人其舍诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153827_comment'></div>然某之所望不敢逮此，但觊执事鉴其好学，少回惠顾，使他人无庸贱之谤，公府减奴隶之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153827_comment'></div>令勾乙之暇，得和铅弄翰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153827_comment'></div>荐举之际，许解官就试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153827_comment'></div>必能昂首掉尾，自求腾踔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153827_comment'></div>上以副先人之心，下以遂为儒之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153827_comment'></div>遂得待问都堂，扬榷今古，射策紫墀，条对急政，将不在他人之后，以辱公举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153827_comment'></div>语其报效，则有先王仁义之道在，惟下执事者裁之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1153827_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，上书两浙转运使姚铉，乞荐己应制科。作品：两浙运使姚铉书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1153826' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153826' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153826?labeling=true' target='_blank'>两浙运使姚铉书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153826")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153826'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153826'>伏以国家之制，内外分职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153826_comment'></div>内则中书以发号令，枢密以掌兵政，三司以计国用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153826_comment'></div>外则输运之司使领方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153826_comment'></div>其职有六，其政有五：纠奸慝、明简稽、察利害、平筦榷、通商贾、重废置，之谓六职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153826_comment'></div>举贤、使能、报功、恤刑、爱民，之谓五政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153826_comment'></div>六职修则国必丰其财，五政举则官皆称其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153826_comment'></div>丰财则无重敛，称职则无弊事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153826_comment'></div>然则六职之要在乎纠奸慝，五政之大在乎举贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153826_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153826_comment'></div>若执事之麾下，地长千馀里，官不啻数十百员，人心如面，罔或纯一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153826_comment'></div>贪夫徇利，皆曰上官烦剧，不暇按省，故安于懈惰，嗜于赇赂，以浼执事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153826_comment'></div>果知而罪之，则为恶者沮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153826_comment'></div>廉吏砥节，皆曰上官明允，有能必举，故服于勤恪，甘于冰檗，以待执事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153826_comment'></div>执事果知而赏之，则为善者劝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153826_comment'></div>然则多纠恶不如多举贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153826_comment'></div>《传》曰：「禹称善人，不善远矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153826_comment'></div>其是之谓欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153826_comment'></div>故某之有待于执事也，非一朝一夕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153826_comment'></div>某本无他材，癖嗜儒学，虽不得经指，而颇知戒训，居贫而固其节，临事而专其守，勾乙案籍之暇，则伏读先王之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153826_comment'></div>日饭寒蔬数十本，若牲牢水陆之味，而又侑之以钟鼓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153826_comment'></div>岁服败绨数千缕，若衣文绣纨绮之裳，而又映之以珩佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153826_comment'></div>非不知富贵之可悦，贫贱之可厌也，盖富而忧不若贫而乐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153826_comment'></div>尝念事父之日，食饫饘藿，衣缯厚絮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153826_comment'></div>无何，近丁家祸，堕于徒劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153826_comment'></div>县官日给斗粟数十百钱，同爨十馀口，嗷嗷然皆有菜色，必货什器、质衣衾而后充其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153826_comment'></div>穷如是，困如是，誓不忍学穿窬之盗，蠹耗苍生而茍且衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153826_comment'></div>虽清白之吏，忠信之民以心许我，而时命艰蹇，终鲜知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153826_comment'></div>昨以道干少卿陈公，公以一言誉之，而未深省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153826_comment'></div>退而度生成之地，无出执事之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153826_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153826_comment'></div>某为童之年尝闻执事豁达正直，提干吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153826_comment'></div>暨今处麾下，复大闻执事荐拔良士，尽公无私，夙夜繄繄然，恨不能负绥执鞭以遂欣慕之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153826_comment'></div>今少卿有鄱阳之命，而执事按行常、润，某之区区如热得濯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153826_comment'></div>但恨偶萦负薪之疾，不能兴，不及稽首衡鉴之下，仰干题品之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153826_comment'></div>岂天复未开某以明公知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153826_comment'></div>愿执事哀恤穷滞，听察言行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153826_comment'></div>若矜其廉慎，擢于行伍，必能恪居官次，守死善道，不敢贪慢，以累明德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153826_comment'></div>若念其愚直，举之谏科，必能待诏公车，对扬王庭，不敢佞媚，以辱通鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153826_comment'></div>《诗》云：「惟其有之，是以似之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153826_comment'></div>《书》云：「举能其官，惟尔之能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153826_comment'></div>是则善有所在，公其舍诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153826_comment'></div>惟昊天皦日知我之不欺于执事也矣，惟执事辨而明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153826_comment'></div>若执事听之以为是，诚幸矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153826_comment'></div>若不听之，以为非，亦幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153826_comment'></div>是与非，穷与达，皆取必执事，愿执事不惜一言而裁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153826_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153826_comment'></div>日月逝矣，功名未立，文以足言，颇至狂直。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1153826_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，作《平边颂》作品：平边颂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1153884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>平边颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153884")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153884'>臣闻四裔交侵，荐食边境，为日久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153884_comment'></div>虞夏有山戎獯鬻之患，成周有昆夷猃狁之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153884_comment'></div>赵筑长城以设险，秦驱诸戎而出塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153884_comment'></div>逮汉而下，种类滋蕃，和之以亲而不庭，怀之以文而不至，要之以盟而无信，饵之以货而无厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153884_comment'></div>疆臣以是发愤，王者于焉赫怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153884_comment'></div>至有空天下以事外人，夺耒耜而授干盾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153884_comment'></div>四海将服，而中原随弊，英主所以疚心，良士所以极虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153884_comment'></div>故汉武震威而损费，光武惜费而损威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153884_comment'></div>李牧知保塞而不议其久，奉春约和亲而不议其叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153884_comment'></div>贾谊陈五饵而不议其贪，晁错论三技而不议其犷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153884_comment'></div>班固述怀御而不议其疆，侯应计屯戍而不议其守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153884_comment'></div>诚哉，严尤所谓无上策者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153884_comment'></div>魏晋已降，羌戎猾乱，或结以姻娅，抗之锋锷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153884_comment'></div>谋者鲜而斗者众，偏议多而胜算寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153884_comment'></div>其间羁御之制，无复可从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153884_comment'></div>五代衰乱，跳梁边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153884_comment'></div>上天有融，眷我圣祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153884_comment'></div>疏凿山河，重造日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153884_comment'></div>东臣九人，南庭百蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153884_comment'></div>武功文德，二帝相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153884_comment'></div>蠢尔戎羯，首鼠西北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153884_comment'></div>讨之则后服，赦之则先叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153884_comment'></div>数十年间，兵用未戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153884_comment'></div>我皇帝天地其德，日月其明，风雨其教，雷霆其威，阴阳其功，造化其智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153884_comment'></div>无穷兵之忿，无和亲之弱，无飞刍辇毂之劳，无迎降畜附之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153884_comment'></div>庙谋动于自然，成算出于无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153884_comment'></div>戎后请命，羌豪献誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153884_comment'></div>北至西归，愿备蕃卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153884_comment'></div>臣百世之所叛乱，服旷代之所犷戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153884_comment'></div>臣下不知其略，亿兆不知其功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153884_comment'></div>巍巍乎，荡荡乎，我皇帝之有天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153884_comment'></div>得御戎之上策，神而化之，圣德无名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153884_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》僖公四年经书「楚屈完来盟于师，盟于召陵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153884_comment'></div>曷为再言盟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153884_comment'></div>仲尼喜服荆楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153884_comment'></div>夫服一荆楚，圣人喜之，况我平三边、降二敌者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153884_comment'></div>臣再拜喜抃，谨献颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1153884'>帝宋经营，戎车四征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153884_comment'></div>东南易王，西北难庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153884_comment'></div>迁寇河陇，戎螫幽并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153884_comment'></div>我泽流春，我威飞霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153884_comment'></div>去如鸟兽，驱若蚊虻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153884_comment'></div>国既厎定，塞犹栖兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153884_comment'></div>吾皇柔克，顺帝之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153884_comment'></div>元造不测，圣功无形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153884_comment'></div>戎后欸塞，羌种乞盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153884_comment'></div>禀我正朔，受我官名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153884_comment'></div>弓櫜象弭，矛偃重英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153884_comment'></div>投烽榆塞，蓺黍戎亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153884_comment'></div>六合无云，纤尘不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153884_comment'></div>日月所到，皆被皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153884_comment'></div>环海为池，倚天为城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153884_comment'></div>恢恢圣谋，洋洋颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153884_comment'></div>有皇上帝，惟德是成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153884_comment'></div>莫忧匪国，我国既宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153884_comment'></div>莫患匪边，我边既平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153884_comment'></div>钦哉钦哉，永万千龄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1153884_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，作《广文颂》<div id='poem_1153885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广文颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153885")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153885'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153885'>景德二年夏六月颁劝学诏于天下，秋九月甲寅诏张六科取士，广文德而励儒业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153885_comment'></div>臣闻圣人仰观乎天，俯察乎地，知文之可以经上下，纬邦国，正礼乐，移风俗，于是乎修经籍为文之器，立庠序为文之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153885_comment'></div>植正化之本，导仁义之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153885_comment'></div>跬步之间，失之则乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153885_comment'></div>故先王谨教劝学，博文训士，以取辅相，以济功业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153885_comment'></div>其道充者其文盛，其政怠者其章缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153885_comment'></div>盖文者匠天下之器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153885_comment'></div>四代而降，文物之制，莫茂于汉，莫茂于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153885_comment'></div>自昔周道不融，青衿起刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153885_comment'></div>七雄分竞，干戈日寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153885_comment'></div>道堙杨墨，辞逸谈说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153885_comment'></div>斯文中否，而汉氏开之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153885_comment'></div>洎三国鼎峙，六朝南渡，义駮仙释，辞放轻丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153885_comment'></div>吾道将微，而唐氏隆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153885_comment'></div>然则汉乘秦弊，去圣犹近，学欲博而益专，文欲华而自质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153885_comment'></div>其取士也，故有贤良有道孝茂之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153885_comment'></div>唐革隋命，去圣踰远，学欲一而滋蔓，文欲典而更丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153885_comment'></div>其取士也，故有进士科目明经之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153885_comment'></div>夫汉之得人莫盛于策问，唐之取材莫精于辞赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153885_comment'></div>虽文质殊轨，而取舍齐致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153885_comment'></div>公卿之材，忠谠之臣，论议之官，博古之士，考之二史，世不乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153885_comment'></div>故制度可遵，历祚皆永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153885_comment'></div>暨五代宿兵，汉唐之制废缺垂尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153885_comment'></div>天启有宋，拯我儒德，曾不崇朝，文明天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153885_comment'></div>我皇帝亲斡文柄，指麾万国，变为政教，发为号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153885_comment'></div>景德之间，坐致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153885_comment'></div>蛮夷柔服，天下归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153885_comment'></div>边城夜开，五谷被野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153885_comment'></div>由是益重儒术，专用文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153885_comment'></div>增汉之科，式求典则；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153885_comment'></div>劝唐之学，以博文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153885_comment'></div>传曰：「周监于二代，郁郁乎文哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153885_comment'></div>虽使汉文武两帝、唐太明二宗生于今日，睹陛下好文之德，将震骇而不暇，岂敢自量其轻重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153885_comment'></div>臣叨预荐绅，窃闻公议，皆愿复三朝之礼，定封禅之制，告文德之成功，终荐神之厚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153885_comment'></div>具瞻圣德，不胜区区，谨昧死上《广文颂》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153885_comment'></div>其辞云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1153885'>星辰日月，丽我天则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153885_comment'></div>山川卉木，贲我坤德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153885_comment'></div>礼乐诗书，经我邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153885_comment'></div>三仪同文，群生茂殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153885_comment'></div>故我皇帝，道以文丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153885_comment'></div>吐耀象天，含章法地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153885_comment'></div>典故周旋，朝廷之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153885_comment'></div>儒雅雍容，卿相之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153885_comment'></div>既和三灵，既庭四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153885_comment'></div>乃监虞夏，式规汉唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153885_comment'></div>高张六科，制诏万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153885_comment'></div>敦劝儒学，亲策贤良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153885_comment'></div>景德之盛，斯文有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153885_comment'></div>励我多士，遂及百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153885_comment'></div>巷隘褒衣，涂歌雅咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153885_comment'></div>学馆渐海，儒宫越境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153885_comment'></div>天下文明，洋洋颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153885_comment'></div>方策鳞萃，礼乐教兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153885_comment'></div>翰墨如云，环佩盈庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153885_comment'></div>济济多士，吾皇以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153885_comment'></div>多士宁矣，纳忠献议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153885_comment'></div>封禅未行，三雍尚废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153885_comment'></div>愿及盛时，超行古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153885_comment'></div>帝曰俞哉，寔朕之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1153885_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，作《广农颂》<div id='poem_1153887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广农颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153887")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153887'>景德三年春正月庚戌，诏颁农田敕于天下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153887_comment'></div>二月癸未，诏郡国领劝农事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153887_comment'></div>崇化源而广农业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153887_comment'></div>臣闻圣人无土不王，无民不君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153887_comment'></div>有土地则王业兴，有人民则君道立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153887_comment'></div>故先王之建国也，土欲广而不用隙，民欲众而不用惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153887_comment'></div>谓地之不辟非吾土也，人之不农非吾民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153887_comment'></div>乃为闾里室家以蕃其生，为畎浍封畛以理其田，为耒耜钱镈以庀其器，为历象气候以授其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153887_comment'></div>立经制以御之，设官司以教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153887_comment'></div>均工商衡虞之税，正车马甲兵之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153887_comment'></div>于是乎仁义礼乐有所加，赏罚号令有所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153887_comment'></div>三代通制，建中经远，民以里居，地以井受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153887_comment'></div>暨秦开阡陌，农战相乘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153887_comment'></div>汉制名田，并无不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153887_comment'></div>旧章缺而仁政坠，经界慢而讻竞起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153887_comment'></div>沿革而下，古之制度不可复矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153887_comment'></div>其政何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153887_comment'></div>盖三季已还，五代而上，有天下者或竟不知天下以地为基，以农为本，以食为源，以教为器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153887_comment'></div>当其拨平祸乱，经始四国，则衽金革，简车马，计怀柔，议聚敛，赏勋旧，治城邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153887_comment'></div>暨边陲既宁，县县既平，功业既成，府库既盈，则思悉华夏以自奉，驱亿兆以从欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153887_comment'></div>有患<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1153887", 1153887, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>边幅</span>未阔，威武未震，则转刍粟，事边境；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153887_comment'></div>有患岁月易逝，容发易朽，则招方士，求神仙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153887_comment'></div>有患登览未远，行乐未极，则增台榭，丽宫室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153887_comment'></div>有患嫔御未广，歌舞未工，则渔声色，选伎艺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153887_comment'></div>有患校猎未快，驰骋未捷，则广苑囿，具毕弋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153887_comment'></div>有患巡幸未遍，游赏未普，则修驰道，飞清跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153887_comment'></div>其间自非负天启神授之资，有圣文灵武之德者，则不能训稼穑，务储峙，舍派而趋源，去末而从本，致天下太康，家给人足者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153887_comment'></div>我国家荷二圣基业，用三王礼乐，足食训农，克立治本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153887_comment'></div>吾皇龙飞，春秋鼎盛，励精百度，旁求黎献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153887_comment'></div>谓守文艰如创业，承平难如治乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153887_comment'></div>深鉴前世，专行王道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153887_comment'></div>羁縻四夷而重兵革，渔猎贤俊而藏网罟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153887_comment'></div>观六艺，虚台馆，听道德，定圣乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153887_comment'></div>功业之大，则成、康、文、景无或比隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153887_comment'></div>河山之远，则秦、汉、隋、唐不能齐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153887_comment'></div>菽麦流衍而红腐，玉帛充牣而露积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153887_comment'></div>陛下尚宸居减丽，御膳辍声，宵衣紫庭，清问多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153887_comment'></div>举三王之故实，修八世之坠典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153887_comment'></div>以为择循吏，守郡国，抚百姓，善则善矣，而未专也，于是授之使领，设为职司，所以循名而责实也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153887_comment'></div>颁宪令，经田畴，劝耕殖，至则至矣，而未一也，于是编其制度，勒为科条，所以建中而示法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153887_comment'></div>循名责实，则官不旷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153887_comment'></div>建中示法，则民不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153887_comment'></div>诏下之日，鬼神称庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153887_comment'></div>太平之风，旋踵可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153887_comment'></div>不终日而争讼息，未踰时而淳卤辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153887_comment'></div>九围之内，一岁之间，衣食足而仓廪实，仁义行而刑罚措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153887_comment'></div>大哉，炎宋功德，陛下教化，垂亿万世，与天无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153887_comment'></div>臣生逢圣明，叨观盛事，谨昧死上《庆农颂》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153887_comment'></div>其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1153887'>皇哉惟圣，躬提天柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153887_comment'></div>亿兆归心，三灵洽庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153887_comment'></div>广我田事，肇修稼政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153887_comment'></div>乃置官名，乃颁号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153887_comment'></div>号令维何，分条建规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153887_comment'></div>恩斯懋斯，流冗攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153887_comment'></div>官名维何，启职庀司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153887_comment'></div>训之导之，播种惟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153887_comment'></div>民曰勤止，服田力穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153887_comment'></div>昼尔于耕，宵尔无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153887_comment'></div>千耦偕飞，百谷咸殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153887_comment'></div>既艺淳卤，越经<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1153887", 1153887, "Clauses/181/Comments/0")'>封洫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153887_comment'></div>官曰涖止，纠力劝能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153887_comment'></div>庤我钱镈，疏我沟塍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153887_comment'></div>乃能灌溉，爰相邱陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153887_comment'></div>污莱以辟，游惰用惩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153887_comment'></div>赫赫圣谋，有作咸睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153887_comment'></div>畎浍四溟，井疆九土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153887_comment'></div>沃野万里，纵横其亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153887_comment'></div>拥耒成林，洒流降雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153887_comment'></div>阳春如膏，原隰如鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153887_comment'></div>我稼既华，六合生云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153887_comment'></div>稻粱黍稷，万井龙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153887_comment'></div>同我妇子，或耨或耘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153887_comment'></div>八月其穫，乃登尔稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153887_comment'></div>滞穗栖原，馀粮压野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153887_comment'></div>盈溢京庾，流衍方夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153887_comment'></div>式歌且谣，土金同价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153887_comment'></div>百姓足矣，君孰不足？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153887_comment'></div>三百之囷，九年之畜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153887_comment'></div>八蜡既通，五礼咸穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153887_comment'></div>藏财于民，所宝惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153887_comment'></div>君哉君哉，乐事训农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153887_comment'></div>炎帝之教，后稷之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153887_comment'></div>方我王度，明而未融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153887_comment'></div>臣之颂之，永矣无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_83_1153887_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　本年，在丹阳主簿任，作《周伯星颂》<div id='poem_1153888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153888?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周伯星颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153888")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153888_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153888'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153888'>景德三年夏四月周伯星见，书瑞应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153888_comment'></div>臣闻日月星辰，天之经也，国之纪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153888_comment'></div>日以象君，月以象臣，星以象民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153888_comment'></div>炎炎君德，不倾不侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153888_comment'></div>仁义文武昭于上，礼乐刑政临于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153888_comment'></div>得至阳之体，于是乎有日瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153888_comment'></div>昭昭臣道，不僭不忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153888_comment'></div>忠信方正积于内，吁谟献替发于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153888_comment'></div>得至阴之体，于是乎有月瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153888_comment'></div>君之灵如日之升，臣之英如月之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153888_comment'></div>照临下土，六合文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153888_comment'></div>赏罚不滥，兵革不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153888_comment'></div>粢盛不害，灾沴不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153888_comment'></div>生民熙熙，家给户足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153888_comment'></div>凿井而饮，耕田而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153888_comment'></div>蒙帝之力，生育蕃息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153888_comment'></div>于是乎上发于天，厥有星瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153888_comment'></div>《书》云：「庶民惟星」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153888_comment'></div>又云：「天聪明自我民聪明」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153888_comment'></div>盖星瑞之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153888_comment'></div>国家受天成命，五十年间，法令宽大，元元仁厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153888_comment'></div>自克殄并土，戎衣不再，年谷荐登，俊乂旅进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153888_comment'></div>我崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下虔巩神器，稽用故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153888_comment'></div>光昭百度，缉熙礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153888_comment'></div>刑赏以御中外，慈俭以率左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153888_comment'></div>群臣有羔羊之洁，公族怀麟趾之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153888_comment'></div>郡国州县，各扬其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153888_comment'></div>景德中，匈奴谨守要约，不敢犯边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153888_comment'></div>塞无宿兵，人用休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153888_comment'></div>齐民之家，不忧岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153888_comment'></div>食饫鸡豚，衣厚缯纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153888_comment'></div>耕有馀器，廪有滞谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153888_comment'></div>扶老携幼，涂歌里咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153888_comment'></div>大哉此时，上无失德，下无遗政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153888_comment'></div>君君臣臣，万国交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153888_comment'></div>虽日瑞于昼，月瑞于夜，曾不足表吾皇之明，朝廷之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153888_comment'></div>于是乎有周伯之象，告生民之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153888_comment'></div>见于首夏，国家火德之应也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153888_comment'></div>躔于角亢，人君寿考之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153888_comment'></div>天意若曰：令陛下寿考万年，平章百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153888_comment'></div>隆火德之光明，昭上帝之休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153888_comment'></div>愿陛下钦之念之，虽休勿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153888_comment'></div>不数年间，图书宝玉，雪霜风雨，山川草木，尽为嘉瑞，史不绝书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153888_comment'></div>故曰阳感天，不终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153888_comment'></div>盖天之于陛下，犹父子之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153888_comment'></div>臣叨列缙绅，仰观灵祉，知在今日，斯文有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153888_comment'></div>谨再拜上《周伯星颂》曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1153888'>帝宋三圣，功成治定，昭融景命，承天庆兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153888_comment'></div>周伯焞焞，经宵耀云，何德之纯，感星辰兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153888_comment'></div>吾君恭让，德音敷畅，盖天垂象，介景贶兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153888_comment'></div>我国文明，儒风炳灵，惟德降祯，发鸿英兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153888_comment'></div>东南委照，苍龙隐曜，徘徊天表，光帝道兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153888_comment'></div>考彼典章，知我天子，享嘉瑞兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153888_comment'></div>上可纪官，下可建元，法象星躔，假于天兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153888_comment'></div>昭我炎宋，永御星统，微臣作颂，歌日用兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1153888_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年2月</a>　二月，在丹阳主簿任，作《朝陵颂》<div id='poem_1153886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝陵颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153886")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153886'>景德四年春二月皇帝朝陵于巩，书礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153886_comment'></div>古者因山为陵，秦始置寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153886_comment'></div>汉氏因而制其礼，以晦望伏腊四时上食，岁正月天子率公卿百官诸侯王以朝，广孝德而尽思慕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153886_comment'></div>三代既往，汉氏文明，专以儒臣表正邦宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153886_comment'></div>千岁之下，垂为旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153886_comment'></div>自非万国厎定，天子仁孝，则不克行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153886_comment'></div>能行其礼者，必有大功茂德格于上下，灵泽庆赐流于百姓，鸿徽盛事纪于史策，声诗雅颂播于弦歌，足使昭感上穹，光被海外，动植所生，无不茂育，人迹所到，无不臣服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153886_comment'></div>盖孝之为德也，际天地而感万物者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153886_comment'></div>我崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下圣性纯孝，加于亿兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153886_comment'></div>郊祀燔瘗以祇事天地，春秋蒸尝以昭奉寝庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153886_comment'></div>俎豆牺牲，躬自执献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153886_comment'></div>尽诚极孝，冠于往初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153886_comment'></div>景德中天下无事，远人内附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153886_comment'></div>尘清九围，通驿万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153886_comment'></div>吾皇帝亲丕丕之基，念祖考之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153886_comment'></div>履霜露以悽怆，感春雨而怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153886_comment'></div>孝思之心，不舍晨夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153886_comment'></div>乃登用汉典，制诰有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153886_comment'></div>庀库辂，简环卫，幸巩洛，朝陵寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153886_comment'></div>崇牲牷之礼，备韶武之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153886_comment'></div>六官毕从，四蕃陪位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153886_comment'></div>锡銮珩佩，震响郊圻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153886_comment'></div>梯航宝玉，骏奔川陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153886_comment'></div>自古庙会祭享之盛未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153886_comment'></div>足以冠虞舜之德，光炎汉之典，昭假鬼神，炳焕方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153886_comment'></div>升闻于天，则日月星辰，雪霜风雨，无有不时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153886_comment'></div>降感于地，则山川江河，昆虫草木，无有失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153886_comment'></div>大哉，孝德之盛也，不可得而名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153886_comment'></div>远郡小臣，以文受禄，无以自效，谨献颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1153886'>皇帝丕显，孝治四国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153886_comment'></div>乃祖有功，乃宗有德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153886_comment'></div>功业且溥，惟帝太祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153886_comment'></div>虔刘巨盗，建邦启土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153886_comment'></div>德昭且融，惟帝太宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153886_comment'></div>表正大中，进贤保庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153886_comment'></div>两朝厌世，龙归波逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153886_comment'></div>葬我弓剑，因山巩地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153886_comment'></div>春日熙熙，惟皇孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153886_comment'></div>乃朝陵寝，于洛之畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153886_comment'></div>左纛倚天，旂旐葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153886_comment'></div>诸侯扈跸，佩玉参差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153886_comment'></div>和銮锵锵，行道迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153886_comment'></div>瞻望松柏，帝心伤悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153886_comment'></div>亦既至止，苾芬孝享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153886_comment'></div>吉蠲牺象，馨香郁鬯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153886_comment'></div>动止心企，音容目想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153886_comment'></div>祖考来格，歆我追养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153886_comment'></div>乐以迎来，哀以送往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153886_comment'></div>命我考嗣，受天灵贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153886_comment'></div>河洛之滨，太和氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153886_comment'></div>庆泽流春，皇风感人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153886_comment'></div>翠华旋归，车服振振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153886_comment'></div>宋虽旧邦，景命惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153886_comment'></div>孝德不匮，永锡下民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153886_comment'></div>下民亲亲，万物皆醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153886_comment'></div>歌颂腾文，竹帛流芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153886_comment'></div>孝哉皇哉，子子孙孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1153886_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临海
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ecc851b75b84477bb62f5b5c2cc4c49a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ecc851b75b84477bb62f5b5c2cc4c49a");'><span id='ecc851b75b84477bb62f5b5c2cc4c49a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1010')">1008-1010年</a>，24-26岁</div><div id='ecc851b75b84477bb62f5b5c2cc4c49a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　本年，在台州通判任，作《大中祥符颂》<div id='poem_1153889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大中祥符颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1008年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153889")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153889'>崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下即位之十二年春正月乙丑，《大中祥符》三篇降于左承天门，书瑞应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153889_comment'></div>以日者谨天命也，以地者大灵贶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153889_comment'></div>臣闻庖牺氏作，结绳而治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153889_comment'></div>天将有命，易以书契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153889_comment'></div>龙马负图出于河，圣人观之，退而画八卦，两仪四象，吉凶悔吝，无所遁其形矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153889_comment'></div>百官以治，万民以察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153889_comment'></div>后世帝王言大政者，自庖牺氏始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153889_comment'></div>夏后氏作，鲧堙洪水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153889_comment'></div>天将有命，奠厥山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153889_comment'></div>神龟负书出于洛，圣人获之，退而叙九畴，五行八政，休咎威福，无所隐其奥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153889_comment'></div>彝伦攸叙，水土俾乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153889_comment'></div>后世帝王言大功者，自夏后氏始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153889_comment'></div>炎宋氏作，三圣政治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153889_comment'></div>天将有命，昭厥中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153889_comment'></div>神人奉符降于汴，圣人受之，退而启三篇，清静简易，道德刑政，无所藏其秘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153889_comment'></div>四夷率服，亿兆可封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153889_comment'></div>后嗣帝王言大中者，自我皇帝始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153889_comment'></div>大哉三氏之德，与天齐盛，皆获符书，并垂典训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153889_comment'></div>混而言之则同，参而言之则异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153889_comment'></div>同者事也，异者道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153889_comment'></div>伏羲以文物未作，朝章汩乱，天授以图，始启其政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153889_comment'></div>夏后以水灾未乂，下民昏垫，天授以书，始启其功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153889_comment'></div>炎宋以太平方至，帝道有融，天授以符，爰建其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153889_comment'></div>是则政也、功也、中也，同为至道，考其异则中也可以兼于政功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153889_comment'></div>图也、书也、符也，同为嘉瑞，考其异则符也可以冠于图书矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153889_comment'></div>河也、洛也、汴也，同为灵川，考其异则汴也可以加于河洛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153889_comment'></div>牺也、禹也、宋也，同为上圣，考其异则宋也可以跨于牺夏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153889_comment'></div>故八卦之始画也，其象隐晦，仲尼赞之，乃著于经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153889_comment'></div>九畴之始类也，其文草昧，箕子衍之，乃列于典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153889_comment'></div>我《大中》三篇，其则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153889_comment'></div>宛有章句，政教出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153889_comment'></div>天作之，天述之，授我皇帝，以七六籍，以锡明命，为万世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153889_comment'></div>故天不敢畀龙马，授神龟，负于河，荐于洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153889_comment'></div>乃命使者奉而降汴魏阙之下，禁门之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153889_comment'></div>知天之恭我皇家且异于古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153889_comment'></div>使仲尼复生，箕子不死，在于今日，舞之蹈之，犹且不暇，讵敢赞之于经，而衍之于典者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153889_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153889_comment'></div>千祀之衰也，天道何远乎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153889_comment'></div>一朝之盛也，天道何迩乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153889_comment'></div>盖我国家揆五代之乱，奄有神器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153889_comment'></div>太祖灵武经始于前，太宗文明光被于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153889_comment'></div>廷四海，詟万灵，枭吴馘蜀，裂广屠并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153889_comment'></div>不二十年，县县穆清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153889_comment'></div>授圣三叶，以致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153889_comment'></div>今上居以天体，化以神声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153889_comment'></div>阴阳有愆伏而圣功无阙，日月有盈昃而皇明不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153889_comment'></div>故强敌北面而受封，羌豪泥首而内附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153889_comment'></div>罢河西之戍，放榆关之马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153889_comment'></div>京洛之间，王气聚为宫阙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153889_comment'></div>良耜不试，嘉谷蕃生于田野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153889_comment'></div>龆龀舞咏于道路，耆寿沐浴于膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153889_comment'></div>桴鼓在庭而罢击，桃李垂路而不攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153889_comment'></div>阡陌服车马，闾阎享粱肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153889_comment'></div>当是时，天虽欲秘图箓，爱符命，其可得乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153889_comment'></div>然则符瑞之至，以五行而言，皆有象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153889_comment'></div>臣以列为三章者阳数也，封黄帛者中色也，时以春者仁也，降承天门者承天嘉号也，门，听政之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153889_comment'></div>天意若曰：王者体阳德，御中道，行至仁，则有图书之瑞，应之以承天之祐，而听万国之政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153889_comment'></div>臣幼学史氏，讲《春秋》大义，以为东周不竞，瑞不当至，先圣削而不书，退有凤鸟河图之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153889_comment'></div>繄自获麟距国初建隆，历二百有四甲子矣，贤材代谢而符命不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153889_comment'></div>臣也何幸，逢时遇主，行年二十有四而叨观不世之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153889_comment'></div>上比圣贤，自庆多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153889_comment'></div>故身在沧海之上，心驰象魏之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153889_comment'></div>恨无文辞以广称述，谨昧死望阙再拜颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1153889'>惟圣有功，功格于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153889_comment'></div>日月星辰，炳其灵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153889_comment'></div>惟圣有道，道格于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153889_comment'></div>山川草木，耀其祥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153889_comment'></div>炎宋氏作，三圣承平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153889_comment'></div>休功无形，至道无名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153889_comment'></div>莫高匪天，莫厚匪地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153889_comment'></div>不足炳其灵，不足耀其祯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153889_comment'></div>三正有神，同开奥秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153889_comment'></div>取图河洛，裁文五纬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153889_comment'></div>爰作受命，王者之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153889_comment'></div>景德之盛，奉之而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153889_comment'></div>先斯吉日，神告有密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153889_comment'></div>仙服降庭，奔精照室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153889_comment'></div>苍龙在申，太蔟歌春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153889_comment'></div>素月哉魄，朱曦始晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153889_comment'></div>皇帝受之，于承天门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153889_comment'></div>宿卫咸观，玉帛骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153889_comment'></div>爰有大夫，进牍而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153889_comment'></div>臣知天意，敢告于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153889_comment'></div>亿兆欢心，宗庙遐福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153889_comment'></div>有感于帝，化为宝箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153889_comment'></div>文武流光，礼乐腾芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153889_comment'></div>上达于天，化为宝文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153889_comment'></div>表我皇家，大中建国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153889_comment'></div>表我天子，大中立极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153889_comment'></div>三篇未至，中道以崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153889_comment'></div>三篇既至，中德益隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153889_comment'></div>建元眚灾，华裔可封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153889_comment'></div>庆赐周旋，囹圄虚空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153889_comment'></div>一之日荐于寝庙，昭穆增耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153889_comment'></div>二之日告于朝廷，雅颂腾声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153889_comment'></div>三之日达于九土，里巷赓歌，鸟兽率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153889_comment'></div>四之日闻于八荒，投戈右衽，九译来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153889_comment'></div>可以象功，制礼修乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153889_comment'></div>三五之事，一旦而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153889_comment'></div>可以告成，登封降禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153889_comment'></div>八九之功，一朝而见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153889_comment'></div>史氏书之，藏于太室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153889_comment'></div>垂厥子孙，遐观茂实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153889_comment'></div>太师歌之，传于乐府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153889_comment'></div>荐厥岱郊，永告嘉祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153889_comment'></div>素王圣哲，见叹河图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153889_comment'></div>臣之庸昧，获观祥符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153889_comment'></div>歌咏功德，职士大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153889_comment'></div>稽首献颂，愿继典谟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_107_1153889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　本年，在台州通判任，奉表进《景德五颂》及《大中祥符颂》，迁著作佐郎。作品：上景德五颂大中祥符颂引表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1153644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上景德五颂大中祥符颂引表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1008年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153644")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153644'>臣某言：准中书劄子，奉圣旨，依奏令进《景德五颂》并《大中祥符颂》者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153644_comment'></div>下臣有请，倾匪石之丹心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153644_comment'></div>上帝曰俞，降如丝之睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153644_comment'></div>震惶无所，欣愧踰涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153644_comment'></div>臣诚感诚惧、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153644_comment'></div>臣闻灵鸟升歌，告汤孙之景贶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153644_comment'></div>昊天著颂，美周室之成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153644_comment'></div>被以管弦，荐之郊庙，振明光于万世，昭茂实于三仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153644_comment'></div>尔后王道陵迟，颁声彫缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153644_comment'></div>非旷大夫之职，岂无博士之官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153644_comment'></div>盖成命未融，则斯文不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153644_comment'></div>我国家圆方右序，中外穆清，拨五代之乱离，继三皇之昭夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153644_comment'></div>黼黻冠冕，正列采而象乾坤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153644_comment'></div>椌楬埙篪，广德音而事祖考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153644_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下春秋鼎盛，圣睿日跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153644_comment'></div>御天球及河图，受元符与黄瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153644_comment'></div>英声蜂涌，惠露春流，承龙翼于咸平，致鸿钧于景德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153644_comment'></div>北戎震叠，泥首幽并；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153644_comment'></div>左纛雍容，朝陵巩洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153644_comment'></div>著训农之懿典，颂劝学之彝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153644_comment'></div>泽浸幅员，仁翔海外，文武际天而接地，灵祇流庆而发祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153644_comment'></div>介瑞星辰，告休符箓，冠黄虞之故实，掩唐汉之声明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153644_comment'></div>道通九夷，执玉万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153644_comment'></div>考典坟而未有，极翰墨以难名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153644_comment'></div>巍乎皇乎，广矣大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153644_comment'></div>当是时，《臣工》《清庙》，讵可以美形容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153644_comment'></div>金牒玉函，岂足以昭姓氏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153644_comment'></div>太史珥笔，不暇纪丰功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153644_comment'></div>良士在庭，未能歌至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153644_comment'></div>岂臣庸昧，敢颂清明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153644_comment'></div>盖念胄绪孤平，艺文浅陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153644_comment'></div>遭逢陛下，拔擢流中，为万乘之门生，登六科之丙第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153644_comment'></div>隶官膳寺，将命南州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153644_comment'></div>虽竭虑以安民，奈无阶而答禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153644_comment'></div>临文振袂，抚剑驰魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153644_comment'></div>幸齿发之未衰，冀君王之可报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153644_comment'></div>以是区分簿领，刻念典谟，极精爽之再三，颂猷徽之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153644_comment'></div>欲输尘露，少拟声诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153644_comment'></div>遂昧死而献言，方伏膺而待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153644_comment'></div>恭惟陛下恢崇至圣，敦劝素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153644_comment'></div>无言不雠，无德不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153644_comment'></div>回曜灵之列景，照时藿之至心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153644_comment'></div>特降纶言，爰从奏请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153644_comment'></div>敢不擢子渊而匠意，效吉甫以裁章，饰陋彫顽，间旒渎纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153644_comment'></div>伏愿皇帝陛下念臣尝叨天奖，曾近帝晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153644_comment'></div>当垂拱之馀时，遇观书之暇日，曲回宸鉴，少听芜音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153644_comment'></div>宽椹斧之严诛，轸昆虫之微意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153644_comment'></div>百世斯幸，万死甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153644_comment'></div>抑又闻，英主难逢，良时罕遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153644_comment'></div>河图不至，宣父兴嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153644_comment'></div>岱岳未封，相如驰恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153644_comment'></div>臣常自庆，生实逢辰，既踰弱冠之年，便遇泥金之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153644_comment'></div>在于今日，万世一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153644_comment'></div>茍不能目睹陶匏，足升坛墠，以斯为士，曷若无生！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153644_comment'></div>今陛下丕奉珍符，恭行大典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153644_comment'></div>适遂群生之欲，岂违庶品之诚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153644_comment'></div>愿令臣随一礼官，执一祭器，凫抃徐銮之后，骏奔缇骑之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153644_comment'></div>瞻云瑞于封中，听神声于岳下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153644_comment'></div>伴禽鱼而舞跃，随耆幼以讴歌，时颂鸿徽，上畴灵泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153644_comment'></div>是则死当不朽，生有馀荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153644_comment'></div>永念丹诚，有如皦日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153644_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣激切恳祷之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1153644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年</a>　约于本年，在台州通判任，有诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年1月</a>　正月，在台州通判任，应孟玄岳之请，作《重建道藏经记》作品：重建道藏经记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《正统道藏》洞玄部记传类《天台山志》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年</a>　春，在台州通判任，召还，迁秘书丞。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
黄冈

-----title
邓州
-----detail

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='33cd9f42465e484f97ac65c6fc723bf2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("33cd9f42465e484f97ac65c6fc723bf2");'><span id='33cd9f42465e484f97ac65c6fc723bf2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1021')">1020-1021年</a>，36-37岁</div><div id='33cd9f42465e484f97ac65c6fc723bf2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年4月</a>　四月，在知襄州任，以赈灾有功，获赐书褒谕，有谢表。作品：谢赐奖谕襄州日公政诏表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1153636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐奖谕襄州日公政诏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1020年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153636")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153636'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153636'>臣某言：伏蒙圣慈以襄州奏，天禧四年中民食荒歉，贼盗相乘，臣在任劝诱得斛斗一十一万石，救济得饥民四十六万一千三百馀口等事，特赐诏书奖谕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153636_comment'></div>孤臣自励，偶著于微劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153636_comment'></div>圣念过深，特颁于温诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153636_comment'></div>退自惟省，罔措心颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153636_comment'></div>伏念臣，顷岁襄樊，庶民饥馑，聚而为盗，烟火相望，系以议刑，狱犴充塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153636_comment'></div>猥当绥抚之职，合思拯济之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153636_comment'></div>乃置醇醪，躬觞右族，谕以朝廷之意，贷其廪给之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153636_comment'></div>并遣属僚，分饩流冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153636_comment'></div>烦使轩之上状，蒙台敕以垂褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153636_comment'></div>伊俾后人，遂刊于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153636_comment'></div>岁当再闰，郡有彝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153636_comment'></div>爰敷述于奏封，请肇编于地志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153636_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下惠深求旧，政切爱民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153636_comment'></div>念兹侍从之臣，尝罄忠劳之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153636_comment'></div>玺书叹赏，式劝于在公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153636_comment'></div>刍效琐微，曷胜于云补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153636_comment'></div>惟期况瘁，少谢鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1153636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1153636'><span class='label'>按：</span>翰林院本、孔本《文庄集》卷八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1153636_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年4月</a>　四月，在知襄州任，有谢皇太后表。作品：谢皇太后表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年6月26日</a>　六月二十六日，在知襄州任，姜遵言其抚俗有方，莅事无滞，受诏褒奖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1021&endYear=1021')">1021年11月</a>　十一月，在知襄州任，有题名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1021&endYear=1021')">1021年</a>　本年，在知襄州任，上言襄州凤林镇道侧地涌事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
凤台
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='44849e0fc61d46a8b949f91f43da6fcb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("44849e0fc61d46a8b949f91f43da6fcb");'><span id='44849e0fc61d46a8b949f91f43da6fcb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1022&endYear=1022')">1022年</a>，38岁</div><div id='44849e0fc61d46a8b949f91f43da6fcb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1022&endYear=1022')">1022年</a>　本年，迁户部郎中，徙知寿州，有启贺晏殊除景灵宫副使。作品：贺晏内翰除景灵宫副使启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一七。晏殊除景灵宫副使事据《续资治通鉴长编》卷九九及欧阳修《观文殿大学士行兵部尚书西京留守赠司空兼侍中晏公神道碑铭》（《居士集》卷二二））</span><div id='poem_1153782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺晏内翰除景灵宫副使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1022年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153782")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153782'>右，某伏审祗奉恩俞，荣加命秩，伏惟庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153782_comment'></div>恭以某官气钟辰律，识贯天渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153782_comment'></div>秉亮节以光朝，鼓英辞而高世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153782_comment'></div>夙昭贤业，茂著师规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153782_comment'></div>慎基命之惟新，罄吁谟而入告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153782_comment'></div>周旋三接，导笔舌于天常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153782_comment'></div>申敕万几，谐笙簧于帝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153782_comment'></div>鸿猷灼叙，群品推高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153782_comment'></div>果由岩近之司，更益便蕃之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153782_comment'></div>开荣琐闼，克重于官联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153782_comment'></div>作贰殊庭，载光于使范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153782_comment'></div>绅绥动色，竹素杨芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153782_comment'></div>实乃眷之是膺，俾斯文而有属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153782_comment'></div>当阳图旧，已旌朱邸之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153782_comment'></div>绝席奋庸，焉避黑头之拜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153782_comment'></div>恭承嘉会，超绝前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153782_comment'></div>某屏去周行，外司汉竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153782_comment'></div>庆登贤之有命，怅申礼以无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153782_comment'></div>仰系门闱，岂任飞越？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153782_comment'></div>伏恨条职所拘，不获躬诣台屏，某无任欣跃依归激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1153782_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
安陆
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a7e5d7642b564f4f914bb41a9574bae6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a7e5d7642b564f4f914bb41a9574bae6");'><span id='a7e5d7642b564f4f914bb41a9574bae6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>，39岁</div><div id='a7e5d7642b564f4f914bb41a9574bae6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年4月</a>　四月，在知安州任，有启贺薛奎知开封府。作品：贺薛待制知开封府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1153789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺薛待制知开封府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1023年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153789")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153789'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153789'>右，某伏审祗奉制恩，荣莅天邑，伏惟庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153789_comment'></div>恭以某官宏猷体远，精识钩深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153789_comment'></div>嘉言奋乎黈聪，懿文缛乎邦宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153789_comment'></div>而自宸帷访逮，计省践扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153789_comment'></div>瑞凤览晖，仪鸿簉羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153789_comment'></div>体貌之荣虽渥，弥纶之业未宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153789_comment'></div>乃眷浩穰，遂兹尹正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153789_comment'></div>群玉上帝之府，克峻于官联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153789_comment'></div>太微三光之庭，茂延于昼接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153789_comment'></div>式夫古训，时厥大中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153789_comment'></div>前赵后王，方仰追于懿范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153789_comment'></div>左辅右弼，伫协赞于吁谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153789_comment'></div>遴柬惟新，游谈胥庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153789_comment'></div>某出麾外服，遐抃吉音，燕厦莫趋，凫藻增跃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1153789_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　本年，在知安州任，赏识宋庠、宋祁兄弟，命作《落花》诗。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b9c2dd5e872849e18fef05d461157df8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b9c2dd5e872849e18fef05d461157df8");'><span id='b9c2dd5e872849e18fef05d461157df8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1024')">1023-1024年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='b9c2dd5e872849e18fef05d461157df8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　本年，由知安州徙知洪州，到任有谢表。作品：洪州到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1023年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153585")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153585'>臣某言：伏奉敕命，就差知洪州军州事，已于今月十三日到任礼上讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153585_comment'></div>孤宦沉迷，累更于郡组；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153585_comment'></div>隆恩横贷，复序于藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153585_comment'></div>惟忖已还，心颜靡措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153585_comment'></div>伏念臣天资浅薄，门绪悴寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153585_comment'></div>幸会先朝，误阶荣次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153585_comment'></div>虔遵孝治，冒触宽科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153585_comment'></div>戚既自诒，孽将安逭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153585_comment'></div>仰赖天宥，尚剖左符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153585_comment'></div>继典五城，连更七祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153585_comment'></div>眩瞀滞疾，圈养自安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153585_comment'></div>孤苦馀生，</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1153585'>丁滋甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153585_comment'></div>徒索累钟之奉，绝无横草之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153585_comment'></div>窃自忧惟，合从澄汰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153585_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇尊位皇帝陛下哀矜庶品，保宥群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153585_comment'></div>躬奋乾刚，肃持威柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153585_comment'></div>恩丰漏目，贳馀党于铜山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153585_comment'></div>礼重斋心，登正人于玉铉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153585_comment'></div>刬除弊杻，崇起化枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153585_comment'></div>事无善而不旌，材有长而毕录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153585_comment'></div>而复勤哀旧物，澄洗非辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153585_comment'></div>太和洽于萌生，广照钧于隙穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153585_comment'></div>岂意伤摧之末，猥叨抆拭之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153585_comment'></div>载锡装钱，就升州寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153585_comment'></div>矧兹洪井，实表重江，襟带七闽，咽喉百粤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153585_comment'></div>使驿相系，军府是司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153585_comment'></div>地望颇雄，禄廪殊厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153585_comment'></div>敢不重苏肝胆，罢怯于虚弦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153585_comment'></div>再整筋骸，渐图于实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153585_comment'></div>永期糜溃，少谢恫矜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1153585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　本年，在知洪州任，上疏请禁左道妖言。作品：洪州请断祅巫奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1153726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州请断祅巫奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1023年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153726")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153726'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153726'>臣闻左道乱俗，祅言惑众，在昔之法，皆杀无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153726_comment'></div>盖以奸臣逆节，狂贼乱规，多假鬼神，摇动耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153726_comment'></div>汉之张角，晋之孙恩，偶失防闲，遂至屯聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153726_comment'></div>国家宜有严制，以肃多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153726_comment'></div>窃以当州东引七闽，南控百粤，编氓右鬼，旧俗尚巫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153726_comment'></div>在汉栾巴，已尝剪理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153726_comment'></div>爰从近岁，传习滋多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153726_comment'></div>假托禨祥，愚弄黎庶，剿绝性命，规取货财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153726_comment'></div>皆于所居，塑画魅魑，陈列幡帜，鸣击鼓角，谓之神坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153726_comment'></div>婴孺襁褓，已令寄育，字曰坛留、坛保之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153726_comment'></div>及其稍长，则传习祅法，驱为童隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153726_comment'></div>民之有病，则门施符术，禁绝往来，斥远至亲，屏去便物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153726_comment'></div>家人营药，则曰神不许服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153726_comment'></div>病者欲饭，则云神未听飧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153726_comment'></div>率令疫人，死于饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153726_comment'></div>洎至亡者服用，又言馀祟所凭，人不敢留，规以自入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153726_comment'></div>若幸而获免，家之所资，假神而言，无求不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153726_comment'></div>其间有孤子单族，首面幼妻，或绝户以图财，或害夫而纳妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153726_comment'></div>浸淫既久，习熟为常，民被非辜，了不为怪，奉之愈谨，信之益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153726_comment'></div>从其言甚于典章，畏其威重于官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153726_comment'></div>奇神异像，图绘岁增；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153726_comment'></div>邪箓祅符，传写日夥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153726_comment'></div>小则鸡豚致祀，敛以还家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153726_comment'></div>大则歌舞聚人，食其馀胙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153726_comment'></div>婚葬出处，动必求师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153726_comment'></div>劫盗斗争，行须作水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153726_comment'></div>蛊耗衣食，眩惑里闾，设欲扇摇，不难连结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153726_comment'></div>在于典宪，具有章条，其如法未胜奸，药弗瘳疾，宜颁峻典，以革祅风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153726_comment'></div>当州师巫一千九百馀户，臣已勒令改业归农，及攻习针炙之脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153726_comment'></div>所有首纳、祅妄、神像、符箓、神衫、神杖、魂巾、魂帽，钟角、刀笏、沙罗等一万一千馀事，已令焚燬及纳官讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153726_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷严赐条约，所冀屏除巨害，保宥群生，杜渐防萌，少裨万一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1153726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　本年，在知洪州任，中使赍御札至，有诗上宋仁宗。作品：谢颁御札。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见夏谱，诗题为代拟。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　本年，在知洪州任，上疏乞与修《真宗实录》，不报。作品：乞与修真宗实录表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1153647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞与修真宗实录表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153647")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153647'>臣某言：伏以缉熙盛节，先圣之鸿徽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153647_comment'></div>䌷绎信书，孤臣之旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153647_comment'></div>冀殚薄技，少谢遗恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153647_comment'></div>仰渎谅阴，伏增震悸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153647_comment'></div>臣某诚恳诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153647_comment'></div>窃念臣材命奇薄，门族悴寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153647_comment'></div>顷事先朝，最承华宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153647_comment'></div>对问轩陛，擢自诸科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153647_comment'></div>第念庸微，久陪法从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153647_comment'></div>旋以上封纳爵，诣理代亲，事敢自明，谊当引罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153647_comment'></div>先皇帝恫矜孝养，昭式礼经，抑去空文，比用宽典，裁令出守，趣使知非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153647_comment'></div>臣敢不梦寐惟忧，夙宵咎痛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153647_comment'></div>使食当去，亦冀改为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153647_comment'></div>傥心可铭，不难自剋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153647_comment'></div>庶伸尺寸，渐积岁年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153647_comment'></div>赎一眚于前辜，答万分于用造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153647_comment'></div>何图凭几，遽迫遗弓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153647_comment'></div>云补无辰，攀号罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153647_comment'></div>恭以真宗皇帝躬训慈俭，颛讲艺文，拓邃古之皇衢，刬叔世之霸轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153647_comment'></div>泽浸九域，雨润而云游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153647_comment'></div>威惮四夷，风翔而电照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153647_comment'></div>临民先悃愊之吏，防边后忿鸷之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153647_comment'></div>恭默道枢，偃仆武节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153647_comment'></div>长养万物，休息群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153647_comment'></div>由是瑞命荐臻，上仪交举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153647_comment'></div>纪姓垂鸿之典，焕衍于苍珉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153647_comment'></div>候日畴圣之符，充溢于金匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153647_comment'></div>仰对在天之烈，莫先垂世之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153647_comment'></div>必当遴简时材，章叙实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153647_comment'></div>礼文至盛，注记尤多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153647_comment'></div>诚须博集简编，广分卷第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153647_comment'></div>宜有冗吏，以备后陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153647_comment'></div>重念臣顷在往年，常参史局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153647_comment'></div>太祖皇帝大功美业，幸预于编研；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153647_comment'></div>太宗皇帝盛德嘉猷，继叨于颂次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153647_comment'></div>成书未几，急景难留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153647_comment'></div>当时史官迭为异物，唯臣与晁迥二人尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153647_comment'></div>臣虽出典五城，连更六祀，弃置刀笔，奔走泥涂，温故无由，属言多废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153647_comment'></div>若乃先圣发明之类例，朝家经济之规模，靡敢暂忘，粗能追忆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153647_comment'></div>傥使编联事实，系叙日时，庶能上给英儒，广资鸿笔，宣赞风美，焕烁古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153647_comment'></div>式效涓诚，仰酬馀烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153647_comment'></div>伏望皇太后陛下布昭宸鉴，祗遹诒谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153647_comment'></div>哀报国之危衷，委容辉之末照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153647_comment'></div>念臣先圣宠绥之日，振拔为优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153647_comment'></div>皇帝潜跃之初，遭逢最旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153647_comment'></div>特垂开可，许以报投，讵敢衒鬻非材，徼冀误宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153647_comment'></div>傥俯容于竭力，乞靡预于畴劳，才获成编，即求为郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153647_comment'></div>永罄朴忠之节，仰酬简照之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1153647_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阜阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0edf6f02ee034adaad57210f4d199957_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0edf6f02ee034adaad57210f4d199957");'><span id='0edf6f02ee034adaad57210f4d199957_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>，49岁</div><div id='0edf6f02ee034adaad57210f4d199957' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年5月12日</a>　五月十二日，到知颍州任，有谢表。作品：颍州到任谢上表。<div id='poem_1153590' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153590' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153590?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153590")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153590_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153590'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153590'>臣某言：伏奉敕命差知颍州军州事，已于今月十二日到任礼上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153590_comment'></div>亲见吏民，奉宣温诏，因望京阙，乍远迩颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153590_comment'></div>伏念臣世本孤平，业惟文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153590_comment'></div>先臣尽节，以忠孝传家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153590_comment'></div>真庙临轩，以贤良中选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153590_comment'></div>涖职数十次，效官三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153590_comment'></div>四海宪章，编研稍备；<div class='inline'
