id='poem_sentence_6_1153590_comment'></div>三朝史策，颂次继成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153590_comment'></div>虽无可纪之勤，颇励当官之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153590_comment'></div>而自一陪钧轴，再贰枢廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153590_comment'></div>固欲罄述远猷，极陈时弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153590_comment'></div>不惟事有深隐，于众意之罕同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153590_comment'></div>而又职在参裨，终大议之难立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153590_comment'></div>但务爱君竭志，率职励精，辑理军防，裁处边奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153590_comment'></div>详言正色，规检于武臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153590_comment'></div>潜计密谋，周旋于兵要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153590_comment'></div>耻捷给口吻，以揣摩上心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153590_comment'></div>耻结托朋游，以自为身计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153590_comment'></div>七周年籥，三奉禋燔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153590_comment'></div>顾每速于人言，亦屡移于病告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153590_comment'></div>既无显著之效，大妨贤俊之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153590_comment'></div>赖圣鉴之保全，得列城之息偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153590_comment'></div>陪京匪远，庇族颇优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153590_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊位皇帝陛下念臣早奉龙姿，最为旧物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153590_comment'></div>怜臣逮事先帝，本是常材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153590_comment'></div>惟天地之至仁，务从善贷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153590_comment'></div>记犬马之前效，特出异恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153590_comment'></div>省过以还，感极以泣，乍遥旒扆，方事米盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153590_comment'></div>保庇之慈，虽君亲之是赖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153590_comment'></div>孤危之迹，誓寒苦以自彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153590_comment'></div>冀集涓尘，少裨海岳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1153590_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年7月23日</a>　七月二十三日，在知颍州任，徙知青州，兼京东灾伤州军体量安抚使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
益都
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='69a3b6a2ee174a9fbd3a66f0ae0fa8da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("69a3b6a2ee174a9fbd3a66f0ae0fa8da");'><span id='69a3b6a2ee174a9fbd3a66f0ae0fa8da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1034')">1033-1034年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='69a3b6a2ee174a9fbd3a66f0ae0fa8da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年8月14日</a>　八月十四日，到知青州任，有谢表。作品：青州到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年8月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153591")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153591'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153591'>臣某言：昨奉敕差知青州，充青淄等州军安抚使，已于今月十四日到任赴上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153591_comment'></div>中降命书，外迁侯服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153591_comment'></div>循涯已过，铭骨殊深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153591_comment'></div>臣某诚感诚忭，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153591_comment'></div>伏念臣本以孤生，早尘上禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153591_comment'></div>不自揆度，强学古人之为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153591_comment'></div>何意遭逢，遂蒙圣主之眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153591_comment'></div>尽忠图报，无意他防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153591_comment'></div>勤劳一事以未成，谗嫉万端而已搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153591_comment'></div>盖朝伦之共弃，独天造以曲全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153591_comment'></div>假以清资，付之近郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153591_comment'></div>始再更于年籥，遄就改于州麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153591_comment'></div>素称表海之雄，乃重抚封之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153591_comment'></div>事权增大，职业夥繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153591_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊位皇帝陛下至德兼容，大明回照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153591_comment'></div>察臣本由直道，知臣不避众嫌，每闻谮毁之辞，常加庇护之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153591_comment'></div>矧推异渥，复委要藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153591_comment'></div>臣方知向之所存，果非失道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153591_comment'></div>死而后已，誓不改为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153591_comment'></div>永坚愚悫之心，上答睿明之施。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1153591_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年1月1日</a>　正月一日，在知青州任，作《青州州学后记》<div id='poem_1153866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青州州学后记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153866")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153866'>国家制天下，肇有十八路，京东首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153866_comment'></div>西起甸服，东渐淮海，南略洙泗，北际河濮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153866_comment'></div>关防之要，控制之重，城闉之大，室居之盛，青复首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153866_comment'></div>建隆距明道继政四十有二，皆岩庙勋旧，台阁材彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153866_comment'></div>方重镇俗，严明驭下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153866_comment'></div>信孚惠洽，吏端刑清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153866_comment'></div>润金石，蔼谣诵，固亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153866_comment'></div>若恢教化之原，崇学校之美，惟丞相太原公有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153866_comment'></div>天圣七载，公委远时柄，来牧故乡，以平章庶务之心，斟酌元化之手，裁量一郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153866_comment'></div>丰功懿迹，不容谈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153866_comment'></div>其最为荐绅所称道者，以公顷奉乡书，偕郡计，冠多士，长百工，洎偃息作藩，雍容立政，事必敦本，仁不遗旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153866_comment'></div>忠也欲报朝廷而不已，德也将流里闬而不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153866_comment'></div>于是出私俸，起官学，天子赐图籍，掾属制油素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153866_comment'></div>三齐怀笔，千里担簦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153866_comment'></div>鼓箧于朝，佔毕于夕，敩学在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153866_comment'></div>若夫明大道之本，观三千之奥，将欲佐人主，庇生民，经纬天地，制作礼乐，刬百代之弊，定一王之法者，可以谓之文矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153866_comment'></div>骋六艺之精，练当时之务，将欲对清閒之问，广漏刻之听，高议云台，以决安危，约史金匮，以定褒贬者，可以谓之学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153866_comment'></div>博贯百氏，并授五业，将欲藻润谟训，劝讲帷幄，主文以陈谏道，托寓以达下情，箴规庶官，粉泽时政者，可以谓之材矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153866_comment'></div>记问之师，句读之学，饰小辨，事空言，诮噪相高，篆刻自嘉，白首弗厎于道，盈编无益于世者，丞相耻之，予亦耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153866_comment'></div>东秦奥区，全齐盛府，俗渐邹鲁之教，人多海岱之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153866_comment'></div>朝家好文，辅臣善诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153866_comment'></div>而不能宝寸阴，刻素志，扶名教，训孝悌，建希世之策，敷及物之德，彼维师赐履于周，平津始封于汉，果何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153866_comment'></div>游于斯者，无自局焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153866_comment'></div>建学后三载，东土荐饥，予猥奉使指，谬踵前良，且以畴昔政司，陪贰台鼎，敢勒舆颂，以永德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153866_comment'></div>《诗》云：「君子能长育人材」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153866_comment'></div>《传》云：「得天下英材而教育之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153866_comment'></div>兹学之谓欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153866_comment'></div>堂皇之建，职次之设，皆备前记，此不复书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153866_comment'></div>时景祐元年正月朔日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1153866_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年1月13日</a>　正月十三日，在知青州任，上疏乞将本州举人定额外合格进士充填诸科阙额人数。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年8月2日</a>　八月二日，在知青州任，罢京东安抚使，进刑部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年8月</a>　八月，在知青州任，有表辞刑部尚书。作品：辞刑部尚书表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞刑部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153592")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153592'>臣某言：今月二十一日，三班借职张守珍到州，伏蒙圣慈赐臣敕牒、官诰各一道，特授臣刑部尚书，依旧知青州军州事，并赐诏书示谕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153592_comment'></div>当官无状，议赏误加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153592_comment'></div>载自裁循，交深震慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153592_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣本惟孤进，逮事先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153592_comment'></div>分圭组以虽多，绝涓尘之可录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153592_comment'></div>昨以东秦旧壤，仍岁阻饥，猥奉诏函，就分使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153592_comment'></div>既营救之无策，徒奔走以为劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153592_comment'></div>所赖天意照临，圣谟优假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153592_comment'></div>漕陕右之粟，西下于洪流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153592_comment'></div>汎淮甸之舟，东浮于沧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153592_comment'></div>出良缣于御府，祷嘉雨于灵祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153592_comment'></div>经费已充，丰润斯洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153592_comment'></div>至若赈恤贫窭，禁止寇攘，靡敢便宜，动皆奏列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153592_comment'></div>唯奉行于宸旨，用祗率于列城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153592_comment'></div>虽岁谷之遽登，每简书而是畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153592_comment'></div>岂期误宠，猥及无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153592_comment'></div>傥开多幸之涂，恐滋流竞之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153592_comment'></div>重念臣名品已峻，齿发甚疏，毗益无闻，满盈甚惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153592_comment'></div>岂可暂驱使领，便欲侥求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153592_comment'></div>贪朝廷之功，以为吏课；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153592_comment'></div>掠州郡之效，上冒主恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153592_comment'></div>何待人言，固当自讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153592_comment'></div>伏望尊位皇帝陛下俯哀旧物，深轸上仁，终始大恩，保全孤迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153592_comment'></div>听辍出纶之命，俾安据蒺之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153592_comment'></div>如此，则赏必及劳，有光于国体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153592_comment'></div>臣无虚授，免渎于朝经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153592_comment'></div>斯实至诚，固非文饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153592_comment'></div>言瞻白水，可誓丹衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153592_comment'></div>陨越战兢，期于得请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1153592_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年8月</a>　八月，在知青州任，有表谢授刑部尚书。作品：谢授刑部尚书表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1153593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授刑部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153593")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153593'>臣某言：今月二十六日，进奏院递到诏书一道赐臣，伏蒙圣慈以臣上表，蒙恩授刑部尚书，乞辍恩命，宜不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153593_comment'></div>宠章非次，成命不回，祗受以还，震惶无措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153593_comment'></div>伏念臣人品至下，天幸何多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153593_comment'></div>先皇初置谏科，臣独膺圣选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153593_comment'></div>陛下未离宫阁，臣首事龙潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153593_comment'></div>自以介拙无徒，孤寒多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153593_comment'></div>历职二十许任，效官三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153593_comment'></div>奔走四方，周旋二府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153593_comment'></div>入朝见嫉，固自古以难逃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153593_comment'></div>直道而行，信安身之不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153593_comment'></div>非先皇始终顾遇，难立于危踪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153593_comment'></div>非陛下特达保全，岂至于今日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153593_comment'></div>报国绝一毫之效，窃禄有五鼎之飧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153593_comment'></div>敢以无功，更当误赏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153593_comment'></div>每露章之至恳，终睿旨之靡俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153593_comment'></div>跪启诏封，交流愧汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153593_comment'></div>此盖伏遇体天法道仁明孝德皇帝陛下识臣面目，察臣肺膺，罔恤人言，动由宸断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153593_comment'></div>上则极至公之道，昭劝于勤劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153593_comment'></div>下则推求旧之仁，敦厚于风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153593_comment'></div>望九重而正远，恨万死以莫酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153593_comment'></div>敢不更励朴忠，俯安疲苶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153593_comment'></div>勉图来效，少答大恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1153593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　约于本年，在知青州任，奇重赵师民，乞回两子恩，授以京秩。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e02a935c3eb142eda5ccef1de17bd332_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e02a935c3eb142eda5ccef1de17bd332");'><span id='e02a935c3eb142eda5ccef1de17bd332_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1038')">1035-1038年</a>，51-54岁</div><div id='e02a935c3eb142eda5ccef1de17bd332' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　春，徙知应天府，兼南京留守，到任有谢表。作品：南京到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷五。系年季节据夏竦《狎鸥亭诗》（《文庄集》卷三六））</span><div id='poem_1153594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南京到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153594")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153594'>臣某言：祗荷宠私，伏增感惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153594_comment'></div>窃念臣孤寒多难，惷直无谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153594_comment'></div>顷事先朝，首依东禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153594_comment'></div>当内閤始开之日，识太阳初出之辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153594_comment'></div>抱椠和铅，皆真皇之密命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153594_comment'></div>解衣推食，尽陛下之深恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153594_comment'></div>式属重熙，仰缘前爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153594_comment'></div>猥蒙误宠，擢预近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153594_comment'></div>再贰枢衡，一陪台鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153594_comment'></div>粗守为臣之节，载倾许国之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153594_comment'></div>三侍禋燔，七周年籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153594_comment'></div>群情寡合，多咎其非才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153594_comment'></div>天鉴察微，独怜于守拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153594_comment'></div>获均劳逸，尽出保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153594_comment'></div>一昨海表荐饥，飞螟肆孽，猥分使指，宣布朝恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153594_comment'></div>上赖皇威，获清寇剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153594_comment'></div>道途至远，叹旅病以无医；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153594_comment'></div>岁月屡迁，望威颜而莫睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153594_comment'></div>方欲少须凉景，虔拜露章，求换郡于京西，冀遵途于阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153594_comment'></div>一对当阳之法坐，少陈东夏之远图，退就蕃宣，永藏顽鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153594_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇尊位皇帝陛下俯怜际遇，尚记姓名，遽锡诏函，俾司留府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153594_comment'></div>惟兹剧地，实首庶邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153594_comment'></div>佳气舂陵，夙比真人之里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153594_comment'></div>青云洛水，聿兴王者之都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153594_comment'></div>漕引江吴，控制淮海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153594_comment'></div>使驿系路，虽驷马之毕迎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153594_comment'></div>厨膳阙供，顾双鸡之不腆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153594_comment'></div>况臣筋骸疲薾，踪迹单危，惧速多言，上孤亲选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153594_comment'></div>愿察守株之拙，更宽如地之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153594_comment'></div>永誓糜捐，上酬覆露。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1153594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　春，徙知应天府，兼南京留守，到任有谢二府启。作品：南京到任谢二府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。系年季节据夏竦《狎鸥亭诗》（《文庄集》卷三六））</span><div id='poem_1153801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南京到任谢二府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153801")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153801'>仰承奖擢，伏积兢荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153801_comment'></div>窃念某本实庸人，妄干荣进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153801_comment'></div>早缘误宠，亦玷近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153801_comment'></div>上赖保全，获均劳逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153801_comment'></div>一昨东秦闵雨，下户将饥，猥奉诏函，就分使竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153801_comment'></div>殊昧敉宁之理，莫宽旰昃之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153801_comment'></div>事虽欲于防虞，言或多于过切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153801_comment'></div>当朝廷责实之际，固岩廊精汰之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153801_comment'></div>襆被自随，屏居是分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153801_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇某官俯矜旧物，深屈至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153801_comment'></div>仰赞恩章，俾釐留府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153801_comment'></div>典铜鱼之宫钥，合银兔之军符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153801_comment'></div>周微子之封圻，汉酂侯之寄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153801_comment'></div>载惟骞短，曷副坯陶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153801_comment'></div>惟更励于驽材，用少酬于元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153801_comment'></div>感惭刻著，倍百常钧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1153801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　春，在知应天府任，有诗上执政。作品：狎鸥亭诗（二首）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文庄集》卷三六。）</span><div id='poem_193275' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193275' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193275?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狎鸥亭诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_193275")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_193275_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_193275_0'>① 按：《湘山野录》卷上云：此为夏竦罢除相，知宋州到任后寄执政。诗中异文均出此。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193275'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193275'>元<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作造）</span>化平分荷大钧，左符新刻玉为<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>麟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193275'>南湖特地<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作不住）</span>栽桃李，拟伴沙鸥<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作禽）</span>过十春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193275'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_193275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_193275'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_193275_0'>⑴ 一作腰间新佩玉麒</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_193275_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_193274' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193274' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193274?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_193274_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193274'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193274'>海雁桥边绿<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作春）</span>水深，绝无尘土近<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作略无尘土到）</span>花阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193274_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193274'>忘机不管人知否，自有溪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作沙）</span>鸥信此心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193274_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193274'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_193274_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年6月</a>　六月，在知应天府任，奉诏撰《传法院碑铭》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年10月</a>　十月，在知应天府任，上《传法院碑铭》作品：传法院碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1153890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153890?labeling=true' target='_blank'>传法院碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153890")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153890_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153890'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153890'>太宗至仁应道神功圣德文武睿烈大明广孝皇帝，以太平兴国七年六月建传法院于太平兴国寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153890_comment'></div>今上体天法道仁明孝德皇帝，以景祐二年六月特诏史官追颂先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153890_comment'></div>史臣某拜手飏言曰：唐氏中微，五代多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153890_comment'></div>三辰昏祲，九服煨烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153890_comment'></div>虎争龙战，糜沸云扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153890_comment'></div>我国家题五精之期，起千岁之统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153890_comment'></div>祛天地之否隔，拯夷夏之涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153890_comment'></div>剪寇剧以靖摇乱，诛僭剧以遏横骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153890_comment'></div>太宗皇帝张天弧，顺斗极，驱除邻敌，驾驭髦杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153890_comment'></div>制礼乐于已坏，振文武于将坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153890_comment'></div>奉艺祖以造大业，由太弟以纂鸿绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153890_comment'></div>归马论道，投干讲艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153890_comment'></div>覆露所及，辙迹所到，罔不辟皇衢，刬霸轨，一文轸，齐量衡者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153890_comment'></div>洎乎六幕谧宁，中宸閒晏，披蠹简，访幽经，观天人之交，探神明之奥，补缀漏遗，讲求希阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153890_comment'></div>朝夕之议必稽于典册，小大之政咸本乎根柢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153890_comment'></div>尝谓佛法之至也，百王不易，历世弥盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153890_comment'></div>中原之区宇，绝域之种落，户讽其书，家图其像，一睇窣堵，一嗅薝卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153890_comment'></div>或因受以悟法，或睹相以趣善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153890_comment'></div>感照以应群动，广大以摄万有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153890_comment'></div>裨德教，省威戮，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153890_comment'></div>先朝乾德中监遣僧行勤等一百五十有七人，各赐装钱访经西域，今继有还者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153890_comment'></div>嗟其翻译之废，载祀二百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153890_comment'></div>非国家削平多垒，奄宅四海，通道夷貉，暨声葱雪，大事因缘，畴能复之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153890_comment'></div>会鄜畤守吏王龟从上中天竺印度僧法天、梵学比邱法进所译经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153890_comment'></div>又北天竺三藏天息灾与其受具母弟施护，各持梵夹来献，符帝雅意，天实启之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153890_comment'></div>乃遣内侍郑守钧肇营兹馆，赐息灾、法天等宣译，命光禄卿汤悦等润文，法进等笔受、缀文，义学苾刍慧达等證义，高品王文寿等监译。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153890_comment'></div>由是宪前轨，稽秘藏，依金刚界，扢种子坛，书字源，布圣位，三成藻饰，四事庄严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153890_comment'></div>三藏主译于坛北；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153890_comment'></div>梵僧證梵义、證梵文，义学僧證义，刊定华字于左右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153890_comment'></div>润文东南，以资笔削；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153890_comment'></div>监译西南，以肃仪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153890_comment'></div>新经既成，制跸临幸，赉物有品，诏赐金额，岁给飧钱一亿六十万，度僧十有一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153890_comment'></div>翻译之制，大备于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153890_comment'></div>御制《三藏圣教序》以冠经首，息灾赐名法贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153890_comment'></div>又诏择京寺童子得惟净等五十人，令肄梵学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153890_comment'></div>每大电纪辰，贝多启译，经成奏御，召对赐坐，进见甚宠，观者荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153890_comment'></div>真庙绍文，鸿徽累盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153890_comment'></div>舞羽而清河右，再驾而羁幕北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153890_comment'></div>銮旗驻于兹馆，篚币班于法席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153890_comment'></div>洎乎勒圜，封禅梁阯，上仪交举，盛节咸备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153890_comment'></div>拥九清之嘉祐，访三空之真谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153890_comment'></div>祗适先训，布昭睿藻，作《圣教序》以赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153890_comment'></div>又诏参知政事赵安仁等，并所降制诏，赐名《大中祥符法宝录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153890_comment'></div>复以宰臣丁谓、王钦若充使，以宠重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153890_comment'></div>圣上慎徽祖服，光启宗范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153890_comment'></div>长养容覆，极两仪之大德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153890_comment'></div>睿哲广运，总列辟之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153890_comment'></div>尽美乎万几，宣精乎三教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153890_comment'></div>悟然灯之授记，当弥勒之嘱累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153890_comment'></div>以无上之知觉，建大中之教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153890_comment'></div>述《三宝赞》，以冠藏录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153890_comment'></div>众圣欢蹈，群生依怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153890_comment'></div>雨花芬都，金光照烂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153890_comment'></div>恩深归救之本，理极名言之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153890_comment'></div>无量功德，非思议之可及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153890_comment'></div>自兴国壬午距今乙亥五十四载，宠灵积累，妙因殊胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153890_comment'></div>有若今右仆射、同中书门下平章事吕夷简以师臣上衮，博达空理，奉制兼使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153890_comment'></div>今参知政事、尚书吏部侍郎宋绶以宏材硕德，了悟真际，被诏润文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153890_comment'></div>有若故枢密使、同中书门下平章事王曙、参知政事张洎、赵安仁、枢密副使杨砺、翰林学士承旨晁迥、李维、翰林学士朱昂、梁周翰、杨亿，皆以学通儒释，继司译润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153890_comment'></div>上哲清流，尽在兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153890_comment'></div>翻宣表率，则有三藏五人，皆赐朝散阶，累迁试光禄卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153890_comment'></div>始法贤，次法天，次施护，并刹帝利氏，深穷秘密，博通华竺，功成顺化，恤礼尤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153890_comment'></div>又次法护，北天竺憍尸迦氏，始隶毗尼，聿修禅诵，先朝以其至自西遐，该明法要，令嗣译度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153890_comment'></div>次曰惟净，故吴王李煜之犹子，七岁依师，选习梵业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153890_comment'></div>真皇以其不游西度，精晓贝文，特命主译。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153890_comment'></div>天圣中法护请还身毒，惟净求往阙塞，累表不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153890_comment'></div>今皆际会昌期，宣隆教典者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153890_comment'></div>其监译内侍则自文寿至今内藏库内常侍陈文一、御药院入主供奉官阎士良、印经院入内高品朱若水，十有七人，皆简擢恭恪，以干院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153890_comment'></div>其笔受、缀文、證义等僧，则自法进至今文一、法凝、鉴深、慧涛、潜政、清漏、善初、义崇、慧素、存行，及梵学僧文涉、道隆、慧灯、七十有九人，皆妙择行业，以塞朝选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153890_comment'></div>其贡经，五印度僧则自法军至法称八十人，取经还华僧，则自辞潮至栖秘一百三十有八人，皆克遂至愿，赞此大缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153890_comment'></div>宠赉之数，咸有差次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153890_comment'></div>其贡献并内出梵经无虑一千四百二十八夹，秘之院阁，译成经论凡五百六十四卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153890_comment'></div>续于藏室娑婆之界，以语言文字作佛事，原本缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153890_comment'></div>体貌丞相，宠数尊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153890_comment'></div>其诞辰翻译，瑞场启罢，并命两府衡弼传香赐会，著为永式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153890_comment'></div>夷简等进诗称谢，有诏刊石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153890_comment'></div>译馆之荣，于斯为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153890_comment'></div>说者云：译者释也，交释华梵，对传句读，办祛楼之笔，简韦陀之辞，本政因以建之，糅杂句以文之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153890_comment'></div>广阴入之津梁，续痴冥之灯炬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153890_comment'></div>宣我象教，功孰大焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153890_comment'></div>然而拟于法者空，几于真者静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153890_comment'></div>染空尚垢，知静犹障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153890_comment'></div>若夫遗照觉，度禅定，应现无方，圆明具足者，岂有髣髴于其间也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153890_comment'></div>但以千觉度人，始自言语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153890_comment'></div>八藏垂教，必假文翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153890_comment'></div>双林示寂，鹫岭罢谈，五百年中，皆称正法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153890_comment'></div>三十四字，广衍右行，充溢诸天，靡迤东土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153890_comment'></div>非传释无以达华夏，舍润色无以足言志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153890_comment'></div>凿五蕴之牖，破三毒之网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153890_comment'></div>塞颠倒之涂，决苦恼之海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153890_comment'></div>俾众生竭爱流，灌毁宅，味甘露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153890_comment'></div>以清凉大士悟始觉證，法身护神，通而游戏，其六度之本源乎，万行之因地乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153890_comment'></div>宜固谛方言，练横字，审缘起，正思惟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153890_comment'></div>贯穿宗极，以了密义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153890_comment'></div>涉猎苍雅，以定华文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153890_comment'></div>备而不繁，直而不略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153890_comment'></div>诃四病之微细，拂二见之邪执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153890_comment'></div>洒之海墨，则诸佛下观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153890_comment'></div>咏以潮音，则百灵潜听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153890_comment'></div>使广劫之下，知朝家崇建之美，叹圣上尊向之仁，不其伟欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153890_comment'></div>臣早游史阁，尝预译场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153890_comment'></div>终以钝根，求补外职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153890_comment'></div>地如亭历，有生之累犹多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153890_comment'></div>笔若须弥，众妙之门难尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153890_comment'></div>上勤哀旧物，俾图懿铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153890_comment'></div>谨奉宸旨，靡敢固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153890_comment'></div>议者以为圣上之建斯铭也，昭贻厥之谋，周文之追孝也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153890_comment'></div>尚记事之美，陶唐之有文也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153890_comment'></div>光大度门，能仁之悲心也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153890_comment'></div>守护正法，有帝之鸿誓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153890_comment'></div>宣是四美，垂厥无穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153890_comment'></div>龙天降格，神祇叹誉，永锡百禄，大庇中区，皇哉焕乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153890_comment'></div>谨为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_112_1153890'>西方圣人，万化幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153890_comment'></div>兆启于周，法至于汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153890_comment'></div>森沉天禄，古经肇焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153890_comment'></div>䆗窱甘泉，金人耸观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153890_comment'></div>机缘合应，梦寤通灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153890_comment'></div>腾兰东入，愔景西迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153890_comment'></div>氎像可传，绘事初形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153890_comment'></div>具偈难解，译法肇兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153890_comment'></div>魏晋洎唐，正闰十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153890_comment'></div>变梵成华，翻传代有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153890_comment'></div>篆隶兼该，典坟旁究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153890_comment'></div>八备咸精，三难尽剖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153890_comment'></div>贞元以降，国步多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153890_comment'></div>戎笳沸路，盗戟横关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153890_comment'></div>悉昙罔学，雷岭谁攀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1153890_comment'></div>法器几堕，慧命将殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1153890_comment'></div>明明上穹，启我有宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1153890_comment'></div>尽殛残暴，并苏愁痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1153890_comment'></div>神武拓迹，圣人垂统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1153890_comment'></div>四貉同文，五天𠨿贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1153890_comment'></div>皇灵有赫，法宝增光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1153890_comment'></div>精庐再考，译席重张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1153890_comment'></div>半满交显，疑伪兼详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1153890_comment'></div>六义垂范，万颂裁章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1153890_comment'></div>竺典岁臻，华经日续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1153890_comment'></div>液金贲字，彫琼丽轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1153890_comment'></div>思文祖祢，尊善导俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1153890_comment'></div>克昌厥后，介尔景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1153890_comment'></div>皇帝孝思，对越无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1153890_comment'></div>碑颂休烈，载刊金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1153890_comment'></div>铺昭上乘，博济含识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1153890_comment'></div>惟皇寿考，时万时亿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_143_1153890_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　本年，在知应天府任，作《颍州莲华漏铭》作品：颍州莲华漏铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1153874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍州莲华漏铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153874")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153874'>夫迎日推策，帝鸿之宪天也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153874_comment'></div>治历明时，成汤之应人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153874_comment'></div>日月有发敛，昼夜有增减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153874_comment'></div>非在璿不能测盈缩，非运仪不能定昏明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153874_comment'></div>以是历数起焉，漏刻生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153874_comment'></div>昼参乎晷景，夜验乎次舍，虽上天之运，不能逃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153874_comment'></div>舜史日永星火者，昼漏多也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153874_comment'></div>日短星昴者，昼漏少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153874_comment'></div>《周官》有以火爨鼎之制，齐诗有折柳樊圃之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153874_comment'></div>由是观之，挈壸之设，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153874_comment'></div>汉承周秦，图籍最备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153874_comment'></div>其令甲第六著常符漏品、二十四气，各为二箭，刻日所在，并黄道去极、晷景刻数、昏明中星于其下，班之计吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153874_comment'></div>自兹厥后，踵事增华，逮施于李兰，始变古法，权器程水，以准时刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153874_comment'></div>唐之诸道，率循此制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153874_comment'></div>至今器有存者而莫能施用，唯司天官漏迄今用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153874_comment'></div>参以中星，因时升降，而置箭之制，世不复传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153874_comment'></div>上躬至圣之姿，极攸纵之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153874_comment'></div>稽古典学，励精百度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153874_comment'></div>讨论希阔，讲求礼术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153874_comment'></div>天圣中，有今龙图阁直学士给事中燕君肃，始考七经载籍，作莲华漏于梓潼，来献阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153874_comment'></div>其制为四分之壸，参差置水器于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153874_comment'></div>剡木为四分之箭，箭四觚，面二十五刻，刻六十分，四面百刻，总六千分，以效日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153874_comment'></div>凡四十八箭，一气一易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153874_comment'></div>铸金莲承箭，铜乌引水下注，金莲浮箭而上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153874_comment'></div>有司唯谨视而易之，为行漏之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153874_comment'></div>又依《周官》水地置臬之法，考二交之景，得午时四刻一十分为五正，南北景中以起漏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153874_comment'></div>时予备职枢府，弗获熟视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153874_comment'></div>君未几作藩青社，建兹漏于白楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153874_comment'></div>予出守汝阴，亟往代君，因得细睹其制，精妙参神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153874_comment'></div>景祐中，君复厌承明，求刺于颍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153874_comment'></div>予亦内徙睢阳，封圻接畛，庆问时通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153874_comment'></div>因请更为颍漏，以广其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153874_comment'></div>君由是再考晷度，以梓潼在南，比古法昼增一刻，夜损一刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153874_comment'></div>青社稍北，昼增三刻，夜损三刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153874_comment'></div>颍处梓青之间，昼增二刻，夜损亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153874_comment'></div>仍作屋秘漏，得天愈密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153874_comment'></div>予旧隶史局，粗亲此学，以为乾体左旋，七曜运舍，皆动物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153874_comment'></div>赤道横带，黄道斜截，复有进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153874_comment'></div>夫物动而有进退者，势久必差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153874_comment'></div>故昔贤制术，以天度乘昼夜漏，减三百而一为定度，以减天度以为明，加正度以为昏，所以追晷景之实，防节气之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153874_comment'></div>然三百岁斗历改宪而异人出焉，今燕君其当之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153874_comment'></div>夫六艺群书，唯天文数术探赜索隐，钩深致远，最为难明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153874_comment'></div>若心所不达，虽通人前识讵测其方？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153874_comment'></div>而世之俗儒或以为非荐绅先生之所称道，何其误欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153874_comment'></div>仲尼作《春秋》，每于朔闰发文以宣明历数，此圣人之深意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153874_comment'></div>《书》不云乎：「敬授人时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153874_comment'></div>《礼》不云乎：「百度得数而有常」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153874_comment'></div>后之观者，幸无忽焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153874_comment'></div>其《漏志》一篇亦刊诸左方，期于不朽云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153874_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1153874'>极星建中，黄道营外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153874_comment'></div>度有迩遐，时有明晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153874_comment'></div>圣人观象，古史诒则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153874_comment'></div>孔壸为漏，浮箭为刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153874_comment'></div>资始巧历，稽合小馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153874_comment'></div>重黎是司，羲和是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153874_comment'></div>秦氏遗法，汉京垂制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153874_comment'></div>历世弥文，旧规加丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153874_comment'></div>玉虬吐水，分灌两壸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153874_comment'></div>金龙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1153874", 1153874, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>转注</span>，下激衡渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153874_comment'></div>天道可观，神化无迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153874_comment'></div>日运波澄，气分箭易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153874_comment'></div>□□□□，都邑屡迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153874_comment'></div>寂寥罔诏，世失其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153874_comment'></div>猗嗟燕君，文学馀力，博贯旧章，肇新景式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153874_comment'></div>象魏既登，潼川既营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153874_comment'></div>建于青闉，作于颍庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153874_comment'></div>五夜持宵，三商定夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153874_comment'></div>杪忽无差，升降靡息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153874_comment'></div>意侔造化，数穷天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153874_comment'></div>茫茫有生，孰参其知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153874_comment'></div>于铄圣宋，世祚无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153874_comment'></div>刊此乐石，永宪万方。</div><div id='poem_sentence_71_1153874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年4月</a>　四月，在知应天府任，与杜衍荐嵇颖试于学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年10月</a>　十月，在知应天府任，作《海雁桥记》<div id='poem_1153867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海雁桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153867")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153867'>顷岁山东旱蝗，予被诏敉宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153867_comment'></div>下穆陵，并潍水，出莱阳，辙黄腄，野无蔬茹，市无血膋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153867_comment'></div>有客馈海雁六，弗忍为膳，育于青州之柳亭，亡其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153867_comment'></div>后数载，予内徙睢阳，辇五雁纵之南湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153867_comment'></div>一夕，旧客过都，知之，抚掌桥侧，五雁悲鸣飞集，围绕膝下，至暮恋恋不能去，观者为之出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153867_comment'></div>斯禽受人之恩，不过稻粱养育岁时耳，尚数年而不忘其主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153867_comment'></div>前史有委质事君，高轩列鼎，而不能尽心于王室者，殊可嗟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153867_comment'></div>《国风》美《关雎》之不淫，嘉《鸤鸠》之均一，盖有资于王化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153867_comment'></div>因题是桥为海雁桥以旌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153867_comment'></div>时景祐三年十月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1153867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年2月1日</a>　二月一日，在知应天府任，作《楞严经序》<div id='poem_1153833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楞严经序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153833")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153833'>夫善言佛者，惟性而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153833_comment'></div>混成不测，况之道乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153833_comment'></div>无方善应，况之神乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153833_comment'></div>湛寂精常，圆满平等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153833_comment'></div>迎之不见其首，随之不见其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153833_comment'></div>生生而不生，化化而不化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153833_comment'></div>包裹万有，含吐十方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153833_comment'></div>资始众缘，具足万行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153833_comment'></div>光明密照而非色，灵通潜运而非空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153833_comment'></div>世界变迁而不移，山岳旋偃而常静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153833_comment'></div>现前而惑者不辨，日用而迷者不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153833_comment'></div>《易》曰：「寂然不动，感而遂通」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153833_comment'></div>老氏曰：「独立而不改，周行而不殆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153833_comment'></div>其性之谓欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153833_comment'></div>无始劫来，一切众生，攀缘外境，忘失本心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153833_comment'></div>分为四缠，叠为五浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153833_comment'></div>驰而为妄想，结而为昏翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153833_comment'></div>聚而为烦恼，流而为生死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153833_comment'></div>累我真源，枉入诸趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153833_comment'></div>如来哀之，此《楞严》之所以作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153833_comment'></div>以众生苦于奔逸，故为之行三观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153833_comment'></div>滞于色相，故为之指八还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153833_comment'></div>误认尘根，故为之辩六入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153833_comment'></div>妄计因缘，故为之谈七大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153833_comment'></div>至于屈伸金臂，绾叠华巾，极善巧之喻，拂微细之惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153833_comment'></div>令瞻宝光者，知见精之不摇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153833_comment'></div>听钟音者，悟闻性之常在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153833_comment'></div>若乃本明旋复，静慧发生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153833_comment'></div>御最上之宝乘，游无边之性海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153833_comment'></div>顾色身若微尘，视太虚如云点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153833_comment'></div>彼无始轮转之根，亿劫颠倒之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153833_comment'></div>我人妄执寿命，浮想若炽炭之燎鸿毛，烈日之晞朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153833_comment'></div>不待思惟，已自消释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153833_comment'></div>大哉，菩提妙圆，本始清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153833_comment'></div>既无妄幻翳于真精，岂有身心受彼生死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153833_comment'></div>水澄滓去，漏尽法除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153833_comment'></div>万行不脩而自圆，六通不求而自澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153833_comment'></div>预于此者非至神乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153833_comment'></div>然而是经撮八藏之精要，穷万化之根源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153833_comment'></div>译之者务简，润之者尚辞，或使潭研泥于句读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153833_comment'></div>故有僧可度为之笺分，详略有叙，华梵兼该。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153833_comment'></div>迨岁再周，能事方毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153833_comment'></div>后之观者应当返梦想之缘气，遗心目之习因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153833_comment'></div>了识精之元，还独妙之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153833_comment'></div>云驶月运，既息于诸旋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153833_comment'></div>木尽灰飞，亦忘于幻法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153833_comment'></div>秋毫不立，真理自冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153833_comment'></div>彼求诸佛无漏胜解者，幸精进于斯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153833_comment'></div>时景祐四年二月朔日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1153833_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年8月1日</a>　八月一日，在知应天府任，作《青州龙兴寺重修中佛殿记》<div id='poem_1153868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青州龙兴寺重修中佛殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153868")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153868'>左海濒，右岱畎，沂蒙亘其南，河济径其北，厥壤广衍，惟青州焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153868_comment'></div>唐以卢水平地，置平卢军，其城萦带山岳，控引川渎，气候高爽，风物楙盛，雅俗杂处，脩涂四达，富焉庶焉，东夏之都会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153868_comment'></div>中有佛图，实曰龙兴寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153868_comment'></div>旧以为田文之第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153868_comment'></div>地势斗绝，堀殁洋水之阴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153868_comment'></div>楼观飞注，翱翔重闉之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153868_comment'></div>东践绝涧，径度于阛阓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153868_comment'></div>西瞰群峰，旁属乎原野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153868_comment'></div>十二之胜，尽于兹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153868_comment'></div>寺中有殿，宋元嘉二年建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153868_comment'></div>甲子十周，楝宇隳圯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153868_comment'></div>常坐比丘昼枢，化青人，得镪三百万以新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153868_comment'></div>又锢以石阶，缭以髹槛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153868_comment'></div>后增二亭，左以荫铭识，右以藏鼓格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153868_comment'></div>世传孟尝饭客，以鼓为节，其格存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153868_comment'></div>载祀寖久，木石刓脱，但上画飞仙，殆非当时器，而寺僧宝之，以传疑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153868_comment'></div>或曰：「佛何为者邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153868_comment'></div>夫太始既分，皇衢既远，舜禹揖逊，汤武干戈，自朴而雕，自淳而漓，奸宄锋起，智诈火驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153868_comment'></div>是以天生圣人于叔世，分三教以救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153868_comment'></div>九州之载，人性淑均，道德可以化焉，礼乐可以教焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153868_comment'></div>故商武丁时生老聃于濑乡，周灵王时生仲尼于昌平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153868_comment'></div>流沙之外，西戎即叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153868_comment'></div>非威神摄受，权实开遮，莫能变犷悍，胜残虐，故昭王时生佛于毗岚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153868_comment'></div>然今古之论，罔不折衷于仲尼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153868_comment'></div>昔夫子自谓则曰：「文王既没，文不在兹乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153868_comment'></div>于老氏则曰：「其犹龙邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153868_comment'></div>于佛则曰：「西方之人，有圣者焉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153868_comment'></div>以是论之，则释老皆圣人之救世者也，夫子不之讥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153868_comment'></div>或曰：「枢之新是殿，有功德邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153868_comment'></div>夫天地者，烦恼之燬宅也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153868_comment'></div>世界者，生死之业流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153868_comment'></div>人之生也，与爱俱生，忸忕乎名利，盖缠者嗜欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153868_comment'></div>鸟惊兽骇，驰走乎烈焰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153868_comment'></div>龟沉鱼跃，出没乎惊波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153868_comment'></div>翳元明而不知，甘众苦而不恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153868_comment'></div>忮忌而得者谓之能，放肆而前者谓之达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153868_comment'></div>其生也与梦寐等，其死也与粪壤俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153868_comment'></div>圣人哀之，故为之御三乘之轮，𫇢六度之航，以接痴冥，以拯昏溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153868_comment'></div>后之登是殿者，若睹相好以摄心，叹宝严而起信，固可以远谢尘垢，坐空妄幻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153868_comment'></div>若瞻白毫之光，悟见精之不动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153868_comment'></div>听宝铎之音，觉闻性之常寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153868_comment'></div>固可以返照真际，旋复本初，證菩提心，成无上道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153868_comment'></div>由是观之，则枢之于兹殿，有无量功德矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153868_comment'></div>予尝守兹境，目枢之勤，聊纪胜因以刊石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153868_comment'></div>时景祐四年八月朔日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1153868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年3月1日</a>　三月一日，在知应天府任，以户部尚书入为三司使，有谢表。作品：谢授三司使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢受三司使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153597")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153597'>臣某言：伏奉制命，特授臣依前行户部尚书、充三司使、加食邑五百户、食实封贰百户，散官勋如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153597_comment'></div>宠章非次，衍食有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153597_comment'></div>载省愚冥，实难堪克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153597_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153597_comment'></div>伏念臣本由孤进，仰会先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153597_comment'></div>掌右掖之赞书，奉西清之密议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153597_comment'></div>真宗皇帝以臣父没身报国，最为忠义之家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153597_comment'></div>以臣制策登科，粗识古今之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153597_comment'></div>察臣持循少过，知臣忧畏小心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153597_comment'></div>当陛下潜跃之初，首东朝陪侍之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153597_comment'></div>解衣推食，最承逮下之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153597_comment'></div>抱椠和铅，日奉重晖之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153597_comment'></div>适属先皇违豫，邪党擅权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153597_comment'></div>六改郡符，十更年籥，但尽心于民政，已绝望于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153597_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下出震承祧，大明继照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153597_comment'></div>猥思旧物，远锡飞毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153597_comment'></div>出自宸衷，擢阶近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153597_comment'></div>当母后临朝之际，是权臣恶直之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153597_comment'></div>更互留身，婉转腾谤，以漂山之巨力，害如线之寒踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153597_comment'></div>非仰赖于保全，已坐成于糜碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153597_comment'></div>又念全齐旧壤，连岁荐饥，贼盗纵横，公私困竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153597_comment'></div>巨猥分使指，躬按海壖，昼夜兼行，须鬓皓白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153597_comment'></div>未容殚于薄效，已先著于流言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153597_comment'></div>此际若非陛下断自不疑，察其非实，力垂明辨，几至倾危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153597_comment'></div>以兹重叠之恩，未申分寸之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153597_comment'></div>旋玷南都之寄，式当万国之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153597_comment'></div>水陆往还，是非薮泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153597_comment'></div>上酬厚禄，唯竭节于公家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153597_comment'></div>曾忤柄臣，已灰心于荣路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153597_comment'></div>止期退伏，远避猜嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153597_comment'></div>岂谓陛下深恻上仁，力排群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153597_comment'></div>念臣孤寒多难，察臣介直无徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153597_comment'></div>简自圣衷，擢司邦计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153597_comment'></div>破朝端之旧党，极天下之至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153597_comment'></div>祗受以还，感极以泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153597_comment'></div>惟当恭勤夙夜，策励疲驽，直剖肺肝，少裨听览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153597_comment'></div>誓毕桑榆之景，仰酬天地之仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1153597_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='265f41050f534eab89c7a7db04e721fd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("265f41050f534eab89c7a7db04e721fd");'><span id='265f41050f534eab89c7a7db04e721fd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>，55岁</div><div id='265f41050f534eab89c7a7db04e721fd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年1月24日</a>　正月二十四日，到知永兴军任，有谢表。作品：永兴谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永兴谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年1月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153598")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153598'>臣某言：伏奉制命，特授臣奉宁军节度使、知永兴军府事、驻泊马步军都总管、泾原秦凤路安抚使，已于今月二十四日于本府上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153598_comment'></div>斋坛授受，拜丽泽以惟优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153598_comment'></div>外阃临戎，望严宸而乍远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153598_comment'></div>寄付尤重，感惧增深<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153598_comment'></div>伏念臣出自孤生，误登制举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153598_comment'></div>既踰弱冠，亟掌训词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153598_comment'></div>抱椠和铅，首预东朝之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153598_comment'></div>解衣推食，独承先帝之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153598_comment'></div>但以赋性至愚，立身多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153598_comment'></div>权臣共恶，众口争非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153598_comment'></div>自揣单危，分甘捐弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153598_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下睿明继体，仁悯象天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153598_comment'></div>轸黄屋之非心，记青宫之旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153598_comment'></div>擢参台鼎，再贰枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153598_comment'></div>耻巧宦以依人，惟朴忠而自竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153598_comment'></div>仰蒙圣庇，获守近藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153598_comment'></div>旋以东夏抚宁，南郡居守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153598_comment'></div>三腰郡组，六换年华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153598_comment'></div>每怀襆被之行，敢有赐环之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153598_comment'></div>岂谓陛下力排舆议，召委计司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153598_comment'></div>爰当视事之初，便主摘山之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153598_comment'></div>群情向背，密疏纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153598_comment'></div>非上赖于辨明，已立成于祸患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153598_comment'></div>寻以禋燔下诏，赏赉均恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153598_comment'></div>为国尽忠，虽明神之可谅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153598_comment'></div>入朝见嫉，鉴前世以堪惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153598_comment'></div>尝因赐对之间，曾沥由衷之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153598_comment'></div>候终考秩，傥议迁除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153598_comment'></div>只祈都省之便安，或预译场之润色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153598_comment'></div>庶未从乎外补，得时望于迩颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153598_comment'></div>况臣自忝三司，始踰八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153598_comment'></div>惟自勤于本局，敢辄预于朝经？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153598_comment'></div>实无片言，偶侵上位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153598_comment'></div>矧伤弓之最甚，惟敛翼之是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153598_comment'></div>岂意羌戎，妄为狂孽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153598_comment'></div>不期公论，误及非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153598_comment'></div>遽由端右之资，擢授元戎之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153598_comment'></div>臣出于将种，粗读兵钤，誓竭素心，仰酬异遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153598_comment'></div>其如边防务重，京阙路遥，动繄帷幄之指踪，方遂藩篱之固圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153598_comment'></div>敢祈睿哲，更赐主张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153598_comment'></div>俾成横草之功，免累知臣之德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1153598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年1月24日</a>　正月二十四日，到知永兴军任，有谢二府启。作品：永兴谢二府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永兴谢二府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年1月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153802")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153802'>自出坯陶，伏深感恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153802_comment'></div>窃念某人品驽下，世胄孤平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153802_comment'></div>继典九城，荐更三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153802_comment'></div>无一毫之可录，怅十驾之空劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153802_comment'></div>向者召自别都，俾司会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153802_comment'></div>服勤徒切，析利非精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153802_comment'></div>矧从视事之辰，便主摘山之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153802_comment'></div>逮成奏格，几汗简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153802_comment'></div>爰以细札垂文，阳郊错事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153802_comment'></div>泰坛备物，方畏瘝官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153802_comment'></div>斋幄还衡，甫宁悸魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153802_comment'></div>摄须稍逸，垂翅将安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153802_comment'></div>弥仰恃于哀矜，冀且参于下吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153802_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇某官，因陪漏刻，误忆姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153802_comment'></div>议四鄙之羽书，按东曹之边琐，拔于端右，付以戎昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153802_comment'></div>六纛启行，光华籍甚，万钱赋禄，訾计差温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153802_comment'></div>中外诮其何功，文武讥其不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153802_comment'></div>载惟求旧，深累至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153802_comment'></div>敢不更励忠规，上酬元化？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153802_comment'></div>灭烽未日，既耻于家为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153802_comment'></div>数级有时，或期于天幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153802_comment'></div>指玉关而非远，瞻铉府以方遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153802_comment'></div>愧荷依投，万倍伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1153802_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年6月</a>　六月，在知永兴军任，受诏上疏议西鄙事。作品：陈边事十策。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1153715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈边事十策</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153715")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153715'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153715'>今月八日，陕西安抚使、天章阁待制庞籍等到府，奉传圣旨，商量西鄙事宜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153715_comment'></div>窃以继迁一族，本党项遗类，居呼韩旧地，东薄银夏，西至灵盐，南趣鄜延，北抵丰会，迤逦平下，辐员千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153715_comment'></div>太平兴国中，继迁逃背，鸠集万骑，屡寇朔方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153715_comment'></div>岁发兵夫，送粮草，每邀险肆掠，为害不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153715_comment'></div>至道初，特遣洛苑使白守荣等率重兵护粮四十馀万，遇寇浦洛河，兵夫溃走，自相蹂籍，粮卒并没，守荣等仅以身免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153715_comment'></div>朝廷旰食，关辅骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153715_comment'></div>太宗皇帝召宰相议之，吕端始欲发卒由麟、府，丹、鄜、延，环庆三路趣平夏，袭其巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153715_comment'></div>太宗难之，且曰：「三道深入，用甲卒几万，何人为将帅，何人护辎重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153715_comment'></div>表里砂碛，何处会合？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153715_comment'></div>须更熟筹，不可轻举」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153715_comment'></div>是时边患方深，议者不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153715_comment'></div>至秋，遂命李继隆出环州，丁罕出庆州，范廷召出延州，王超出夏州，张守恩出麟州，五路趣平夏，竭内帑之国财，罄关中之民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153715_comment'></div>继隆与丁罕合行十数日，不见贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153715_comment'></div>张守恩见贼不击，相继引还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153715_comment'></div>王超、范廷召至乌白池，以诸将失期、士卒困乏而回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153715_comment'></div>此际先臣隶于廷召，备见轻举之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153715_comment'></div>然是时继迁当兄继捧入朝之后，为曹光实掩袭之馀，遁逃之迹，穷蹙可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153715_comment'></div>凉州博啰齐、沙州曹延禄皆受朝廷节度，使掎角追讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153715_comment'></div>灵州河外大凉、小凉，河西北藏擦勒等数十蕃族皆有雠怨，愿助国讨除，尚犹累岁积年，不能扑灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153715_comment'></div>太宗又问宰臣曰：「卿等莫别有擘画」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153715_comment'></div>当时宰相但错愕，莫之能对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153715_comment'></div>太宗亦不悦久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153715_comment'></div>先皇帝即位，鉴追讨之弊，悯关辅之劳，惟戒疆吏谨烽堠，严卒乘，来即驱逐去，勿追捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153715_comment'></div>尝出陕西地图，自指山川堡塞示宰臣，令移兵简费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153715_comment'></div>又以泾原地最要害，屯兵甚众，命增置钤辖、都监，以备奔轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153715_comment'></div>此实先帝之圣断远图也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153715_comment'></div>然拓跋之境，自灵武陷没之后，银、绥割弃以来，假朝廷威灵，聚中原禄赐，略有河外，役属小蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153715_comment'></div>德明、元昊久相继袭，贸易华戎，捃剥财用，拓地千馀里，积货数十年，较之继迁，势已相万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153715_comment'></div>其于妄作名器，僭制车舆，誇咤旃庐，跳梁沙幕，亦有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153715_comment'></div>朝廷待以遐荒，置而不问，刍豢过饱，猖蹶遽彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153715_comment'></div>所宜诛夷，以塞公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153715_comment'></div>然而兵者凶器，战者危事，圣人不得已而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153715_comment'></div>自昔兵家皆欲先胜后战，则举无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153715_comment'></div>以继迁穷蹙，比元昊富实，势可知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153715_comment'></div>以先朝累胜之士，较当今关东之兵，勇怯可知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153715_comment'></div>以兴国习战之帅，方沿边未试之将，工拙可知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153715_comment'></div>继迁逃伏平夏，元昊窟穴河外，地势可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153715_comment'></div>若分兵深入，则军行三十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153715_comment'></div>自赍粮糗，则不能支久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153715_comment'></div>须载刍粟，则难于援送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153715_comment'></div>师行贼境，利于速战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153715_comment'></div>傥进则贼避其锋，退则敌蹑其后，昼设奇伏，夜挠营栅，师老粮少，深可虞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153715_comment'></div>若穷其巢穴，须渡大河，既无长舟巨舰，则须浮囊挽绠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153715_comment'></div>茍贼列寨河上，以逸待劳，我师半渡，左右夹攻，未知何谋可以捍御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153715_comment'></div>臣以为不较主客之利，不计攻守之便，议追讨者是谓无策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153715_comment'></div>若缮完壁垒，修利器械，约束将佐，控扼险隘，但辄过于岁月，不豫计于胜负，是今之常制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153715_comment'></div>则虑体分势异，众力不齐，旷日持久，军食难继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153715_comment'></div>事不先定，则有后忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153715_comment'></div>若威以文诰，格以干羽，胜决帷幄，师行衽席，必有成算，系于前筹，此非臣之所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153715_comment'></div>臣今但有十策十事列上如左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1153715'>一、今之关塞，延安险阻，秦州地远，易为控扼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153715_comment'></div>所最忧者泾原，次则环庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1153715_comment'></div>泾原莫急于镇戎，环庆莫急于庆州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1153715_comment'></div>戎人狡猾，必不肯舍平易而趣险阻，此敌情之易料也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1153715_comment'></div>古之用兵，皆择其精锐，先当矢石，谓之握奇跳荡，是为奇兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1153715_comment'></div>其次疲软，则以守城壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1153715_comment'></div>近年之弊，强弱兼用，强为弱累，战多无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1153715_comment'></div>又中国长技，莫先强弩，近年之弊，参以他兵，不能专用己长，攻彼之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1153715_comment'></div>今若令泾原、环庆两路各于土兵、禁兵或弓箭手内择弓刀枪槊手三二千副之，泾原令高继嵩、张亢主之，环庆令刘平、赵振主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1153715_comment'></div>日夕训练，常如寇至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1153715_comment'></div>如有警急，则令自泾原界望环庆路横绝边徼，数百里间往来交击，互为首尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1153715_comment'></div>傅矢持满，俟中而发，一发万矢，三得一中，则十发之矢，以殪三万馀人，羌戎毡毳，不易支也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1153715_comment'></div>仍乞立为强弩指挥，特升兵额，稍增月给，以震军声，以壮士心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1153715_comment'></div>但恐贼界闻有此谋，必不敢容易窥塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1153715_comment'></div>其偏裨将校，道路堡塞，并委刘平等临时选择处当，此实制胜之大端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1153715'>二、缘边熟户，号为蕃篱，除延州李金明、胡继谔二族与贼世雠，受国厚恩，势必向汉，自馀熟户如二族者十无一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1153715_comment'></div>羌戎之性，贪利畏威，若不结以恩信，惮以威武，而欲仓卒驱之御敌，汉强则助汉，贼盛则助贼必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1153715_comment'></div>其敏珠尔等蕃族又纳质贼境，居既首鼠，战必倒戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1153715_comment'></div>元昊窥见此隙，所以勾招打敌，胁以锋镝，诱以货财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1153715_comment'></div>国家非不知其若此，所宜速见良画，深破贼计，及早羁束，以固藩篱，此西陲之急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1153715_comment'></div>臣前后累状陈启，未蒙开可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1153715_comment'></div>伏乞采臣前奏下臣，令勘会逐州部族首领，量人马事力，授以职名，第给禄赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1153715_comment'></div>蕃官俸料至微，所费不厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1153715_comment'></div>若控制有宜，得其死力，则为利至大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1153715_comment'></div>或其间向汉不坚，即令重纳有力量质子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1153715_comment'></div>或有自恃凶强，招抚不至者，则令刘平等非时伺便以强弩屠其种落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1153715_comment'></div>此策若行，足以破贼计而张国威也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1153715_comment'></div>军志云：「先人，有夺人之心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1153715_comment'></div>伏乞观此事机，早赐裁定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1153715'>三、甘凉首领，河西大族，继迁赐爵之后，德明承袭以来，仰恃国威，吞噬略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1153715_comment'></div>回鹘、吐浑，去朝廷地远，难收其效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1153715_comment'></div>惟有吐蕃与贼世仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1153715_comment'></div>罝勒斯赉住总噶尔，对贼巢穴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1153715_comment'></div>辖戬来都锡，据贼上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1153715_comment'></div>臣累奏乞昭罝勒斯赉进讨，破贼之日，许以西平之封，授二子灵夏节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1153715_comment'></div>又乞遣使都锡，抚存辖戬，令父子和协，共力破贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1153715_comment'></div>未奉回旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1153715_comment'></div>窃虑议者以为元昊既破，地入吐蕃，则罝勒斯赉势大，复生一敌，此议乃计之不熟者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1153715_comment'></div>平夏逆党，习于劫掠，吐蕃虽众，兵技不敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1153715_comment'></div>但欲使且牵贼势，必未能尽平狡穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1153715_comment'></div>若此际不收实效，而徇空言，非国家之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1153715_comment'></div>伏乞采臣前奏，早赐指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1153715_comment'></div>先朝博啰齐充灵州西面都巡检使，尚欲蛮夷相攻，遥制迁贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1153715_comment'></div>况罝勒斯赉向化，父子受官，不于此时遂其忠愤，差之毫釐，深可惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1153715_comment'></div>若前议得行，必恐昊贼未敢轻离巢窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1153715_comment'></div>伏乞圣鉴，深察此议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_1153715'>四、陕西四路兵甲不少，但地有险易，路有远近，寨栅有多少，军分有勇怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1153715_comment'></div>易防处合减兵，难守处当增兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1153715_comment'></div>兵之增减，即须察其险易，量其远近，计其城寨，均其勇怯，使各尽其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1153715_comment'></div>朝廷去边陲远，但因逐路所乞，差发士卒，所以臣前后累奏乞均匀加兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1153715_comment'></div>今来伏蒙朝旨，许令那移驻泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1153715_comment'></div>尚虑边臣占吝甲兵，鲜克公共。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1153715_comment'></div>方今西鄙，唯泾原、环庆最须备御，其两路犬牙相入，烽候相望，分之则势孤，并之则势大，物理之常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1153715_comment'></div>欲乞刘平罢鄜延安抚，兼泾原总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1153715_comment'></div>所贵表里相助，首尾相应，张大军势，壮励士心，亦防边之最要害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_104_1153715'>五、设使元昊谋犯边境，量其事势，岂能四路俱来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1153715_comment'></div>必是择一平易路分，并兵冲突。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1153715_comment'></div>其馀边界即分三二千骑往来出没，牵制我师，此贼计之可前料者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1153715_comment'></div>今来沿边兵马总而计之，数亦不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1153715_comment'></div>若各守路分则不足，互相策应，则最近者虽奉朝旨许令互相照应，窃恐缓急，边臣执守文义，不肯分兵相援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1153715_comment'></div>欲乞朝廷详酌，特降指挥，有贼马犯边，令四路互相关报，分兵策应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1153715_comment'></div>鄜延可以策环庆，秦陇可以策泾原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1153715_comment'></div>若此则沿边势合，军声大振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1153715_comment'></div>是计傥行，固足以预制狂贼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_113_1153715'>六、元昊旅拒以来，陕西加兵，所费粮饷不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1153715_comment'></div>尚赖累年关辅大稔，易为计置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1153715_comment'></div>今夏稍旱，二麦薄熟，粟豆苗晚，秋成未克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1153715_comment'></div>设使元昊复称臣纳款，沿边亦未敢班师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1153715_comment'></div>若宿兵塞上，边稼不丰，持久之谋，未知安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1153715_comment'></div>所以臣前奏乞令陕西诸州各招置神虎、保捷等军，各一两指挥，令遂州训练精熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1153715_comment'></div>却乞那移关东兵马归回，有警急则令逐州量留士卒外，并勾赴边臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1153715_comment'></div>一则关中土兵劲悍，耐于驰骋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1153715_comment'></div>二则减省沿边刍粟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1153715_comment'></div>三则可为悠久之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_123_1153715'>七、关右沿边，旧俗轻悍，喜为寇盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1153715_comment'></div>山林深阻，难为搜捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1153715_comment'></div>加以近边蕃户，以藏盗为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1153715_comment'></div>若敌骑犯边，人情恐动，或飞挽稍频，丁夫逃溃，互相扇摇，聚而为盗，关中官司不可不预为之计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1153715_comment'></div>咸平中，陕西转运司曾抄点保毅军六万八千馀人，防城备边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1153715_comment'></div>今来西陲安静多年，若遽行此法，则恐人户惊扰，别生寇剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1153715_comment'></div>前奏乞添置弓手三两倍，及乞置壮丁猎户，缓急可以防守城壁，把截要害，却那得正兵出入野战，此实今之寓令也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1153715_comment'></div>朝廷检详前奏，早赐行下付臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1153715_comment'></div>当司差官添置，候贼平日，即却罢遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1153715_comment'></div>一则不费供馈，坐获其用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1153715_comment'></div>二则不动群情，易为办集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1153715_comment'></div>比点保毅军及抄弓箭手，利害相万也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_135_1153715'>八、沿边小寨，多是曹玮建置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1153715_comment'></div>常时御备雠寨，防遏逋逃，似有小利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1153715_comment'></div>羌戎入寇，则难于处当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1153715_comment'></div>分兵固守，则州郡势危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1153715_comment'></div>守御不定，则所蓄刍粟，翻为寇粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1153715_comment'></div>又远近传闻，亦是亡一城寨，滋益贼气，且损军声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1153715_comment'></div>欲乞宣旨，沿边总管司勘会小寨，有兵少粮多，不关要害，先支沿边巡检等军马就食，尽粮草所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1153715_comment'></div>小寨逐月廪给，却令就大寨旋请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1153715_comment'></div>如有大段警急，势必难敌，则令并小寨士卒入大寨，把隘相杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1153715_comment'></div>一则免资寇盗，二则并得兵力，于要冲之处以御奔冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_145_1153715'>九、方今备边之计，最宜积谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1153715_comment'></div>故赵充国云：「籴三万斛谷，羌人不敢动矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1153715_comment'></div>况关辅税租有限，岁时丰俭难常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1153715_comment'></div>若卒调兵食，急赋横歛，则秦民轻悍，咨怨易兴，此不可不预计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1153715_comment'></div>近者有诏，入粟拜爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1153715_comment'></div>须是巨富之民，方能佐县官之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1153715_comment'></div>欲望朝廷诏关中州县，有犯过误连累之罪，情愿收赎者，许令召保，于沿边诸郡入粟赎罪，每铜一斤准粟五斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1153715_comment'></div>良民救患，何止乐输？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1153715_comment'></div>谅不踰年，塞下之粟必稍充羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1153715_comment'></div>宽宥过误，全民肤体，足以上副陛下至仁之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1153715_comment'></div>又虑议者以为国家全盛之际，不当货刑示弱，此议亦思之未切也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1153715_comment'></div>且爵者名器，尚许拜授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1153715_comment'></div>若宽刑赦过，得粟便民，比之拜爵，此为优矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_158_1153715'>十、候教习劲弩指挥，招置土兵，添差弓手，各有次序，即乞委任当司，差官拣选沿边冗兵于近里州军，及减骑军回关东，仍省沿边閒冗吏员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1153715_comment'></div>古者将帅授命本朝，皆假之威权，许以便宜，使得尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1153715_comment'></div>今来朝廷傥采所陈，则乞特依古制，借以衔勒，令竭疲驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1153715_comment'></div>仍乞指挥诸路总管司臣僚，今后每事遵禀安抚司指挥，不得怯懦自谋，妄说事理开奏，上惑朝听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1153715_comment'></div>如有寇贼奔冲，并须出兵，守险持重，伺便痛行杀戮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1153715_comment'></div>不得披城玩寇，放过贼马，令入他处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1153715_comment'></div>如违，以军法处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1153715_comment'></div>如此令行下，则边防畏懦之臣预谋战斗，不敢只作守城自全之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1153715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_166_1153715'>右谨具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1153715_comment'></div>伏以国家富有四海，重熙累洽，物力全盛，忠贤间出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1153715_comment'></div>昔魏有一段干木，晋人不敢窥西河；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1153715_comment'></div>江左有一谢安，苻坚丧百万之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1153715_comment'></div>以此计之，蠢尔羌戎，岂敢轻犯边境？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1153715_comment'></div>但元昊资性凶忍，轻背国恩，鬼得而诛，灭亡可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1153715_comment'></div>未授首间，朝廷之议，不得不过为备御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1153715_comment'></div>然贼境最多奸人，尽知缘边虚实，料其逆党聚谋，必须潜窥间隙，方敢作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1153715_comment'></div>若国家处置得宜，任人不杂，使陕西内外城邑，战守有备，元昊岂敢容易轻离巢穴，自取败亡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1153715_comment'></div>况关塞防秋，古今常事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1153715_comment'></div>《传》云：「无恃寇之不至，恃吾有以待之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1153715_comment'></div>此言诚得守边之要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1153715_comment'></div>顷继迁亡没，德明尚幼，族中亲属强梁者众，德明甚惧，仓惶送款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1153715_comment'></div>当时有司不能裂河南之地，封拓跋诸亲，令其势分间起，自相残贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1153715_comment'></div>而乃并锡真命，爱一孽童。<div class='inline'
