id='poem_sentence_180_1153715_comment'></div>数十年间，禄赐豢养，资寇粮者多矣，至今义士为之叹惋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1153715_comment'></div>是知此际岩廊裁处，不可不深图远算也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1153715_comment'></div>臣素业刀笔，不谙军旅，昨蒙推择，付以西事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1153715_comment'></div>虽继陈方略，多以迂阔，不合廷议，进退维谷，忧骇可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1153715_comment'></div>岂谓天慈更容访逮，拜恩沥恳，敢不自竭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1153715_comment'></div>其所陈十事，实臣在职见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1153715_comment'></div>夙夜惟忖，心虑所及，咸罄于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1153715_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈下两府裁酌，如稍近于理，即乞特赐详择施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1153715_comment'></div>敢不处奉德音，渐图远迹？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1153715_comment'></div>然而成大益者忌小害，获远利者无近效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1153715_comment'></div>方今许国者多，言事者众，或不周知利害，别议建明，事未成间，遽有更改，则边臣之计惑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1153715_comment'></div>此则须赖陛下倍赐主张，敕左右大臣专主斯议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1153715_comment'></div>自古内外相维则有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1153715_comment'></div>羊祐、杜预非张华主之，则不能平吴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1153715_comment'></div>石雄、刘沔非李德裕主之，则不能平上党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1153715_comment'></div>布在方策，较然可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1153715_comment'></div>若臣所陈庸昧，不远前谈，徒烦聪听，无足采录，即乞早选能吏，代臣经略西事，别询奇画，免误公朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1153715_comment'></div>矧将者三军司命，国家安危之主，不可一日轻付常才，忽于大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1153715_comment'></div>若西陲失备，则他寇相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1153715_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷深赐哀察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1153715_comment'></div>干冒宸严，臣无任祈天沥恳激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1153715_comment'></div>谨录状陈乞以闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_202_1153715_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年7月29日</a>　七月二十九日，在知永兴军任，徙知泾州，兼泾原秦凤路缘边经略安抚使、泾原路都部署。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b07f7fc4908c46749ad169bc580904c9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b07f7fc4908c46749ad169bc580904c9");'><span id='b07f7fc4908c46749ad169bc580904c9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1041')">1040-1041年</a>，56-57岁</div><div id='b07f7fc4908c46749ad169bc580904c9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年6月30日</a>　六月三十日，到知永兴军任，有谢表。作品：永兴再任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永兴再任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年6月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153602")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153602'>臣某言：伏奉敕命，就差充陕西路马步军都总管、兼经略安抚沿边招讨等使、知永兴军府事，已于六月三十日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153602_comment'></div>全秦地重，分陕寄隆，私窃忧惟，实难堪副<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153602_comment'></div>臣闻忠臣结绶之始，皆欲图报于本朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153602_comment'></div>义士执卷之初，尽期有济于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153602_comment'></div>或则封陲彻警，拳勇无自试之涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153602_comment'></div>或则贵要盈廷，寒素绝干进之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153602_comment'></div>鹓鸾困于羁緤，琬琰屈于煨尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153602_comment'></div>眇观旧编，代有遗叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153602_comment'></div>如臣者偶承人乏，出守军屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153602_comment'></div>蠢戾逋诛，暄凉改序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153602_comment'></div>连营谓之无勇，邻城诮其不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153602_comment'></div>数级未辰，何颜自处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153602_comment'></div>方祈退伏，式避劳能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153602_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇尊位皇帝陛下图制国经，召还枢辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153602_comment'></div>尽以虎臣之职，付兹虫篆之材，俾摅辕下之勤，得宣闑外之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153602_comment'></div>上可以建明策虑，裨宗社之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153602_comment'></div>下可以进退否臧，拯生灵之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153602_comment'></div>而况并护诸道，总摄列城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153602_comment'></div>要骈组于关中，宾从动色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153602_comment'></div>陈赐金于庑下，营府相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153602_comment'></div>渐倚办于官联，或有成于天幸，是则追芳往躅，获有竹帛之藏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153602_comment'></div>没齿九泉，免均粪壤之朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153602_comment'></div>敢不愈张胆势，益厉忠规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153602_comment'></div>戎警遂清，傥擅三明之猛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153602_comment'></div>恩章尽在，岂徒七宝之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153602_comment'></div>惟冀庙朝，更宽辔策，察持边之至重，念善后之为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153602_comment'></div>庶毕铢分，上酬覆焘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1153602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年6月30日</a>　六月三十日，到知永兴军任，有谢二府启。作品：永兴再任谢二府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永兴再任谢二府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年6月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153804")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153804'>右，某蒙恩授前件职，并知永兴军府，到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153804_comment'></div>出自坯陶，伏增感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153804_comment'></div>窃念某顷尝佔毕，素不知兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153804_comment'></div>特假幢麾，比长关中之戍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153804_comment'></div>亲临矢石，俄为陇上之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153804_comment'></div>徒肄业于蟠矛，罔追功于横草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153804_comment'></div>猥荷向隅之悯，犹书守塞之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153804_comment'></div>箕颍奥区，方膺于外徙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153804_comment'></div>河潼右壤，亟复于故栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153804_comment'></div>实总摄于百城，且并获于诸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153804_comment'></div>金印骈组，尽兼数使之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153804_comment'></div>玉帐建牙，爰当上将之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153804_comment'></div>倚办尤重，堪副诚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153804_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官登翼皇猷，布昭元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153804_comment'></div>图殪目中之敌，先增阃外之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153804_comment'></div>首念朴忠，骤加宠数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153804_comment'></div>既腾讥于帅贱，将责效于功除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153804_comment'></div>敢不祇慎戎昭，恪遵庙略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153804_comment'></div>武畅西海，傥横厉之有成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153804_comment'></div>生入玉关，固哀怜之是望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153804_comment'></div>永言报塞，敢惮勤劬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1153804_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年7月</a>　七月，在知永兴军任，有贺表。作品：贺皇太子授官表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇太子授官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153577")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153577'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153577'>臣某言：进奏院状报，伏审皇子授守太尉、忠正军节度等使、封寿国公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153577_comment'></div>宸闱集祉，天序飞荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153577_comment'></div>书轨所臻，人祇交庆<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153577_comment'></div>伏以帝出万物，苍震效乎长男；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153577_comment'></div>龙见大辰，前星表乎世子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153577_comment'></div>盖知有国之重，莫越元良之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153577_comment'></div>允属熙辰，宜崇钜典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153577_comment'></div>伏以皇帝陛下慎徽百度，为宪太宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153577_comment'></div>忠厚以布淳风，吉蠲以修明祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153577_comment'></div>万国被泽，溥洽于至和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153577_comment'></div>三圣在天，日监于盛治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153577_comment'></div>以是璿源浚发，真荫诞章，羲御吉祥，天枝毓粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153577_comment'></div>洪惟初载之美，丕显徇齐之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153577_comment'></div>仰尊宗庙之威，颇缓景风之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153577_comment'></div>是稽礼制，肇启国藩，袭惟帝之旧封，承曼寿之遐祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153577_comment'></div>瑞发文象，欢震华戎，凡在有生，率同大赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153577_comment'></div>臣出司边警，方谨秋防，阻诣太微之朝，仰庆少阳之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153577_comment'></div>望云载跃，倍万欣荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1153577_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年8月1日</a>　八月一日，在知永兴军任，与晁宗慤、王惟忠议边事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年8月</a>　八月，在知永兴军任，荐田况为陕西经略安抚司判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年9月</a>　九月，在知永兴军任，受诏遇紧急情况可便宜施行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年12月</a>　十二月，在知永兴军任，以宋仁宗手诏问师期，画攻守二策，遣韩琦、尹洙驰驿至京师，求决于宋仁宗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年1月18日</a>　正月十八日，在知永兴军任，上疏言攻守之策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年1月27日</a>　正月二十七日，在知永兴军任，拜宣徽南院使，有谢表。作品：谢授宣徽使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授宣徽使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年1月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153603")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153603'>臣某言：今月某日，男开封府推官、都官员外郎安期到府，蒙恩赐臣制告敕牒各一道，授臣依前官充宣徽南院使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153603_comment'></div>外廷敷告，近禁升荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153603_comment'></div>赏异及劳，感深沦髓<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153603_comment'></div>伏念臣性惭弦直，识本榆瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153603_comment'></div>列仕籍者四十年，贰柄臣者十五载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153603_comment'></div>一昨六周东夏，式荷于赐环；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153603_comment'></div>八月计廷，未遑于温席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153603_comment'></div>委朱墨而提剑，褫绅佩以属鞬，急骛秦关，旋驱陇道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153603_comment'></div>四迁岁景，顾蓐寝以何尝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153603_comment'></div>三徙军屯，恨胁疽之犹滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153603_comment'></div>宿师有日，敛策未辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153603_comment'></div>岂图不次之恩，误拜宣猷之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153603_comment'></div>入则奉承眷旨，切近中枢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153603_comment'></div>出则统率戎昭，总临诸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153603_comment'></div>铢分罔效，名数太优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153603_comment'></div>鸡忘失旦之愆，灰有再然之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153603_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊位皇帝陛下记怜遭遇，矜悯孤寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153603_comment'></div>推东禁之旧恩，缘先朝之雅意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153603_comment'></div>念臣省闱并命，止攀满岁之郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153603_comment'></div>边琐例迁，独授远藩之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153603_comment'></div>天心不忍，圣造曲成，置于五府之后陈，俾参四贵之荣缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153603_comment'></div>武非将表，诚乏于雄棱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153603_comment'></div>形在目中，誓平于蠢戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153603_comment'></div>庶阶尘雾，仰谢照临。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1153603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年1月27日</a>　正月二十七日，在知永兴军任，拜宣徽南院使，有谢二府启。作品：授宣徽使谢二府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授宣徽使谢二府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年1月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153803")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153803'>右，某蒙恩特授前件官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153803_comment'></div>元化均分，近司进拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153803_comment'></div>殆非功次，有误宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153803_comment'></div>伏念某偶以孤生，谬缘薄技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153803_comment'></div>攀仕涂者四十载，窃民政者十五城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153803_comment'></div>而况兼护将屯，怅绝弦之未逐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153803_comment'></div>创图羌事，惭唾掌以难裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153803_comment'></div>猥升四贵之华，颇玷十连之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153803_comment'></div>人讥多幸，自讼何劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153803_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官登翼大猷，矜嗟旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153803_comment'></div>量众恩于边琐，较前职于省闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153803_comment'></div>昭衡石之至平，洒霖雨之馀润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153803_comment'></div>万金屡费，适宽责帅之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153803_comment'></div>十使兼加，方切摧凶之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153803_comment'></div>敢不益张睛胆，更厉偏裨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153803_comment'></div>庶集群劳，仰酬坯冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153803_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1153803_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年1月28日</a>　正月二十八日，在知永兴军任，请以耿传参议军事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在知永兴军任，上疏请查近臣监督鄜延一路进兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年2月</a>　二月，在知永兴军任，劾奏尹洙擅自发兵，尹洙因此降授濠州通判。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年2月</a>　二月，在知永兴军任，上疏为韩琦伸冤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年4月6日</a>　四月六日，在知永兴军任，朝廷以陈执中为同陕西都部署，兼经略安抚缘边招讨等使，知永兴军，受诏判永兴军如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年5月3日</a>　五月三日，在知永兴军任，有诏令候陈执中至，领兵出巡边。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年5月23日</a>　五月二十三日，在知永兴军任，因与陈执中议事不合，受诏屯鄜州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泾川
-----detail

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1040')">1039-1040年</a>，55-56岁</div><div id='dcc06b6fb725498b8064e7f0785334cd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年8月28日</a>　八月二十八日，到知泾州任，有谢表。作品：泾州谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泾州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年8月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153601")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153601'>臣某言：伏奉诏敕，就差知泾州、充泾原秦凤路沿边经略安抚使兼泾原路驻泊马步军都总管，已于今月二十八日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153601_comment'></div>祗奉选抡，岂容胜任<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153601_comment'></div>伏念臣孤寒多难，愚拙自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153601_comment'></div>效官三十八年，临民十有一郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153601_comment'></div>尽心报国，竭节首公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153601_comment'></div>未尝自叙勤劳，苟求进用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153601_comment'></div>亦不潜附朋党，暗作阶缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153601_comment'></div>谗害至多，颠危不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153601_comment'></div>上则赖于圣世，次则恃于明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153601_comment'></div>况已及于暮龄，誓不移于前节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153601_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下照齐日月，道法乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153601_comment'></div>辨臣子之忠邪，察人情之真伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153601_comment'></div>念臣逮事先帝，早奉东朝，知臣静退不争，察臣朴忠有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153601_comment'></div>向者一离枢府，六换年华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153601_comment'></div>陛下召自别京，俾司邦计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153601_comment'></div>主摘山之议，较射策之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153601_comment'></div>定赏给之科，设禋燔之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153601_comment'></div>动畏入朝之嫉，始踰半岁之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153601_comment'></div>陛下察臣孤危，力垂保庇，属填边琐，付以戎昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153601_comment'></div>矧关辅之不宁，洎边防之少警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153601_comment'></div>臣兼程到职，庶事创图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153601_comment'></div>奏牍实繁，盖欲细闻于圣听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153601_comment'></div>当官不顾，实恐有误于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153601_comment'></div>所赖陛下远布宸聪，力排群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153601_comment'></div>念臣不为身计，务答主恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153601_comment'></div>罢陕右之剧繁，付回中之边要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153601_comment'></div>诏函俯降，使驲继临，过赐抚存，俾安惊惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153601_comment'></div>惟临泾之孤垒，控西鄙之要津，贼境不遥，烽烟在望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153601_comment'></div>戎事久废，楼橹未完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153601_comment'></div>敢不特创规模，渐加绥葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153601_comment'></div>又须陈请，上浼穆清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153601_comment'></div>乞倍赐于主张，庶早平于猖獗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153601_comment'></div>皇天后土，实鉴丹诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1153601_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年8月28日</a>　八月二十八日，到知泾州任，有谢二府启。作品：泾州谢二府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泾州谢二府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年8月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153807")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153807'>仰戴坯镕，实难堪副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153807_comment'></div>伏念某本由寒进，妄齿清流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153807_comment'></div>三品崇高，屡更于都座；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153807_comment'></div>十城罔养，遽剖于军符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153807_comment'></div>未尝练达兵钤，习知戎警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153807_comment'></div>猥奉临泾之后，敢辞负羽之行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153807_comment'></div>汉惟六郡之雄，唐兼四镇之重，宜得飞将，倚为长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153807_comment'></div>岂谓伏遇某官登翼大猷，斟酌元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153807_comment'></div>曲矜嗟于旧物，特选补于边屯，仍加置于使联，俾专司于武旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153807_comment'></div>望岩涂而驰恋，抚骈组以知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153807_comment'></div>惧上累于甄升，益俯加于策励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153807_comment'></div>兼程赴治，周览根心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153807_comment'></div>顾楼雉之未完，且租更之甚阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153807_comment'></div>烽烟在望，固当西鄙之咽喉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153807_comment'></div>营壁空存，无复北庭之组练。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153807_comment'></div>愿更宽于辔策，庶渐葺于封陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153807_comment'></div>愧荷依投，倍百伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1153807_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年11月</a>　十一月，在知泾州任，上疏请徙环庆部署刘谦为泾原部署。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年闰12月</a>　闰十二月，在知泾州任，上疏请于陕西增置土兵，因杨偕反对，议遂屈。作品：募土兵奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1153716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>募士兵奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年闰12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153716")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153716'>陕西防秋之弊，无甚东兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153716_comment'></div>一则不惯登陟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153716_comment'></div>二则不耐寒署；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153716_comment'></div>三则饮食难充，骄懦相习；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153716_comment'></div>四则廪给至厚，倍费钱帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153716_comment'></div>今募土兵，一则劲悍便习，各护乡土，人自为战；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153716_comment'></div>二则识山川道路，堪耐饥寒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153716_comment'></div>三则代东兵归卫京师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153716_comment'></div>四则岁省刍粮钜万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153716_comment'></div>五则今岁霜早，收聚小民，免至春饥，起而为盗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153716_comment'></div>六则增数十指挥精兵，詟伏贼气，乃国家万世之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153716_comment'></div>臣尝奏云，虑有不忠小人，以谋非己出，或为人所使，曲要破坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153716_comment'></div>果有杨偕上书，荧惑圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153716_comment'></div>且偕云「以寡击众，以一当百」，以臣所见，此乃虚言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153716_comment'></div>古者名将王剪，南取荆楚，须六十万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153716_comment'></div>韩信北举燕、赵，亦请益兵三万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153716_comment'></div>惟光武昆阳之战，乘累捷之后，前史曾云无不一当百，乃一时之言，非持久之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153716_comment'></div>若偕能之，乞命以代臣，尽减并边兵马，万人留百，百人留十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153716_comment'></div>果以此数平凶荡寇，即乞不次旌赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153716_comment'></div>如其不能，乃是挟私，或怀希望，亦乞严谴，以戒谗慝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1153716_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年4月</a>　四月，在知泾州任，荐周美为延州都监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年5月9日</a>　五月九日，在知泾州任，改忠武军节度使，有表辞忠武军节度使。作品：辞忠武军节度使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞忠武军节度使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年5月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153599")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153599'>今月臣男都官员外郎安期到州，伏蒙圣慈加食邑七百户、实封二百户，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153599_comment'></div>关塞宿兵，未歼于寇剧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153599_comment'></div>藩垣进律，遽改于旌麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153599_comment'></div>自揣非功，岂当虚受？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153599_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念猥承人乏，擢总戎昭，再徙军屯，连更岁籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153599_comment'></div>千金空费，曾无拙速之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153599_comment'></div>数级未闻，方省不能之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153599_comment'></div>甘从吏议，以避仕途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153599_comment'></div>敢谓恩章，亟迁土宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153599_comment'></div>虎符龙节，韬蔀室以生辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153599_comment'></div>画戟油幢，拥和门而增壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153599_comment'></div>然念兵氛尚盛，外寇未攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153599_comment'></div>田井惊骚，藩篱震荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153599_comment'></div>戎亭在望，交凑于边烽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153599_comment'></div>斋钺空存，未涂于衅血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153599_comment'></div>岂宜爵号，更及庸常？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153599_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下任人不疑，虚己求旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153599_comment'></div>镇以大体，责其成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153599_comment'></div>猖獗异谋，固非一日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153599_comment'></div>仓皇守备，恐失万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153599_comment'></div>乞更赐于主张，庶渐图于剪灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153599_comment'></div>南标铜柱，素尚于伏波；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153599_comment'></div>西出玉关，敢希于定远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153599_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1153599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年5月</a>　五月，在知泾州任，有表谢授忠武军节度使。作品：谢授忠武军节度使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授忠武军节度使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153600")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153600'>臣某言：伏奉诏书，以臣所上表，为蒙恩授忠武军节度使，乞且守旧官，所乞宜不允，即断来奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153600_comment'></div>西遐叛寇，未即灵诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153600_comment'></div>南夏奥区，误更宠爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153600_comment'></div>恭膺诏版，倍积腼颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153600_comment'></div>臣闻汉疏国封，由远近为别；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153600_comment'></div>唐制藩郡，以雄望为差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153600_comment'></div>逮于本朝，参用前典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153600_comment'></div>量次舍之遐迩，当功伐之重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153600_comment'></div>非服大劳，岂容妄受？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153600_comment'></div>如臣者比从省禁，出守边屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153600_comment'></div>虽乃志厉怀霜，力图尽敌，终以不知兵革，空骛岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153600_comment'></div>讫无毫纤，称报恩效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153600_comment'></div>众讪以之坌涌，名论由是顿衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153600_comment'></div>方乞避藏，式蔽蹇短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153600_comment'></div>岂谓遽颁制命，进改使麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153600_comment'></div>骤加衍食之荣，横窃景风之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153600_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下勤哀旧物，深恻上仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153600_comment'></div>念戍役之甚艰，悯关防之云远，特访攸司之议，曲推外徙之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153600_comment'></div>责实靡闻，无功增诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153600_comment'></div>重念保边之吏，再岁以还，或换郡进资，或书劳加秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153600_comment'></div>兵卫职重，止拜廉车；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153600_comment'></div>勋戚地尊，但加留务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153600_comment'></div>臣独涓刚日，诞告外廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153600_comment'></div>再望印章，重制旌节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153600_comment'></div>向则卿省并授，是以近而为荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153600_comment'></div>今则边琐递迁，矧以远而为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153600_comment'></div>超踰俦匹，度越等威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153600_comment'></div>不谓孤生，冒此殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153600_comment'></div>敢不根心励下，毕力防秋，冀效涓埃，仰酬覆载。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1153600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年5月25日</a>　五月二十五日，在知泾州任，徙陕西都部署，兼经略安抚使、缘边招讨使，知永兴军。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
富县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='989d2c928db94d529676317c9d5b6678_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("989d2c928db94d529676317c9d5b6678");'><span id='989d2c928db94d529676317c9d5b6678_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，57岁</div><div id='989d2c928db94d529676317c9d5b6678' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月7日</a>　七月七日，在知永兴军任，上疏乞调兵夫修浚鄜州城隍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　秋，在知永兴军任，上表乞换文资。作品：宣徽使乞换文资表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣徽使乞换文资表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153604")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153604'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153604'>臣某言：伏以文武设官，所以审材用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153604_comment'></div>小大制禄，所以辨勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153604_comment'></div>仰属昌辰，岂容冒处<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153604_comment'></div>伏念臣本由孤进，幸会先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153604_comment'></div>以直谅备史官，以忠实供言职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153604_comment'></div>斥奸邪之党比，减土木之修营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153604_comment'></div>以至外补江湖，内迁藩郡，刬除疾苦，赈济困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153604_comment'></div>累奉诏函，继褒吏课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153604_comment'></div>爰遇圣神出震，聪哲宣慈，靡替前恩，远颁宸翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153604_comment'></div>旋由起夺，入备论思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153604_comment'></div>力抗强臣，独持公议，建明国制，脩定刑章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153604_comment'></div>无一事曲佞宫闱，无一言阴结朋援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153604_comment'></div>帘箔之内，睿听熟闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153604_comment'></div>台阁之间，正人具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153604_comment'></div>而自出司东夏，六换流年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153604_comment'></div>救海岱之饥，生存之命亿计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153604_comment'></div>平黄腄之盗，安帖之城十馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153604_comment'></div>爰就改于别都，亦粗修于治迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153604_comment'></div>以是景祐四祀，进掌版图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153604_comment'></div>宝元初年，召计金谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153604_comment'></div>摘山奏格，齐议论于参差；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153604_comment'></div>备物成郊，均赏赉于丰约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153604_comment'></div>适属羌豪背惠，武旅乏人，遽董戎旃，出填边琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153604_comment'></div>谋皆凿空，事必创图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153604_comment'></div>躬冒险艰，常废寝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153604_comment'></div>若乃再临酆、霸，继戍泾、鄜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153604_comment'></div>新断川涂，肇营楼雉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153604_comment'></div>申严守备，耻较力于干戈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153604_comment'></div>禁止交关，谋困贼于岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153604_comment'></div>图上之策非一，采择之言亦多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153604_comment'></div>天地谅臣尽忠，吏民哀臣竭节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153604_comment'></div>但以数奇罕偶，众少难分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153604_comment'></div>不能饮马河源，灌烽陇坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153604_comment'></div>徒施固圉之力，克谨边防；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153604_comment'></div>讫无汗马之勋，能书竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153604_comment'></div>逮终更而罢使，叨善止以作藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153604_comment'></div>勤远至劳，积忧成疢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153604_comment'></div>是以恳祈内徙，求复故栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153604_comment'></div>虽叨中豫之迁，尚冒西陲之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153604_comment'></div>露章屡上，温诏未从，坐窃隆名，又兹踰岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153604_comment'></div>惟经费之犹广，享厚禄以何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153604_comment'></div>矧夫四贵之崇，实均三事之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153604_comment'></div>当任英武，入宣圣猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1153604_comment'></div>至乃六纛启行，万钱赋禄，自非勇冠行阵，功载旂常，眇觌前闻，未始虚授，讵容铅椠之士，久私玉帐之荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1153604_comment'></div>此者幸遇尊位皇帝陛下茂育时材，哀怜旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1153604_comment'></div>责实群后，分治九围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1153604_comment'></div>伏乞念臣忝事两朝，早更二府，罄输忠款，恪奉官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1153604_comment'></div>在公四十馀年，夙宵匪懈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1153604_comment'></div>临民一十五郡，勤拙粗施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1153604_comment'></div>冀以省闼前资，计廷旧职，近司印绶，两镇节旄，改职文资，俾安危恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1153604_comment'></div>誓竭当官之效，仰酬从欲之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1153604_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　秋，在知永兴军任，再上表乞换文资。作品：再乞换文资表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞换文资表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153605")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153605'>臣某言：伏奉诏书，以臣所上表，乞换文资，宜不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153605_comment'></div>优容过分，震悸交怀<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153605_comment'></div>伏以四贵联华，礼次丞弼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153605_comment'></div>十连作长，宠冠公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153605_comment'></div>若乃擢从武人，迁自勇爵，固当永锡车服，遐佩印章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153605_comment'></div>其或素隶简编，蚤备台阁，偶缘戎警，特假将麾，逮于终更，理当罢使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153605_comment'></div>而况幅员至广，经费实繁，亭候虽虚，租更尚阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153605_comment'></div>在于供拟，犹减旧常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153605_comment'></div>岂容具臣，横叨大禄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153605_comment'></div>矧惟五府，实总百工，象枢极之运行，系宗社之轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153605_comment'></div>端朝体国，礼绝地尊，讵宜州郡之寮，妄厕峰廊之列？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153605_comment'></div>伏望尊位皇帝陛下矜怜衰老，轸恤孤寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153605_comment'></div>念一介之常材，有千载之荣遇，录四方奔走之效，记两朝夙夜之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153605_comment'></div>采子方哀马之言，形汉宣求剑之意，倍推恩于前奏，俾归节于上台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153605_comment'></div>幸及桑榆之阴，再登鹓鹭之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153605_comment'></div>傥或全于危仆，誓更竭于朴忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153605_comment'></div>俯偻彷徨，期于得请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1153605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月18日</a>　十月十八日，在知永兴军任，罢节制，徙判河中府。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永济
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='385b3658695a4ceea4f56b820841fc72_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("385b3658695a4ceea4f56b820841fc72");'><span id='385b3658695a4ceea4f56b820841fc72_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1042')">1041-1042年</a>，57-58岁</div><div id='385b3658695a4ceea4f56b820841fc72' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年11月20日</a>　十一月二十日，到知河中府任，有谢表。作品：河中府到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河中府到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153611")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153611'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153611'>臣某言：伏奉敕命，就差判河中军府事，今月二十日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153611_comment'></div>十月期归，将终远戍，三年更尽，获改列城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153611_comment'></div>仰荷保全，敢忘循省<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153611_comment'></div>伏念臣本阶平进，逮事两朝，攀仕涂者四十春，陪时政者十五祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153611_comment'></div>大劳虽阙，薄效粗陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153611_comment'></div>向者六载徂东，班条盖久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153611_comment'></div>八月主计，座席未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153611_comment'></div>亟自省闱，出分将钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153611_comment'></div>军屯屡改，年籥四迁，徒历险艰，未歼蠢戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153611_comment'></div>又以谋皆凿空，事或创图，利远效迟，望轻人嫉，多言坌涌，沮议丛兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153611_comment'></div>每下列章，尚宽薄责，弥深策厉，冀塞矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153611_comment'></div>由是寝食外亏，精爽中耗，毒炭熏目，双瞳斗昏，边风切肌，两臂将废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153611_comment'></div>惧戎谍之窥间，常力疾以治戎，夙夜在勤，人神可谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153611_comment'></div>矧惟阃外之得失，实系天下之安危，一毫或差，九殒焉赎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153611_comment'></div>傥便文而自卫，固罔上以非忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153611_comment'></div>况复功名，良繄运命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153611_comment'></div>猿臂不耦，必难立于乃勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153611_comment'></div>虎颈飞行，将有待于来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153611_comment'></div>是以常布危欸，冀解剧权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153611_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下从欲象天，宝慈体道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153611_comment'></div>恤繇戍之忧苦，察臣下之艰辛，因分道以更张，俾班条而得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153611_comment'></div>穿杨善止，虽谢于前劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153611_comment'></div>有杕勤归，差安于众听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153611_comment'></div>傥逢针艾之益，稍扶蒲柳之衰，誓属右櫜，重趋绝塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153611_comment'></div>庶成来效，仰答大恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1153611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　本年，在知河中府任，徙知蔡州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汝南
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5171b17a79be4d728bdb863ad391fdb0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5171b17a79be4d728bdb863ad391fdb0");'><span id='5171b17a79be4d728bdb863ad391fdb0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1043')">1042-1043年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='5171b17a79be4d728bdb863ad391fdb0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　本年，到知蔡州任，有谢表。作品：蔡州到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153606")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153606'>臣某言：伏奉敕命，就差臣判蔡州军州事，仍放朝辞，取便路发赴本任，臣已于今月二十七日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153606_comment'></div>垂死馀息，特许生还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153606_comment'></div>陪京近藩，仍容卧治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153606_comment'></div>再造之赐，九殒莫酬<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153606_comment'></div>伏念臣谬忝艺文，妄干仕进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153606_comment'></div>先帝临轩之际，独首于六科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153606_comment'></div>陛下出阁之初，最先于诸傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153606_comment'></div>每惟际会，敢不矜修？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153606_comment'></div>其如资性庸驽，赋分蹇薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153606_comment'></div>虽圣君哀其拙直，而多士嫉其愚狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153606_comment'></div>出入两朝，当官者四十馀载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153606_comment'></div>周旋万里，典民者一十五城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153606_comment'></div>夙夜在公，固鬼神之可谅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153606_comment'></div>进退维谷，实孤孑之无依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153606_comment'></div>向者才入三司，始踰数月，属河湟旅拒，关辅绎骚，首得戎麾，往填边琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153606_comment'></div>肇谋器备，创设规模，经始关防，召募军旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153606_comment'></div>居则饮食无暇，出则昼夜兼行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153606_comment'></div>本先固圉之谋，冀成长辔之驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153606_comment'></div>其如众议罕合，物论易喧，朝廷切于平凶，搢绅惜其殚费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153606_comment'></div>所以未能出师陇首，饮马河源，尽坑豺狼，高筑京观，以致对分将阃，远戍边屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153606_comment'></div>冒暑中乾，饮泉内冷，药石无效，支体将堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153606_comment'></div>惟力疾以临戎，誓捐生而报主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153606_comment'></div>式逢例罢，就委藩条，方敢自陈，仰丐馀喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153606_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下仁深念旧，德务含生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153606_comment'></div>察三载之勤劳，辨多言之虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153606_comment'></div>念臣年光老暮，知臣纵迹单危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153606_comment'></div>深恻上仁，俾迁中豫，京畿颇近，医诊易逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153606_comment'></div>倘或稍驻桑榆，未填沟壑，誓竭狗马之效，仰答天地之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1153606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　本年，在知蔡州任，上表辞宣徽南院使，乞守旧官。作品：乞守旧官表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞守旧官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153607")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153607'>右，臣昨再上章，乞守旧官，就移汝蔡养疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153607_comment'></div>今蒙圣恩，移判蔡州，已奉表上称谢讫，所有乞守旧官仍奉朝请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153607_comment'></div>三岁终更，方求医于便郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153607_comment'></div>万钱赋禄，尚均宠于近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153607_comment'></div>深自忧惟，不遑启处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153607_comment'></div>伏念臣出于寒绪，幸会昌期，偶缘岁月之劳，叨尘文武之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153607_comment'></div>向以小羌旅拒，西鄙绎骚，特换戎旃，往填边琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153607_comment'></div>仰贪误选，曾不固辞，谓天幸可以横逢，谓战功可以妄立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153607_comment'></div>岁时骛过，诛纳无闻，仰荷宽恩，止从例罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153607_comment'></div>爰以饮泉感疾，伏枕踰时，形容已枯，支体交废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153607_comment'></div>命轻恩重，既报国之未终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153607_comment'></div>福过灾生，固徼荣之可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153607_comment'></div>以是恳祈旧职，望改近藩，冀遂养颐，或苏朽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153607_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下曲矜老暮，深悯勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153607_comment'></div>中豫名区，已更于郡组；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153607_comment'></div>元戎重器，尚假于戎麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153607_comment'></div>矧乃宣徽使名，所以表率诸将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153607_comment'></div>节制禄赐，所以宴犒三军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153607_comment'></div>当羌事之未平，顾经费之滋广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153607_comment'></div>若以拓边之宠，犹私卧治之臣，深屈至公，岂容虚受？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153607_comment'></div>望并俞于前请，庶克济于馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153607_comment'></div>梦寤徬徨，仰俟开可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1153607_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　本年，在知蔡州任，有表谢不允辞宣徽南院使。作品：谢诏书不允辞宣徽使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢诏书不允辞宣徽使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153608")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153608'>臣某言：今月十八日，进奏院递到诏书一道，伏蒙圣慈以臣三上章乞守旧官不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153608_comment'></div>爱下并容，尚假无功之宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153608_comment'></div>量能自愧，弥增有腼之颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153608_comment'></div>拜受以还，跼蹐无地<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153608_comment'></div>伏念臣早缘薄技，偶预辞林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153608_comment'></div>仰际休明，宠重文雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153608_comment'></div>以是沈迷篆刻，况瘁简编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153608_comment'></div>寤寐经营，止于粉墨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153608_comment'></div>出入闻见，不及弓刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153608_comment'></div>岂意误列将坛，谬分阃寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153608_comment'></div>三周岁律，四改军屯，备历艰危，躬践劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153608_comment'></div>怅靡逢于天幸，莫少振于军声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153608_comment'></div>罔养终更，忧虞成疢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153608_comment'></div>荐叨藩卫之便，获遂药石之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153608_comment'></div>曲被矜怜，已难胜负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153608_comment'></div>岂容更参四贵，犹长十连，隳多士廉退之风，索县官经给之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153608_comment'></div>以是屡罄肝胆，乞上印章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153608_comment'></div>仰干本朝，安敢饰避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153608_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下记怜旧物，勤恤外徭，不责犬马之劳，务推雨露之施，特颁诏检，靡辍使麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153608_comment'></div>渗漉之恩，诚为优绝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153608_comment'></div>支离之质，何以遑宁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153608_comment'></div>敢不励志米盐，精心医砭，抚养贫细，安聚荒饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153608_comment'></div>冀策励于尪残，用仰酬于焘育。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1153608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年3月21日</a>　三月二十一日，在知蔡州任，进户部尚书，充枢密使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年3月</a>　三月，在知蔡州任，有表辞户部尚书。作品：辞户部尚书表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞户部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153595")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153595'>臣某言：今月十九日，马递到府，伏蒙圣恩赐臣诰敕各一道，特授臣行户部尚书，散官勋封赐食邑如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153595_comment'></div>私悃再倾，宠章误分，俯循涯及，罔措心颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153595_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣获事两朝，仅逾三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153595_comment'></div>中外更践，微半策以堪书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153595_comment'></div>阀阅自窥，绝寸长之可录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153595_comment'></div>幸尹兴王之壤，矧兼主籥之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153595_comment'></div>地望甚高，朝委尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153595_comment'></div>但以孟诸之泽，旧为卑湿之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153595_comment'></div>向夏载涂，方冬未燥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153595_comment'></div>年光若是，疾势可虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153595_comment'></div>是以甫及再期，恭布危欸，冀更爽垲，以避郁蒸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153595_comment'></div>盖仰恋于清宸，望茍延于馀喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153595_comment'></div>岂期天造，特改地官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153595_comment'></div>载惧凿墉，甚于据蒺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153595_comment'></div>若乃庆恩均霈，久次例迁，伏限通规，所宜祗授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153595_comment'></div>而况臣东秦进秩，岁始三周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153595_comment'></div>雎水书劳，官无一善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153595_comment'></div>岂可因求僻左，邀取恩荣，倡侥倖之风，坏廉耻之俗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153595_comment'></div>舆情共骇，自讼何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153595_comment'></div>伏惟尊位皇帝陛下旰食九重，励精百度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153595_comment'></div>梦卜得于贤佐，物色访于良臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153595_comment'></div>方精汰于否臧，难误施于爵赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153595_comment'></div>伏望陛下识臣面目，察臣肺膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153595_comment'></div>念臣稍涉艺文，粗知廉耻，乞却还于旧职，誓永守于别都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153595_comment'></div>庶当责实之朝，免累及劳之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153595_comment'></div>天鉴在上，公议盈庭，傥不由衷，必有馀戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153595_comment'></div>实非矫节，愿赐允俞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1153595_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6e05c6a079a14b63b6444fbf75c9382c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6e05c6a079a14b63b6444fbf75c9382c");'><span id='6e05c6a079a14b63b6444fbf75c9382c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>，59岁</div><div id='6e05c6a079a14b63b6444fbf75c9382c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　本年，在知蔡州任，荐魏廷坚试学士院。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
许昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='461dc61c12eb4fa2aabe52fdb5a5c0ec_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("461dc61c12eb4fa2aabe52fdb5a5c0ec");'><span id='461dc61c12eb4fa2aabe52fdb5a5c0ec_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>，59岁</div><div id='461dc61c12eb4fa2aabe52fdb5a5c0ec' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月25日</a>　四月二十五日，到忠武军节度使本任，有谢表。作品：许州到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>许州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年4月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153609")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153609'>臣某言：伏奉敕命差赴本任，已于今月二十五日上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153609_comment'></div>出自保全，伏增感泣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153609_comment'></div>窃念臣人品驽下，世绪寒微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153609_comment'></div>事国四十馀年，临民十有五郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153609_comment'></div>言行无取，政化靡闻，空度岁时，动成嗤鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153609_comment'></div>策励之心徒切，顽闇之禀莫移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153609_comment'></div>昨以守塞终更，濒涯养疾，求还使节，未奉俞音，蒙降侍医，仅存残喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153609_comment'></div>日惭厚禄，内讼无功，安敢萌心，更欲希进？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153609_comment'></div>不图驿传，猥赐诏函，职尚备于藩侯，地又遥于边琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153609_comment'></div>敢稽召节，预述无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153609_comment'></div>爰夙驾以载驱，将晨趋而沥款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153609_comment'></div>有烦公议，合寘简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153609_comment'></div>一则臣尝假戎麾，首图羌事，三周岁籥，四改军屯，惟竭虑以保边，靡出师而尽敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153609_comment'></div>一则臣久从外补，罕遇时英，或但采于风闻，未深谅于衷悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153609_comment'></div>分甘弃置，式儆庸愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153609_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下察臣朴忠，念臣孤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153609_comment'></div>以遽申于避逊，况匪自于干祈，力辨群言，听还本任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153609_comment'></div>望宸居而至迩，瞻幄座以无由，伤弦之感自多，沦髓之恩难叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153609_comment'></div>都门回首，雨涕交颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153609_comment'></div>敢不深务省循，永怀兢畏，更励当官之节，上酬哀老之仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1153609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年7月4日</a>　七月四日，在忠武军节度使任，徙判亳州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年7月21日</a>　七月二十一日，在忠武军节度使任，罢宣徽南院使、忠武军节度使，改除吏部尚书、知亳州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
亳州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6046d4a45ac44bfa8beec6fe434ac51b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6046d4a45ac44bfa8beec6fe434ac51b");'><span id='6046d4a45ac44bfa8beec6fe434ac51b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>，59岁</div><div id='6046d4a45ac44bfa8beec6fe434ac51b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年8月14日</a>　八月十四日，到知亳州任，有谢表。作品：亳州到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1153610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亳州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年8月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153610")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153610'>臣某言：蒙恩就差知亳州军州事，今月十四日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153610_comment'></div>辞繁就逸，冀保于阽危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153610_comment'></div>竭志服劳，未酬于再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153610_comment'></div>深自惟忖，讵敢遑宁<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153610_comment'></div>伏念臣少失父兄，长无师友，守简编之陈迹，昧台阁之远猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153610_comment'></div>谓委分可以率天真，谓直躬可以成世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153610_comment'></div>独任蹇短，动至颠跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153610_comment'></div>一昨罢使洛郊，卧疾蒲阪，恳祈中豫，就访良医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153610_comment'></div>幸残喘之偶存，实荣望之都绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153610_comment'></div>不图星使，忽降芝函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153610_comment'></div>敢稽就日之行，仰废出纶之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153610_comment'></div>岂谓都门始入，遽隔中参；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153610_comment'></div>诏字未乾，亟还本任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153610_comment'></div>矧惟旧许，实首近藩，控亭传之要途，多衣缨之贵胄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153610_comment'></div>漂流之际，间隙易乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153610_comment'></div>在涣汗之尚还，何飞条之难集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153610_comment'></div>式属近臣致政，便郡濒淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153610_comment'></div>老物可憎，傥知惭而匿迹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153610_comment'></div>来宠将授，或观过以回心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153610_comment'></div>爰布恳私，上祈开可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153610_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下哀矜恤下，仁悯好生，察群议之忠邪，照物情之真伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153610_comment'></div>幽枉斯达，务昭责实之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153610_comment'></div>穷蹙可怜，特徇换州之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153610_comment'></div>载惟涡涣之下，适当湟潦之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153610_comment'></div>敢不修谨米盐，缮完图籍，励伤摧之晚节，苏震悸之羁魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153610_comment'></div>永罄涓诚，仰酬大庇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1153610_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cc739eb097c24fab8101e040337c5228_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc739eb097c24fab8101e040337c5228");'><span id='cc739eb097c24fab8101e040337c5228_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1045')">1043-1045年</a>，59-61岁</div><div id='cc739eb097c24fab8101e040337c5228' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　本年，在知亳州任，以台谏之议，上疏自辩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年1月18日</a>　正月十八日，在知亳州任，上疏乞降密旨，许便宜处断作乱者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年2月24日</a>　二月二十四日，在知亳州任，上新集《古文四声韵》五卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年3月</a>　三月，在知亳州任，荐张掞试学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年6月</a>　六月，在知亳州任，伪造书诏，倾陷石介、富弼等作乱，致范仲淹不安于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　九月，在知亳州任，荐裴明允试学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年12月16日</a>　十二月十六日，在知亳州任，加资政殿大学士，上表辞资政殿大学士。作品：辞资政殿大学士表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1153612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞资政殿大学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年12月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153612")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153612'>臣某言：某月日，三班奉职庞显到州，伏蒙圣慈赐臣敕牒一道，官诰一道，特授臣依前本官充资政殿大学士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153612_comment'></div>及准中书劄子，奉圣旨赐臣对衣金带鞍辔马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153612_comment'></div>恩惟图旧，讵可妄要？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153612_comment'></div>赏异及劳，岂容虚受？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153612_comment'></div>虔瞻出綍，愧极无颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153612_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153612_comment'></div>伏念臣本以孤生，误攀隽轨，顷由端右，出总戎机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153612_comment'></div>儒服治兵，易腾于众诽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153612_comment'></div>丹诚许国，惟誓于明祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153612_comment'></div>而继戍泾鄜，尝婴疾疠，昼则力疾备寇，夜则丸艾灼肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153612_comment'></div>矧夫义重于生，固知死且不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153612_comment'></div>委形骸于马革，等性命于鸿毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153612_comment'></div>初无片言，曾丐馀喘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153612_comment'></div>终更三岁，罢守一麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153612_comment'></div>视事踰时，中乾卧病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153612_comment'></div>累旬不起，九殒是滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153612_comment'></div>况乃萍津，计居内地，别无戎羌之御，遂祈汝蔡之迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153612_comment'></div>蒙降侍医，奔救沉瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153612_comment'></div>傥未邻于万鬼，誓复守于三边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153612_comment'></div>昨兹春夏之交，获逢针石之益，尚闻外警，临遣辅臣，爰拜露章，请陪边候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153612_comment'></div>但以于蕃之僻左，未知异俗之怀来，遽烦恩私，过极褒宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153612_comment'></div>伏见朝廷待下，赏劝从宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153612_comment'></div>臣子立身，出处有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153612_comment'></div>病不任事，则请告营医；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153612_comment'></div>疾既有瘳，则首公复业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153612_comment'></div>顾无可录，是惟厥常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153612_comment'></div>又念前春，常膺诏召，官有拥旄之重，礼无俟驾之行，不敢豫拜封章，力避贤路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153612_comment'></div>洎还旧许，方悟颛蒙，职巨寡谋，累国伤体，尚蒙宽宥，特逭简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153612_comment'></div>而况今者窃处近城，宴安自逸，求备边琐，跬步未前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153612_comment'></div>傥不恳辞，更贪异渥，固当自讼，何待人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153612_comment'></div>此者伏遇尊位皇帝陛下躬奋乾刚，布昭天律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153612_comment'></div>浚发明诏，洞判忠邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153612_comment'></div>登用正人，昈分枉直，陶唐之堲谗说，虞舜之察迩言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153612_comment'></div>臣方敢备列危衷，乞还成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153612_comment'></div>庶获全于晚节，更免遂于前非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153612_comment'></div>讵敢饰情，自昧丹臆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1153612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月</a>　正月，在知亳州任，有表谢授资政殿大学士。作品：谢授资政殿大学士表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1153613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授资政殿大学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153613")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153613'>臣某言：今月十二日，准枢密院马递到诏书一道，以臣所上表，为曾乞边任，蒙除资政殿大学士，及有恩赐，不敢当受，陈乞宜不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153613_comment'></div>人言可畏，实骇虚弦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153613_comment'></div>天听盖高，靡收涣汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153613_comment'></div>载揆官阀，罔措心颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153613_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>洪惟先朝，经始内殿，敞访对之地，谨备问之员，择人甚难，其职多阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153613_comment'></div>臣齿发空悴，绩效靡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153613_comment'></div>遭值圣时，叨窃荣禄，出入宰属，尘点皇僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153613_comment'></div>岂宜无功，更冒清选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153613_comment'></div>而况向者边书插羽，逻骑具装，秦陇威兵，酆雍谋帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153613_comment'></div>本朝以年辈最旧，勤拙粗施，擢于计廷，付于戎警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153613_comment'></div>力小负重，自见甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153613_comment'></div>就约辞危，臣节安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153613_comment'></div>内惟策励，誓首险艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153613_comment'></div>四改师屯，三周岁籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153613_comment'></div>羌事图上，必深料于安危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153613_comment'></div>王师务全，敢挑取于功誉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153613_comment'></div>终更罢戍，感疾营医，方丐近城，以救沉瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153613_comment'></div>不图诏检，促觐宸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153613_comment'></div>权舆谶工，据岗敢辨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153613_comment'></div>季长辞锐，饰貌难申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153613_comment'></div>省咎归涂，逃形近邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153613_comment'></div>监司按其粟错，都鄙陈于平条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153613_comment'></div>诗会馀蚳之文，简凝含酖之墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153613_comment'></div>寓趾泮水之罅，侧身攒羽之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153613_comment'></div>分沉死灰，趣毕残喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153613_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下宣精百度，观象九乾，刚健博临，高明广照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153613_comment'></div>深惟累洽之盛，宜杜私党之萌，或宗社阻凭干于众愤，则郊庙对越契于神欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153613_comment'></div>中发芝函，诞告鹓序，开悛止之路，戒浇竞之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153613_comment'></div>俾弃私于所天，当首公于王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153613_comment'></div>三辰增焕，六合顿清，人祇阜安，道路鼓舞，复我醲化，曾不崇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153613_comment'></div>臣方敢自上疾瘳，请还边候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153613_comment'></div>亟瞻出綍之训，翻诒跃冶之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153613_comment'></div>况夫愧汗未乾，悸胆犹破，茍遂非于覆辙，必腾诮于刑章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153613_comment'></div>爰叙忧兢，祈寝褒进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153613_comment'></div>仰承日月之鉴，俯哀蝼蚁之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153613_comment'></div>延登正人，访逮公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153613_comment'></div>谅臣孤立，察臣前劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153613_comment'></div>观靡盬之篇，采勤归之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1153613_comment'></div>诏驭幸之柄，图劝后之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1153613_comment'></div>敦谕至明，拜授斯宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1153613_comment'></div>忠臣共慰，旅魄交宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1153613_comment'></div>期报德于万分，誓捐生于百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1153613_comment'></div>感极惟涕，陈叙罔周。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1153613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年8月17日</a>　八月十七日，在知亳州任，拜宣徽南院使、河阳三城节度使、河东都部署、经略安抚使，判并州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
太原
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1e9636aca02b4cbeaf0e7924f4d0407d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1e9636aca02b4cbeaf0e7924f4d0407d");'><span id='1e9636aca02b4cbeaf0e7924f4d0407d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1046')">1045-1046年</a>，61-62岁</div><div id='1e9636aca02b4cbeaf0e7924f4d0407d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年9月</a>　九月，到知并州任，有谢二府启。作品：并州谢二府启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1153805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>并州谢二府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153805")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153805'>右，某蒙恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153805_comment'></div>西陲用武，寸效曾无；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153805_comment'></div>北道乏人，佥谋猥及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153805_comment'></div>负责斯重，戴恩则深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153805_comment'></div>咽喉要冲，股肱旧地，旁连马邑，直控雁门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153805_comment'></div>周宣中兴，兹尝薄伐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153805_comment'></div>汉武怀远，此焉观兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153805_comment'></div>屹然形胜之区，纷尔转斗之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153805_comment'></div>思得良士，倚为大藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153805_comment'></div>某素无兼才，暗于临事，精诚内耗，齿发久衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153805_comment'></div>上马据鞍，虽自矜于矍烁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153805_comment'></div>登车揽辔，尚有志于澄清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153805_comment'></div>然念孤蹇多艰，功名难偶，事方创置，谤辄随生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153805_comment'></div>孤根易摇，众口难辨，指尝戾臂，志不酬心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153805_comment'></div>尚赖丹扆至明，黄閤垂庇，曲藏痕殿，勤赐保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153805_comment'></div>勉策暮年，俾图后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153805_comment'></div>孟明屡辱，定收三战之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153805_comment'></div>孙膑何堪，终期万弩之发。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1153805_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年9月15日</a>　九月十五日，在知并州任，受诏军事不及中覆者，听便宜行之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年9月</a>　九月，在知并州任，请复置宦者为走马承受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年10月13日</a>　十月十三日，在知并州任，受诏升祔支赐，准两府例。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年10月19日</a>　十月十九日，在知并州任，上疏言己前充宣徽南院使，进奉、请受、赏赐皆准两府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年11月</a>　十一月，在知并州任，上疏言石介诈死，富弼使其入契丹谋起兵，朝廷因下诏验石介生死。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　约于本年，在知并州任，使其仆贸易，为所侵盗，至杖杀之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年1月11日</a>　正月十一日，在知并州任，上疏请亲领兵巡边，经置西北事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在知并州任，上疏言将来分屯河东路军马事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在知并州任，拜同中书门下平章事、河北安抚使，判大名府，兼北京留守。<br /></div>
-----end
