-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ac7d40c7fb264c41a689d8676eb78eb6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ac7d40c7fb264c41a689d8676eb78eb6");'><span id='ac7d40c7fb264c41a689d8676eb78eb6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1049')">1048-1049年</a>，64-65岁</div><div id='ac7d40c7fb264c41a689d8676eb78eb6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年6月9日</a>　六月九日，到知河南府任，有谢表。作品：河南府到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1153614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河南府到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年6月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153614")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153614'>臣某言：伏奉制命，差判河南府兼西京留守司公事，已于今月九日到任讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153614_comment'></div>遍陪五府，历守三都，逢辰之荣，旷古无并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153614_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣人品至下，门绪素寒，孤苦一生，迍邅万状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153614_comment'></div>岁月迈如邮置，筋力困于泥涂，谋已弗臧，举世诒诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153614_comment'></div>往岁召于中豫，入长近枢，昧逊让于时贤，实格废于成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153614_comment'></div>间者起自涡曲，往帅晋阳，尝面对于迩颜，乞永从于外补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153614_comment'></div>惧以危迹，复玷清时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153614_comment'></div>不图再岁之间，忽补鼎司之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153614_comment'></div>遽迁右府，逮越周星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153614_comment'></div>掌虎旅之伍符，宣龙韬之圣略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153614_comment'></div>虽矍铄而自勉，终邅坎以难工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153614_comment'></div>朝多正人，日有公议，烦黄屋之掩蔽，辱丹扆之辨明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153614_comment'></div>备位无颜，谢负何地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153614_comment'></div>而况钜贤让爵，哲士辞荣，晏然自安，亦不知避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153614_comment'></div>尚赖伏遇尊位皇帝陛下察臣闇懦，止是颛愚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153614_comment'></div>悯臣忧劳，别无他累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153614_comment'></div>力排时论，敷告外廷，进秩师垣，均劳洛邑，俾其休逸，保乃衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153614_comment'></div>息偃无营，冀渐生于髀肉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153614_comment'></div>责望不及，将永脱于风波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153614_comment'></div>誓输乐职之勤，仰酬哀老之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153614_comment'></div>瞻望阙廷，臣无任戴天荷圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153614_comment'></div>谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153614_comment'></div>臣某诚荣诚感，顿首顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1153614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年12月</a>　十二月，在知河南府任，有贺表。作品：留司官吏贺表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1153578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留司官吏贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153578")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153578'>臣某等言：伏睹进奏院状报，十二月三日册婉容张氏为贵妃者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153578_comment'></div>扬命外朝，讲仪中禁，褒进天妃之贵，顺承宸极之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153578_comment'></div>盛典惟行，群生共庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153578_comment'></div>臣等诚欢诚抃，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153578_comment'></div>恭惟尊位皇帝陛下穆清居位，浚哲在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153578_comment'></div>舜治无为，禹功不伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153578_comment'></div>既格太宁之化，允资内辅之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153578_comment'></div>申敕柄臣，奉将册礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153578_comment'></div>分采章于六服，冠品列于九嫔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153578_comment'></div>弥增轩曜之光，实亚坤仪之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153578_comment'></div>用宣阴教，永助帝猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153578_comment'></div>臣等幸预通班，获逢熙运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153578_comment'></div>仰宫闱之多庆，倾海县以同欢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1153578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年7月4日</a>　七月四日，在知河南府任，受诏赴河阳三城节度使本镇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年7月11日</a>　七月十一日，在知河南府任，加兼侍中，上表辞兼侍中。作品：辞兼侍中表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1153616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞兼侍中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年7月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153616")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153616'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153616'>臣某言：今月十八日，侄女婿权国子监主簿高直温到西京，伏蒙圣慈赐臣制命官诰，特授臣依前检校太师兼侍中，仍加食邑实封者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153616_comment'></div>拥旄本镇，已俯遂于厥诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153616_comment'></div>参乘东台，实迥踰于初望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153616_comment'></div>闻命震恐，启处不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153616_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣近以衰残，迫于迎劳，求还近便之任，止避旷殆之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153616_comment'></div>向或所镇并边，郡将无阙，稍涉毫芒之幸，敢萌迁徙之求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153616_comment'></div>况在前章，备陈丹款，实无一字，少饰片言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153616_comment'></div>其或外叙衰残，内怀希觊，有腼颜面，更睹士流，设逭典刑，当有阴罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153616_comment'></div>不图圣眷，遽锡制恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153616_comment'></div>若以念旧均慈，则臣累官已重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153616_comment'></div>若以畴劳第赏，则臣宣力无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153616_comment'></div>伏况朝廷要官，挑取者难久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153616_comment'></div>天下公议，巧避者愈彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153616_comment'></div>傥诒有隧之深讥，将累挂车之善止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153616_comment'></div>此者伏遇尊位皇帝陛下慎徽百度，精汰庶官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153616_comment'></div>赏必计功，禄无废德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153616_comment'></div>矧乃纳言之重，当图汗马之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153616_comment'></div>岂容蒲柳之衰，更窃金貂之赐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153616_comment'></div>伏望陛下哀臣介拙，悯臣忧危，特寝异恩，听守前职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153616_comment'></div>垂皤皤之发，庶无责于时贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153616_comment'></div>伐坎坎之轮，免有妨于来宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153616_comment'></div>誓坚廉让之节，仰酬覆露之仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1153616_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
孟州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='da1795e7cdab42cc9d305661a5d6ee91_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("da1795e7cdab42cc9d305661a5d6ee91");'><span id='da1795e7cdab42cc9d305661a5d6ee91_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1051')">1049-1051年</a>，65-67岁</div><div id='da1795e7cdab42cc9d305661a5d6ee91' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年7月21日</a>　七月二十一日，到知孟州任，有谢表。作品：孟州到任谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1153615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孟州到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年7月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153615")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153615'>臣某言：伏奉敕命赴孟州本任，于今月二十一日上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153615_comment'></div>班宽大之诏，存拊吏民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153615_comment'></div>歌中和之诗，祗见参佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153615_comment'></div>勉厉衰朽，少谢矜怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153615_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣蚤以诸生，幸逢清世，勤劳四纪，险易一生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153615_comment'></div>筋力困于泥涂，髀骨消于亭隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153615_comment'></div>迄无纤效，纪在本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153615_comment'></div>昨以窃位枢廷，均劳洛宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153615_comment'></div>宠冠九域，地首三都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153615_comment'></div>太高则危，暴长将折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153615_comment'></div>而况驿传至远，迎劳尤艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153615_comment'></div>属本镇之缺官，爰露章而布款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153615_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下宝慈体道，求旧敦仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153615_comment'></div>老马力殚，靡忘前效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153615_comment'></div>伤禽胆破，知避虚弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153615_comment'></div>特允三城之求，俾纾四体之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153615_comment'></div>然而据河山之要，控魏晋之冲，古多重兵，代委名将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153615_comment'></div>方今租庾至阙，闾里尤虚，浮梁有搴茭之役，长堤乏为楗之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153615_comment'></div>生以驭福，实衔佚老之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153615_comment'></div>职思其忧，敢怠匪躬之节？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153615_comment'></div>唯期夙夜，仰答照临。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1153615_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年7月</a>　七月，在知孟州任，有表谢授兼侍中。作品：谢授兼侍中表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文庄集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1153617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授兼侍中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153617")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153617'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153617'>臣某言：今月二十二日伏奉诏命，以臣所上表，蒙恩特授检校太师兼侍中，乞守旧官，不许辞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153617_comment'></div>芝函睿札，谕旨于十行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153617_comment'></div>蝉冕要官，升华于一品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153617_comment'></div>顾兹非据，何但若惊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153617_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏以参乘东台，纳言内幄，访延密政，出纳大猷，制爵至崇，兼官尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153617_comment'></div>或以尊懿戚，或以驭战功，近世儒臣，罕得超授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153617_comment'></div>如臣者材品至下，门地素寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153617_comment'></div>偶阶片文，仰会先圣，冠制策之亲选，预东禁之精求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153617_comment'></div>夜寐夙兴，更中外者四纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153617_comment'></div>兴利除害，贯险易而一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153617_comment'></div>若乃赈汉右饿殍四十五万馀口，屏江西巫觋一千三百馀家，屡承纶綍之褒，颇首循良之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153617_comment'></div>伏遇尊位皇帝陛下重晖继照，求旧推恩，擢参垂箔之近班，实罄戴君之亮节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153617_comment'></div>洎乃海隅聚寇，责以敉宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153617_comment'></div>关内治兵，委之经画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153617_comment'></div>偶无愆素，粗得全师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153617_comment'></div>圣念畴劳，召长枢府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153617_comment'></div>又以并汾帅满，起付戎轺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153617_comment'></div>赵魏卒骄，就更边戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153617_comment'></div>载严军律，稍契前筹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153617_comment'></div>宸慈记功，命亚台席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153617_comment'></div>终以久供外役，罕接隽游，靡恤寸长，务责全德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153617_comment'></div>一则以聚羌远塞，是臣尽敌无能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153617_comment'></div>一则以雨土中都，乃臣治边所召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153617_comment'></div>乞放还以旧任，洎追返于涣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153617_comment'></div>上赖陛下谅臣朴忠，悯臣穷蹇，力排群议，特逭简书，断自穆清，裁于宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153617_comment'></div>伤摧自悼，矍铄何堪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153617_comment'></div>寻蒙进秩师垣，均劳洛宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153617_comment'></div>而又密涂交会，右族盛强，寘法未能，废刑岂敢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153617_comment'></div>至有诬其加箠，搆以凭舆，复赖保全，为臣辩雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153617_comment'></div>再念臣本镇甚迩，郡将未除，爰叙艰危，求换繁剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153617_comment'></div>得请之日，被赐已深，如脱樊笼，顿解缰锁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153617_comment'></div>岂谓荐颁明制，误赏无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153617_comment'></div>补外常仪，靡谐于三让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153617_comment'></div>发中温诏，促预于七车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153617_comment'></div>敢不策励羸躯，矜持晚节，毕桑榆之暮齿，答穹厚之鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1153617_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年8月6日</a>　八月六日，在知孟州任，上疏乞长假，于东京寻求医药。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年10月2日</a>　十月二日，在知孟州任，以明堂礼成，改武宁军节度使、徐州大都督府长史，徙封郑国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年10月</a>　十月，在知孟州任，以明堂礼毕，受赐袭衣、金带、器币、鞍勒马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年4月14日</a>　四月十四日，在知孟州任，作《重校妙法莲华经序》<div id='poem_1153832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1153832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1153832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重校妙法莲华经序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年4月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24192, "北宋", "夏竦", "poem_title_1153832")'>夏竦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1153832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1153832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1153832'>三世诸佛为众生出现，證无所證，得无所得者，一大士而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1153832_comment'></div>妙万化而无象，应群有而难名，不著世间，犹如莲华，故竺乾大士集灵鹫遗言，曰《萨达磨奔茶利迦》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1153832_comment'></div>魏梵僧支强梁接译于交阯，初成六卷，翻萨达磨为妙法，奔茶利迦为莲华，是名《法华三昧》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1153832_comment'></div>晋燉煌僧竺法护译为十卷，名《正法华》，分二十七品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1153832_comment'></div>后秦鸠摩罗什益《普门》一品，译为七卷，名《妙法莲华》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1153832_comment'></div>隋崛那笈多益《药草喻品》之半，以《提婆达多品》入《塔品》，名《添品法华》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1153832_comment'></div>唐道宣律师叙云：「三经文旨互陈，时所崇尚皆用秦本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1153832_comment'></div>自汉至唐六百馀祀，受持盛者无出此经」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1153832_comment'></div>五代以还，诸侯僭据，字音句读，方言多误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1153832_comment'></div>国家混一寰海，圣上尊用三教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1153832_comment'></div>余家世奉佛，乃取世传诸本及化外旧经，释文擿句，数自参较。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1153832_comment'></div>又以悉昙梵夹，傍行右读，中原传译，始创卷轴，讨论重复，卷舒繁数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1153832_comment'></div>因观近世图籍，镂刻摹印，缀黏成册，差便于古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1153832_comment'></div>由是命工仿则，肇制此经，庶几学者易为究览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1153832_comment'></div>此经《序品》至《劝发》十馀万言，贯穿诸宗，融通万法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1153832_comment'></div>或伽陀孤起，或祗夜应颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1153832_comment'></div>文有广略，以接三根；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1153832_comment'></div>机有深浅，以酬众请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1153832_comment'></div>丧实际者为之譬宝藏，执涅槃者为之指髻珠，沦世苦者为之谕污宅，乐小法者为之演化城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1153832_comment'></div>辟甘露之门以来众轨，均大云之泽以遍群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1153832_comment'></div>大方无隅，则有地墨劫尘之谈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1153832_comment'></div>至神无方，则有眉毫舌相之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1153832_comment'></div>会权实之戏论，设顿渐之假名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1153832_comment'></div>使三兽渡河，并臻其量；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1153832_comment'></div>五愆凭轼，各应其缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1153832_comment'></div>讽诵可以殖福田，解说可以标慧炬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1153832_comment'></div>大慈方便，其在兹乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1153832_comment'></div>至哉，清净灵觉，廓大虚而含法界；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1153832_comment'></div>光明宝藏，消幻想以契真如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1153832_comment'></div>境既对忘，心将安寄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1153832_comment'></div>见有迷悟，体无去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1153832_comment'></div>妙本圆常，超然独立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1153832_comment'></div>资始万行，孰除其方？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1153832_comment'></div>若乃以解脱为盖缠，以照觉为封累，掩室摩竭，杜口毗耶，名言道断，思惟路绝，则神而明之，在乎其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1153832_comment'></div>然而能趣百善者信也，善度众苦者解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1153832_comment'></div>信解之初，必由缘感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1153832_comment'></div>皦月不能现空器，膏雨不能生槁木，后学菩萨幸精进而求诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1153832_comment'></div>时皇祐三年夏四月乾元节日谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1153832_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

禹州
